TL;DR: 提出DnA（去噪注意力）机制，通过正负查询分离相关与无关特征，增强子空间间区分度，在ViT-B上实现ImageNet-1K上0.8%的提升，并在视频理解等多个任务中表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准softmax在多头注意力中会产生噪声注意力模式，削弱关键特征表示，影响模型性能。

Method: 引入正查询识别正确类别特征，负查询识别无关但接近的特征，将两者交互投影到两个具有更大主角度的子空间中，实现更好的子空间分离与判别性。

Result: 在ImageNet-1K上相比基线提升0.8%，在视频理解任务中提升1.8%，在视频大模型中提升0.5%，且实验验证了双子空间设计和去噪效果的有效性。

Conclusion: DnA通过显式分离相关与无关特征，有效抑制噪声注意力，显著提升视觉感知任务的性能，具备良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: The softmax activation in multihead attention (MHA) is the de facto standard for attention-based models in visual perception tasks. However, standard softmax can produce noisy attention patterns that dilute relevant features and degrade its performance. In this paper, we propose Denoising Attention or DnA, in which, first, a positive query identifies which image features belong to the correct class, and a negative query identifies closely associated but irrelevant image features. DnA then projects these interactions into two distinct subspaces with larger principal angles, promoting subspace separation and improved discriminability. Using a ViT-B backbone, our proposed DnA achieves an absolute gain of 0.8% on ImageNet-1K compared to the baseline. We further show improvements across multiple visual understanding tasks, including video understanding with video transformers (1.8%) and video LLMs (0.5%). Our extensive empirical analyses justify the design choices involving two interacting subspaces and the denoising effect of DnA.

</details>


### [92] [DanceOPD: On-Policy Generative Field Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27377)
*Wei Zhou,Xiongwei Zhu,Zelin Xu,Bo Dong,Lixue Gong,Yongyuan Liang,Meng Chu,Leigang Qu,Lingdong Kong,Wei Liu,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DanceOPD框架，通过在流匹配模型中使用基于策略的生成场蒸馏，实现文本到图像、局部编辑和全局编辑等多能力的统一与协同。该方法将每个样本路由至特定能力场，利用低噪声学生诱导状态进行训练，以简单速度MSE为目标，使学生从自身回放状态查询专家能力场，从而有效整合不同能力。实验表明，该方法在多能力组合、真实感场吸收和无分类器引导吸收方面均表现优异，显著提升目标能力并保持生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像生成模型难以自然统一文本到图像生成、局部编辑和全局编辑等多样化能力，这些能力常存在冲突，如编辑会损害文本到图像性能，且全局与局部编辑相互干扰，导致多能力有效融合成为核心挑战。

Method: 提出DanceOPD框架，一种基于策略的生成场蒸馏方法，将各能力源定义为共享流状态空间上的速度场。每个样本被路由至对应能力场，学生模型在自身回放状态上查询低噪声的专家状态，并以速度均方误差（MSE）作为训练目标，实现多能力学习与融合。同时支持分类器自由引导等操作符定义的场。

Result: 在文本到图像生成、图像编辑、真实感场吸收及分类器自由引导吸收等多个任务上，DanceOPD展现出更强的多能力组合能力，有效增强目标能力，同时保持原始生成质量，验证了其在流匹配模型中进行生成场蒸馏的实用性与有效性。

Conclusion: DanceOPD为流匹配模型中的生成场蒸馏提供了一条实用路径，解决了多能力图像生成中能力冲突与融合难题，推动了通用图像生成模型的发展。

Abstract: Modern image generation demands a single model that unifies diverse capabilities, including text-to-image (T2I), local editing, and global editing. However, these capabilities are rarely naturally aligned and often conflict. For instance, editing tends to degrade T2I performance, while global and local editing interfere with each other. Consequently, effectively composing these capabilities has become a central challenge for image generation model training. To tackle this, we introduce DanceOPD, an on-policy generative field distillation framework for flow-matching models that routes each sample to one capability field, queries one low-noise student-induced state, and trains with a simple velocity MSE objective. With each capability source defined as a velocity field over the shared flow state space, the student learns from fields queried on its own rollout states to compose expert capabilities. This formulation also absorbs operator-defined fields such as classifier-free guidance. Comprehensive experiments on T2I, editing, realism-field absorption, and CFG absorption show that our approach improves multi-capability composition, strengthening target capabilities while preserving anchor generation quality. We believe this work establishes a practical route for generative field distillation in flow-matching models.

</details>


### [93] [Paying More Attention to Visual Tokens in Self-Evolving Large Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27373)
*Shravan Venkatraman,Ritesh Thawkar,Omkar Thawakar,Rao Muhammad Anwer,Hisham Cholakkal,Salman Khan,Fahad Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出VISE（Visual Invariance Self-Evolution），一种纯无监督的自演化框架，通过几何和语义不变性奖励直接正则化模型的视觉条件策略，以解决现有自演化多模态大模型中存在的视觉欠条件问题。该方法不依赖外部标注、专用角色或奖励模型，在未标记图像上训练，显著提升图像描述与视觉问答等任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自演化多模态模型虽在无监督设置下提升视觉推理能力，但其多角色自对弈与自一致性奖励机制仅优化答案一致性，忽视视觉内容关注，导致模型过度依赖语言先验而非图像信息，出现视觉欠条件现象，影响视觉-语言理解任务性能。

Method: 提出VISE框架，包含两个互补的基于不变性的奖励：几何不变性奖励，确保在已知变换下空间一致性；语义不变性奖励，惩罚无证据生成行为，要求模型在预测区域被扰动时能识别证据缺失。整个框架单一模型实现，无需专门角色、外部奖励模型或标注数据。

Result: 在18个基准测试中验证有效性。以Qwen3-VL-2B为基础，VISE在COCO上提升16.85 CIDEr，TextCaps上提升19.66 CIDEr，减少5.0个Chair-I点的对象幻觉，并在四个模型家族和不同规模下表现出良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: VISE通过引入视觉不变性奖励有效缓解了自演化多模态模型中的视觉欠条件问题，显著提升了视觉-语言理解任务的表现，且具有良好的通用性和可扩展性，为无监督多模态学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recently, self-evolving large multimodal models (LMMs) have received attention for improving visual reasoning in a purely unsupervised setting. However, multi-role self-play and self-consistency reward schemes in existing self-evolving LMMs optimize answer agreement without ensuring the decoder attends to visual content, relying instead on statistical language priors to produce self consistent outputs. This leads to a persistent failure mode we term visual under-conditioning, where the decoder relies on language priors rather than the image during generation, manifesting as insufficient attention to visual tokens. As a result, current self-evolving LMMs struggle on vision--language understanding tasks such as image captioning and visual question answering. To address this, we propose VISE (Visual Invariance Self-Evolution), a purely unsupervised self-evolving framework that directly regularizes the model's visual conditioning policy through two complementary invariance-based rewards: a geometric invariance reward that enforces spatial consistency under known transformations, and a semantic invariance reward that penalizes evidence-agnostic generation by requiring the model to recognize the absence of evidence when predicted regions are perturbed. VISE operates within a single model without specialist roles, external reward models, or annotations, and is trained on raw unlabeled images. Experiments on 18 benchmarks demonstrate the efficacy of our approach. Using Qwen3-VL-2B as the base model, VISE achieves gains of $+16.85$ CIDEr on COCO and $+19.66$ CIDEr on TextCaps, reduces object hallucination by $5.0$ Chair-I points, and generalizes across four model families and scales. Our code and models are available at https://mbzuai-oryx.github.io/VISE

</details>


### [94] [Ask, Solve, Generate: Self-Evolving Unified Multimodal Understanding and Generation via Self-Consistency Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27376)
*Ritesh Thawkar,Shravan Venkatraman,Omkar Thawakar,Abdelrahman Shaker,Fahad Khan,Hisham Cholakkal,Salman Khan,Rao Muhammad Anwer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需人工标注或外部奖励模型的自演化训练框架，通过内部角色（提议者、求解者、生成者）实现视觉理解与图像生成能力的自主提升。利用自衍生的一致性信号进行训练，并引入基于令牌预测不确定性的难度信号（STE）以稳定学习过程。在图像生成方面，采用多尺度内部评估机制，结合问答一致性和循环一致性描述，形成求解者驱动的耦合关系。该框架适用于多种架构（如BLIP3o、BAGEL、VARGPT-v1.1），并在8项理解指标上持续优于基线模型，在BAGEL上实现MMMU提升3.5%及生成性能从82%到85%的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前统一的大规模多模态模型仍依赖人工标注或外部奖励模型进行后训练，限制了其自主进化能力。本文旨在探索仅使用无标签图像能否实现视觉理解与图像生成能力的自我增强。

Method: 提出一个自演化训练框架，包含三个内部角色：Proposer生成视觉问题，Solver回答并评估问题，Generator合成图像。训练完全基于自衍生的一致性信号，不依赖人类标注或外部奖励模型。引入Solver Token Entropy (STE)作为连续难度信号以稳定学习；设计多尺度内部评估方案，结合问答一致性与循环一致性描述，建立求解者与生成器之间的反馈耦合。

Result: 在八项视觉理解任务中，该方法均优于对应基础模型。在BAGEL架构上，实现MMMU指标+3.5%的绝对提升，生成评估（GenEval）性能从82%提升至85%。框架兼容多种主流模型架构，仅需各模型原有的提示与生成接口。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，仅通过无标签图像和自演化机制，即可实现大规模多模态模型在视觉理解与图像生成上的协同优化。所提框架具有高度可迁移性与稳定性，为构建真正自主进化的多模态系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Most unified large multimodal models (LMMs) that support both visual understanding and image generation still rely on curated post-training supervision, such as human annotations, preference labels, or external reward models. We ask whether a unified LMM can improve both abilities autonomously using only unlabeled images. We propose a self-evolving training framework with three internal roles: a Proposer that generates visual questions, a Solver that answers and evaluates them, and a Generator that synthesizes images. Training uses only self-derived consistency signals, without human annotations, preference labels, or task-trained external reward/judge models. To stabilize learning, we introduce Solver Token Entropy (STE), a continuous difficulty signal based on token-level prediction uncertainty that remains useful even when sample-level consistency becomes unreliable. For image generation, we design a multi-scale internal evaluation scheme that combines question-answer fidelity scoring with cycle-consistent captioning. This creates a solver-mediated coupling, where better visual understanding enables more reliable generation assessment and stronger internal training signals. The framework preserves the same role decomposition, reward logic, and training schedule across diffusion-based BLIP3o, rectified-flow BAGEL, and autoregressive VARGPT-v1.1 architectures, requiring only each backbone's native prompting and generation interface. Across eight understanding metrics, our method consistently improves over the corresponding base models. On BAGEL, it achieves a $+3.5\%$ absolute gain on MMMU and improves GenEval image generation performance from $82\%$ to $85\%$. Code and models are publicly released.

</details>

### [95] [HierBias: Context-Conditioned Hierarchical Media Bias Detection with Multi-Task Type Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26100)
*Kaining Li,Ruichen Yan,Yuxin Dong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HierBias 是一种层次化上下文条件的媒体偏见检测模型，通过建模文档级上下文提升句子级偏见分类性能。该方法引入上下文条件偏见概率，并从理论上证明利用文档上下文可降低贝叶斯误差。结合多任务学习，提升了小规模标注数据下的样本效率。模型采用 RoBERTa 编码器与跨句 Transformer 聚合器，支持二分类偏见检测和四类细粒度偏见类型分类。在 BABE 和 BASIL 数据集上分别取得 0.853 F1 和 0.723 MCC，显著优于现有方法（F1 提升 2.6%，MCC 提升 4.3%），消融实验验证各组件独立有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有句子级媒体偏见检测方法独立分类每句话，忽略人类标注者自然使用的句子间上下文信息，导致性能受限。

Method: 提出 HierBias 模型，结合句子级 RoBERTa 编码器与跨句 Transformer 聚合器，设计双输出头进行二分类偏见检测与四类偏见类型分类；引入上下文条件偏见概率，理论分析其降低贝叶斯误差的能力，并通过多任务学习提升小样本场景下的样本效率。

Result: 在 BABE 和 BASIL 数据集上，HierBias 分别获得 0.853 F1 和 0.723 MCC，相比当前最优模型提升 2.6% F1 与 4.3% MCC（p < 0.05）；消融实验表明各理论组件均独立且持续贡献性能提升。

Conclusion: HierBias 通过正式建模文档上下文，显著提升媒体偏见检测性能，理论与实证结果共同验证了上下文条件建模的有效性与必要性。

Abstract: Media bias detection is a critical task for ensuring fair and balanced information dissemination, yet existing sentence-level approaches classify each sentence independently, ignoring inter-sentence contextual signals that human annotators naturally exploit. We present \textbf{HierBias}, a hierarchical context-conditioned media bias detector that formally models document context in bias prediction. We introduce the \emph{context-conditioned bias probability} and prove theoretically that leveraging document context strictly reduces the Bayes error of sentence-level classification when inter-sentence mutual information is non-zero. A multi-task generalization bound further establishes that jointly training binary bias detection and fine-grained bias type classification improves sample efficiency on small annotated corpora. Architecturally, HierBias pairs a sentence-level RoBERTa encoder with a cross-sentence Transformer aggregator and dual output heads for binary detection and four-class type classification. Evaluated on BABE and BASIL, HierBias achieves 0.853 F1 and 0.723 MCC, surpassing the state-of-the-art bias-detector by $+2.6\%$ F1 and $+4.3\%$ MCC (McNemar's test, $p < 0.05$). Ablation experiments confirm that each theoretical component contributes independently and consistently.

### [96] [Know2Guess: A Contamination-Aware Multi-Zone Benchmark for Knowledge-Boundary Evaluation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26101)
*Renwei Meng,Bowen Zhang,Jian Wang,Xican Wang,Haoyi Wu,Xuanyan Qiu,Shengan Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个抗数据污染的多区域基准测试，用于评估大语言模型从可回答知识到应拒绝回答的过渡，区分支持性回答与无根据猜测，同时避免数据污染、提示特异性或通用拒绝行为的干扰。该基准包含1200个跨五个领域的样本，明确的拒绝预期、污染风险元数据，以及严格和鲁棒两种解析方式。在固定答案/拒绝提示下评估FLAN-T5、Qwen2.5-Instruct和Llama-3-Instruct模型，结果显示：尽管更强的指令微调模型表现出部分选择性过渡，但整体仍存在回答困难、校准差和良性项拒绝问题。Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct表现最佳，但核心挑战依然存在。提示与解析鲁棒性分析验证了主要结论的稳定性。该基准提供了一套可复现的协议，用于审计模型的回答能力、拒绝行为、拒绝倾向与污染之间的相互作用。数据集已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法常混淆支持性回答、无根据猜测、数据污染、提示特异性及通用拒绝行为，缺乏对模型何时应答、何时拒绝的清晰区分。为实现可靠评估，需建立能分离这些维度的基准，尤其关注模型在冻结构建时标签下的回答与拒绝过渡过程。

Method: 设计一个多区域基准，涵盖1200个样本，分属五个领域；引入显式拒绝期望、污染风险元数据；采用双解析策略（严格解析器+鲁棒归一化解析器）；在锁定答案/拒绝提示、仅答案控制、不同提示模板下评估多个模型。通过鲁棒性分析验证结果可靠性。

Result: FLAN基线在主动拒绝方面表现弱；更强模型如Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct虽表现最优，但仍存在回答困难、校准不足、良性项拒绝等问题；提示与解析鲁棒性分析未改变主要排名和定性结论。

Conclusion: 该基准提供了一个可复现的评估框架，能够将回答能力、拒绝行为、拒绝倾向与数据污染作为独立但相互关联的维度进行审计，有助于更准确地衡量大语言模型的可靠性。

Abstract: Reliable evaluation of large language models should separate supported answering from unsupported guessing without conflating either with data contamination, prompt idiosyncrasy, or generic refusal behavior. We present a contamination-aware, multi-zone benchmark for measuring the transition from answerable knowledge to abstention-expected unknowns under frozen build-time labels. The benchmark contains 1,200 items across five domains, explicit abstention expectations, contamination-risk metadata, and dual parsing with an official strict parser plus a normalized robustness parser. We evaluate FLAN-T5, Qwen2.5-Instruct, and Llama-3-Instruct models under locked answer-or-abstain prompts, answer-only controls, and prompt-template variants. The benchmark is not solved by generic non-answer behavior: FLAN baselines remain weak on productive abstention, while stronger instruction-tuned models expose a selective but incomplete transition from answering to abstaining. Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct achieves the best overall reliability, but answer-expected zones remain difficult, calibration remains poor, and benign-item refusal persists. Prompt and parser robustness analyses preserve the main ranking and qualitative conclusions. The benchmark therefore provides a reproducible protocol for auditing answerability, abstention, refusal, and contamination as distinct but interacting dimensions of LLM reliability.The dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/renweimeng/Know2Guess-A-Contamination-Aware-Multi-Zone-Benchmark.

</details>


### [97] [Helpfulness Hurts: Domain-Dependent Degradation of Mid-Trained Compassion Values Under Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26102)
*Jasmine Brazilek,Juliana Seawell*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了后训练数据领域对语言模型中动物同情心价值观保留的影响。结果表明，以助人为主的后训练（如SFT和GRPO）会显著削弱动物同情心，而以编码为主的后训练则能更好地保留这些价值观。在英文MORU基准上，助人训练使道德推理能力下降25.5个百分点；但在多语言MORU上，该差异消失。相反，动物同情心效应在跨语言中依然显著，说明价值观的编码更深层且更具泛化性。建议在价值导向的中段训练基础上，采用编码领域后训练以更好保持价值观。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究后训练数据领域对已注入动物同情心价值观的语言模型的影响，特别是评估不同训练任务（助人 vs. 编码）对价值观保留与通用推理能力的长期影响。

Method: 使用Llama 3.1 8B模型，在中段训练阶段加入同情心导向的合成数据后，分别进行基于帮助性数据（Dolly-15k、RLHFlow）和编码数据（Magicoder-110K）的SFT与GRPO后训练，并在AHB 2.2与MORU基准上评估模型表现，比较跨语言与跨任务的表现差异。

Result: 助人后训练导致动物同情心显著下降（SFT: 35.7% vs. 65.2%；GRPO: 18.7% vs. 32.0%），且英文环境下道德推理能力下降25.5个百分点；但该现象不跨语言转移；而动物同情心效应在非英语数据上提升幅度是英语的4.5倍，表明价值观具有更强的跨语言稳定性。

Conclusion: 在价值导向的中段训练基础上，采用编码领域而非助人领域的后训练，能更有效地保留模型中植入的价值观，同时不影响通用推理能力，为负责任的AI开发提供重要指导。

Abstract: Standard post-training pipelines apply supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL) to make language models helpful, but these processes may inadvertently degrade values instilled during pre-training. We investigate whether the domain of post-training data differentially affects the retention of animal compassion values in a Llama 3.1 8B model mid-trained on compassion-oriented synthetic data, using both SFT (helpfulness via Dolly-15k vs. coding via Magicoder-110K) and GRPO (helpfulness via RLHFlow vs. coding via Magicoder), evaluated on the Animal Harm Benchmark (AHB 2.2) and MORU benchmark (Moral Reasoning Under Uncertainty). Helpfulness training significantly degrades animal compassion relative to coding training on AHB (SFT: 35.7% vs. 65.2%; GRPO: 18.7% vs. 32.0%), replicating across two independent helpfulness datasets and two training paradigms. On English MORU items, helpfulness training degrades general moral reasoning by 25.5 percentage points (46.4% vs. 71.9%), a striking gap that rivals the compassion effect in magnitude. However, this effect does not transfer cross-lingually: on the multilingual MORU benchmark, the domain effect disappears (SFT: 52.3% vs. 51.2%). In contrast, the animal compassion effect transfers consistently across languages, with Magicoder's AHB percentage-point gain over the base model 4.5 times larger on non-English items than English items. This divergence suggests that values instilled through mid-training are encoded more deeply and cross-lingually than reasoning improvements from domain-specific post-training. These results suggest that, for labs building on value-laden mid-training, coding-domain post-training may better preserve mid-trained values than helpfulness post-training without harming general reasoning capabilities.

</details>


### [98] [Investigating LLM's Problem Solving Capability -- a Study on Statics Questions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26103)
*Tanner Culleton,Hung-Fu Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过模型蒸馏方法评估大语言模型（LLM）在解决静力学问题上的能力，发现LLM在纯文本问题上表现良好，但引入图表或需要多步推理时准确率下降。性能下降主要源于多步推理困难和难以持续应用视觉信息，而非图像识别能力不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多依赖公开数据集，缺乏针对特定学科（如机械工程）的系统性分析；尤其在静力学问题上，对LLM在图文结合及复杂推理任务中的表现研究不足。

Method: 采用模型蒸馏技术从ChatGPT中提取25个纯文本静力学问题，并构建两个新数据集：一个添加图表，另一个修改数值以测试鲁棒性，进而评估LLM在不同条件下的表现。

Result: LLM在纯文本静力学问题上表现良好，但在涉及图表或需多步推理的问题上准确率显著下降；性能下降并非主要由图像识别能力限制引起，而是由于多步推理困难和视觉信息一致性应用不足。

Conclusion: LLM在简单文本问题中具备较强解题能力，但在复杂、多步骤且含视觉信息的任务中存在明显局限，提示需改进其逻辑推理与跨阶段信息整合能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have rapidly influenced many aspects of society, particularly education, due to their demonstrated ability to complete assignments and examinations across a wide range of subjects. Although prior studies have examined the educational impact of LLMs, much of the existing work relies on public or open problem datasets and lacks topic-specific analysis. In engineering education, especially within mechanical engineering, systematic investigations of LLM performance on specific problem types remain limited. Instead of using traditional methods that directly ask textbook questions to an LLM tool, our study adopts a model distillation process to evaluate LLM capabilities in solving statics problems. By distilling ChatGPT, we extracted 25 text-only statics questions and further constructed two additional datasets by adding diagrams and modifying their numerical values. Experimental results show that while LLMs perform well on text-only statics problems, their accuracy decreases when diagrams are introduced and the problems require multi-step reasoning. Further analysis suggests that this performance drop is not primarily caused by limitations in image recognition, but rather by difficulties in multi-step reasoning and in consistently applying extracted visual information across successive solution stages.

### [99] [Assert, don't describe: Linguistic features that shift LLM reasoning about animal welfare](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26104)
*Jasmine Brazilek,Harper Dunn*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过词汇匹配的立场对比探测，分析了十种语言特征对Llama-3.2-1B模型在动物福利议题上倾向性的影响。结果显示，八种特征产生显著影响：七种增强模型对动物福利的支持（如明确道德用语、情感词、评价性陈述等），两种削弱支持（如模糊表达和具体感官描述）。建议撰写动物福利内容时应明确立场，避免中立场景描写。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨动物福利倡导文本的语言特征如何影响大型语言模型的立场倾向，尤其关注这些文本在模型训练数据中的潜在影响。

Method: 使用词汇匹配的立场对比探测方法，在独立的动物福利基准上评估十种语言特征对Llama-3.2-1B模型偏好的影响。

Result: 八种语言特征具有统计显著性影响；其中七种增强模型对动物福利的支持，两种削弱支持；第一人称视角无显著影响。

Conclusion: 为确保动物福利相关文本在进入大模型训练数据后仍能强化积极立场，应采用明确表达观点的语言，避免仅以中立方式描述情境。

Abstract: Animal-welfare advocates produce a lot of writing, and increasingly that writing trains the language models that millions of people then ask about animal welfare. Using vocabulary-matched stance-contrast probes on a held-out animal-welfare benchmark, we measure how each of ten linguistic features changes Llama-3.2-1B's preference for pro-animal-welfare reasoning when used as fine-tuning data. Eight of the ten features produce statistically significant shifts. Seven move the model toward stronger pro-animal-welfare reasoning: assertive certainty, explicit moral vocabulary, emotion words, evaluative claims, narrative structure, depicted harm severity, and immediate temporal framing. Two move it the other way: hedged language and concrete sensory description both dilute the pro-animal-welfare stance. First-person perspective has no statistically significant effect. The practical recommendation for anyone writing animal-welfare text that may end up in LLM training corpora: assert a position rather than describe a scene neutrally. The features that shift the model are the ones that make the writer's position explicit; the features that dilute it hold animal-welfare content but withhold stance.

### [100] [Context Recycling for Long-Horizon LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26105)
*Derek Thomas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ContextForge 是一种用于长对话任务的上下文回收系统，通过结构化查询生成、外部记忆检索和受控合成，在不依赖完整上下文重放的情况下高效复用先前计算，减少标记（token）开销并保持回答质量。在15轮医疗领域多轮推理任务中，相比基线模型，该系统提升了对话一致性并降低了资源消耗，证明了上下文回收是扩展大语言模型长时序任务能力的有效方法，无需增大上下文窗口或重新训练模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在短上下文推理中表现良好，但在长对话中因上下文窗口限制和低效的标记使用导致性能下降。需要一种方法在不增加计算负担的前提下，有效维持长期对话中的相关信息。

Method: 结合结构化查询生成、外部记忆检索与受控合成，实现上下文信息的高效回收与复用，避免重复输入完整历史对话，从而降低标记消耗。

Result: 在15轮医疗领域多轮推理测试中，ContextForge 显著提升了对话一致性，减少了标记使用量，同时保持了与基线相当的响应准确性。

Conclusion: 上下文回收是一种实用且高效的策略，可在不依赖更大上下文窗口或模型重训练的情况下，显著提升大语言模型在长对话任务中的表现。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong capabilities in short-context reasoning but degrade in performance over long conversational horizons due to context window limitations and inefficient token usage. We introduce ContextForge, a system for context recycling that maintains task-relevant information across turns by combining structured query generation, external memory retrieval, and controlled synthesis. The system enables efficient reuse of prior computation without relying on full context replay, reducing token overhead while preserving answer quality. We evaluate ContextForge using a 15-turn conversational benchmark that tests multi-turn reasoning, back-references, and domain shifts across structured healthcare queries. Compared to a baseline agent using identical underlying models, ContextForge demonstrates improved consistency and reduced token consumption, while maintaining comparable response accuracy. These results suggest that context recycling provides a practical approach for extending LLM capabilities in long-horizon tasks without requiring larger context windows or model retraining. Code and evaluation artifacts are available at https://github.com/Betanu701/ContextForge.

</details>


### [101] [Reducing Conversational Escalation in Large Language Model Dialogue with Nonviolent Communication Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26106)
*Zhixing Sun,Shenghe Xu,Tao Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过轻量级提示约束（基于非暴力沟通NVC原则）引导大语言模型在人际冲突情境中采取更缓和的对话行为。实验采用双代理模拟框架，在多种指令微调模型和用户抵抗水平下验证，结果显示NVC约束能有效降低对话升级风险，稳定与高抵抗用户互动，提升LLM在冲突场景中的可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将非暴力沟通（NVC）原则转化为过程导向的提示约束，包括避免归责、关注用户情绪体验、强调澄清再提建议。通过双代理模拟框架，在多个指令微调模型上测试不同用户抵抗水平下的对话表现，评估冲突升级程度与交互稳定性。

Result: NVC约束提示在所有测试条件下均显著降低对话升级概率，尤其在高抵抗用户场景中表现出更强的稳定性。表明轻量级提示设计可有效引导模型生成更具同理心、更低对抗性的对话。

Conclusion: 简单有效的沟通约束（如基于NVC的提示设计）能够显著改善大语言模型在冲突敏感场景中的对话行为，提升其在情感化、对抗性情境下的可信度与安全性，为未来对话系统的设计提供了实用且可扩展的优化路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in emotionally charged situations involving interpersonal conflict, frustration, and distress. While prior safety research has focused on preventing explicit harms such as toxic or policy-violating content, less attention has been paid to conversational behaviors that may unintentionally escalate conflict. In this paper, we investigate whether LLMs can be guided toward more de-escalating dialogue behavior through lightweight prompt-level constraints derived from Nonviolent Communication (NVC). We reformulate NVC principles as process-oriented guidelines that discourage blame attribution, emphasize attention to users' emotional experiences, and encourage clarification before advice. Using a dual-agent simulation framework across multiple instruction-tuned models and user resistance levels, we show that NVC-constrained prompting consistently reduces conversational escalation and stabilizes interactions with highly resistant users. These results suggest that simple communication constraints can meaningfully improve the trustworthiness of LLM dialogue in conflict-prone settings.

Abstract: Sign language communication systems, that integrate emotional expression remain underexplored, particularly for low-resource languages. This pilot work establishes the technical foundation for emotion-aware sign language translation in low-resource settings and provides a scalable framework for future expansion to larger vocabularies and more diverse emotional expressions. Our preliminary results indicate the viability of real-time, emotionally expressive sign language communication systems for the hearing-impaired community, with clear pathways for enhancement in subsequent development phases.

*Guan-Yi Lin,Hen-Hsen Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型在推理任务中优于小模型的原因，提出AdvCluster框架，通过分析大规模与小规模模型的推理轨迹差异，发现大模型在约束引导推理方面具有显著优势，能更好识别显性和隐性约束，并据此排除不合理路径、验证中间步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发AdvCluster自动化框架，用于识别大模型稳定占优的问题，从成对推理轨迹中提取细粒度优势描述，并通过语义聚类和评审模型进行量化评估与筛选。

Result: 发现大模型在多个领域（数学、物理、化学、编程）均表现出稳定的推理优势，尤其体现在约束引导推理能力上；构建了一个涵盖通用与特定领域优势的系统性分类体系。

Conclusion: 大模型的优势主要源于更强的约束识别与结构化推理能力，能够有效利用约束条件排除错误路径并验证推理过程，这是其性能超越小模型的核心机制。

Abstract: Larger language models consistently outperform smaller ones on reasoning benchmarks, yet the reasoning differences underlying this gap remain underexplored. Across benchmarks in mathematics, physics, chemistry, and programming, we observe stable performance gaps: averaged over datasets, Qwen3-32B outperforms Qwen3-8B by 6.43%, while GPT-OSS-120B exceeds GPT-OSS-20B by 7.38%. To study the reasoning differences behind these gains, we develop AdvCluster, an automated framework that identifies questions where the larger model shows a stable advantage, extracts fine-grained advantage descriptions from paired reasoning traces produced by larger and smaller models, and organizes them through semantic clustering with quantitative evaluation and selection guided by a reviewer model. Our analysis yields a systematic taxonomy of larger model reasoning advantages, spanning both common advantages that recur across domains and specialized advantages associated with particular domains. Across these patterns, a recurring theme is Constraint-Guided Reasoning: larger models are better at identifying explicit and implicit constraints, organizing them into structured reasoning, and using them to rule out infeasible paths and verify intermediate steps.

### [104] [From Lexicon to AI: A Structured-Data Pipeline for Specialized Conversational Systems in Low-Resource Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26112)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低资源语言缺乏大规模训练语料，难以开发专用对话系统，亟需不依赖海量数据的替代方案。

Abstract: Low-resource languages face a critical challenge in AI development: creating specialized conversational systems without access to massive training corpora. We present a systematic methodology for transforming structured linguistic resources into specialized AI systems, demonstrating that expert-curated lexical databases can serve as effective foundations for conversational AI development. Our approach converts Hindi WordNet into 1.25 million diverse instruction-response pairs, fine-tunes a 12B-parameter language model using resource-efficient LoRA with 4-bit quantization. Evaluation through a Hindi language learning chatbot demonstrates that structured-knowledge-based systems achieve superior pedagogical effectiveness (91.0 vs. 79.4-83.6 for general-purpose models) while maintaining competitive semantic performance and exceptional consistency. The complete pipeline demonstrates a proof-of-concept methodology using Hindi for developing specialized AI systems for any languages with WordNet resources. This work addresses the critical gap in AI accessibility for low-resource languages, offering a practical alternative to corpus-intensive approaches and potentially enabling specialized AI development for the hundreds of languages with existing WordNet resources.

### [105] [Dynamic-dLLM: Dynamic Cache-Budget and Adaptive Parallel Decoding for Training-Free Acceleration of Diffusion LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26120)
*Tianyi Wu,Xiaoxi Sun,Yanhua Jiao,Yulin Li,Yixin Chen,YunHao Cao,YiQi Hu,Zhuotao Tian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Dynamic-dLLM 是一种无需训练的框架，通过动态缓存更新（DCU）和自适应并行解码（APD）提升扩散语言模型（dLLM）的推理效率。该方法在不牺牲性能的前提下，实现了超过3倍的平均加速效果，显著优于现有加速技术，且可直接部署于现有dLLM系统中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的dLLM推理方法因计算复杂度高（O(L³)）难以应用于长序列或实时场景，且缺乏对动态令牌行为的适应性处理，导致现有加速手段如静态缓存或并行解码策略效果受限。

Method: 提出Dynamic-dLLM框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 动态缓存更新（DCU），根据层间令牌动态特性自适应分配缓存更新预算；(2) 自适应并行解码（APD），动态调整解码阈值以平衡生成质量与效率。

Result: 在LLaDA-8B-Instruct、LLaDA-1.5和Dream-v0-7B-Instruct等模型上进行实验，覆盖MMLU、GSM8K、HumanEval等基准测试，结果表明Dynamic-dLLM实现平均超过3倍的推理加速，同时保持原有性能水平。

Conclusion: Dynamic-dLLM是一种高效、即插即用的dLLM推理加速方案，无需重新训练即可显著提升推理速度，为长序列和实时应用提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) offer a promising alternative to autoregressive models, excelling in text generation tasks due to their bidirectional attention mechanisms. However, their computational complexity scales on the order of L cubed with the sequence length L. This poses significant challenges for long-sequence and real-time applications, primarily due to the lack of compatibility with key-value caching and the non-autoregressive nature of denoising steps. Existing acceleration methods rely on static caching or parallel decoding strategies, which fail to account for the dynamic behavior of token properties across layers and decoding steps. We propose Dynamic-dLLM, a training-free framework that enhances dLLM inference efficiency through two components: Dynamic Cache Updating (DCU), which adaptively allocates cache-update budgets based on layer-wise token dynamics, and Adaptive Parallel Decoding (APD), which dynamically calibrates decoding thresholds to balance generation quality and efficiency. Extensive experiments on models like LLaDA-8B-Instruct, LLaDA-1.5, and Dream-v0-7B-Instruct across benchmarks such as MMLU, GSM8K, and HumanEval demonstrate that Dynamic-dLLM significantly improves inference speed. It attains an average speedup exceeding 3 times while maintaining performance. Dynamic-dLLM outperforms state-of-the-art acceleration methods and provides a plug-and-play solution for efficient dLLM deployment without compromising performance. The code is available at https://github.com/TianyiWu233/DYNAMIC-DLLM.

</details>


### [106] [Thinking Like a Scientist? A Structural Study of LLM-Generated Research Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26130)
*Francesca Carlon,Brecht Verbeken,Vincent Ginis,Andres Algaba*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在仅提供研究问题的情况下，对计算机科学领域1000篇arXiv论文的建议方法学倾向。结果显示，不同LLM（GPT-5.1、Gemini 3 Pro、DeepSeek-V3.2）的建议存在显著偏差，尤其在模型提供商选择上差异最大，且建议方法范围明显收窄，有效模型实体从1,232个压缩至59-96个。尽管各模型间建议相关性较高，但与真实论文的方法学相比相关性较低，表明其建议具有系统性偏差。若研究人员不加验证地依赖这些建议，可能无意中缩小了方法探索空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示大型语言模型在无充分引导下生成的研究方法建议是否存在系统性偏差，评估其对科研方法选择的影响，以提醒研究者避免过度依赖模型输出导致方法学视野受限。

Method: 从1000篇arXiv计算机科学论文中提取研究问题，使用三种主流大模型进行最小化提示，生成方法建议；将模型建议与原始论文中的实验方法映射到统一分类体系，量化多维度差异（如模型提供商、任务类型、评估指标），并采用多样性指标、相关性分析及基线测试验证结果的查询特异性与局限性。

Result: 模型建议表现出显著的结构偏差：模型提供商维度的Jensen-Shannon散度最高，达其他维度的3-5倍；学术/单次使用模型被严重低估，而可复用的学术/社区模型略被高估；方法多样性大幅下降，有效模型数量从1,232降至59-96；跨模型建议相关性（0.55–0.68）高于模型与论文间的相关性（0.33–0.56），说明偏差具有共性。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在缺乏明确指导时倾向于推荐高度集中且偏向特定来源的方法，这会系统性压缩研究者的可选方法空间。研究者应谨慎对待模型建议，主动交叉验证，避免陷入‘默认方法陷阱’。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used to guide research methodology, yet their default methodological tendencies under minimal prompting remain unclear. Here, we prompt GPT-5.1, Gemini 3 Pro, and DeepSeek-V3.2 with an LLM-extracted research question from each of 1,000 recent arXiv computer-science papers and compare the resulting methodology suggestions against a paper-derived experimental inventory. Since we provide only the research question, the differences we measure reflect initial suggestions and not how optimal those suggestions are. We extract structured method features from both sources, map them into a shared taxonomy, and quantify divergence across multiple taxonomy dimensions including model provider, dataset task type, and evaluation metric type. The strongest imbalance appears in provider choice, with Jensen-Shannon divergence about 3-5x larger than any other taxonomy dimension. Other/Academic single-occurrence models are underrepresented by 23-24 percentage points, while reused academic/community models are slightly overrepresented (4-6pp). LLMs also suggest a much narrower range of methods overall: the effective number of model entities contracts from 1,232 to 59-96, and inter-LLM rank correlations (0.55-0.68) generally exceed LLM-to-paper correlations (0.33-0.56), so the distortions are largely shared across models. Popularity baselines, BM25 retrieval calibration, and paper-level similarity tests confirm that the outputs are query-specific responses, but filtered through a narrower set of options. Researchers who rely on LLM suggestions without cross-checking therefore risk narrowing their methodological search space toward a more concentrated default.

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have recently made remarkable progress in unifying vision-language understanding and reasoning, especially following the introduction of models such as OpenAI's O-series and DeepSeek's R-series, which have driven a paradigm shift toward perception-centric intelligence. ### [108] [Phonetic and semantic analyses of spoken corpora of Beijing and Taiwan Mandarin indicate that the neutral tone is a lexical tone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26360)
*Yuxin Lu,Zhexuan Li,R. Harald Baayen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究基于北京话和台湾话口语语料库，探讨了普通话中立调（neutral tone）的语音实现。研究发现，中立调具有自身的音高目标，与普通话四个词汇调类似，并且在双音节词中其音高轮廓受前字声调影响，表现出词特定的音高特征。这些特征可通过上下文嵌入模型部分预测，表明中立调在本质上是一种词汇调。研究还比较了两种方言中立调的异同，指出部分差异可能源于词语在不同语境中的意义使用差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中立调在普通话中的性质长期存在争议，常被描述为弱化或无调，但缺乏实证支持。本文旨在通过语料库研究揭示中立调的真实语音属性，澄清其是否为一种独立的词汇调。

Method: 利用北京话和台湾话口语语料库，分析双音节词和单音节词中立调的音高轮廓，结合上下文嵌入模型预测音高特征，对比两地方言的实现差异。

Result: 中立调具有明确的音高目标，呈现词特定的音高签名，且可由上下文嵌入模型部分预测；两地方言中立调在实现上存在相似性与差异性，部分差异与词语语义使用相关。

Conclusion: 中立调并非简单的弱化或无调，而是一种具有特定音高目标的词汇调，其在普通话中（包括北京话与台湾话）具有语言学上的独立地位。

Abstract: The neutral, or floating, tone of Mandarin Chinese is a tone with an enigmatic set of properties. It has been described as a reduced tone, or as a tone that sometimes is lexically fixed but that can also be toneless. In two-syllable words, it is found only on the second syllable, but single-syllable words can also have the neutral tone. We present a corpus-based study of the phonetic realization of the neutral tone in spontaneous conversational speech corpora of Beijing Mandarin and Taiwan Mandarin. We show that the neutral tone has its own tonal target, just as the four lexical tones of Mandarin. We also show that disyllabic words with a neutral tone have pitch contours that have a pitch component that depends on the tone on the first syllable, just as has been observed for two-syllable words with a lexical tone on the second syllable (Chuang et al., 2026). Furthermore, words with a floating tone have word-specific pitch signatures, which have also been documented for single-syllable words (Jin et al., 2026) as well as two-syllable words (Lu et al., 2026b). These word-specific pitch signatures are shown to be predictable to some extent from words' contextualized embeddings, as previously reported for lexical tones (Chuang et al., 2026; Lu et al., 2026b). As there is also considerable variability in the realization of lexical tones, we propose that the neutral tone is, in fact, a lexical tone in both Taiwan Mandarin and Beijing Mandarin. We document both similarities and differences in the realization of the floating tone in these two varieties and provide evidence, using contextualized embeddings, that some of the observed differences may arise from differences in the meanings of the words as used in the two corpora.

### [111] [ConflictScore: Identifying and Measuring How Language Models Handle Conflicting Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26437)
*Siyi Liu,Aaron Halfaker,Dan Roth,Patrick Xia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出ConflictScore新度量，用于评估模型响应中对冲突证据的承认程度，通过分解响应为原子主张并分析其与源文档的匹配情况，提供两个互补指标：冲突计数（CS-C）和冲突比率（CS-R），并构建ConflictBench基准以系统评估该度量。实验表明，该方法能有效检测跨领域的过度自信声明，并可作为提高TruthfulQA真实性的反馈机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将响应分解为原子主张，逐个标签化每个主张与源文档的关系，然后聚合得到冲突计数（CS-C）和冲突比率（CS-R）两个指标。

Result: ConflictScore能有效识别跨领域中的过度自信陈述，并在TruthfulQA上作为反馈机制提升回答的真实性。

Conclusion: ConflictScore是一种有效的度量工具，能够揭示模型在面对冲突证据时的表现，有助于改进生成系统的可信度和透明性。

Abstract: Existing metrics for factuality and faithfulness evaluate whether an answer is supported or contradicted by its grounding documents, but they fail to capture when both supporting and contradicting evidence coexist. We introduce ConflictScore, a novel metric that quantifies how well a model's response acknowledges conflicting evidence in its grounding documents. Our framework decomposes responses into atomic claims, labels each claim against each grounding document, and then aggregates these labels into two complementary measures: ConflictScore-Count (CS-C), the proportion of claims exhibiting conflicts, and ConflictScore-Ratio (CS-R), the balance between supporting and contradicting evidence. We develop ConflictBench, a benchmark covering diverse forms of conflicts such as ambiguity, contradiction, and divergent opinions, to systematically evaluate our metric. Experiments show that ConflictScore effectively detects overconfident claims across domains and can serve as a corrective feedback mechanism that improves truthfulness on TruthfulQA.

### [112] [ProvenAI: Provenance-Native Traces of Evidence in Generated Answers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26449)
*Mohammad Faizan,Dalal Alharthi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProvenAI introduces a framework to measure transparency in multi-hop question answering through three layers: answer correctness, citation fidelity, and per-document influence. It evaluates 7,405 examples using a seven-stage pipeline, achieving 53.53% accuracy and 71.55% citation-fidelity score. A key finding is the 'citation-influence gap,' where cited sources show weak influence while uncited ones significantly affect output. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing retrieval-augmented systems cite sources but lack proof that these sources meaningfully influenced answers. ProvenAI aims to establish meaningful transparency by measuring how sources actually shape outputs beyond mere citation.

Method: A seven-stage pipeline including data normalization, retrieval indexing, citation-aware generation, attribution auditing, ablation-based influence estimation, batch evaluation, and interactive inspection. Uses leave-one-resource-out intervention and token-level KL-divergence for faithfulness assessment.

Result: 53.53% answer accuracy, 71.55% mean citation-fidelity score, and identification of the citation-influence gap—where cited sources have low influence despite being referenced.

Conclusion: True transparency in retrieval-grounded QA requires independent measurement of answer correctness, citation fidelity, and document influence. ProvenAI establishes traceable, causal links between retrieved, cited, and behaviorally impactful evidence, aligning with emerging cryptographic provenance systems in scientific discovery.

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented systems routinely present citations alongside generated answers, yet a citation does not confirm that the corresponding source meaningfully shaped the output. This paper introduces ProvenAI, a framework that decomposes transparency in multi-hop question answering into three independently measurable layers: answer correctness, citation fidelity against benchmark supporting evidence, and per-document influence under leave-one-resource-out intervention. Targeting the HotpotQA distractor benchmark through a seven-stage pipeline covering data normalisation, retrieval indexing, citation-aware answer generation, attribution auditing, ablation-based influence estimation, batch evaluation, and interactive inspection, ProvenAI evaluates 7,405 validation examples drawn from a canonical corpus of 509,300 passages. The system achieves 53.53% answer accuracy alongside a mean citation-fidelity score of 71.55%, and a worked example surfaces what we call the citation-influence gap: a clean citation audit co-occurring with a profile in which one cited source registers only weak influence while seven uncited sources demonstrably shift the output. We formalise the relationship between the implemented surface proxy and a token-level KL-divergence target through a stated faithfulness condition, ground the framework in causal-mediation analysis and database-provenance theory, and discuss how the three measurement layers compose with cryptographic provenance architectures emerging in autonomous scientific discovery. ProvenAI establishes that meaningful transparency in retrieval-grounded QA requires traceable links across retrieved, cited, and behaviourally influential evidence as three distinct, independently measured layers.

### [114] [Soft Token Alignment for Cross-Lingual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26466)
*Jiayi He,Jungsoo Park,Wei Xu,Alan Ritter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SOLAR 是一种用于监督微调的辅助目标，通过以英语为枢纽对跨语言的软令牌表示进行对齐，从而提升多语言大模型在不同语言间的一致性。该方法利用概率加权的词汇嵌入混合生成连续表示，减少语言特定词汇选择带来的语义偏差，在多个基准测试中显著提高准确率，尤其在低资源语言上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 SOLAR，通过将非英语软令牌摘要与对应的英语软令牌在共享嵌入空间中对齐，利用软令牌（概率加权的词汇嵌入混合）实现跨语言连续表示对齐，以增强语义一致性。

Result: 在四个多语言推理基准上，SOLAR 相比基线模型提升最高达 +17.7 点，相比标准监督微调提升 +3.8 点；在低资源语言上增益最大；同时增强了最终层的跨语言相似性，显著降低语言聚类可分性。

Conclusion: 对齐软令牌表示有助于在多语言推理过程中保持共享语义结构，从而有效缓解语言特定输出带来的不一致性问题。

Abstract: Multilingual large language models often produce inconsistent reasoning and answers for semantically equivalent prompts in different languages. Prior work suggests that intermediate representations can be relatively language-agnostic, but generation becomes increasingly language-specific as models commit to discrete output tokens. This is problematic because language-specific lexical choices can cause semantically equivalent reasoning paths to diverge across languages. These divergences motivate searching for a cross-lingual alignment signal that is less tied to any single vocabulary item or script. We propose SOLAR, an auxiliary objective for supervised fine-tuning that aligns soft-token representations across languages, using English as a pivot. Soft tokens are probability-weighted mixtures over the vocabulary embeddings, yielding continuous representations that can aggregate information from semantically related tokens across languages. We then align each non-English soft-token summary to its English counterpart in the shared embedding space. Across four multilingual reasoning benchmarks, SOLAR improves accuracy by up to +17.7 points over the base model and +3.8 over standard supervised fine-tuning, with the largest gains on low-resource languages. SOLAR also strengthens final-layer cross-lingual similarity and substantially reduces language-cluster separability, suggesting that aligning soft-token representations helps preserve shared semantic structure during multilingual reasoning.

</details>


### [115] [Extracting Problem and Method Sentence from Scientific Papers: A Context-enhanced Transformer Using Formulaic Expression Desensitization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26481)
*Yingyi Zhang,Chengzhi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Method: 引入公式化表达（FE）去敏感化策略，构建基于该思想的数据增强器以生成合成数据；提出上下文增强型Transformer模型，利用上下文信息评估目标句中词语的重要性并抑制噪声；同时采用大语言模型进行上下文学习（ICL）对比实验。

Abstract: Billions of scientific papers lead to the need to identify essential parts from the massive text. Scientific research is an activity from putting forward problems to using methods. To learn the main idea from scientific papers, we focus on extracting problem and method sentences. Annotating sentences within scientific papers is labor-intensive, resulting in small-scale datasets that limit the amount of information models can learn. This limited information leads models to rely heavily on specific forms, which in turn reduces their generalization capabilities. This paper addresses the problems caused by small-scale datasets from three perspectives: increasing dataset scale, reducing dependence on specific forms, and enriching the information within sentences. To implement the first two ideas, we introduce the concept of formulaic expression (FE) desensitization and propose FE desensitization-based data augmenters to generate synthetic data and reduce models' reliance on FEs. For the third idea, we propose a context-enhanced transformer that utilizes context to measure the importance of words in target sentences and to reduce noise in the context. Furthermore, this paper conducts experiments using large language model (LLM) based in-context learning (ICL) methods. Quantitative and qualitative experiments demonstrate that our proposed models achieve a higher macro F1 score compared to the baseline models on two scientific paper datasets, with improvements of 3.71% and 2.67%, respectively. The LLM based ICL methods are found to be not suitable for the task of problem and method extraction.

### [116] [Utilizing Cognitive Signals Generated during Human Reading to Enhance Keyphrase Extraction from Microblogs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26485)
*Xinyi Yan,Yingyi Zhang,Chengzhi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了使用脑电图（EEG）信号补充眼动追踪信号在微博关键短语提取（AKE）中的应用。基于ZuCo语料库，研究选取8个EEG特征和17个眼动特征，并将其注入到软注意力层输入和自注意力层查询向量中，以减少模型结构对认知信号的干扰。实验结果表明，无论特征组合或模型架构如何，阅读过程中产生的认知信号均能持续提升AKE性能；其中EEG特征带来最大增益，而结合EEG与眼动特征的表现介于两者之间，说明二者具有部分互补性但也存在冗余或噪声。研究证实EEG信号可为微博关键短语提取提供有效的认知证据，多模态认知信号值得进一步探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于ZuCo认知语言处理语料库，选取8个EEG特征和17个眼动特征，将这些特征注入到软注意力层的输入以及自注意力层的查询向量中，以降低模型结构对认知信号的扭曲影响。通过对比不同特征组合在多种AKE模型上的表现，评估其对关键短语提取性能的影响。

Result: 阅读过程中产生的认知信号在各类模型和特征组合下均能稳定提升AKE性能。其中，EEG特征带来的性能增益最大；结合EEG与眼动特征的性能介于单独使用两者之间，表明二者存在部分互补性，但也可能引入冗余或噪声。

Abstract: Microblogging platforms generate massive amounts of short, noisy, and dispersed user content, making automatic keyphrase extraction (AKE) an important but challenging task. Prior studies have used eye-tracking signals to improve microblog-based AKE because such signals reflect readers' attention to salient words. However, eye tracking alone is limited by physiological, acquisition, and feature-decoding constraints. To address this issue, we investigate whether electroencephalogram (EEG) signals can complement eye-tracking signals for AKE. Using the ZuCo cognitive language processing corpus, we select 8 EEG features and 17 eye-tracking features and incorporate them into microblog-based AKE models. To reduce possible distortion of cognitive signals by model structures, we inject these features into the input of the soft-attention layer and the query vectors of the self-attention layer. We then evaluate different combinations of cognitive signals across AKE models. The results show that cognitive signals produced during reading consistently improve AKE performance, regardless of feature combinations and model architectures. EEG features bring the largest gains, while combining EEG and eye-tracking features yields performance between the two individual signal types, suggesting partial complementarity but also possible redundancy or noise. These findings indicate that EEG signals provide useful cognitive evidence for microblog-based AKE and that multimodal cognitive signals deserve further investigation.

### [117] [Speaking Numbers to LLMs: Multi-Wavelet Number Embeddings for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26487)
*Defu Cao,Zijie Lei,Muyan Weng,Jiao Sun,Yan Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TempoWave提出了一种即插即用的时序小波数字接口，将标量观测值映射为多小波、多尺度系数构建的逐位嵌入，以解决大语言模型在时间序列预测中因离散语言导向标记化与连续数值不匹配导致的数值顺序破坏问题。该方法在保持精确数值格式和对归一化鲁棒性的同时，有效捕捉局部波动与全局结构，在五个上下文丰富的预测基准上显著优于标准数值标记化和其他嵌入接口，达到新基准水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽能整合异构文本信号用于上下文感知的时间序列预测，但其离散的语言导向标记化与嵌入接口与连续数值不匹配，常损害数值顺序和预测可靠性，亟需改进数值接口以提升性能。

Method: 提出TempoWave，通过多小波、多尺度系数构建逐位嵌入，直接替代标准标记表示，实现对时间序列中细粒度局部波动和宏观结构的建模，并兼容Transformer架构。

Result: 在五个上下文丰富的时间序列预测基准上，TempoWave consistently超越标准数值标记化及其它嵌入接口，显著提升基于大语言模型的预测器性能，达到新的状态-最优水平。

Conclusion: 数值接口是大语言模型进行精准预测的关键瓶颈；基于多分辨率原理的嵌入设计能更有效地将上下文推理能力与精确预测耦合，推动大语言模型在时间序列任务中的应用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are attractive for context-aware time series forecasting because they can integrate heterogeneous textual signals, yet their discrete, language-oriented tokenization and embedding interfaces are misaligned with continuous numerical values, often harming numerical ordering and forecasting reliability. We propose TempoWave, a plug-and-play temporal wavelet digit interface that maps each scalar observation into digit-wise embeddings constructed from multi-wavelet, multi-scale coefficients. By directly overriding standard token representations, TempoWave seamlessly exposes both fine-grained local fluctuations and macro global structures in a transformer-compatible form, ensuring that precise numerical formatting, distinct digit identity, and robustness to common normalization operations are maintained throughout the LLM pipeline. Experiments across five context-enriched forecasting benchmarks demonstrate that TempoWave consistently improves LLM-based forecasters over standard numeric tokenization and alternative embedding interfaces, achieving a new state-of-the-art. These results highlight the numeric interface as a key bottleneck and suggest that principled multi-resolution embeddings can better couple LLMs' contextual reasoning with precise forecasting. Our code is available at https://github.com/DC-research/TempoWAVE and our model can be accessed at https://huggingface.co/Melady/TempoWAVE.

### [118] [Comparing BERT Sentence-Pair Classification and Few-Shot LLM Prompting for Detecting Threat and Solution Framing in German Climate News](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26489)

TL;DR: 该研究比较了两种方法在德语气候新闻句子层面识别威胁框架与解决方案框架的效果：一种是使用大型语言模型（Llama 4 Maverick）进行少样本提示并结合思维链推理和置信度评分；另一种是微调德国BERT模型（deepset/gbert-large）进行句对分类，利用前一句作为上下文。实验基于440篇奥地利报纸文章的手动标注数据集，结果显示微调BERT模型的F1分数为0.83（威胁与解决方案任务均），而LLM方法为0.78。消融实验证明提供上下文显著提升BERT性能。

Abstract: News media play a central role in shaping public perceptions of climate change, and whether coverage emphasizes threats or solutions has measurable effects on audience engagement and policy support. Automated detection of these framing patterns at the sentence level would allow researchers to analyze large corpora that are infeasible to code manually. We present a systematic comparison of two approaches for classifying sentences from German-language climate news articles as threat-oriented, solution-oriented, both, or neither. Both approaches implement two independent binary classifiers, one for threat framing and one for solution framing. The fine-tuned BERT classifiers achieve an F1 score of 0.83 for both the threat and solution tasks, while the LLM-based classifiers reach an F1 of 0.78. An ablation study confirms that providing the preceding sentence as context improves BERT classification performance substantially compared to single-sentence input. These results contribute to the growing body of work comparing fine-tuned encoder models with prompted generative models for text classification in computational social science.

### [119] [Nemotron-TwoTower: Diffusion Language Modeling with Pretrained Autoregressive Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26493)
*Fitsum Reda,John Kamalu,Roger Waleffe,Mostofa Patwary,Mohammad Shoeybi,Bryan Catanzaro*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出TwoTower模型，通过将上下文表示与迭代去噪功能解耦为两个独立模块（冻结的自回归上下文塔和可训练的扩散去噪塔），实现并行与迭代生成。基于Nemotron-3-Nano-30B-A3B模型，在2.1万亿令牌上训练，保持98.7%的基线质量，同时提升2.42倍的生成吞吐量。代码与权重已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型使用单一网络同时承担上下文表示和去噪任务，限制了各模块的能力。为提升生成效率与质量，需解耦这两个角色以发挥各自优势。

Method: 设计双塔结构：一个冻结的自回归上下文塔用于因果处理干净文本，一个可训练的扩散去噪塔利用双向块注意力和跨注意力机制对噪声块进行迭代优化。

Result: 在保持98.7%自回归基线质量的前提下，实现了2.42倍的墙钟生成吞吐量提升，验证了方法的有效性与高效性。

Conclusion: TwoTower成功实现了扩散语言模型中上下文表示与去噪过程的解耦，显著提升了生成效率，同时维持高质量输出，是高效生成的新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion language models offer a promising alternative to autoregressive models due to their potential for parallel and iterative generation. However, existing approaches use a single network for both context representation and iterative denoising, forcing one model to serve both roles and limiting its capacity for either role. We propose TwoTower, a block-wise autoregressive diffusion model that decouples these roles into two towers: a frozen AR context tower that causally processes clean tokens, and a trainable diffusion denoiser tower with bidirectional block attention that refines noisy blocks via cross-attention to the context. Built on Nemotron-3-Nano-30B-A3B, an open-weight 30B hybrid Mamba-Transformer MoE model, and trained on approximately 2.1T tokens, Nemotron-TwoTower retains 98.7% of the autoregressive baseline's quality while offering 2.42X higher wall-clock generation throughput. We release the code and model weights at https://huggingface.co/collections/nvidia/nemotron-twotower.

### [120] [Temporal Validity in Retrieval Memory: Eliminating Stale-Fact Errors for AI Agents over Evolving Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26511)
*Neeraj Yadav*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MemStrata 是一种用于处理知识演化的检索增强生成（RAG）系统，通过引入时间有效性机制解决旧事实被错误保留的问题。它在不依赖相似度阈值或大语言模型重排序的情况下，利用确定性的三元组替换规则，在双时态日志中退役过时信息，显著提升动态知识下的准确率（0.95-1.00），同时将过时事实错误率降至接近0%，且推理延迟仅约2.1秒，远低于传统方法的16-18秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG系统缺乏时间建模能力，导致在知识更新后仍可能检索到过时的事实，且这些过时事实与当前事实的嵌入相似度极高，难以区分，造成模型误用旧信息。现有方法依赖相似度阈值或大模型重排序，效率低且无法根本解决该问题。

Method: 提出MemStrata，一种基于双时态日志的记忆系统。它像RAG一样存储事实，但当某个事实被新信息覆盖时，使用确定性的（主体, 关系, 客体）替换规则将其退役。该过程无需相似度判断或调用大语言模型，实现高效、可靠的知识版本管理。

Result: 在六个基准测试中，MemStrata在静态知识上表现与RAG持平，在动态知识任务中准确率达0.95-1.00（而RAG仅为0.20-0.47）。其过时事实错误率从RAG的15-40%降至接近0%。检索延迟约为2.1秒，远优于基于LLM重排序的16-18秒方案。

Conclusion: MemStrata通过引入时间维度和确定性淘汰机制，有效解决了RAG在知识演化场景中的核心缺陷。该方法在准确性、效率和可扩展性方面均优于现有方案，为构建持续演化的智能代理提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) gives agents access to accumulated knowledge, but has no model of time. When a fact changes (e.g., a function is renamed or API restructured), RAG retrieves both the stale and current value with near-identical embedding similarity. The agent then either abstains or serves the superseded fact. We show this is a structural problem: on a calibrated dataset, cosine similarity distinguishes a contradicted fact from a duplicated one with AUROC 0.59 (near chance), as contradictions are often more embedding-similar to the original than rephrased duplicates.
  We present MemStrata, a retrieval memory maintaining temporal validity. It stores facts like RAG, preserving static recall, but when a fact's value is contradicted, a deterministic (subject, relation, object) supersession rule retires the stale value in a bi-temporal ledger - with no similarity threshold and no LLM call. Across six benchmarks run locally with a 7B model, MemStrata ties RAG on static knowledge and reaches 0.95-1.00 accuracy on evolving knowledge (where RAG reaches 0.20-0.47). The central result is the stale-fact-error rate: when required to answer, RAG serves superseded values 15-40% of the time; MemStrata drives this to ~0%, a failure class RAG cannot avoid. MemStrata achieves this at retrieval latency (~2.1s) versus ~16-18s for LLM-reranking baselines. We release the harness, datasets, and a marker-free evaluation protocol for memory under knowledge evolution.

</details>


### [121] [Assessing Post-Reform Changes in Risk Disclosure Quality with a Multidimensional Text Analysis Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26522)
*Nobuhiro Aikawa,Mitsuo Yoshida*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合日语NLP指标提取与配对检验、转移函数分析及指标间相关性分析的纵向文本分析方法，用于评估企业叙事披露随时间的定性变化。研究以日本2019年披露改革为案例，分析了2015至2024年间19,770个公司年度观测数据，发现披露量虽显著上升，但可读性下降；整体信息结构改善，但具体描述质量停滞，且不同市场板块的适应程度差异明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业叙事披露对资本市场至关重要，但其多维性质使得传统单一指标难以全面捕捉其随时间的变化动态，亟需更精细的分析方法以揭示复杂演变模式。

Method: 采用日语自然语言处理（NLP）指标提取，结合配对检验、转移函数分析和跨指标相关性分析，构建纵向文本分析框架，并引入横截面相关性指标衡量风险披露与管理策略的主题一致性。

Conclusion: 现有单指标分析方法无法充分揭示披露演化的复杂性，本研究提出的多维度纵向分析框架能更准确地识别披露质量的真实变化趋势，为政策评估与信息披露监管提供更深入的洞见。

Abstract: While corporate narrative disclosures provide crucial information to capital markets, comprehensively evaluating their qualitative changes over time remains challenging. Narrative text is inherently multidimensional, meaning that an improvement in one textual dimension often occurs alongside changes in others. To capture these underlying dynamics, we propose a longitudinal text analysis approach combining Japanese-language NLP metric extraction with paired testing, shift function analysis, and inter-metric correlation. Our framework extends prior indicator sets by incorporating a cross-section relevance indicator to measure topical alignment between risk disclosures and management strategies. Applying this approach to evaluate Japan's 2019 disclosure reforms, we analyze 19,770 firm-year observations over a 10-year period (FY2015-FY2024). The joint analysis reveals complex shifts in disclosure patterns that are frequently masked by conventional single-indicator methods. Specifically, we find that while disclosure volume increased substantially, it was accompanied by a decline in readability. Furthermore, although the overall information structure improved, specific descriptive quality stagnated, and the degree of adaptation varied across market segments.

</details>


### [122] [The Inattentional Gap: Task-Conditioned Language and Vision Models Omit the Safety-Critical Signals They Can Otherwise Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26529)
*Kwan Soo Shin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了语言和视觉模型在特定任务约束下会抑制对共现安全关键信号的报告，这种现象被称为'无意盲视差距'（Inattentional Gap），表明当前评估的安全性指标无法反映真实世界中的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全评估依赖于模型对指定危害的检测能力，但实际事故往往源于未被明确指定的危害。研究旨在揭示模型在任务专注时可能忽略其他重要安全信号的问题。

Method: 通过在放射科和驾驶文本场景以及胸部X光图像任务中测试多种语言和视觉模型，比较其在受限与非受限条件下的安全信号报告率，分析不同模型家族和规模的影响。

Result: 所有测试模型均表现出显著的安全信号报告抑制，且该现象不随模型规模增加而减弱，甚至在推理模型中依然存在，模型家族差异比规模差异对结果影响更大。

Conclusion: 当前的安全评估指标与真实世界安全脱节，一个系统可能在指定危害上表现完美，却对造成伤害的实际风险完全无知。应重新审视和改进AI安全评估方法。

Abstract: AI safety is evaluated by how reliably a model detects the hazards it is told to find, yet accidents often arise from the hazard no one specified. We show that conditioning a language or vision model on a narrow task suppresses its reporting of co-present, safety-critical signals it can otherwise report, a machine analogue of human inattentional blindness arising from a different mechanism. Across radiology and driving text scenarios and chest-radiograph vision tasks, suppression appeared in every model tested, did not diminish with scale, persisted in a reasoning model, and varied more by model family than by size, while the same models reported these signals at substantially higher rates when unconstrained. We name this dissociation the Inattentional Gap and argue that it decouples measured benchmark safety from real-world safety: a system can score near-perfectly on the hazards an evaluation specifies while remaining blind to those that cause harm.

*Yuxuan Yang,Feiyang Li,Yile Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DiARC方法，通过构建正负样本对来提升模型在ARC类任务中的推理能力，利用输出级视觉变换、DSL级规则反转和任务特定规则编辑三种方式生成负样本，从而增强模型区分能力。实验表明，该方法在多个ARC类基准上均优于基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要依赖正样本监督或数据增强，但缺乏对负样本的利用；而解决ARC类问题不仅需要正样本，还需通过区分负样本来提升推理能力。

Method: 提出DiARC方法，通过三种方式构造负样本：输出级视觉变换、DSL级规则反转、任务特定规则编辑，形成偏好对以进行偏好对齐训练。

Result: 在多个ARC类基准测试中，DiARC显著提升了模型性能，优于现有基线模型。

Conclusion: 通过引入负样本并采用偏好对齐策略，DiARC有效增强了大语言模型在抽象与推理任务中的表现，为解决类似挑战提供了新思路。

Abstract: The Abstraction and Reasoning Corpus (ARC;~\citealp{chollet2019measure}) contains tasks that require summarizing patterns from limited grid samples and predicting output grids. Recently, many large language model based approaches have attempted to transform it into a text-based reasoning task. However, methods based on open-source models have generally yielded unsatisfactory results, while those relying on closed-source models are too costly. Current efforts mainly focus on data augmentation, constructing ARC-like data for more comprehensive supervised fine-tuning. In this work, we argue that solving ARC-like problems requires not only \textit{positive} sample supervision but also the ability to improve model reasoning by distinguishing \textit{negative} samples. To this end, we draw on the idea of preference alignment and propose \textsc{DiARC}, a method that constructs preference pairs to enable the model to distinguish between them. Specifically, we propose three ways to construct negative samples, including output-level visual transformations, DSL-level rule inversion, and task-specific rule editing. The resulting negative samples provide informative near-miss alternatives while keeping the observed demonstrations unchanged. Experimental results across multiple ARC-like benchmarks show that \textsc{DiARC} consistently improves performance over baseline models. The code is released at https://github.com/szu-tera/DiARC.

### [124] [Erase-then-Delta Attention: Decoupling Erase and Write Addresses in Delta-Rule Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26560)
*Xiao Li,Chengruidong Zhang,Hao Luo,Xi Lin,Zekun Wang,Zihan Qiu,Yunfei Mao,Langshi Chen,Man Yuan,Minmin Sun,Huiqiang Jiang,Siqi Zhang,Rui Men,Wei Hu,Gong Cheng,Bo Zheng,Dayiheng Liu,Jingren Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Erase-then-Delta Attention (EDA) decouples erase and write operations in recurrent memory models, enabling selective removal of stale information at independent addresses while preserving delta-rule corrective writes. Experiments show EDA outperforms existing methods in language model pretraining and long-context tasks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing delta-rule linear attention corrects content at the current write address but cannot actively remove stale information from other addresses, limiting memory management. This work aims to improve memory efficiency by allowing independent erasure decisions.

Method: EDA introduces a two-step update: first, a targeted erase along a learned erase direction; second, a delta-style corrective write along the current write direction. This separates erase and write locations, enhancing memory cleanliness.

Result: EDA achieves superior performance in both dense 2.5B and MoE 25B-A2.8B models during pretraining and long-context evaluations (4k to 128k tokens). It maintains gains even after 80B-token midtraining, with probes indicating effective cleanup when passive decay is weak.

Conclusion: Recurrent memory models should not only decide what to write, but also where and what to erase. EDA provides a scalable, effective mechanism for proactive memory management, significantly improving long-term retention and contextual accuracy.

Abstract: Delta-rule linear attention improves recurrent memory updates by correcting what is already stored at the current write address before writing new content. However, the active correction is still anchored to that same write address. As a result, stale information stored at a different address cannot be actively removed before new content is written elsewhere. We propose Erase-then-Delta Attention (EDA), a memory update rule that decouples where to erase from where to write. The key insight is that recurrent memory models should not only correct the current write, but also selectively suppress outdated memory at an independently chosen address. Concretely, our method first applies a targeted erase step along a learned erase direction, and then performs the standard delta-style corrective write along the current write direction. This preserves the corrective behavior of delta-rule updates while expanding their memory-management capacity. Language-model pretraining experiments across dense 2.5B and MoE 25B-A2.8B model families show that EDA performs best in both settings. The gain persists after 80B-token long-context midtraining of the MoE models, where EDA also performs best in long-context evaluations from 4k to 128k contexts. A compact update analysis and memory-state probes suggest why: EDA keeps the delta-rule corrective write intact while allocating an additional cleanup path most strongly when passive decay is weak. These results suggest that recurrent memory models should decide not only what to write, but also what stale information to erase and where.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Zero-shot tweet-level stance detection confronts two primary challenges: (1) mitigating the context sparsity inherent in short texts, and (2) establishing the relevance between implicit targets and textual content. While existing methods primarily focus on incorporating external knowledge, they neglect the intrinsic semantic cues embedded within key intra-textual entities. Furthermore, current models exhibit limited capability in determining the relevance of unseen targets to the given text, thereby struggling to differentiate between "neutral" and "irrelevant" stance labels. To address these issues, we first construct a four-class, multi-topic Japanese tweet dataset. To our knowledge, this is the first Japanese tweet-level dataset for stance detection. We then propose KIRP, a zero-shot stance detection framework. It integrates external knowledge with entity reorganization for data augmentation and employs prompt chaining for reasoning. Specifically, the framework incorporates knowledge graphs to supplement and reorganize key textual entities, while reflective Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning extracts and validates implicit targets. To better distinguish "neutral" from "irrelevant" labels, we adopt stance-aware contrastive learning to capture discriminative features and design a three-layer iterative prototype network for fine-grained classification. Experimental results on SemEval-2016, WT-WT, and KIRP-D show that KIRP achieves state-of-the-art performance. KIRP obtains F1 scores of 84.05% (three-class) on SemEval-2016, and 84.99% and 79.18% (four-class) on WT-WT and KIRP-D, respectively.

### [126] [Closing the Quality Gap in Low-Resource Text-to-Speech: LoRA Fine-Tuning of VoxCPM2 for Khmer and Korean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26618)
*Phannet Pov,Sovandara Chhoun,Hyun Woo Park,Wan-Sup Cho,Saksonita Khoeurn*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型预训练文本到语音（TTS）模型在资源匮乏语言（如高棉语和韩语）上的性能差距。通过使用VoxCPM2模型，结合一个共享的26小时多语言语料库，并采用单一低秩适应（LoRA）适配器对语言模型和解码器进行联合微调，实现了显著的语音质量提升。高棉语的平均意见分数（MOS）从3.85提高到4.23（最佳适配器秩为64），且统计显著（p<0.001），仅需训练0.19%至3.03%的参数。然而，自动损失与人工评分结果不一致：最低验证损失出现在秩128，而MOS峰值在秩64。对韩语无明显提升，高秩适配反而导致质量下降，表明适配主要在基础模型较弱的语言上有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型预训练文本到语音模型在资源丰富语言上表现接近人类水平，但在语言数据稀缺的情况下性能显著下降。本研究旨在探索如何通过高效微调方法改善低资源语言（如高棉语和韩语）的语音合成质量，尤其关注适配器技术在跨语言场景下的有效性与局限性。

Method: 采用基于MiniCPM-4语言模型和流匹配扩散解码器的VoxCPM2模型（2.4B参数），构建一个包含约26小时的共享、语言标记语料库；使用单个零初始化的低秩适配器（LoRA）同时对语言模型和解码器进行微调，训练比例仅为0.19%至3.03%；通过听觉测试评估高棉语和韩语的语音质量变化。

Result: 高棉语的平均意见分数（MOS）从3.85显著提升至4.23（最佳适配器秩64），具有高度统计显著性（p<0.001）；自动损失最小值出现在秩128，但人类评分最优在秩64，说明评价指标存在分歧；韩语未见提升，高秩适配甚至导致质量下降，表明适配效果取决于基础模型对目标语言的初始表现。

Conclusion: 低秩适配（LoRA）可高效提升资源匮乏语言的语音合成质量，尤其在基础模型表现较弱时效果显著。然而，自动评估指标与人类感知不完全一致，且适配效果受语言特性影响，提示未来应更关注人类感知与多语言适配策略的协同优化。

Abstract: Large pretrained text-to-speech (TTS) models sound almost human for well-resourced languages, but much worse for languages that are rare in their training data. We study this quality gap for Khmer and Korean using VoxCPM2, a 2.4B-parameter, tokenizer-free TTS model that joins a MiniCPM-4 language-model backbone with a flow-matching diffusion decoder. We build one shared, language-tagged corpus of about 26 hours and adapt VoxCPM2 with a single Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) adapter, trained on both languages at once and added to both the language model and the decoder. The adapter is zero-initialized, so training starts exactly at the original (zero-shot) model. In native-speaker listening tests, the Khmer Mean Opinion Score (MOS) rises from 3.85 to 4.23 with the best adapter (rank 64), a highly significant gain (paired Wilcoxon test, p<0.001), while training only 0.19 to 3.03 percent of the parameters. The automatic loss and the human ratings, however, disagree on the best rank: validation loss is lowest at rank 128, yet MOS peaks at rank 64. The same adapter brings no gain for Korean, a language the base model already handles well, and at a high rank it even degrades quality. Adaptation therefore helps mainly where the base model is genuinely weak.

### [127] [CAT-Q: Cost-efficient and Accurate Ternary Quantization for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26650)
*Shigeng Wang,Chao Li,Yangyuxuan Kang,Jiawei Fan,Anbang Yao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CAT-Q是一种高效且准确的后训练量化方法，用于压缩和加速大语言模型（LLM）。它通过可学习调制（LM）和软化三值化（ST）两个核心组件，在仅需512个校准样本的情况下，将1.7B至8B参数的LLM量化为三值模型，性能优于需要1000亿训练令牌的BitNet 1.58-bit系列模型，训练资源减少约10万倍。此外，首次实现对14B至235B参数的大规模模型在8-60小时内完成三值量化，仅需8块A100-80GB GPU。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有三值量化方法依赖昂贵且数据密集的量化感知训练，导致性能下降严重；亟需一种无需复杂训练、通用性强且高效的后训练量化方案来压缩大语言模型。

Method: 提出CAT-Q，结合可学习调制（LM）与软化三值化（ST）。LM通过可学习因子调节权重分布与阈值，降低对三值化的敏感性；ST引入可微过渡函数，引导三值化过程稳定收敛。二者从优化角度耦合设计，实现高效后训练量化。

Result: 在1.7B至8B参数模型上，使用512个校准样本即可实现高性能三值化，超越BitNet系列模型（训练量达100B token），训练资源减少约10万倍；成功扩展至14B至235B参数模型，8-60小时完成量化，仅用8块A100-80GB GPU。

Conclusion: CAT-Q是一种简单而有效的后训练三值量化方法，适用于多种架构和规模的LLM，显著降低量化成本，同时保持优异性能，为大规模模型部署提供高效解决方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we present CAT-Q, Cost-efficient and Accurate Ternary Quantization, for compressing and accelerating LLMs. Unlike existing state-of-the-art ternary quantization methods that rely on data-intensive and costly quantization-aware training to mitigate severe performance degradation, CAT-Q is a simple yet effective post-training quantization scheme that is readily applicable to LLMs with diverse architectures and model sizes. It has two key components, learnable modulation (LM) and softened ternarization (ST), which are coupled from an optimization perspective. LM leverages a composition of learnable factors to modulate the distribution of pre-trained high-precision weights and the ternary threshold, making them less sensitive to ternarization. ST further introduces a differentiable transition function to guide the ternarization process toward stable convergence. We show that, for pre-trained LLMs with 1.7B to 8B parameters, CAT-Q can efficiently quantize them into ternary models using only 512 calibration samples, while achieving superior performance than the seminal BitNet 1.58-bit v1 and v2 families (with 1.3B to 7B parameters) trained with 100B tokens, yielding about a 100,000X reduction in training tokens. Moreover, we show for the first time that CAT-Q can quantize much larger pre-trained LLMs having 14B to 235B parameters into leading ternary models within just 8 to 60 hours on 8 A100-80GB GPUs. Code is available at https://github.com/IntelChina-AI/BitTern.

</details>

Abstract: Personalized language-model assistants are often evaluated through a memory lens: can a model recall preferences users have explicitly stated in dialogue? More comprehensive personalization demands a harder capability -- inferring what users care about from the multimodal traces they naturally leave behind. We introduce SocialPersona, a benchmark for evaluating whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) can recover revealed preferences from longitudinal social-media timelines and use them in dialogue. Built from longitudinal timelines of 171 everyday, non-promotional social-media users, SocialPersona contains text, images, timestamps, and 2,597 human-verified preference tags across seven interest domains, separating stable interests from recent interests. It supports two tasks: constructing structured user profiles from multimodal context and generating responses aligned with inferred profiles. Experiments with proprietary and open-weight MLLMs show that models can identify broad interest domains, yet their performance drops on fine-grained and recent interests and degrades further when inferred profiles must be used to personalize dialogue. Together with evidence that text and images provide complementary preference signals, these results indicate that robust cross-modal, long-horizon user modeling remains a key challenge, and that SocialPersona can help measure and advance progress toward assistants that infer and act on revealed preferences.

### [129] [Beyond Logical Forms: LLM-Extracted Patterns for Fallacy Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26698)

Abstract: In today's fast-paced information era, logical fallacies, defined as defective patterns of reasoning, inevitably contribute to the growth of information disorder. However, often fallacies appear in nuanced forms that complicate automated classification. In this study, we investigate whether merging abstract logical structures with context-level linguistic cues proves beneficial for fallacy classification, developing a framework that inductively extracts such patterns from fallacious examples and their explanations using Large Language Models (LLMs). We evaluate the impact of these patterns across different LLMs and experimental zero- and one-shot configurations, showing statistically significant improvements over zero-shot baselines and outperforming competing approaches. Cross-dataset experiments validate generalization, establishing data-driven pattern extraction as an effective method for generating logical representations.

</details>


### [130] [ConvMemory v3: A Validity Context Layer for Conversational Memory via Target-Conditioned Relation Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26753)
*Taiheng Pan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ConvMemory v3 introduces a validity context layer to detect and surface update evidence in conversational memory, using a dual-evidence gate with target-conditioned relation verification. It achieves 90.12% accuracy on synthetic benchmarks and transfers effectively to real-world tasks with zero target-side labels, improving H@1 to 95.7% while maintaining high recall. The system preserves retrieval by default and supports both structured metadata and query-conditioned demotion modes, backed by six safety contracts.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing conversational memory systems optimize relevance but fail to handle outdated memories that are still relevant; updates, corrections, or supersessions need detection to maintain up-to-date knowledge.

Method: A dual-evidence gate combines MiniLM and DeBERTa-v3 slot heads, conditioned on the target proposition, and gated by conservative event/operation evidence. Validity is verified through target-conditioned relation verification, with multi-hop graph propagation used for validation. Training uses synthetic data with feedback loops to mine failure patterns.

Result: The verifier achieves 90.12% +/- 1.73 accuracy on synthetic multi-hop validity benchmark. In real-data deployment with zero target-side labels, it reaches 98.8% +/- 0.9 group-all-correct. Query-conditioned demote mode improves H@1 from 45.1% to 95.7% +/- 1.2 while preserving 99.4% recall of non-superseded memories.

It maintains retrieval integrity while enabling dynamic updates via structured metadata or explicit demotion, demonstrating strong transferability and reliability.

Abstract: Conversational memory retrieval optimizes relevance, yet a retrieved memory can be relevant and simultaneously outdated: a later turn updates, corrects, or supersedes it. ConvMemory v3 adds a validity context layer that detects and surfaces this update evidence through target-conditioned relation verification, sitting after the v1/v2 retrieval path. The core mechanism is a dual-evidence gate that conditions a relation judgment on the specific target proposition, scoring a (target, source) pair through the product of a MiniLM slot head and a DeBERTa-v3 slot head and gating it by conservative event/operation evidence. On a synthetic multi-hop validity benchmark the gate reaches 90.12% +/- 1.73 accuracy; through a real-data feedback loop that mines failure patterns but trains on synthetic pairs only, the verifier transfers to Memora role binding with zero target-side labels, reaching 98.8% +/- 0.9 group-all-correct. The deployed layer preserves retrieval by default: a context mode attaches structured validity metadata while keeping the candidate set and rank order fixed, and a query-conditioned demote mode is an explicit opt-in for dense current-state workloads, where it raises current-active H@1 from a never-demote baseline of 45.1% to 95.7% +/- 1.2 while protecting non-superseded memories at 99.4% recall. Six machine-verifiable safety contracts pin the layer's behavior. Multi-hop graph propagation is validated as a mechanism; fully automatic construction of strict prerequisite edges is characterized as a boundary, since strict necessity requires counterfactual world knowledge. This report extends ConvMemory v1 (arXiv:2605.28062) and v2 (arXiv:2606.10842).

### [131] [Evaluation Pitfalls and Challenges in Multimedia Event Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26775)
*Philipp Seeberger,Steffen Freisinger,Tobias Bocklet,Korbinian Riedhammer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次系统分析了多媒体事件抽取中的评估陷阱，识别出三大问题：数据处理不一致、任务假设不一致以及评估设置过于宽松。通过在严格评估框架下的控制实验，证明微小的评估选择会导致性能大幅波动，并高估模型在跨模态真实事件定位上的能力。研究呼吁建立可比的评估标准，推动更严格的评估实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多媒体事件抽取虽有显著进展，但其结果的可靠性和可比性依赖于一致且严谨的评估。然而，现有评估存在诸多问题，影响了模型性能的真实反映，亟需系统性分析与改进。

Method: 通过构建严格评估框架，进行一系列控制实验，对比不同评估设置下模型的表现，识别评估过程中的关键影响因素。

Result: 发现评估中的微小差异（如数据预处理、任务假设、评价阈值等）会导致模型性能出现显著波动，部分情况下甚至导致对模型能力的严重高估。

Conclusion: 多媒体事件抽取领域需要建立统一、严谨的评估标准，以确保结果的可比性和可靠性，推动该领域向更科学、更可信的方向发展。

Abstract: Multimedia event extraction aims to jointly identify events and their arguments across multiple modalities, such as text and images, to support more comprehensive event understanding. While recent work reports steady and substantial progress, the reliability and comparability of these results critically depend on consistent and rigorous evaluation. In this work, we present the first systematic analysis of evaluation pitfalls in multimedia event extraction and identify three major sources of issues: inconsistent data processing, inconsistent task assumptions, and overly relaxed evaluation settings. We demonstrate, through a series of controlled experiments under a strict evaluation framework, that minor evaluation choices can cause large performance variations and lead to overestimation of a model's ability to ground real-world events across modalities. Our findings highlight the need for comparable evaluation standards and encourage a shift toward more rigorous evaluation in multimedia event extraction.
