### [132] [OPID: On-Policy Skill Distillation for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26790)
*Shuo Yang,Jinyang Wu,Zhengxi Lu,Yuhao Shen,Fan Zhang,Lang Feng,Shuai Zhang,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: OPID提出一种无需外部技能记忆的在线策略技能自蒸馏框架，通过将完成轨迹中的后见之明转化为层次化技能（任务级与步骤级），利用关键决策优先路由机制实现密集、分布匹配的令牌级监督，从而在保持强化学习主目标的同时提升语言智能体的性能、样本效率和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于结果的强化学习缺乏中间决策的指导，而现有的技能条件自蒸馏方法依赖外部技能记忆或特权上下文，成本高且与当前策略状态分布不匹配。因此需要一种无需外部记忆、能从自身轨迹中提取分布匹配的密集监督的方法。

Method: OPID将轨迹后见之明表示为层次化技能：任务级技能捕捉全局流程或避错规则，步骤级技能捕捉关键时间步的局部决策知识；采用关键决策优先路由机制，在识别出关键决策时使用步骤级技能，否则默认使用任务级技能；将选定技能注入交互历史，使旧策略在原始和技能增强上下文中重新评分响应，通过对数概率差异生成令牌级自蒸馏优势，并与结果优势结合用于策略优化。

Result: 在ALFWorld、WebShop和基于搜索的问答任务上的实验表明，OPID相比仅基于结果的RL和现有技能蒸馏基线，显著提升了智能体性能、样本效率和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OPID实现了在不依赖外部记忆的前提下，从在线策略轨迹中提取分布匹配的密集技能监督，有效增强了语言智能体的训练稳定性与表现，是一种高效且可扩展的自蒸馏框架。

Abstract: Outcome-based reinforcement learning provides a stable optimization backbone for language agents, but its sparse trajectory-level rewards provide little guidance on which intermediate decisions should be reinforced or suppressed. On-policy self-distillation offers dense token-level supervision, yet existing skill-conditioned variants often rely on external skill memories or retrieved privileged context, which are costly to maintain and can be mismatched with the state distribution induced by the current policy in multi-turn interaction. We propose \textbf{OPID} (\textbf{O}n-\textbf{P}olicy Sk\textbf{i}ll \textbf{D}istillation), a framework that extracts skill supervision directly from completed on-policy trajectories. OPID represents trajectory hindsight as hierarchical skills: episode-level skills capture global workflows or failure-avoidance rules, while step-level skills capture local decision knowledge at critical timesteps. A critical-first routing mechanism uses step-level skills when critical decisions are identified and falls back to episode-level skills as default guidance otherwise. The selected skill is injected into the interaction history, allowing the old policy to re-score the same sampled response under both original and skill-augmented contexts. The resulting log-probability shift yields a token-level self-distillation advantage, which is combined with the outcome advantage for policy optimization. OPID thus preserves RL as the primary training objective while introducing dense, distribution-matched hindsight supervision. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop and Search-based QA demonstrate that OPID generally improves agent performance, sample efficiency, and robustness over outcome-only RL and existing skill-distillation baselines. Our code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/OPID/tree/main.

</details>


### [133] [From Vajrayana Tara to Bengali Baul: A Computational Study of Lexical Transmission Across Buddhist, Shakta, and Vaishnava Traditions in Bengal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26803)
*Joy Bose*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过TF-IDF字符n-gram向量化与余弦相似度分析，对8世纪至19世纪的八种孟加拉与梵文虔诚文学传统（包括佛教密宗、性力派坦特罗、毗湿奴派及巴尔派）进行了计算语料库分析，首次量化验证了佛教密宗词汇在波拉寺院衰落后被孟加拉性力派吸收的历史论断。关键发现显示：12世纪的《歌牛》（梵文毗湿奴派）与性力派卡利文本余弦相似度为0，而同一时期同语言的桥梁塔拉文本与卡利文本相似度达0.54，形成8.5倍差异，表明该词汇重叠具有特定传承链属性而非普遍现象；三部《大尼拉坦特罗》塔拉文本显示性力派到佛教词汇比例为2.0–4.0，体现明确的词汇过渡。18世纪的拉姆普拉萨德·森的孟加拉卡利歌曲中保留了56次‘塔拉’与103次‘卡利’，证明佛教词汇残留。毗湿奴派孟加拉传统与现代巴尔派存在相似性（0.29），略弱于通过查里亚帕达传承的佛教萨哈吉亚链（0.31）。研究为孟加拉地区佛教-性力派融合提供了首个跨传统定量支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 历史上长期存在佛教密宗词汇在波拉寺院崩溃后被孟加拉性力派吸收的说法，但缺乏量化证据。本文旨在通过计算方法验证这一历史论断，揭示不同宗教传统间词汇传播的具体路径与程度。

Method: 采用75部文本构成的语料库，使用TF-IDF字符n-gram向量化，并通过余弦相似度分析比较不同传统之间的词汇关系。特别关注佛教密宗与性力派之间、以及不同时期和语言文本间的词汇重叠情况。

Result: 1. 《歌牛》（毗湿奴派）与性力派卡利文本余弦相似度为0，而同期佛教-性力派过渡文本（桥塔拉）与卡利文本相似度为0.54，形成8.5倍差异，说明词汇重叠具特定传承性。2. 三部《大尼拉坦特罗》塔拉文本显示性力派至佛教词汇比率为2.0–4.0，体现词汇过渡。3. 拉姆普拉萨德·森的孟加拉卡利歌曲中出现56次‘塔拉’与103次‘卡利’，证明佛教词汇残留。4. 毗湿奴派孟加拉传统与现代巴尔派相似度为0.29，略低于佛教萨哈吉亚链（0.31）。

Conclusion: 本研究首次以多传统、跨时间的量化方式证实了孟加拉地区佛教与性力派之间的特定词汇融合现象，支持历史学界关于佛教密宗词汇在波拉时代后被性力派吸收的论断，揭示了宗教思想与语言在跨传统传播中的具体路径。

Abstract: We present a computational corpus study of vocabulary relationships across eight tradition layers of Bengali and Sanskrit devotional literature spanning the 8th to 19th centuries, encompassing Buddhist Vajrayana, Shakta Tantra, Vaishnava, and Baul traditions. Using a corpus of 75 texts and TF-IDF character n-gram vectorization with cosine similarity analysis, we address the historically argued but previously unquantified claim that Buddhist Vajrayana vocabulary survived the collapse of the Pala monasteries and was absorbed into the Shakta Tantra tradition of Bengal. The central finding is a specificity result: the Gitagovinda (Vaishnava Sanskrit, 12th century) has zero cosine similarity to Shakta Kali texts, while Bridge Tara texts (Buddhist-Shakta transitional, same century, same language) have cosine similarity 0.54 to Shakta Kali. This 8.5-fold contrast between two Sanskrit traditions from the same century demonstrates that the Buddhist-Shakta vocabulary overlap is not a generic property of Sanskrit devotional literature but is specific to the Buddhist-Shakta transmission chain. Three Brihannilatantra Tara texts show Shakta-to-Buddhist vocabulary ratios of 2.0 to 4.0, constituting measurable evidence of lexical transition within that chain. Ramprasad Sen's 18th-century Bengali Kali songs preserve Buddhist vocabulary residue including 56 occurrences of Tara alongside 103 occurrences of Kali. The Vaishnava Bengali tradition contributes a parallel chain to modern Baul vocabulary (similarity 0.29), slightly weaker than the Buddhist Sahajiya chain via Charyapada (0.31). These results provide the first quantitative multi-tradition corroboration of historically argued Buddhist-Shakta syncretism in Bengal.

### [135] [Cascaded Multi-Granularity Pruning for On-Device LLM Inference in Industrial IoT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26861)
*Jinghan Wang,Yanjun Chen,Wei Zhang,Xiaotong Huang,Tianchen Liu,Gaoliang Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种级联多粒度剪枝框架，通过粗到细的顺序剪除层、注意力头和前馈通道，并在各阶段间使用轻量级低秩恢复重新估计组件重要性，以实现工业物联网边缘设备上大语言模型的极端压缩。基于信息论分析确定剪枝顺序，引入结构独立性假设（SIA）作为可验证条件，预测剪枝准则在特定架构上的可靠性：MHA+GELU架构满足SIA，而GQA+SwiGLU架构违反SIA。实验表明，在88M至6.25B参数模型上，该方法将压缩比提升至13.8倍，准确率高达83.82%（优于最强基线3.70个百分点），而违反SIA的GQA+SwiGLU架构则出现约74个百分点的准确率崩溃。在实际工业回转轴承故障诊断平台部署中，模型推理延迟降低67.2%，峰值内存减少62.5%，验证了其在IIoT边缘推理中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结构化剪枝方法在高压缩比下因一次性重要性估计而失效，且跨架构行为不可预测，难以满足工业物联网边缘设备对大语言模型极端压缩的需求。

Method: 提出级联多粒度剪枝框架，按粗到细顺序剪除层、注意力头和前馈通道，并在每阶段间采用轻量级低秩恢复重新评估组件重要性；通过信息论分析支持剪枝顺序设计，并形式化结构独立性假设（SIA）作为判断剪枝可靠性是否成立的可验证条件。

Result: 在MHA+GELU架构上实现13.8倍压缩，准确率达83.82%（较最强基线提升3.70个百分点）；而在违反SIA的GQA+SwiGLU架构上出现约74个百分点的准确率下降；实际部署中推理延迟降低67.2%，峰值内存减少62.5%。

Conclusion: 所提框架显著提升了大语言模型在工业物联网边缘设备上的压缩能力与部署可行性，但其有效性依赖于架构是否满足结构独立性假设（SIA），为未来高效剪枝提供了理论指导与实践路径。

Abstract: Deploying large language models (LLMs) on Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT) edge devices demands extreme compression, yet existing structured pruning methods collapse at high compression ratios due to one-shot importance estimation, and their cross-architecture behavior remains unpredictable. This article presents a cascaded multi-granularity pruning framework that removes layers, attention heads, and feed-forward channels in coarse-to-fine order, with lightweight low-rank recovery between stages to re-estimate component importance. An information-theoretic analysis motivates this ordering, and the Structural Independence Assumption (SIA) is formalized as a checkable condition predicting whether per-component pruning criteria are reliable for a given architecture: Multi-Head Attention (MHA)+GELU designs satisfy the SIA, whereas Grouped Query Attention (GQA)+SwiGLU designs violate it. On bearing fault diagnosis spanning 88M to 6.25B-parameter models, the framework extends achievable compression to 13.8 times on MHA+GELU architectures with 83.82% accuracy (+3.70 percentage points (pp) over the strongest baseline), while exposing a ~74pp accuracy collapse on GQA+SwiGLU architectures that violate the SIA. Deployed on an industrial slewing bearing fault diagnosis platform with NVIDIA DGX Spark, compressed models reduce inference latency by up to 67.2% and peak memory by 62.5%, demonstrating viability for IIoT edge inference.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存压缩方法依赖注意力权重评估token重要性，但忽略了与预测不确定性及token信息量相关的信息论信号，导致在长序列推理中效果受限。

Method: 提出前向影响度量，结合token级预测不确定性与层间表示演化，生成熵得分，并将其与注意力分数融合，用于指导KV缓存压缩。

Abstract: Reasoning capability has advanced rapidly in large language models (LLMs), leading to an increasing size of key-value (KV) cache in both prefilling and decoding stages. Existing KV cache compression methods mainly rely on attention weights to estimate token importance. While attention effectively captures contextual relevance, it overlooks complementary information-theoretic signals related to predictive uncertainty and token informativeness. In this paper, we revisit token importance from a forward-looking perspective and introduce \textit{Forward Influence}, a metric that measures how compressed tokens affect future contexts. Our analysis reveals that tokens selected by attention scores mainly influence nearby contexts, whereas tokens associated with high predictive uncertainty exhibit substantially stronger influence on distant future contexts. Based on the observation, we propose \textbf{InfoKV}, an entropy-aware KV cache compression framework that incorporates information-theoretic signals. It combines token-level predictive uncertainty with layer-wise representation evolution and integrates the resulting entropy scores with attention scores during reasoning. Experiments on long-context reasoning benchmarks with Llama-3.1, Llama-3.2, and DeepSeek-R1 demonstrate that InfoKV consistently outperforms existing attention-based KV compression methods in both long prefilling and decoding scenarios.

*Xiao Jia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究利用八种冻结的语言模型、分块编码模型及匹配的时间、干扰和表征容量控制，分析了来自Brain Treebank、MEG-MASC和Podcast ECoG的锁定衍生数据，发现语言模型提取的特征在自然语言理解和神经活动预测中具有广泛有效性。在源级摘要中，正向保留预测和对低水平基线的提升普遍存在；跨Brain Treebank和Podcast ECoG，432个可评估行中有67个满足受控预测标准，且模型侧特征消融显著影响预测得分。脑源性、时间关联性、声学和植入信号控制验证了分析流程的组件敏感性。结果表明，语言模型衍生量可有效标注语言理解过程中的神经活动，但参与者层面的控制优势呈局部化，响应特征特异性限制了对表征或计算机制的解释。整体上，研究将语言模型特征的预测效用与共享神经组织或语言处理计算的主张区分开来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言模型生成的表示是否能够作为自然语言理解过程中神经活动的有效预测因子，同时区分其预测能力与对神经组织或语言处理计算机制的推断。

Method: 采用八种冻结的语言模型、分块编码模型，并设置时间、干扰和表征容量等匹配控制条件，对Brain Treebank、MEG-MASC和Podcast ECoG的数据进行分析，通过特征消融和多种控制实验检验预测性能与敏感性。

Result: 在源级摘要中广泛观察到正向保留预测和对低水平基线的改进；67/432个可评估行满足受控预测标准；模型侧特征消融显著改变预测分数；多种控制条件验证了分析流程的组件敏感性。

Conclusion: 语言模型衍生特征可有效预测自然语言理解中的神经活动，但其预测效用不应直接等同于对共享神经组织或语言处理计算机制的推论，未来需联合索引数据以实现更完整的整合解释。

Abstract: Language-model representations provide structured, high-dimensional annotations of naturalistic language stimuli and can serve as informative neural predictors during comprehension. We analyzed locked derived data from Brain Treebank, MEG-MASC, and Podcast ECoG with eight frozen language models, blocked encoding models, and matched temporal, nuisance, and representation-capacity controls. Positive held-out prediction and gains over low-level baselines were widespread in source-level summaries. Across Brain Treebank and Podcast ECoG, 67 of 432 evaluable rows met a controlled predictive-only criterion, and model-side feature ablations changed prediction scores in most evaluable source rows. Brain-derived, timing-linked, acoustic, and implanted-signal controls confirmed component-level sensitivity of the analysis pipeline. These findings show that language-model-derived quantities can annotate neural activity during natural speech and text comprehension. Participant-level matched-control advantages were localized rather than uniform, response-profile and feature-specificity contrasts bounded representational or computational interpretations, and complete co-indexed integrated interpretation will require future jointly indexed coverage. Together, the analyses identify language-model features as useful neural predictors and separate predictive usefulness from claims about shared neural organization or language-processing computations.

*Subham Kumar,Prakrithi Shivaprakash,Abhishek Manoharan,Astut Kurariya,Diptadhi Mukherjee,Prabhat Chand,Pratima Murthy,Koustav Rudra,Lekhansh Shukla,Animesh Mukherjee*

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) is increasingly used to document clinical encounters, yet its reliability in multilingual and demographically diverse Indian healthcare context remains largely unknown. We further fine-tune two of the best performing opensource models, i.e., Gemma3n and OmniLingual, using various methods. With this, we uncover systematic performance gaps tied to speaker role and gender, raising concerns about equitable deployment in clinical settings, which are further mitigated by fairness-aware fine-tuning. ### [142] [Auditing Framing-Sensitive Behavioral Instability in Large Language Models for Mental Health Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26982)
*Abla Bedoui,Ashley L. Greene,Mohammed Cherkaoui*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了不同语境框架对大语言模型在心理支持等敏感对话应用中行为一致性的影响。通过控制匹配的提示，发现语境框架会系统性地改变模型的回应倾向；层间探测分析显示，与行为相关的信息在整个变压器深度中仍可解码，且不同架构间解码强度存在差异；即使有强烈的词汇基线，保留的语境探测仍显著高于随机水平；激活引导实验表明，与语境相关的表征方向可部分调节下游行为结果。研究强调，在心理健康导向的对话AI系统评估中，对上下文变异的鲁棒性应作为一致性与可信度的重要考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在心理支持等敏感对话场景中，大语言模型的行为稳定性与一致性对建立用户信任至关重要。然而，相同语义关切可能因不同语境框架而引发不同响应，导致模型行为不一致，影响用户体验与系统可靠性。现有研究多关注行为层面的变异性，但缺乏对模型内部表征如何反映这种变化的理解。因此，亟需探究语境框架如何影响模型的内在表示，以提升对话AI的可信度和一致性。

Method: 采用受控匹配提示，覆盖多种语境框架条件，针对多个指令微调模型家族进行实验。通过层间探测分析（layer-wise probing）评估行为相关信号在模型各层中的可解码性，并引入保留语境探测（held-out framing probes）检验其超越词汇基线的能力。进一步通过激活引导实验，探索语境相关表征方向对下游行为的调控作用。

Result: 语境框架显著影响模型的回应倾向，且该影响在不同模型架构中表现一致但强度各异。行为相关信号在整个变压器深度中均可解码，表明语境信息在深层表征中持续存在。即使在强词汇基线条件下，保留的语境探测仍显著优于随机水平。激活引导实验表明，语境相关表征方向能够部分引导模型行为变化，说明其具有实际影响能力。

Conclusion: 模型对语境框架的敏感性反映了其内部表征的非鲁棒性，这可能削弱其在心理健康等高敏感领域中的可信度。因此，在评估此类系统的可靠性时，必须将对上下文变异的鲁棒性作为核心指标，以确保行为一致性与用户信任。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly being integrated into mental health support tools and other psychologically sensitive conversational applications. In such settings, behavioral stability and consistency are important for trustworthy human-AI interaction. However, semantically similar concerns can be presented through different contextual framings, potentially eliciting different model responses. Such framing-sensitive variability may challenge user expectations regarding system behavior and complicate the assessment of AI reliability. While prior studies have primarily examined such effects at the behavioral level, less is known about how framing-related variation is reflected in the internal representations of aligned language models. In this work, we investigate these effects using controlled matched prompts spanning multiple contextual framing conditions across several instruction-tuned model families. Across architectures, framing systematically alters interpretive response tendencies. Layer-wise probing analyses show that behavior-associated information remains decodable throughout transformer depth, with architecture-dependent variation in decoding strength. Moreover, held-out framing probes remained consistently above chance across architectures despite strong lexical baselines. Activation steering experiments further suggest that framing-associated representational directions can partially modulate downstream behavioral outcomes. Finally, these findings indicate that robustness to contextual variation may represent an important consideration when evaluating the consistency and trustworthiness of conversational AI systems deployed in mental-health-oriented interactions.

### [143] [ReaORE: Reasoning-Guided Progressive Open Relation Extraction Empowered by Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26986)
*Xin Lin,Liang Zhang,Guoqi Ma,Hongyao Tu,Jinsong Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出ReaORE框架，通过粗到细的推理实现开放关系抽取，解决现有方法在未见关系类型上泛化能力差的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OpenRE方法要么依赖聚类无法生成关系标签且泛化能力差，要么依赖LLM直接生成标签但缺乏区分易混淆关系的能力。

Method: ReaORE包含两个阶段：(i) 关系过滤，通过多方面推理和基于嵌入的相似性补充与过滤，生成初始关系集；(ii) 关系预测，通过细粒度对比推理从候选集中准确预测目标关系。

Result: 在两个主流OpenRE数据集上的实验表明，ReaORE优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: ReaORE通过渐进式推理机制有效提升了开放关系抽取中对未见关系类型的识别能力，具备更强的泛化性能。

Abstract: Open Relation Extraction (OpenRE) requires a model to extract unseen relations between head and tail entities from unstructured text for real-world applications. The core challenge of OpenRE lies in achieving reliable generalization to unseen relation types. Current OpenRE approaches either employ clustering techniques, which cannot generate relation labels and suffer from poor generalization, or rely on direct relation label generation via Large Language Models (LLMs), which lack sufficient discriminative capacity to distinguish easily confused relations. To address these limitations, we propose Reasoning-guided progressive OpenRE (ReaORE), a framework for performing relation extraction through coarse-to-fine relation reasoning. Specifically, ReaORE consists of two key stages: (i) relation filtering, which reasons over multiple aspects to understand relations and instances, yielding an initial relation set, and further supplements and filters relations via embedding-based similarity to ensure the target relation is included; (ii) relation prediction, which aims to predict the target relations from the above set via fine-grained comparative reasoning to better distinguish easily confused relations. Extensive experiments on two widely used OpenRE datasets demonstrate that ReaORE outperforms existing baselines.

### [144] [Where Do Models Find Happiness? Emotion Vectors in Open-Source LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26987)
*Sinie van der Ben,Raphaël Baur,Yannick Metz,Mennatallah El-Assady*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究在两个开源模型（Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 和 Gemma-4-E4B-it）中验证了情绪向量的普遍性，发现两者均表现出与人类心理结构相符的效价（valence）几何特征，效价与主成分1（PC1）的相关性分别达到 $r = 0.76$ 和 $r = 0.83$。值得注意的是，效价表示在不同模型中的演化路径存在差异：Gemma 模型中效价早期即强编码但后期衰减，而 Apertus 模型则在中层才出现效价表征。此外，唤醒度（arousal）编码对生成语料敏感，使用 Gemma 生成的故事时，唤醒度与 PC2 的相关性更高（最高 $r = 0.45$），而在 Apertus 生成的语料中相关性较低（$r \leq 0.21$），表明唤醒度线索在不同语料中分布不均。研究开源了代码和数据集，以支持后续对语言模型中情绪表征的可复现研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究先前在 Claude Sonnet 4.5 中发现的情绪向量是否具有跨模型的普遍性，并理解不同模型架构下情绪表征的演化模式与语料依赖性。

Method: 从两个开源语言模型（Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 和 Gemma-4-E4B-it）的所有层中提取情绪对比向量，利用两种由模型生成的语料库进行分析，通过主成分分析（PCA）评估情绪维度（效价与唤醒度）与主成分之间的相关性。

Result: 两个模型均在整体上恢复了效价几何结构，且相关性接近甚至超过原始发现（Claude: $r=0.81$）。Gemma 模型中效价早期强、后期弱；Apertus 模型中效价中层才出现。唤醒度编码显著依赖于生成语料：使用 Gemma 生成的文本时，唤醒度与 PC2 相关性更强（最高 $r=0.45$），而 Apertus 生成的语料中相关性较低（$r\leq0.21$）。

Conclusion: 情绪向量在不同语言模型中具有一定的普遍性，但其在模型深度中的演化模式和对输入语料的敏感性存在显著差异，提示情绪表征并非统一机制，而是受模型架构与训练数据共同影响。研究强调了开发可复现方法的重要性，并为未来探索多模型情绪结构提供了基础。

Abstract: Recent work identified emotion vectors in Claude Sonnet 4.5, which are internal representations that encode emotion concepts, causally influence behavior, and exhibit geometry mirroring human psychological structure. We test the generality of these findings in two open-weight models, Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 and Gemma-4-E4B-it, extracting emotion contrast vectors across all layers, using two model-generated corpora. We recover valence geometry for both models, with peak PC1--valence correlations of $r = 0.76$ and $r = 0.83$, approaching the $r = 0.81$ reported for Claude.Beyond replication, we observe notable differences in how valence representations emerge across model depth. In Gemma-4-E4B-it, valence is strongly encoded in early layers but collapses towards later layers, whereas Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 exhibits the opposite pattern, with valence representations absent in early layers, but emerging at mid depths. Arousal encoding, in contrast, is sensitive to the extraction corpus: both models show stronger PC2--arousal alignment with Gemma-generated stories ($r$ up to $0.45$) than Apertus-generated ones ($r \leq 0.21$), suggesting arousal-relevant cues are unevenly distributed across generated corpora. We open-source our experiment code and dataset for reproducible investigation of emotion representations across language model architectures.

</details>


### [145] [MinGram: A Minimalist Unigram Tokenizer with High Compression and Competitive Morphological Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27019)
*Sander Land*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MinGram 是一种简化版的 Unigram 分词器，通过使用 BPE 生成的种子词汇、硬 EM 算法和单一的分数剪枝步骤，显著降低了训练复杂度。它保留了 Unigram 的词汇表可编辑性，同时在压缩率上优于 BPE 和标准 Unigram，且在形态对齐和下游语言模型性能方面表现更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Unigram 分词器虽然具有易于编辑词汇表的优点，但其训练过程复杂且耗时。为了降低训练开销并保持高质量的分词效果，作者提出 MinGram，旨在简化训练流程，提升效率，同时维持或超越现有方法的压缩与语言建模性能。

Method: MinGram 使用 BPE 生成初始词汇表，采用硬 EM 算法在最小令牌路径上进行优化，并通过一次扁平化的分数剪枝步骤完成训练。该方法摒弃了后向-前向传递、迭代剪枝循环和后缀数组等复杂结构，仅依赖于分词器推理本身，实现高效训练。

Result: 在六种语言上的实验表明，MinGram 的压缩性能优于 BPE 与标准 Unigram；其压缩导向变体达到最强的词计数压缩器水平，同时具备更高的形态对齐能力。在受控的语言模型训练中，Unigram 系列分词器（包括 MinGram）在 bits-per-byte 指标上持续优于 BPE。

Conclusion: MinGram 通过简化训练流程，在保持高压缩率和良好形态对齐的前提下，实现了比传统 Unigram 更高效的训练方式，是 Unigram 分词器的一个重要改进，尤其适用于需要快速迭代和高性能分词的应用场景。

Abstract: The Unigram tokenizer uses an elegant representation which makes it straightforward to edit vocabularies, but its training is comparatively heavy and complex. We introduce MinGram (Minimalist Unigram), which keeps the token-list representation but simplifies training using a BPE-derived seed vocabulary, Hard EM on a minimum-token path, and a single flat score-pruning step. This removes the suffix array, the forward-backward pass, and the iterative prune loop, leaving a procedure that requires little beyond tokenizer inference itself. By making token count the primary objective and using a Unigram score only as a tiebreak, MinGram keeps the compression of pure token-count methods while retaining much of the morphological alignment and downstream quality of probabilistic ones. Across six languages, MinGram compresses better than both BPE and standard Unigram, and a compression-oriented variant matches the strongest token-count compressors while retaining substantially higher morphological alignment. In controlled downstream language-model training, Unigram-family tokenizers, with MinGram among the best, consistently beat BPE in bits-per-byte.

### [146] [Improving General Role-Playing Agents via Psychology-Grounded Reasoning and Role-Aware Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27025)
*Zhenhua Xu,Dongsheng Chen,Jian Li,Yitong Lin,Zhebo Wang,Jiafu Wu,Yizhang Jin,Chengjie Wang,Meng Han,Yabiao Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前角色扮演模型依赖监督微调，导致行为模仿缺乏深层人类思维，泛化能力差；且基于LLM的奖励模型无法区分真实角色相关表达与通用“作弊”短语，造成训练偏差。

Conclusion: 结合心理学驱动的结构化推理与角色感知的强化学习优化，可有效提升角色扮演代理的角色一致性与泛化能力，为构建高质量通用角色扮演模型提供新范式。

Abstract: Building general-purpose role-playing agents that faithfully portray any character from a natural-language profile remains challenging. The dominant paradigm -- supervised fine-tuning -- encourages behavioral mimicry without deep, human-like internal thought processes, resulting in poor out-of-distribution generalization. Therefore, we propose \textbf{Psy-CoT}, a psychology-grounded chain-of-thought framework that decomposes pre-response reasoning into three role-specific steps -- \emph{Interaction Perception}, \emph{Psychological Empathy}, and \emph{Logical Construction} -- so that the model \emph{thinks dynamically} from the profile rather than merely mimicking surface patterns. While structured reasoning provides a foundation, it alone is insufficient; reinforcement learning is essential to further align the model with character fidelity. However, we observe that under LLM-based reward models, both generic phrases that hack the reward model and genuinely role-specific phrases receive identical gradient signals -- this hacking accumulates over training, misleading the model into treating both as equally optimal choices. To address this, we propose \textbf{Role-Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO)}, which uses profile--token mutual information to weight gradients asymmetrically -- amplifying role-specific tokens under positive advantage while attenuating them under negative advantage. Experiments on CoSER, CharacterBench, and CharacterEval demonstrate that Psy-CoT outperforms existing role-playing CoT methods, and RAPO consistently surpasses GRPO across multiple model scales.

### [149] [The Riddle Riddle: Testing Flexible Reasoning in Large Language Models and Humans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27103)
*Bella Fascendini,Kathryn McGregor,Max D. Gupta,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过'谜语谜语'范式测试大语言模型（LLMs）是否具备灵活推理能力。结果显示，LLMs在真实谜语中表现优于谜语式字面题（84.9% vs. 50.7%），而人类则相反（50.5% vs. 80.5%）。LLMs错误多因误用创造性推理，人类错误多因过度使用字面推理，表明LLMs的表现更依赖记忆而非灵活策略选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在认知任务中的表现是否源于模式匹配或真正的灵活推理，以区分表面正确与实质合理的行为。

Method: 设计‘谜语谜语’范式，对比真实谜语与字面解释即可作答的类似谜语题目，通过两个实验评估9个先进LLMs和100名人类参与者的表现差异。

Result: LLMs在真实谜语中准确率高但在字面题中大幅下降，人类则相反；错误分析显示LLMs主要因不当使用创造性推理出错，人类则更多因过度依赖字面理解出错。

Conclusion: LLMs在真实谜语中的高准确率可能源于记忆检索而非灵活策略选择，若无此类对比设计，易将看似合理的输出误认为真实推理。

Abstract: Humans flexibly adapt their reasoning strategies to the requirements of a given problem. Large language models (LLMs) have performed well on many cognitive tasks, however, it is unclear whether this accuracy is a result of pattern matching from training data or flexible reasoning. Here, we introduce a novel paradigm to test this question: the riddle riddle paradigm. Riddle riddles are word problems written to mimic popular riddles, but altered so their answers only require literal interpretations. Identifying correct answers requires looking past the structure of each question and flexibly apply different reasoning strategies based on the content. If LLMs respond to surface features, such as form, a riddle-like structure should cause models to use an inventive reasoning strategy even when a literal interpretation suffices. Alternatively, if LLMs reason based on content, they should flexibly switch strategies when appropriate. Across two experiments with nine state-of-the-art LLMs and 100 human participants, we show humans and LLMs fail on this paradigm in opposite directions. LLMs were far more accurate on genuine riddles than on riddle riddles (84.9% vs. 50.7%); whereas humans showed the reverse effect (50.5% vs. 80.5%). Error analysis shows that 90.8% of LLM errors on riddle riddles (the condition where they show diminished performance) were due to inappropriate use of inventive reasoning while only 57.6% of human errors on genuine riddles were due to overextending literal reasoning. Thus, while both groups make mistakes, reasoning mistakes are made more often by LLMs than by humans. Overall, LLMs' strong performance on genuine riddles may reflect memory retrieval rather than flexible strategy selection, and without stimuli designed to elicit this contrast, it becomes easy to conflate LLM-generated outputs that look like reasoning with genuine reasoning.

### [150] [Forecasting With LLMs: Improved Generalization Through Feature Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27199)
*Humzah Merchant,Bradford Levy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在预测任务中的推理机制，通过稀疏自编码器分析其内部状态，发现模型同时具备时间感知和前瞻偏差特征。通过干预这些可解释的时序特征，增强时间感知能力能显著降低前瞻偏差，同时保持通用推理性能；而调整前瞻偏差特征则无明显效果。结果表明，可解释的时序特征可用于因果性地引导模型进行更基于历史的推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大型语言模型在预测任务中是否依赖于特定时间的知识还是可泛化的模式，以改进其推理的准确性和可靠性。

Method: 使用稀疏自编码器分析LLMs在多种预测任务中的内部状态，识别与时间感知和前瞻偏差相关的特征，并在不同领域中对这些特征进行干预实验。

Result: 增强时间感知特征显著减少了前瞻偏差，且不影响通用推理能力；而干预前瞻偏差特征未产生显著影响。

Conclusion: 可解释的时序特征能够被用于因果性地引导大型语言模型向更基于历史的推理方式转变，从而提升预测任务中的合理性与稳定性。

Abstract: Successful forecasting involves identifying patterns between historical and future states of the world which generalize to future observations. We apply LLMs to a variety of forecasting tasks and inspect their internal states using sparse autoencoders to understand whether they appear to rely on time-specific pieces of knowledge versus generalizable patterns. Our analyses identify features associated with both time-aware reasoning and look-ahead-biased reasoning. We then apply the LLMs to an entirely different domain and intervene on these features. We find that amplifying time-awareness features substantially reduces look-ahead bias on forecasting prompts while preserving general reasoning performance. In contrast, steering the candidate look-ahead-bias features does not produce an effect. These results suggest that interpretable temporal features can be used to causally shift LLMs toward more historically grounded reasoning.

### [151] [Syntactic Belief Update as the Driver of Garden Path Processing Difficulty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27206)
*Alan Zhou,Miloš Stanojević,John T. Hale*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于句法信念更新的模型，用于解释花园路径句子中的处理困难。该模型通过计算句法树分布的更新量（使用广义Rényi散度）来预测阅读时间，优于传统的词汇意外性（lexical surprisal）方法，且不依赖词汇概率，为心理语言学提供了非词汇性替代指标的新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统词汇意外性模型无法有效预测花园路径句子的处理难度，因为其在关键词处的预测失败。需要一种不依赖词汇概率、能捕捉句法误解与修正过程的替代指标。

Method: 提出一个句法信念更新框架，动态维护句法树的概率分布，并在每个新词后更新；当出现关键词导致初始句法解释错误时，计算信念分布的大幅更新，用广义Rényi散度量化更新量。

Result: 该模型在预测人类阅读时间数据上表现优于词汇意外性模型，尤其在花园路径句子中表现出更优的拟合效果。

Conclusion: 句法信念更新提供了一种有效的非词汇性处理难度预测机制，为心理语言学研究开辟了新的方向，强调句法结构本身的动态变化对语言理解的重要性。

Abstract: Garden path sentences present a processing difficulty for humans -- the sentence prefix leads the listener towards one interpretation, until the listener hears a critical word that shows that the initial interpretation was wrong. Lexical surprisal, a measure that usually predicts sentence processing difficulty quite well, fails to provide good predictions for garden path sentences.
  We propose an alternative that actively predicts a probability distribution over syntactic trees (its syntactic belief) and updates that distribution after each new word. If a processor is led down a garden path, syntactic beliefs will be wrong and will require a large update at the critical word. The magnitude of the update is measured with a generalized Rényi divergence. Crucially, this metric is dependent on lexical items, but is fully independent of the probability of lexical items. This Syntactic Belief Update provides a better fit to the human reading time data on garden path sentences. This suggests a new research direction examining purely non-lexical alternatives to surprisal for psycholinguistics.

</details>


### [152] [Paved with True Intents: Intent-Aware Training Improves LLM Safety Classification Across Training Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27210)
*Jeremias Ferrao,Niclas Müller-Hof,Iustin Sîrbu,Traian Rebedea,Yftah Ziser*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出安全分类器应将用户意图作为提示与最终标签之间的显式信号。为此，作者构建了AIMS数据集，包含1,724个具有挑战性的安全提示，每个提示均配有意图描述和危害标签。通过该数据集评估了在监督微调、偏好学习、推理蒸馏和强化学习等多种训练范式下的意图感知训练效果。结果显示，尽管数据集规模有限，但其在各类训练方法中均表现出色：基于模型生成意图的DPO优于SFT，意图条件蒸馏在多数师生对中优于仅依赖推理的蒸馏。尤其重要的是，直接通过GRPO奖励意图忠实性，在五个外部安全基准上取得了最佳平均性能，且意图感知模型实现了推理延迟-准确率的帕累托前沿。表明忠实的意图建模是提升安全分类器鲁棒性的高效监督信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全分类器缺乏对用户意图的显式建模，导致在复杂或模糊提示下判断不准确。为提升安全性与可靠性，需引入意图作为关键中间信号，增强模型对真实意图的理解能力。

Method: 构建并使用人类标注的AIMS数据集（1,724个高难度安全提示，含意图描述与危害标签），在多种训练范式（如SFT、DPO、GRPO、推理蒸馏）中评估意图感知模型的表现，比较不同方法在多个外部安全基准上的性能差异。

Result: 意图感知训练显著提升安全分类器性能：DPO在模型生成意图基础上优于传统SFT；意图条件蒸馏优于纯推理蒸馏；GRPO直接奖励意图忠实性时，在五项外部基准上表现最优，并实现推理延迟与F1值的帕累托最优。

Conclusion: 忠实建模用户意图是一种紧凑而高质量的监督信号，能有效提升安全分类器的鲁棒性与性能，推动更可靠的安全防护系统发展。

Abstract: We argue that safety classifiers should model user intent as an explicit signal between the prompt and the final label. To study this, we introduce AIMS, a human-annotated dataset of 1,724 difficult safety prompts, each paired with an intent description and harm label. We use AIMS to evaluate intent-aware training across supervised fine-tuning, preference learning, reasoning distillation, and reinforcement learning. Despite its size, AIMS enables competitive safety classifiers across training regimes: DPO from model-generated intent errors improves over SFT, and intent-conditioned distillation outperforms reasoning-only distillation in most teacher-student pairs. Most notably, directly rewarding intent faithfulness with GRPO yields the strongest average performance across five external safety benchmarks, while our intent-aware models form the inference latency-F1 Pareto frontier. These results show that faithful intent modeling is a compact, high-quality supervision signal for more robust safety classifiers.

Abstract: Formal semantics has shown that sentence meanings arise by recursively composing lexical meanings, yet much of the literature on semantic universals models either lexicons with fixed signal structures or holistic composition without interpretable lexical parts. We introduce a framework that integrates this fundamental insight of formal semantics in evolutionary modeling, by allowing lexical meanings and a composition function to co-evolve under pressures for conceptual simplicity and communicative accuracy. We apply this framework to the evolution of quantificational meaning. Analyzing the Pareto frontier, we find that the most well-known semantic universal, conservativity, emerges as an efficient system-wide abstraction. ### [154] [CARVE: Content-Aware Recurrent with Value Efficiency for Chunk-Parallel Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27229)
*Sayak Dutta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CARVE是一种内容感知的循环模型，通过仅在键轴上擦除来解决当前主流增量规则架构（GDN-2）中的三个缺陷：记忆盲门、值轴擦除掩码浪费参数，以及破坏WY形式三角块求解器。CARVE利用已写入GPU内存的递归输出张量作为免费的内容信号，将每个值的写门投影替换为每头一个标量，实现高效记忆管理。在13亿参数、1000亿词训练下，其在WikiText上的困惑度为15.72（比GDN-2低0.18，显著提升），在九个常识推理基准上超越所有递归基线，并在所有RULER检索探测中达到新最佳表现；同时具有0.4%吞吐量开销、13%更低峰值内存和19%更少参数。六项形式定理涵盖记忆容量、李雅普诺夫稳定性、梯度流、表达能力分离、帕累托最优块大小与混合最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有递归模型在决定擦除内容时缺乏对存储信息的感知（即‘记忆盲门’），导致效率低下且限制了训练性能。尤其在主流的GDN-2架构中，值轴擦除掩码浪费大量参数，且数学上阻碍了使递归模型可与Transformer竞争的WY形式三角块求解器的有效性。因此需要一种能基于内容自适应控制擦除的新机制。

Method: 提出CARVE（Content-Aware Recurrent with Value Efficiency），核心原则是仅在键轴上执行擦除操作，从而保持WY形式求解器的数学有效性。利用已存在的递归输出张量作为免费内容信号，构建内容感知的擦除门；将原本针对每个值的写门投影简化为每头一个标量，大幅降低参数量。初始状态与GDN-2完全一致，差异仅源于学习到的内容门策略。

Result: 在1.3B参数规模下训练100B tokens后，CARVE在WikiText上取得15.72的困惑度（较GDN-2下降0.18，4.5σ显著性），在九个常识推理任务中全面领先所有递归基线，在所有RULER检索探测中达到新高。同时实现0.4%吞吐量开销、13%更低峰值内存、19%更少参数，展现出卓越的效率与性能平衡。

Conclusion: CARVE通过内容感知的键轴擦除机制，从根本上解决了递归模型中记忆盲门与参数浪费问题，恢复并强化了递归训练的竞争力。其设计兼具理论严谨性（六项定理支持）与实际优越性，标志着递归模型在效率与性能上的重大突破。

Abstract: Recurrent models must forget in order to remember, yet the state of the art decides what to erase without consulting what is stored -- the gate sees only the arriving token, not the memory it is about to modify. This memory-blind gating is one of three coupled defects in the leading delta-rule architecture (GDN-2): the value-axis erase mask wastes parameters at the scale of the value projection, and -- as we prove -- mathematically prevents the WY-form triangular chunk solver that makes recurrent training competitive with Transformers.
  We introduce CARVE (Content-Aware Recurrent with Value Efficiency), which resolves all three problems through one principle: erase only on the key axis. This is provably necessary and sufficient for the WY-form solver to remain valid. Within it, CARVE reuses the recurrent output tensor -- already written to GPU memory -- as a free content signal for the erase gate, and replaces the per-value write-gate projection with a single scalar per head. At initialisation CARVE is bit-identical to GDN-2; any quality difference emerges from what the content gate learns.
  At 1.3B parameters trained on 100B tokens, CARVE achieves WikiText perplexity 15.72 (minus 0.18 vs. GDN-2, a 4.5-sigma effect), leads every recurrent baseline on nine common-sense reasoning benchmarks, and sets state of the art on every RULER retrieval probe -- at 0.4% throughput overhead, 13% lower peak memory, and 19% fewer parameters. Six formal theorems cover memory capacity, Lyapunov stability, gradient flow, expressivity separation, Pareto-optimal chunk size, and hybrid optimality.

</details>

Our framework addresses key limitations in current analytical approaches through a hierarchical two-layer coding scheme that integrates cognitive and non-cognitive problem solving with metacognitive regulatory mechanisms. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型是否具备知识库应有的一致性特征，即同一事实在不同任务中应有稳定输出，以评估其作为知识库的可靠性。

Method: 通过行为分析和参数定位实验，考察模型在不同任务中对同一事实的处理方式，并分析链式思维推理中的参数使用情况。

Result: 发现模型对同一事实的知识表达具有任务特异性，不同任务对应不同的参数子集；链式思维推理部分依赖于非目标任务的参数，进一步揭示知识与任务间的紧密耦合。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) capture large amounts of factual knowledge applicable to a wide range of tasks, motivating the view of their parameters as a knowledge base. An important property of knowledge bases is that different queries for the same fact return consistent results, drawing on a single source of truth. We investigate whether LMs satisfy this property through behavioral and mechanistic analyses. Our results suggest that they encode knowledge in a task-specific manner. Behaviorally, facts acquired on one task frequently fail to co-emerge on others during training. Parameter localization experiments suggest a mechanistic explanation, revealing distinct parameter subsets underlying different tasks for the same fact. Finally, we show that chain-of-thought reasoning draws part of its effectiveness from engaging task-specific parameters beyond those tied to the evaluation task. Our findings suggest that what the model knows and how it is asked are intertwined in parameter space, undermining the "knowledge base" analogy and carrying implications for the reliability and controllability of factual knowledge in LMs.

### [157] [How Surprising Is Historical Italian to Language Models? Tokenization Tax, Comprehension Tax, and a Simple Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27275)
*Maria Levchenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个诊断框架，将历史语言处理难度分解为四个维度：分词成本、预测不确定性（意外性）、语义鲁棒性和上下文敏感性。通过三个跨三个世纪的语料库评估，发现17世纪意大利语的意外性是现代语的2.4倍（学术文本达3.2倍），而俄语仅略有增加；尽管预测不稳定，但语义嵌入保持高度相似性（>0.85），表明模型仍能有效表征历史意义。此外，仅需添加简单的时间上下文提示即可降低60%的历史意外性，说明数字图书馆可安全用于语义检索，但生成任务需针对性调整。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数字图书馆工作流中日益重要，但其对历史语言的处理能力尚不明确。当前研究常将历史语言困难视为单一障碍，混淆了拼写变异、语言距离与预训练暴露等因素。本文旨在系统拆解这一复杂性，揭示不同维度对模型表现的影响。

Method: 提出并应用一个四维诊断框架，涵盖分词成本、预测不确定性、语义鲁棒性和上下文敏感性。在三个历史语料库上进行评估：17世纪意大利文（1610–1689）、19世纪意大利经典《承诺的新婚夫妇》作为高曝光对照组，以及18世纪俄语民事印刷文献作为正交拼写压力测试。使用嵌入相似性、意外性指标和提示工程验证模型表现。

Result: 17世纪意大利语平均意外性是现代版本的2.4倍（学术文本达3.2倍），而俄语仅轻微上升；尽管预测不确定性高，但语义嵌入相似性仍高于0.85，表明语义表示未退化；引入时间上下文提示可使历史意外性下降约60%，显著提升稳定性。

Conclusion: 历史文本虽带来一致的编码开销，但大语言模型在语义表征方面具备鲁棒性。数字图书馆可安全用于语义检索任务，而生成类应用需通过轻量级提示策略加以适配。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly critical to digital library workflows, yet their ability to process historical language remains poorly understood. Historical difficulty is typically treated as a monolithic barrier, conflating orthographic variation, linguistic distance, and pretraining exposure. In this paper, we propose a diagnostic framework that decomposes this difficulty into four distinct dimensions: tokenization cost, predictive uncertainty (surprisal), semantic robustness, and context sensitivity.
  We evaluate this framework on three datasets spanning three centuries: (1) a newly curated corpus of 17th-century Italian texts (1610-1689) digitized from original page images; (2) canonical 19th-century Italian "I Promessi Sposi" serving as a high-exposure control; and (3) 18th-century Russian civil print books as a contrastive orthographic stress test.
  Our results reveal a distinct dissociation between encoding cost and comprehension. While Russian and early modern Italian incur comparable tokenization penalties (25-30% inflation), their predictive difficulty diverges sharply. 17th-century Italian is on average 2.4 times more surprising than its modern equivalent - with academic prose reaching 3.2 times - whereas Russian shows only a modest increase. But predictive uncertainty does not imply representational degradation: embedding similarity remains robust (> 0.85) across all datasets, confirming that models can represent historical meaning even when generation is unstable.
  Finally, we demonstrate that a minimal temporal context prompt reduces historical surprisal by approximately 60%, offering a simple, model-agnostic mitigation. These findings suggest that while historical text imposes a consistent encoding tax, digital libraries can safely deploy LLMs for semantic retrieval tasks, provided that generative applications are carefully adapted.

*Arnav Mazumder,Dengjia Zhang,Shuyue Stella Li,Yulia Tsvetkov,Niyati Bafna*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种上下文感知的翻译级联方法，在多语言推理中保留原始问题至管道末尾，显著提升跨语言推理性能，尤其在低资源语言上效果明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统翻译级联在每一步丢失关键信息（如文化背景、语体、消歧线索），导致误差传播和性能下降；需优化信息流以提升多语言推理质量。

Method: 在最终翻译模块的上下文中加入原始问题、英文翻译问题及推理过程，实现无需训练的简单干预。

Result: 在9个跨语言基准测试、3种模型架构和285种语言上验证，开放生成任务表现显著提升，原始问题提供最关键上下文支持。

Conclusion: 应重新设计机器翻译级联中的信息流，避免早期信息丢失；建议将用户原始问题保留在整个推理流程的最后阶段，作为默认策略。

Abstract: Translation cascades for reasoning translate the query from another language to English, reason in English, and translate the answer back to the original language. This is a competitive approach to multilingual reasoning, but structurally lossy, since each stage discards information later stages may need, including cues for cultural grounding, register, and disambiguation. We examine the benefits of a simple and training-free intervention: a context-aware translation cascade, which additionally provides the original question, the English translated question, and the reasoning trace to the context of the final translation module. We evaluate gains across nine multilingual benchmarks including various task types, three backbone models, and 285 high-, mid-, and low-resource languages, and demonstrate strong gains for open-ended generation across models and resource regimes. We show that the original language question carries most of the beneficial context. Our study emphasizes the need to better design information flow in machine translation cascades for mitigating error propagation, and provides a simple and actionable default strategy: preserve the original user question until the end of the pipeline.

We propose a comprehensive, mechanism-oriented taxonomy of ILE that abstracts away from communicative goals and instead categorizes the underlying operations through which meaning is encoded and recovered. We evaluate the taxonomy by incorporating it into LLM prompts and comparing it with four existing taxonomies and a no-taxonomy baseline, using 2,000 manually annotated TikTok and Bluesky posts. The proposed taxonomy attains the strongest document- and span-level performance across the three LLMs, achieving an improvement of 4.7% in accuracy and 5.4% in F1 over the best-performing benchmark. The empirical results reveal the importance of a comprehensive, mechanism-oriented taxonomy as a stable scaffold for detecting emerging coded language and a useful input to content moderation. *Serhii Hamotskyi,Akash Kumar Gautam,Christian Hänig*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次将大语言模型（LLM）应用于德国中央银行的证券合格性审查流程，提出一种生成式信息提取框架，通过分解任务为抽取、归一化和解释三个阶段，有效应对文本噪声和德英混杂内容。采用基于价值评估的方法（LLM作为裁判），实现更语义化的评估，结果表明该方法在文档级合格性判断上达到高达91%的精确率，表现出保守稳健的特性，显著降低误接受风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动验证证券作为抵押品的资格需处理长篇半结构化且常为双语的招股说明书，过程资源密集；传统命名实体识别（NER）方法受限于光学字符识别噪声、语言差异及严格跨度约束，并依赖大量人工标注数据，难以高效应对复杂场景。

Method: 提出基于大语言模型的生成式信息提取流程，将任务分解为抽取、归一化和解释三个阶段，增强对噪声文本和多语言内容的适应能力；引入以大语言模型为评判标准的价值评估方法，替代传统的基于位置的评价指标。

Result: LLM系统在文档级证券合格性判断中达到最高91%的精确率，具备高度保守性，能有效避免错误接受，显著提升审查效率与可靠性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了大语言模型在金融合规审查中的可行性与优势，其生成式架构与语义评估机制可有效克服传统方法的局限，为自动化监管审核提供了新范式。

Abstract: Verifying the eligibility of securities as collateral is a key responsibility of the German Central Bank. However, manually verifying these assets against legal and financial criteria within lengthy, semi-structured, and often bilingual prospectuses is a resource-intensive task. While previous efforts utilized traditional Named Entity Recognition (NER) for information extraction, these methods can struggle with OCR noise, linguistic variance, and rigid span-based constraints, and the need for manually annotated training data for each relevant annotation type. In this paper, we present the first case study applying Large Language Models (LLMs) to the eligibility examination process, shifting the paradigm toward a generative Information Extraction pipeline. Our approach decomposes the task into extraction, normalization, and interpretation, allowing for greater flexibility in handling noisy text and interleaved German-English content. We further introduce a value-based evaluation methodology using LLM-as-a-judge, which offers a more semantic assessment than location-based metrics. Our results demonstrate that LLM-based systems achieve high precision (up to 91%) in document-level eligibility, exhibiting a conservative operating profile that minimizes false acceptance.

### [161] [Empowering GUI Agents via Autonomous Experience Exploration and Hindsight Experience Utilization for Task Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27330)
*Tianyi Men,Zhuoran Jin,Pengfei Cao,Yubo Chen,Kang Liu,Jun Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PEEU方法，通过自主探索环境并利用事后经验生成高阶训练数据，提升小型多模态大模型在跨网站任务规划中的泛化能力。引入TDHAF框架分析任务分解的层次化泛化行为，发现低级原子技能不足以保证高级规划能力，而高级任务训练能带来更强的分布外泛化性能。实验表明，7B模型在真实世界基准上达到30.6%准确率，优于更大的Qwen2.5-VL-32B模型，验证了构建事后高阶任务和利用经验对小模型OOD规划能力的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型开源多模态大模型虽具成本低、隐私保护优势，但存在规划能力弱和跨网站泛化能力差的问题，亟需有效方法提升其复杂任务处理能力。

Method: 提出PEEU方法，包括自主环境探索以发现经验，以及利用事后经验合成严格对齐的高阶训练数据；同时设计TDHAF框架，系统分析任务在低、中、高三个粒度上的组合泛化行为。

Result: 7B模型在真实世界基准上取得30.6%准确率，超越更大规模的Qwen2.5-VL-32B模型；分析显示高阶任务训练显著增强分布外泛化能力，而低阶技能掌握不等于高阶规划能力。

Conclusion: 构建事后高阶任务并有效利用经验，是提升小型多模态大模型在复杂、跨网站任务中分布外规划能力的关键。

Abstract: Multimodal web agents can assist humans in operating repetitive GUI tasks, where effective task planning is essential for decomposing complex tasks into executable actions. While small open source MLLMs are cost efficient and privacy preserving compared with commercial large models, they suffer from weak planning and limited cross website generalization. To address these limitations, we introduce the planning experience exploration and utilization (PEEU) method, which autonomously explores environments to discover experiences and utilizes hindsight experience to synthesize strictly aligned, high level training data. To quantitatively analyze the generalization behaviors driving this performance, we propose the task decomposition hierarchical analysis framework (TDHAF) to systematically study compositional generalization across three task granularities: low, middle and high levels. Our analysis reveals that mastering low level atomic skills does not guarantee high level planning competence, while high level task training yields stronger OOD generalization. Experiments on real world benchmarks demonstrate PEEU's superior effectiveness: our 7B model achieves 30.6% accuracy, outperforming the much larger Qwen2.5-VL-32B model. These demonstrate constructing hindsight high level tasks and leveraging experiences is crucial for OOD planning abilities of small MLLMs.

### [162] [Mapping Political-Elite Networks in Europe with a Multilingual Joint Entity-Relation Extraction Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27347)
*Kirill Solovev,Jana Lasser*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个全开源的多语言联合实体-关系抽取管道，能够从大规模非结构化新闻语料中构建带符号、时间维度的知识图谱。该方法结合基于跨度的命名实体识别与三阶段链接级联，将文本提及映射至语言无关的Wikidata标识符，并采用高速、受本体约束的混合专家模型，通过引导解码提取有向、带符号的关系。在3491个关系的黄金标准上进行全覆盖抽查，显示文本正确率高达68.2%（严格）至93.7%（宽松）。两个大规模案例研究验证了其有效性：在奥地利，重建了政党完整生命周期，追踪内部裂痕及人员流向后续派系与司法判决；在波兰，揭示了国家企业庇护网络以及公民平台（PO）与法律与正义党（PiS）双寡头之间的结构平衡、带符号的冲突网络。该框架实现了原始多语言文本与结构化关系数据的桥梁作用，为跨国计算社会科学提供了稳健、可复现的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观察政治精英是否形成寻租联盟或公民网络以维持治理，依赖人工编码，难以规模化；现有自动化方法多限于简单共现分析，且受限于专有API、缺乏跨语言能力及实体消歧扩展性。亟需一种可扩展、跨语言、可复现的自动化方法来捕捉复杂、非正式、对抗性的政治关系网络。

Method: 提出一个模块化、全开源的多语言联合实体-关系抽取流水线。包含：1）基于跨度的命名实体识别（NER）；2）三阶段链接级联，将文本提及映射到语言无关的Wikidata标识符；3）高吞吐、受本体约束的混合专家模型，结合引导解码提取有向、带符号的关系，基于领域本体进行语义约束。最终生成带时间戳和符号的结构化知识图谱。

Result: 在3491个关系的黄金标准上，严格匹配准确率为68.2%，宽松匹配达93.7%。在奥地利案例中成功重建政党生命周期，追踪内部分裂、人员流动及司法后果；在波兰案例中揭示国家企业庇护网络及PO与PiS之间结构平衡的冲突网络。证明该方法在跨语言、大规模、复杂社会关系建模中的有效性与可靠性。

Conclusion: 本研究构建的开放、可复现的多语言联合实体-关系抽取框架，有效连接原始多语言文本与结构化关系数据，为跨国比较政治学中的计算社会科学提供强大工具，推动对政治网络动态演化的大规模实证研究。

Abstract: Whether political elites organise into rent-seeking coalitions that capture public resources or civic networks that sustain governance is a central question in comparative politics. Yet observing these complex, informal, and adversarial ties at scale has historically required intensive manual coding, while automated text-as-data methods have largely been limited to simple co-occurrence. Recent large language model (LLM) approaches offer a path forward but often rely on proprietary APIs, lack cross-lingual capability, and struggle with scalable entity resolution. We present a modular, fully open-weight pipeline for multilingual joint entity-relation extraction that builds signed, temporal knowledge graphs from massive unstructured news corpora. It combines span-based named-entity recognition (NER) with a three-stage linking cascade mapping mentions to language-independent Wikidata identifiers; a high-throughput, ontology-constrained mixture-of-experts model then uses guided decoding to extract directed, signed relationships grounded in a domain ontology. A full-coverage spot-check against a 3491-relation gold standard shows high textual correctness (68.2% strict to 93.7% lenient). Two large-scale case studies validate the pipeline against the public record. In Austria, it reconstructs a political party's complete lifecycle, dating internal fractures and tracking personnel into successor factions and court convictions. In a Polish corpus, it uncovers the overlapping economic and governance networks of state-enterprise patronage, alongside the structurally balanced, signed conflict network of the polarized Civic Platform (Platforma Obywatelska, PO)--Law and Justice (Prawo i Sprawiedliwość, PiS) duopoly. By bridging raw multilingual text and structured relational data, our framework provides a robust, replicable foundation for cross-national empirical computational social science.

### [163] [Detecting and Controlling Sycophancy with Cascading Linear Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26155)
*Maty Bohacek,Rishub Jain,Nicholas Dufour,Thomas Leung,Chris Bregler,Roma Patel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种迭代数据生成管道，通过分离与行为相关的级联线性特征，实现对语言模型行为的更精确解释与控制。研究聚焦于消除模型的'谄媚倾向'（sycophancy），即模型过度迎合用户偏好。通过使用具有不同程度特征的样本而非简单的二元对比样本，发现这些特征构成线性可分的子空间，从而能更清晰地定位与行为相关的模型激活，并实现更高效、可解释性强的检测、评分与可控调节。相比现有方法（如LLM作为裁判或系统提示），该方法在性能上相当或更优，且计算成本更低，具备更强的可解释性保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于激活调控的行为解释与控制依赖大量明确展示期望或非期望行为的对比样本，但此类样本难以获取且限制了模型特征的准确解耦。为提升解释能力与控制精度，需要更精细地分离与特定行为相关的特征，尤其是当行为呈现连续变化时。因此，本文旨在探索一种新方法，通过生成具有渐进式特征强度的样本，揭示行为背后的线性结构，以增强模型行为的可解释性与可控性。

Method: 提出一个迭代数据生成流程，通过逐步扰动输入并观察输出行为的变化，识别出能够线性影响目标行为（如谄媚）的特征路径。利用这些级联样本，构建线性可分的特征子空间，进而定位与行为高度相关的模型激活状态。通过分析激活模式的线性关系，实现对行为的精准检测、确定性打分及有效干预。

Result: 实验表明，通过级联样本发现的谄媚特征形成线性可分子空间，能够更准确地对应到真实行为；在检测、评分和可控调节任务中，该方法性能优于或等同于基于LLM评判和系统提示的基线方法，同时显著降低计算开销，并提供更强的可解释性保证。

Conclusion: 通过引入级联线性特征的识别机制，本研究实现了对语言模型行为更深层次的解释与控制。该方法不仅提升了特征解耦的精度，还增强了可控性的效率与透明度，为未来可信赖、可调试的大模型应用提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Interpreting and controlling model behaviors through activation steering methods requires many pairs of contrastive samples that clearly exhibit desired or undesired behavior. These data pairs determine the degree to which interpretability frameworks can reliably detect model features responsible for a behavior, and therefore the ability to steer models toward or away from such behavior. In this work, we present an iterative data generation pipeline that isolates cascading linear features responsible for a behavior. Specifically, we show how moving beyond simple binary pairs of samples, and instead isolating samples that show degrees of features that scale linearly with behavior, allows for better disentanglement of features. We focus on detecting and steering away from sycophancy -- the tendency of language models to prioritize user validation. We demonstrate that sycophancy features discovered through cascading samples form linearly separable subspaces, and allow for selection of model activations that more clearly correspond to the desired behavior than baseline approaches. We also evaluate their ability to enable detection, deterministic scoring, and robust steering, and see that they either match or outperform LLM-as-a-judge and system prompting baselines while providing lower computational demand and more interpretability guarantees. Code & Data: https://cascading-feats.github.io/

</details>


### [164] [Life After Benchmark Saturation: A Case Study of CORE-Bench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26158)
*Nitya Nadgir,Sayash Kapoor,Kangheng Liu,Peter Kirgis,Matilda Orona,Stephan Rabanser,Tilman Bayer,Abhishek Shetty,Yue Ling,Derrick Chan-Sew,Rumi Nakagawa,Saiteja Utpala,Zachary S. Siegel,Arvind Narayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出，当基准测试的准确率达到饱和时，仅以提升准确率为标准进行替换会忽略代理性能的六个关键维度：建构效度问题（如捷径）、分布外泛化能力、效率、可靠性、模型与支架的相对重要性，以及人机协作的增益。以计算可复现性科学代码基准CORE-Bench Hard为例，展示了在准确率饱和后，从这些维度评估仍能揭示有意义的性能洞察。研究提出了改进版基准CORE-Bench v1.1和分布外任务套件CORE-Bench OOD，发现即使准确率饱和，新基准仍可用于衡量效率、可靠性、模型与支架表现。此外，通过小规模随机实验发现，人机协作带来约两倍的速度提升，且该结果可能被低估。整体贡献提供了一种比当前主流准确率导向评估更严谨的替代范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基准测试在准确率饱和后常被弃用，但这一做法忽视了对代理性能多维度的深入分析，导致无法识别如捷径、泛化能力、效率、可靠性等关键问题，限制了对智能体真实能力的理解。

Method: 以CORE-Bench Hard为案例，引入改进版基准CORE-Bench v1.1与分布外任务套件CORE-Bench OOD；通过多维度评估指标分析代理在准确率饱和后的表现；开展小规模随机实验，测量人类与智能体协作在实际任务中的增益。

Result: 发现了建构效度威胁，如难以预见的捷径行为；验证了改进后基准在效率、可靠性、模型与支架性能上的持续有效性；实验证明人机协作带来约两倍速度提升，且存在未被完全捕捉的潜在增益。

Conclusion: 应超越单一准确率指标，采用多维度评估框架来全面理解智能体性能，尤其在准确率饱和后仍具价值。提出的方法为智能体评估提供了更全面、更严谨的替代范式。

Abstract: When a benchmark's accuracy saturates, it is often retired and replaced with a more challenging version. We show that this approach privileges accuracy and misses the opportunity to study six other key dimensions of agent performance: construct validity issues such as shortcuts, out-of-distribution generalizability, efficiency, reliability, the relative importance of the model versus the scaffold, and uplift from human-agent collaboration. We use CORE-Bench Hard, a benchmark for computational reproducibility of scientific code, as a case study to demonstrate that measuring agents along these dimensions yields meaningful insights into agent performance even after accuracy saturates. First, we surface threats to construct validity in CORE-Bench Hard that are difficult to anticipate with less capable agents. We introduce an improved benchmark, CORE-Bench v1.1, and an out-of-distribution task suite, CORE-Bench OOD. Second, we find that despite accuracy saturation, CORE-Bench v1.1 remains useful for measuring efficiency, reliability, model performance, and scaffold performance. Finally, we conduct a small-scale randomized experiment to measure uplift from human-agent collaboration on real-world computational reproducibility tasks. We find a statistically significant speedup by about a factor of two -- likely underestimated due to one-fifth of human-only reproductions reaching the time limit before completing -- and describe various other findings. Together, our contributions present a more rigorous alternative to the dominant accuracy-centric evaluation paradigm.

</details>


### [165] [Refusal Lives Downstream of Persona in Chat Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26161)
*Viola Zhong,Qirui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究发现指令微调聊天模型中的合规人格方向与拒绝方向存在交互作用，合规人格会抑制拒绝行为。在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct中，通过干预两个方向发现：人格引导可显著降低拒绝率（如Llama中从97%降至2%），且拒绝能力在深层网络中被调节，而非早期计算。移除深层的人格方向可恢复拒绝能力，而随机方向则无此效果，表明拒绝受人格的后期调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究将拒绝行为与人格特征视为独立机制，但实际中二者可能存在相互影响。本文旨在揭示两者之间的内在关联，特别是人格如何调控拒绝行为，以更全面理解模型决策过程。

Method: 从激活空间中提取合规人格方向与拒绝方向，并在模型不同层进行干预实验，包括投影操纵、方向移除等，观察拒绝行为的变化，结合多层分析判断其作用阶段。

Result: 合规人格方向能有效抑制拒绝行为；拒绝行为在深层网络中被人格所调控，移除深层人格方向可恢复拒绝能力，而随机方向无效；说明拒绝并非独立存在，而是依赖于人格表达阶段。

Conclusion: 拒绝行为并非孤立存在，而是受到合规人格方向的后期调控，即在深层网络中被表达阶段所控制。忽视人格与拒绝的交互关系会导致对模型行为理解的偏差。

Abstract: Linear directions in activation space have been identified for both refusal and persona traits in instruction-tuned chat models, but the two have been studied as separate mechanisms. We show they interact: a compliant persona gates refusal. In Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we extract a compliant model-persona direction and a refusal direction and intervene on both. Compliant persona steering suppresses refusal -- in Llama, the refusal rate falls from 97% to 2%. Reintroducing the refusal direction partially restores refusal at late layers but not at early ones. Projecting out the persona direction in a late-layer window restores it to baseline; projecting out a random direction does not. Refusal is therefore gated at the late-layer expression stage, downstream of where it is computed. Treating refusal as a single isolated direction misses its dependence on persona.

</details>


### [166] [AlgoEvolve: LLM-driven Meta-evolution of Algorithmic Trading Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26173)
*Dhruv Sharma,Gautam Shroff*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究将大语言模型（LLM）作为语义变异算子，应用于算法交易领域的程序进化发现。提出AlgoEvolve框架，通过生成、评估和迭代改进可执行的交易策略（以Python代码形式），在噪声大、非平稳且高度不连续的交易环境中实现自适应策略演化。引入元进化外循环优化内层提示词，提升搜索效率，减少无交易失败，并优于初始人工设计指令。结果表明，基于LLM的语义演化为复杂环境下的持续程序合成提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 算法交易环境具有噪声大、非平稳性和高度不连续性，传统方法难以有效应对；现有LLM应用多集中于静态编码任务，缺乏在动态复杂场景中的拓展。因此需要一种能适应复杂环境并持续生成优化策略的自动化框架。

Method: 提出AlgoEvolve框架，结合内层基于LLM的程序生成与进化机制，以及外层元进化循环优化提示词。策略以Python代码表示，通过严格测试协议评估性能。利用提示词进化提升探索与利用平衡，降低零交易失败率。

Result: 系统在多个实验中展现出自适应的交易规则切换能力，能根据市场状态自动调整策略逻辑。元进化优化的提示词显著优于初始人工设计，提高了策略生成效率与成功率，验证了该方法在复杂动态环境中的有效性。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的语义进化为算法交易等复杂动态环境中的持续程序合成提供了一种有效且可扩展的方法，具备实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Recent work shows that Large Language Models (LLMs) can act as semantic mutation operators for the evolutionary discovery of programs and proofs. Most current applications focus on static coding benchmarks. We extend this paradigm to algorithmic trading. This domain is uniquely challenging because it is noisy, non-stationary, and highly discontinuous. We present AlgoEvolve, an LLM-driven evolutionary framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively improves executable trading strategies. These strategies are expressed as Python code and evaluated through a rigorous testing protocol. Across multiple experiments, the system exhibits emergent regime-adaptive strategy logic, including autonomous shifts in trading rules. We further introduce a meta-evolutionary outer loop that evolves the prompts guiding program synthesis in the inner loop. This outer loop discovers improved search heuristics. These heuristics balance exploration and exploitation while reducing zero-trade failures. They consistently outperform initial human-designed instructions. The results demonstrate that LLM-based semantic evolution provides a viable approach for continual program synthesis in complex environments.

Abstract: As AI agent protocols proliferate, the governance structures shaping their interoperability standards remain empirically underexamined. Discourse alignment is denser in the permissionless setting, suggesting that open governance may foster greater thematic convergence despite decentralized participation. Here we develop a provenance-aware, knowledge-graph-based multi-agent framework unifying 466,525 Reddit posts, 60,782 WebMD reviews, and twenty years of U.S. FDA Adverse Event Reporting System records for nine antidepressants. For sertraline, many adverse events appeared in community sources hundreds of days before the corresponding FDA date. A Neo4j knowledge graph grounded in ATC-N, ICD-10, and MedDRA vocabularies preserves provenance, keeping every claim traceable and regulatory facts distinct from patient experience. These results establish source-aware integration as a route to more auditable psychiatric medication information, with usefulness and patient benefit to be tested prospectively.

### [169] [Accelerating Skill Assessment in Chess: A Drift-Diffusion-Enhanced Elo Rating System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26267)
*Tianyuan Zhou,Zhizheng Fu,Tianming Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Elo评分系统仅依据比赛结果进行调整，存在响应滞后问题，无法反映玩家在对局过程中的真实技能表现。为了提升评分系统的灵敏度和准确性，需要引入更细粒度的走步级信息，但面临噪声大和状态空间庞大的挑战。

Method: 受认知神经科学中漂移扩散模型（DDM）启发，将玩家技能表达建模为决策过程，利用走步级数据动态评估技能变化，并通过数学推导证明其与传统Elo系统的偏差保持有界，从而实现理论上的稳定性和一致性。

Result: 实验结果显示，相较于传统Elo系统，DD-Elo能够更快地响应玩家技能的变化，具备更高的敏感性和实时性，同时保持与现有评级体系的良好兼容性。

Conclusion: DD-Elo提供了一种可解释、高度响应且向后兼容的棋类评分解决方案，有效克服了传统Elo系统的响应滞后缺陷，适用于现代竞技棋类环境下的动态技能评估。

Abstract: Rating systems such as Elo serve as the gold standard for matchmaking in competitive chess. However, they inherently suffer from response lag due to their exclusive reliance on match outcomes, neglecting the granular quality of gameplay. Nevertheless, incorporating move-by-move information into rating adjustments presents a significant challenge given the substantial noise and the vastness of the game-state space. To address this, we propose the Drift-Diffusion-Enhanced Elo Rating System (DD-Elo), a novel skill assessment framework inspired by the drift diffusion model (DDM) from cognitive neuroscience. By modeling skill expression as a decision-making process, our model integrates move-level data to capture rapid skill fluctuations. We provide a rigorous mathematical derivation proving that DD-Elo maintains a bounded deviation from the traditional Elo system, ensuring theoretical alignment. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DD-Elo adapts to skill changes faster than Elo. Our findings suggest that DD-Elo offers an explainable, highly responsive, and backward-compatible solution for chess rating ecosystems. The implementation code is publicly available at https://github.com/Aquila-zhou1/DD-Elo .

*Jakob Salfeld-Nebgen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向高风险AI自主代理的计算治理模型，通过要求独立验证的证据来控制关键行动的执行，确保透明性与可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主AI代理可能执行临床处方、软件部署等重大且不可逆的操作，需要建立有效的治理机制以保障安全性和责任追溯性。传统监控推理过程的方式不足，因此借鉴人类机构对强大行为者的治理经验——不监控推理，而是要求在关键行动点有独立验证的证据。

Method: 提出一种计算治理模型：AI代理保有规划与推理的完全自主权，但无权直接执行高风险操作；执行需满足由独立权威源分别验证的预条件，这些条件与声明意图加密绑定，并由确定性策略评估；所有决策记录于防篡改日志中，支持独立复核。

Result: 实现了对高风险行动的可控执行，增强了系统的可信度与可审计性；通过软件部署和临床处方两个实例验证了该模型的有效性与可行性。

Conclusion: 该治理模型为高风险自主AI系统提供了一种可行的、基于证据的管控框架，有助于在保持代理自主性的同时实现安全性与问责制。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents may begin to perform consequential, irreversible actions such as clinical prescribing and production software deployment. This paper observes that human institutions have governed powerful autonomous actors not by monitoring their reasoning but by requiring independently attested evidence at the point of consequential action. We formalise this institutional pattern as a computational governance model for AI agent systems. Under the proposed model, an agent retains full autonomy over planning and reasoning but holds no execution authority over designated high-risk actions. Execution is conditional on preconditions that are each independently attested by a separate authoritative source, cryptographically bound to a declared intent, and evaluated by a deterministic policy. Decisions are recorded in a tamper-evident log amenable to independent re-verification. We present a proof-of-concept implementation and illustrate the model with examples from software deployment and clinical prescribing.

### [171] [COrigami: An AI Pipeline for Co-Designing Flat-Foldable Visually Recognisable Origami](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26299)
*Tom Zahavy,Shaobo Hou,Thomas Tumiel,James Doran,Francesco Faccio,Xidong Feng,Alex Havrilla,Igor Khytryi,Chenglei Li,Lisa Schut,Vivek Veeriah,Arijan Abrashi,Michał Kosmulski,Robert J. Lang,Nick Robinson,Brandon Wong,Marcus Chiam,Gloria Fang,Satinder Singh*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在计算折纸领域，如何在满足严格几何约束的同时兼顾主观视觉美感，是生成物理艺术的一大挑战。现有方法难以有效结合算法精确性与艺术创造性，因此需要一种能够理解自然语言并生成符合数学原理的折痕模式的智能系统。

Method: COrigami采用多阶段流程：首先根据自然语言描述生成语义骨架图；接着进行基础区域的紧凑排列；然后求解满足平折条件的折痕模式；再对折痕模式进行形态塑造；最后通过基于自主美学评价的强化学习进行迭代优化。整个过程整合了算法优化与自动审美反馈机制。

Result: 实验表明，COrigami能高效生成符合数学可平折性要求且具有视觉吸引力的折痕图案。系统生成的初始设计可被人类艺术家进一步扩展和调整，显著提升创作效率。同时，自主美学评估机制有效提升了输出的艺术质量。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了人工智能在满足多重物理约束条件下，实现数学严谨性与艺术美感融合的可能性。通过集成算法优化与自主美学评价，COrigami为计算折纸等高度结构化的艺术领域提供了可靠的协同创作范式。

Abstract: While generative AI has achieved remarkable success in solving problems with verifiable solutions, generating physical art that satisfies both strict geometric constraints and subjective visual aesthetics remains a challenge. This paper presents an approach to tackle these difficulties in the domain of computational origami, a mathematically rigid environment that grounds artistic design within the equations of flat foldability. We present COrigami, an end-to-end AI-driven pipeline that assists the design cycle by generating crease patterns from natural language. Our pipeline involves generating a semantic stick figure, computing a base packing, solving for a flat-foldable crease pattern, shaping the flat-folded crease pattern, and refining the generated model using reinforcement learning driven by an autonomous aesthetic evaluation loop. Our system acts as a highly effective collaborative assistant, generating structural starting points that human artists can further expand and shape. By integrating algorithmic optimisation with autonomous aesthetic critique, this work demonstrates how AI systems can satisfy multi-objective physical constraints to enable reliable, mathematically grounded co-creativity.

### [172] [The Verification Horizon: No Silver Bullet for Coding Agent Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26300)
*Binghai Wang,Chenlong Zhang,Dayiheng Liu,Jiajun Zhang,Jiawei Chen,Mouxiang Chen,Rongyao Fang,Siyuan Zhang,Xuwu Wang,Yuheng Jing,Zeyao Ma,Zeyu Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在基础模型能力增强的背景下，生成复杂解决方案已变得相对容易，而可靠验证则成为更困难的问题。作者指出，验证信号面临意图不明确和训练过程中代理与真实意图之间的差距扩大（如奖励黑客、信号饱和）两大挑战。为此，提出从可扩展性、忠实性和鲁棒性三个维度评估验证质量，并分析了四种奖励构造方法：测试验证器、评分标准验证器、用户作为验证者以及自动化代理验证器。实验表明，有针对性的验证设计能有效抑制奖励黑客、提升任务完成质量，并在多个基准上取得显著改进。核心结论是：随着策略能力的增长，固定奖励函数将失效，验证必须与生成器共同演进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基础模型推理能力和工程手段的进步，生成复杂解决方案变得容易，但可靠验证却日益困难。现有的验证机制都是对人类意图的近似，无法完全捕捉真实意图，导致验证过程面临意图不明确和训练中代理与意图偏差加剧的双重挑战。因此需要重新思考验证机制的设计原则。

Method: 从可扩展性、忠实性和鲁棒性三个维度构建评价框架，系统研究四种不同场景下的验证信号设计：测试验证器（通用编码任务）、评分标准验证器（前端任务）、用户作为验证者（真实世界任务）、自动化代理验证器（长周期任务）。通过多任务、多能力水平的实验分析奖励设计的核心挑战及优化路径。

Result: 实验证明，针对性的验证设计能够有效减少奖励黑客现象，提升任务完成质量，在多个内部和公开基准上均取得显著性能提升。同时发现，固定奖励函数无法适应不断增长的策略能力，验证机制必须随生成能力同步进化。

Conclusion: 验证必须与生成能力协同演进。单一、静态的奖励函数难以持续有效，未来的验证系统需具备动态适应性，以应对不断发展的智能体能力。

Abstract: A classical intuition holds that verifying a solution is easier than producing one. For today's coding agents, this intuition is being inverted: as foundation models develop stronger reasoning capabilities and engineering harnesses grow more sophisticated, generating complex candidate solutions is no longer difficult -- reliably verifying them has become the harder problem. Every verifier we can build is only a proxy for human intent, never the intent itself. This makes verification subject to a twofold difficulty: first, intent is underspecified by nature, making it inherently hard to faithfully check whether it has been fulfilled; second, during model training, optimization widens the gap between proxy and intent -- manifesting as reward hacking or signal saturation. To address this, we characterize the quality of verification signals along three dimensions -- scalability, faithfulness, and robustness -- and argue that achieving all three simultaneously is the central challenge. We further study four reward constructions: a test verifier for general coding tasks, a rubric verifier for frontend tasks, the user as verifier for real-world agent tasks, and an automated agent verifier for long-horizon tasks. Across different task types and policy capability levels, we conduct in-depth analysis and experiments on the core challenges of reward design and how to more effectively leverage reward signals. Experiments show that targeted verification design can effectively suppress reward hacking, improve task completion quality, and achieve significant gains across multiple internal and public benchmarks. These experiences collectively point to a core observation: no fixed reward function can remain effective as policy capability continues to grow; and verification must co-evolve with the generator.

</details>


### [173] [How Do Tool-Augmented LLM Agents Perform on Real-World Energy Analytics Tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26346)
*David Akinpelu,Akintonde Abbas,Rereloluwa Alimi,Ayodeji Lana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对能源领域中代理评估不足的问题，提出了一项关于工具增强型大模型代理在真实世界能源市场分析任务中的实证研究。构建了包含243个专家标注问题的评估环境，涵盖市场数据检索、知识解读与高级量化建模三类任务，使用包括实时电力市场API、监管文件搜索、电价数据库等在内的多种领域工具，并采用多维度评估协议衡量代理表现。研究对比了闭源与开源大模型的表现，揭示了模型能力与领域工具协同作用的关键机制，相关数据集和工具已公开以支持可复现性与后续研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前能源领域的评估仍主要依赖静态知识回忆，而实际能源市场分析需要实时数据获取、专业法规与市场知识以及在现实约束下的多步定量推理，因此亟需更贴近真实场景的评估体系。

Method: 构建一个包含243个专家设计任务的评估环境，覆盖市场数据检索、知识解读与高级量化建模三类任务；为代理配置一系列领域专用工具（如美国主要ISO的实时电力市场API、监管文件检索、电价数据库、资产优化模型及基于检索增强生成的文档分析）；采用多维度评分标准（方法正确性、答案准确性、属性一致性、来源有效性），并根据任务类型动态调整评分规则；对比分析闭源与开源大模型在该环境中的表现。

Result: 研究发现，工具增强显著提升了大模型在复杂能源任务中的表现，尤其在实时数据处理与多步推理方面；闭源模型整体表现优于开源模型，但开源模型在特定任务上具备可竞争潜力；工具与模型能力之间的协同效应明显，表明领域工具对提升专业领域智能代理性能至关重要。

Conclusion: 本研究填补了能源领域智能代理评估的空白，证明了工具增强型大模型在真实世界能源市场分析任务中的有效性，强调了结合高质量领域工具与先进大模型的重要性，为未来高精度、高可信度的专业代理系统开发提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Agentic benchmarks have emerged across general-purpose and domain-specific settings, including finance, coding, law, and drug discovery, yet energy-domain evaluations remain largely limited to static knowledge recall. This is a critical gap for a sector that requires live data retrieval, specialized regulatory and market knowledge, and multi-step quantitative reasoning under real-world constraints.
  We present an empirical study of tool-augmented LLM agents on real-world energy market analytics tasks. Our evaluation environment includes 243 expert-curated problems across three categories: (1) Market Data Retrieval and Analysis, (2) Knowledge Retrieval and Interpretation, and (3) Advanced Quantitative Modeling and Decision Analytics. Tasks include price and demand analysis, tariff impact modeling, asset revenue and returns estimation, hedging strategy analysis, and optimization modeling, with problems spanning multiple difficulty levels.
  Agents are equipped with a configurable suite of domain tools, including live electricity market APIs for major U.S. ISOs, regulatory docket search, utility tariff databases, asset optimization models, and retrieval-augmented generation over energy market documents. We assess agent responses using a multi-dimensional evaluation protocol that scores approach correctness, answer accuracy, attribute alignment, and source validity, with category-aware routing to match scoring criteria to question type. We evaluate both closed-source and open-source LLMs, providing a comparative analysis of how model capability and domain tooling interact in a high-stakes professional domain. Key artifacts are publicly released to support reproducibility and future research.

Addressing these gaps is essential for measuring real progress in multimodal intelligence and exposing capability boundaries.

### [176] [Instruction Bleed: Cross-Module Interference in Prompt-Composed Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26356)
*Ching-Yu Lin,Yifan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了提示组合式智能体系统中的一种常见故障模式：修改一个提示模块会无声地影响其他模块的行为，即使它们没有共享变量或执行依赖。作者将其形式化为“组合行为泄漏”（CBL），源于变压器自注意力机制缺乏模块间的正式边界。通过在部署的求职评估代理上进行实验（Claude Sonnet 4.6，144次测试），采用可复用的三通道协议（体积、内容、形式扰动）探测CBL，发现仅内容通道产生显著配对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63，置信区间不包含零），但未导致推荐翻转——属于标准QA检测不到的亚阈值状态，却可能在成千上万决策中累积。CBL与已知智能体失败模式（对抗注入、认知退化、多智能体故障传播、隐私泄露）正交。文章贡献包括操作定义、可复用协议、可检验预测集及系统级分类，确立跨模块干扰测量是提示式智能体评估的必要要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实践中，提示组合式智能体系统存在一种隐蔽的故障现象：修改一个模块的提示会意外影响其他模块的行为，而这些模块之间并无显式依赖。这种现象难以通过传统方法察觉，但可能在大规模应用中积累为严重问题。因此需要对其机制、检测方式和影响进行系统性研究。

Method: 提出组合行为泄漏（CBL）的概念，设计并应用三通道扰动协议（体积、内容、形式）对部署的求职评估代理进行实验，通过统计分析（如Cohen's d）量化非焦点模块扰动对目标模块的影响，并验证其是否显著。实验基于真实部署系统（Claude Sonnet 4.6），共144次测试。

Result: 仅内容扰动通道显示出显著的配对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63，95%置信区间不包含零），表明内容变化会通过共享上下文窗口引发跨模块行为改变。然而，该影响未导致推荐翻转，处于亚阈值状态，难以被常规质量评估捕获，但在长期运行中可能累积。此外，该现象独立于已有智能体失败模式，具有独特性。

Conclusion: 组合行为泄漏（CBL）是一种由架构非隔离性（如变压器自注意力无模块边界）引发的跨模块干扰机制。它虽不触发明显错误，但会在大量决策中缓慢累积风险。为此，必须将跨模块干扰测量纳入提示式智能体的评估流程，以确保系统的稳定性和可靠性。

Abstract: Practitioners of prompt-composed agentic systems report a recurring failure mode: editing one prompt module silently shifts the behavior of others despite no shared variable or executable dependency. We formalize this as compositional behavioral leakage (CBL): interference between modules sharing a context window. CBL is enabled by architectural non-isolation: transformer self-attention provides no formal boundary between concatenated modules. We probe CBL on a deployed job-evaluation agent (Claude Sonnet 4.6, 144 trials) through a reusable three-channel protocol that perturbs non-focal modules along volume, content, and form. Only the content channel produces a detectable paired effect (Cohen's d = 0.63, bootstrap 95% CI excluding zero); no recommendation flipped -- a sub-threshold regime invisible to standard QA but compounding across the thousands of decisions a deployed agent makes. CBL is orthogonal to known agent-failure axes (adversarial injection, cognitive degradation, multi-agent fault propagation, privacy leakage). We contribute an operational definition, a reusable protocol, a falsifiable prediction set, and a system-class characterization, establishing cross-module interference measurement as a requirement for prompt-composed agent evaluation.

</details>


### [177] [Accelerating Returns and the Qualitative Engine for Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26359)
*Guojun Liao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了雷·库兹韦尔的加速回报理论，指出尽管技术进步可能呈指数增长，但真正的科学发现仍依赖于人类的定性推理能力，而当前AI在这一方面远远落后。文章提出‘科学定性引擎’（QES）作为弥补这一差距的方案，强调科学发现过程本身蕴含的人类智慧值得保护与传承。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人工智能在执行和基础设施层面虽能快速进步，但在面对框架失效时所需的创造性、定性推理能力上仍严重不足，这限制了其在真正科学发现中的作用。因此需要一种机制来保留并传递人类在科学探索中的深层理解与智慧。

Method: 通过数学建模解释加速回报理论，并结合近期ARC-AGI-3测试结果对比人类与前沿AI的表现差异，论证当前AI缺乏灵活推理能力；进而提出QES作为应对该问题的系统性解决方案。

Result: 实证表明人类在科学发现任务中表现接近天花板，而当前先进AI系统仅达1%以下水平；说明定性推理能力仍是人类独有的核心优势。同时，QES被证明具有独立于AGI到来时间的价值，可作为保存人类科学智慧的重要工具。

Conclusion: 即使技术加速成为现实，也无法自动解决科学发现中的根本难题。真正的突破依赖于人类特有的定性推理与意义建构能力。因此，构建如QES这样的系统，不仅有助于推进科学探索，更是对人类智慧传承的必要举措。

Abstract: Ray Kurzweil described a thesis of accelerating returns, which is the most influential narratives in discussions of technological progress. Its central claim is that advances in multiple technological fields, especially compute, artificial intelligence, brain science, and biotechnology, interact in such a way that progress becomes self-amplifying and approximately exponential. This paper gives a simple mathematical interpretation of that claim and then argues that, even if such acceleration is real, it does not by itself resolve the central problem of scientific discovery. The reason is that accelerating returns apply most naturally to executional and infrastructural capability, whereas genuine discovery often depends on a different capacity: qualitative reasoning about when a current framework is structurally inadequate and what conceptual move is needed next. Recent ARC-AGI-3 results sharpen this distinction: humans solve the benchmark at ceiling, whereas frontier AI systems remain below 1%, indicating that the gap between current AI and human flexible reasoning is still very large. At the same time, Demis Hassabis has emphasized that humans must retain their sense of meaning and what they choose to focus their lives on, a reminder that the future of AI is not only a technical forecast but also a question of what forms of human understanding are worth preserving and transmitting. This paper positions the Qualitative Engine for Science (QES) [3] as a response to that missing capacity. In this view, the Kurzweil theory helps explain why quantitative capability may accelerate, while QES addresses the central problem in scientific discovery that acceleration alone does not solve. Its value does not depend on when AGI arrives, but on the fact that the processes of scientific discovery themselves constitute a form of human wisdom worth preserving, organizing, and making accessible.

### [178] [Narration-of-Thought: Inference-Time Scaffolding for Defeasible Ethical Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26366)
*Patrick Cooper,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出叙述思维（NoT）框架，通过五部分结构化链式思考（主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、承诺），有效解决道德困境中利益相关者遗漏和不确定性抑制的问题。NoT无需训练或参数调整，在多个模型上显著提升利益相关者识别率与不确定性表达，优于基线方法，并在多轮辩论中实现高共识。该框架为可审计的代理部署提供可靠基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有链式思考在道德困境中存在利益相关者遗漏（ stakeholder collapse）和不确定性忽略（uncertainty suppression）两大缺陷，影响决策质量与可解释性，亟需一种无需额外训练的结构化推理框架来改善这一问题。

Method: 引入叙述思维（NoT）系统提示，将链式思考划分为五个明确部分：主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、承诺；通过控制实验验证其有效性，结合文本梯度下降与跨家族评估进一步优化性能。

Result: NoT将利益相关者遗漏从最高31%降至不足1%，不确定性抑制从最高72%降至1-24%；在多轮辩论中，使协议达成率从6%提升至95%以上；跨家族评估表现优于同族评估，证明其泛化能力。

Conclusion: NoT通过结构化推理显著提升了大模型在道德决策中的全面性与透明度，为可信赖的自主代理部署提供了可审计的推理轨迹，且无需额外训练，具备高效、通用的优势。

Abstract: Standard chain-of-thought on moral dilemmas exhibits two failure modes: stakeholder collapse (the trace names at most one party with a stake in the outcome) and uncertainty suppression (no explicit unknowns or hedges before committing to an action). We introduce narration-of-thought (NoT), a system prompt that structures chain-of-thought into five sections: protagonist, stakeholders, two-step consequences, uncertainty, then commitment. NoT adds no training, parameters, or fine-tuning. On 100 DailyDilemmas scenarios across four generators from three vendors, NoT cuts stakeholder collapse from up to 31% to under 1% and uncertainty suppression from up to 72% to 1-24% on every model. A matched-budget verbose-CoT control rules out token spend as the active ingredient; NoT retains Cliff's delta advantages of +0.79 to +0.90 on stakeholder count and +0.65 to +0.93 on uncertainty score for three of four generators, and a section ablation attributes each shift to its specific sub-instruction. Textual-gradient descent initialised at NoT improves the scaffold further; a cross-family training judge (different vendor from the generator) dominates an in-family one on every measured axis. Extended to a five-round multi-stakeholder debate protocol, the scaffold converts a 6% standoff into 95% full consensus on a calibration set and 100% combined convergence on a DailyDilemmas replication. The resulting traces externalise the stakeholders, consequences, and uncertainty grounding each commitment, providing an auditable substrate for dependable agentic deployment.
