### [179] [Geometry-Aware MCTS for Extremal Problems in Combinatorial Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26399)
*Luoning Zhang,Xu Zhuang,Tianhao Wang,Nathan Kaplan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种几何感知的蒙特卡洛树搜索（Geometry-Aware MCTS）框架，用于解决组合几何中的极值问题，如无三点共线问题（Max-N3IL）和最小完全集问题。该方法通过增量更新可行动作空间，严格遵守几何约束，将约束检查复杂度从O(n³)降低至O(n²)；同时利用几何对称性进行剪枝和批量转移，显著提升搜索效率。实验表明，在六个问题中的五个上取得了新的最优结果：在Max-N3IL中发现约1.8n大小的配置（n=82~119），在最小完全集问题中发现约0.95n大小的配置，提供了新的上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统精确求解器在处理具有全局几何约束的组合几何极值问题时面临组合爆炸；而标准强化学习与Transformer模型则受限于稀疏奖励的‘有效性悬崖’及二次级的令牌消耗限制，难以有效探索此类问题。因此亟需一种高效且能严格满足几何约束的新方法。

Method: 提出几何感知蒙特卡洛树搜索（Geometry-Aware MCTS）框架。通过增量式维护可行动作空间以严格保证几何约束；针对共线点等约束，设计高效检查机制，将复杂度由O(n³)降至O(n²)；利用几何对称性实施节点扩展时的规范剪枝与对称批量转移，减少搜索空间并加速收敛。

Result: 在六类组合几何问题中，五类取得新最佳已知结果；在Max-N3IL问题中，实现约1.8n规模的解（n=82~119）；在最小完全集问题中，构造出约0.95n规模的解，提供新上界。验证了该框架在发现新颖几何构型方面的强大适应性与高效性。

Conclusion: Geometry-Aware MCTS是一种高度可拓展的框架，能够有效应对组合几何中复杂的全局几何约束，克服传统方法的瓶颈，在多个经典问题上实现了突破性进展，为该领域提供了一种强有力的计算工具。

Abstract: We study certain extremal problems in combinatorial geometry that ask about configurations of points in an $n \times n$ grid that satisfy strict, global geometric constraints. Classical exact solvers suffer from combinatorial explosion for these types of problems, and standard reinforcement learning and transformer-based models struggle with the sparse reward "validity cliff" and quadratic token-consumption limits. To overcome these bottlenecks, we propose a Geometry-Aware Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) framework. Our approach strictly enforces geometric constraints through incremental updates to the feasible action space. For constraints about collections of collinear points, like those that occur in the classic No-Three-in-Line problem (Max-N3IL), this mechanism reduces the constraint checking complexity from $O(n^3)$ to $O(n^2)$. To improve search efficiency, we exploit geometric symmetries in two ways: canonical pruning during node expansion to reduce the branching factor, and symmetric batch transitions to accelerate the discovery of promising configurations. We perform extensive experiments and establish new best-known computational results on five out of six of the problems that we considered. Notably, for Max-N3IL we find configurations of size roughly $1.8 n$ for grids of size $82 \le n \le 119$. For the Smallest Complete Set problem, we find configurations of size roughly $0.95 n$, providing new upper bounds within the tested grids. This work establishes Geometry-Aware MCTS as a highly adaptable framework for discovering novel configurations in combinatorial geometry.

### [180] [When Agents Meet Electric Bus Fleet Operations: Pricing Behavior, Trade-offs, and Policy Implications in an Aggregator Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26400)
*Jônatas Augusto Manzolli,Ali Eslami,Luis Miranda-Moreno,Jiangbo Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于代理的聚合框架，用于协调电动公交车队的复杂运营任务，结合优化模型与监督代理，实现对充电、电池状态、电价波动及车网互动（V2G）等多因素的动态管理。通过案例研究验证了该框架在日前与实时调度中的有效性，证明其能提升调度可行性与灵活性利用效率，但同时也揭示了以盈利为导向的定价机制可能从公交运营商处攫取价值，因此需建立透明的协调模式、可审计的计价机制和明确的价值分配规则。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个代理聚合框架，包含基于优化的电动公交车调度核心与多个监督代理（负责扰动检测、电价适应与调度评估）。优化核心确保物理可行性，代理层实时响应环境变化，触发重优化，并决定灵活性价值在聚合商与公交运营商之间的分配。

Result: 案例研究表明，该框架可在多种扰动条件下维持可行调度，选择性激活重优化，有效提升充电与V2G灵活性利用；但以利润为导向的配置会削弱公交运营商利益，存在价值提取风险。

Conclusion: 代理聚合器在电动公交与电网协同中具有潜力，但在公共车队场景中部署时必须确保协调机制透明、计价可审计、价值分配明确，以保障各方公平性。

Abstract: Agentic systems are changing how complex operational tasks are coordinated, introducing a new paradigm for connecting heterogeneous data sources and automating processes. Electric bus fleets provide a relevant test case. Their operation requires continuous coordination between service reliability, battery state-of-charge, charger availability, electricity prices, route-energy uncertainty, and vehicle-to-grid (V2G) opportunities. This paper proposes an agentic aggregator framework that streamlines this decision environment by coupling an optimization-based electric bus scheduling model with supervisory agents for disturbance detection, tariff adaptation, and schedule evaluation. The optimization core enforces physical feasibility across routes, chargers, batteries, and V2G exchanges, while the agentic layer interprets changing operating conditions, triggers real-time re-optimization when needed, and defines how flexibility value is allocated between the aggregator and the public transport operator (PTO). A realistic depot case study evaluates day-ahead and real-time operations under profit-based and operation-based coordination modes, considering service delays, route-energy deviations, electricity price shocks, and combined disturbances. The results show that agentic aggregation can support adaptive fleet-grid coordination by maintaining feasible schedules, activating re-optimization selectively, and improving the use of charging and V2G flexibility. However, they also reveal a critical trade-off: the same agentic capability that reduces operational complexity can extract value from the PTO when configured around profit-oriented pricing. These findings suggest that agentic aggregators can become useful for managing electric bus V2G operations, but their deployment in public-fleet contexts requires transparent coordination modes, auditable tariff-setting, and explicit value-sharing rules.

</details>


### [181] [Unbiased Canonical Set-Valued Oracles Via Lattice Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26418)
*Jobst Heitzig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了非代理型‘预言家’AI在预测未来事件概率时面临的自我参照问题：其预测一旦被采纳并影响行为，就会改变原本要报告的概率。传统做法是提出反事实问题（即假设预测不影响现实），但这类答案在被知晓后往往变得无关紧要，因为前提已不成立。为此，作者提出一种自参照的替代方案：预言家不报告单一概率，而是报告一个既无偏又与自身被采纳后果自洽的信念集（credal set）。由于直接的自洽性要求会包含太多解（如[0,1]这一无用解），关键在于从中选出一个唯一且非平凡的典型解。作者利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，在闭信念集构成的完全格上定义一个单调算子，并取其最小不动点作为标准解；另一变体则选取包含所有自洽点估计的最小不动点。文中证明了该构造的存在性、自洽性及非空性，并表明当问题不具行动影响（非表演性）时，该方法退化为经典点估计。对于二元事件，在自然凸包分解假设下，标准答案是一个区间。整个推导纯属格论，可自然推广至任意随机变量，将条件概率P(B|A,C)替换为条件分布L(X|A,C)。最后提出若干开放问题，特别是该区间特征是否能在一般化中保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决预言型AI在自我参照情境下的预测失效问题：当预测本身会影响现实，传统概率报告失去意义。尤其反事实方法因前提不再成立而变得无关。因此需要一种能同时保持无偏性和自洽性的新框架。

Method: 基于格论，利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，在闭信念集构成的完全格上构造一个单调算子，通过取最小不动点来获得唯一的非平凡自洽信念集。另一种变体要求该集合包含所有自洽的点估计，并取最小满足此性质的不动点。

Result: 构造出具有存在性、自洽性与非空性的唯一可信信念集；在非表演性问题下还原为经典点估计；对二元事件，在合理假设下答案为区间；整个理论可推广至任意随机变量的条件分布。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种新颖的自参照概率报告机制，通过格论中的不动点方法实现无偏与自洽的统一。该方法不仅克服了传统反事实路径的局限，还为可行动影响下的智能预测提供了形式化基础，未来研究可探索其在高维或连续情形下的区间特性保持问题。

Abstract: A non-agentic "oracle" AI that estimates probabilities of future events faces a self-reference problem: once its answer is learned and acted upon, it can change the very probability it was asked to report. One response, advocated for the Scientist AI programme, is to ask only counterfactual questions, evaluated as if the answer had no influence. We observe that such answers tend to become irrelevant the moment they are learned, precisely because their premise is then false. We therefore explore a self-referential alternative in which the oracle reports not a single probability but a credal set that is simultaneously unbiased and self-consistent with the consequences of being learned. The naive self-consistency requirement is satisfied by too many sets (including the useless answer $[0,1]$), so the problem is to single out a canonical, nontrivial member. We do so with the Knaster--Tarski fixed-point theorem on the complete lattice of closed credal sets, taking the least fixed point of a suitably defined isotone operator; a variant instead reports the least fixed point that contains every self-consistent point estimate. We prove existence, self-consistency, and nonemptiness, show that the construction collapses to the classical point answer for non-performative questions, and that for a binary event the canonical answer is, under a natural hull-factoring assumption, an interval. The development is purely lattice-theoretic and extends unchanged from a binary event $B$ to an arbitrary random variable $X$, with $P(B\mid A,C)$ replaced by the conditional law $\mathcal{L}(X\mid A,C)$. We close with open questions, including whether the interval characterization itself survives that generalization.

</details>


### [182] [Estimating Uncertainty in Classifier Performance with Applications to Large Language Models and Nested Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26422)
*Kylie Anglin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文评估了在社会科学研究中常见的小到中等样本量、罕见构念和文本嵌套于个体的条件下，性能度量的置信区间方法。发现默认方法如Wald区间和基本百分位数自助法准确性最低，而Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson及一种新的伪计数正则化自助法（尤其适用于F1分数）表现更优。当文本嵌套于个体时，调整有效样本量和适当自由度对获得准确分析区间至关重要。在自助法中，分层自助法在个体产生中等数量文本时更准确，但在个体文本较少时过于保守。研究旨在提升机器学习应用的透明度，并强调设计阶段应关注验证样本量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本分类研究中，尽管使用召回率和精确率等指标来衡量自然语言构建的有效性，但这些指标的不确定性常被忽略或以不恰当的方法报告，尤其是在小样本或高精度情况下。因此，需要改进置信区间的报告方式，以增强研究的可信度与透明性。

Method: 通过模拟实验评估多种置信区间方法在典型社会科学研究条件下的表现，包括小至中等样本量、罕见构念、文本嵌套于个体等情况；比较了Wald区间、基本百分位数自助法、Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson以及新提出的伪计数正则化自助法；同时考察了分层自助法与聚类自助法在不同个体文本产出情况下的表现差异。

Result: Wald区间和基本百分位数自助法覆盖概率远低于名义95%水平，准确性最差；Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson及伪计数正则化自助法显著提高准确性；当文本嵌套于个体时，必须调整有效N和自由度；分层自助法在中等文本产出情况下更优，而在个体文本少时过于保守。

Conclusion: 为提升机器学习在社会科学中的透明度与可信度，应采用更合适的置信区间估计方法，并在研究设计阶段充分考虑验证样本量的重要性。

Abstract: Researchers increasingly use text classification--supervised models or large language models--to measure constructs from natural language, providing metrics such as recall and precision as evidence of their validity. Yet, though these metrics are point estimates subject to sampling variation, measures of uncertainty are inconsistently reported alongside them. Further, when they are reported, they are often estimated with methods that are not appropriate when relevant labelled datasets are small or performance is high. To increase and improve confidence interval reporting in the field, this paper evaluates confidence interval methods for performance metrics under conditions typical of social science text classification: small to moderate sample sizes, infrequent constructs, and texts nested within individuals. Across simulations, default methods such as the Wald interval and the basic percentile bootstrap are the least accurate, with coverage sometimes far below the nominal 95% level. Accuracy is improved with the use of Agresti-Coull, Wilson, Clopper-Pearson, and a novel pseudo-count regularized bootstrap (which is particularly relevant to the calculation of F1). When texts are nested within individuals, we demonstrate that adjustment for both effective N and the appropriate degrees of freedom is necessary for producing accurate analytic intervals. Among bootstrap intervals, the hierarchical bootstrap is more accurate than the cluster bootstrap when individuals produce a moderate number of texts but overly conservative when individuals produce only a few. By providing guidance to the field on appropriate interval estimation, we aim to improve the transparency of machine learning applications, and to encourage greater attention to the validation sample size at the design stage.

### [183] [Data-driven Machine Learning Cannot Reach Symbolic-level Logical Reasoning -- The Limit of the Scaling Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26454)
*Tiansi Dong,Mateja Jamnik,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了数据驱动的机器学习系统在逻辑推理能力上是否能通过增加训练数据和时间达到符号级三段论推理水平。研究指出，监督式深度学习存在两个方法论局限：一是训练数据无法区分全部24种有效的三段论形式；二是从前提到结论的端到端映射导致神经组件在模式识别与逻辑推理之间产生矛盾的训练目标。实验表明Euler Net无法实现严格的三段论推理。对最新ChatGPT模型（GPT-5-nano和GPT-5）的测试显示，表面形式（如文字、符号等）会影响推理表现，尽管某些情况下准确率可达100%，但解释仍可能错误。由于训练在达到100%准确率后停止，研究结论为：监督学习系统无法获得符号逻辑推理的严谨性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索数据驱动机器学习系统能否通过扩大训练规模实现与符号系统相当的严格三段论推理能力，揭示当前深度学习在逻辑推理上的根本局限。

Method: 结合理论分析与实验验证，包括对Euler Net模型的实验测试，以及对GPT-5系列模型在四种不同表面形式下的三段论推理任务表现评估。

Result: 训练数据不足以区分所有有效三段论类型，且端到端映射引入训练目标冲突；Euler Net无法实现严格推理；即使模型达到100%准确率，其解释仍可能不正确；表面形式显著影响推理表现。

Conclusion: 监督学习系统由于方法论限制，无法达到符号逻辑推理的严谨性，即便在大量数据和长时间训练下亦然。

Abstract: Sphere neural networks have achieved symbolic level syllogistic reasoning without training data, raising the question of where the limit of the scaling law for logical reasoning lies, i.e., whether data-driven machine learning systems can achieve the same level by increasing training data and training time. We show two methodological limitations that prevent supervised deep learning from reaching the symbolic-level syllogistic reasoning: (1) training data can not distinguish all 24 types of valid syllogistic reasoning; (2) end-to-end mapping from premises to conclusion introduces contradictory training targets between neural components for pattern recognition and logical reasoning. Beside theoretical analysis, we experimentally illustrate that Euler Net cannot achieve rigorous syllogistic reasoning. We further challenge the most recent ChatGPTs (GPT-5-nano and GPT-5) to determine the satisfiability of syllogistic statements in four surface forms (patterns): words, double words, simple symbols, and long random symbols, showing that surface forms affect the reasoning performance and that ChatGPT GPT-5 may reach 100% accuracy but still provide incorrect explanations. As empirical training processes are stopped after achieving 100% accuracy, we conclude that supervised machine learning systems will not attain the rigour of symbolic logical reasoning.

In practice, retrieval is a critical bottleneck: multimodal knowledge is heterogeneous, difficult to align across modalities, and often poorly served by retrievers designed for unstructured corpora. To address this gap, we introduce MKG-RAG-Bench, a cross-domain benchmark explicitly designed to evaluate retrieval in MKG-RAG. By isolating retrieval as a first-class evaluation target, MKG-RAG-Bench provides a principled foundation for diagnosing current limitations and advancing multimodal knowledge graph RAG systems.

Here, we apply automated discovery techniques to the project of generating theories in computational cognitive science, with an agent-based system collecting human data independently through crowdsourced survey experiments. As a testbed, we use a classic case study from cognitive psychology: judging which sequences of coin flips seem subjectively more random. ### [187] [Humans Disengage, Reasoning Models Persist: Separating Difficulty Registration from Deliberation Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26502)
*Han-yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究大推理模型（LRMs）与人类在解决难题时的反应时间差异。尽管两者在整体上表现出相似的难度-时间相关性（跨项目对齐），但在固定题目下，其资源分配策略截然相反：当模型出错时会消耗更多标记（token），而人类则在错误时花费更少时间。这种差异揭示了两种不同的元认知策略——人类倾向于坚持可解问题、放弃难题；而模型因不确定而延长推理链，导致错误时更耗时。该发现基于公开的人类与模型对比数据集，且在多种数据集中稳定复现，非思考型基线无此现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大推理模型与人类在面对困难问题时的决策机制差异，特别是反应时间与错误之间的关系，以理解二者在资源分配上的根本不同。

Method: 使用公开匹配的人类-模型数据集（如H-ARC），分析在固定题目条件下，人类与五种思维型大推理模型在正确与错误试次中的响应时间（以标记数表示）差异。通过控制题目固定效应，检验跨项目对齐与项目内分配模式的分离，并排除非思考基线的影响。

Result: 所有五种思考型大推理模型均表现出显著的‘错误比正确消耗更多标记’效应（Cohen's d = 1.47–3.13），而人类则表现出相反趋势。该差异在多个数据集上一致存在，且在控制题目固定效应后依然显著，非思考基线不具此特征。

Conclusion: 人类与大推理模型虽在总体上呈现相似的难度-时间关联，但其内在资源分配机制完全不同：人类体现为‘投入可解题、放弃难题’的参与策略，而模型则因不确定性驱动推理链延长，导致错误时更耗资源。这表明仅依赖响应长度作为难度信号会掩盖关键的认知控制差异，需结合元认知策略进行更深层分析。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) take longer on harder problems, just as humans do. This surface similarity hides an opposite pattern within items. When an LRM gets a problem wrong, it spends more tokens than when it gets the same problem right; humans do the reverse, spending less time on the trials they get wrong. We separate two levels of deliberation: how response time tracks difficulty across items (registration), and, with item identity held fixed, whether an agent spends more on its own failures or successes (allocation). On a public matched human-LRM corpus, humans and all five thinking LRMs reproduce the known cross-item alignment (registration) but diverge within items (allocation): every LRM shows a large wrong-vs-right effect (Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13 on H-ARC) while humans show the opposite sign. The comparison stays inside each agent's own scale; we never put seconds and tokens on one axis. The dissociation holds under item fixed effects, replicates across datasets, and is absent in a non-thinking baseline. We read the human pattern as engagement versus abandonment: people stay on items they expect to solve and give up on the rest. We read the LRM pattern as length driven by uncertainty: chains grow when the model is unsure, which is exactly when it tends to fail. Both policies produce the same cross-item correlation with difficulty, so they look aligned on the measure prior work has used; the divergence shows up only once item identity is fixed. Under resource-rational metareasoning, the split is between two stopping policies that share a difficulty signal but implement opposite control; trace length captures the signal and misses the control.

</details>


### [188] [NeuraDock Visual Cognitive Load Agent Tutorial: A Quality-Gated Open-Source EEG Workflow for Alpha Dynamics and Real-Time Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26518)
*Zhiyuan Xu,Yueqing Dai,Junling Li,Junwen Luo*

Method: 采用质量门控的工作流设计：所有下游阿尔法波动态与认知负荷指标均在完成预处理与质量控制后才进行计算。通过逐步教程指导用户完成安装、数据处理、可视化、在线仪表板启动、外部应用调用实时API，以及利用大语言模型（LLM）解释质量风险。

Result: 在包含18个记录的迷你数据集验证中，该代理成功生成10次受试者内比较，7/10显示出任务相关的后部阿尔法波抑制；初步验证了个体内部重复性，并测量了本地在线API的延迟性能。整个流程实现从原始EEG到实时认知负荷分析原型的完整闭环。

Conclusion: NeuraDock Agent为研究者和开发者提供了一条从原始脑电数据到实时可视化认知负荷原型的透明路径，显著降低构建高质量实时神经反馈系统的技术门槛，是连接传统离线分析与现代实时应用的重要桥梁。

Abstract: This tutorial paper provides a step-by-step, reproducible walkthrough of NeuraDock Agent, an open-source EEG agent focused on Alpha dynamics and visual cognitive-load analysis. The goal is practical: a reader should be able to install the agent, run EEG preprocessing and quality control, generate Alpha dynamics figures, perform within-subject Rest/Task visual cognitive-load comparison, run the public mini-dataset analyses and compare them with the reference validation summary, start an online dashboard, call the real-time API from an external application, and use the LLM interpretation layer to explain quality risks. Existing EEG toolkits provide excellent offline analysis, but assembling a real-time, quality-gated cognitive-load pipeline often requires manually bridging acquisition, custom QC, Alpha feature extraction, and a web API; this tutorial closes that offline-to-online gap. The tutorial uses a quality-gated workflow: downstream Alpha and workload metrics are computed only after preprocessing and QC gating rather than directly from raw EEG. In the included mini-dataset validation, the agent processed 18 recordings, generated 10 within-subject comparisons, observed task-related posterior Alpha suppression in 7 of 10 contrasts, estimated initial evidence of within-subject repeatability, and benchmarked local online API latency. The tutorial is intended for researchers, developers, and applied teams who want a transparent path from EEG files to real-time visual cognitive-load prototypes.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can make scientific software easier to use. These distinctions are especially important for low-channel electroencephalography (EEG), where sparse spatial coverage and variable signal quality make plausible but unsupported interpretations easy to produce. The numerical engine parses recordings, performs quality control, executes reviewed spectral workflows, and writes machine-readable artifacts. The LLM receives only a compact, allowlisted summary and a versioned context pack. The context describes the seven-channel hardware, reviewed workflows, result fields, implementation boundaries, scientific limits, and reference cases. Raw EEG and dense per-sample arrays remain local
  We evaluate the system at three levels. First, 12 recordings produced identical structured results over ten numerical repetitions, and a complete Rest/Task run produced identical result, report, and figure hashes over three repetitions. Second, request-capture and failure-injection experiments confirmed the tested data boundary and preservation of local artifacts under HTTP, malformed-output, and connection failures. Third, a boundary-awareness benchmark tested 36 ordinary and adversarial questions under four context ablations and two LLMs, yielding 288 outputs.These results support hardware- and implementation-aware grounding as a practical mechanism for calibrating what an EEG agent accepts, qualifies, or refuses; they do not establish clinical validity or a validated absolute cognitive-load index.

### [190] [Radical AI Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26523)
*Daniel A. Herrmann,Benjamin A. Levinstein*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个将人工智能系统视为代理的解释框架，结合了哲学中的激进解释传统与机制可解释性工具。核心问题是：基于系统的计算事实，如何推断其信念、欲望和意义？该研究对AI安全至关重要，有助于信任系统或检测欺骗行为。文章提出了表征主义和解释主义方法的标准，并将其与当前可解释性技术的测试相联系。关键发现是这些归因不能零散进行，信念、欲望及其命题结构相互约束，任何单一变量的固定都会引入扭曲。这种整体性在概念不共享的AI系统中尤为突出，但也提供了分析杠杆：系统的态度约束其命题结构，而结构又限制可归因的态度，机制可解释性可帮助测量两者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统在实际部署中日益重要，理解其目标或检测潜在欺骗行为成为关键问题。当前可解释性工具虽能读取模型内部的信念和欲望，但缺乏明确的成功标准，因此需要一个统一的理论框架来评估这些工具的有效性。

Method: 结合哲学中的激进解释理论与机制可解释性方法，提出表征主义与解释主义两种路径的评价标准，并设计可操作的测试以验证这些标准在现有技术中的适用性。强调信念、欲望与命题结构之间的整体性关系，避免局部归因带来的偏差。

Result: 确立了可解释性工具成功与否的判断标准，揭示了归因必须整体进行，不能割裂处理；证明即使在概念不一致的情况下，通过机制可解释性仍可识别系统态度与其命题结构间的相互约束关系。

Conclusion: 本研究为AI系统的可解释性提供了一个坚实的理论基础，强调整体性归因的重要性，并指出机制可解释性在验证系统信念与意图方面的关键作用，推动了安全可信AI的发展。

Abstract: We develop a framework for interpreting AI systems as agents, drawing on the philosophical tradition of radical interpretation and the tools of mechanistic interpretability. The core question is: given the computational facts about a system, how do we solve for its beliefs, desires, and meanings? This matters increasingly for safety. We want to be able to trust the systems we deploy, whether by understanding their goals or, more modestly, by reliably detecting deception. Interpretability researchers are building tools to read beliefs and desires off a model's internals, but there is no settled account of when such a tool has succeeded. This book supplies one. We propose criteria on both representationalist and interpretationist approaches, and tie each to tests current interpretability methods can carry out. A central lesson is that these attributions cannot be made piecemeal. Beliefs, desires, and the propositional structure they presuppose are jointly constrained, and a method that fixes one while measuring the others inherits whatever distortions that introduces. This holism becomes pressing for AI systems, which may not share the interpreter's concepts. However, it also provides leverage: a system's attitudes constrain its propositional structure, that structure constrains which attitudes can be attributed, and mechanistic interpretability can help us measure both.

### [191] [PMDformer: Patch-Mean Decoupling Information Transformer for Long-term Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26549)
*Ao Hu,Liangjian Wen,Jiang Duan,Yong Dai,He Yan,Dongkai Wang,Jun Wang,Yukun Zhang,Ruoxi Jiang,Zenglin Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PMDformer提出了一种新的时间序列预测方法，通过分离趋势与残差形状信息（即patch-mean decoupling, PMD），并结合Trend Restoration Attention (TRA) 和 Proximal Variable Attention (PVA) 模块，有效捕捉长程依赖和跨变量关系，在多个基准测试中表现出更高的准确性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的模型在处理长时序预测时，难以准确建模不同片段和变量间的形状相似性，尤其受尺度差异影响。因此需要一种方法来解耦趋势与形状特征，以提升注意力机制对真实形状相似性的捕捉能力。

Method: 提出Patch-Mean Decoupling (PMD)，将每个patch的均值减去以分离趋势和残差形状；引入Trend Restoration Attention (TRA) 用于恢复趋势信息并计算注意力输出；设计Proximal Variable Attention (PVA) 聚焦于最近且相关的变量时间片段，避免过拟合旧相关性。最终构建PMDFomer模型。

Result: 在多个长期时间序列预测基准上，PMDformer在准确率和稳定性方面均优于现有先进方法，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: PMDformer通过解耦趋势与形状信息，并结合有效的注意力机制，显著提升了长期时间序列预测性能，为未来研究提供了新思路。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting (LTSF) plays a crucial role in fields such as energy management, finance, and traffic prediction. Transformer-based models have adopted patch-based strategies to capture long-range dependencies, but accurately modeling shape similarities across patches and variables remains challenging due to scale differences. To address this, we introduce patch-mean decoupling (PMD), which separates the trend and residual shape information by subtracting the mean of each patch, preserving the original structure and ensuring that the attention mechanism captures true shape similarities. Futhermore, to more effectively model long-range dependencies and capture cross-variable relationships, we propose Trend Restoration Attention (TRA) and Proximal Variable Attention (PVA). The former module reintegrates the decoupled trend from PMD while calculating attention output. And the latter focuses cross-variable attention on the most relevant, recent time segments to avoid overfitting on outdated correlations. Combining these components, we propose PMDformer, a model designed to effectively capture shape similarity in long-term forecasting scenarios. Extensive experiments indicate that PMDformer outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods in stability and accuracy across multiple LTSF benchmarks. The code is available at https://github.com/aohu1105/PMDformer.

Abstract: Hepatitis C is a liver infection caused by a virus, which results in mild to severe inflammation of the liver. Over many years, hepatitis C gradually damages the liver, often leading to permanent scarring, known as cirrhosis. Patients sometimes have moderate or no symptoms of liver illness for decades before developing cirrhosis. Cirrhosis typically worsens to the point of liver failure. Patients with cirrhosis may also experience brain and nerve system damage, as well as gastrointestinal hemorrhage. Treatment for cirrhosis focuses on preventing further progression of the disease. Detecting cirrhosis earlier is therefore crucial for avoiding complications. Machine learning (ML) has been shown to be effective at providing precise and accurate information for use in diagnosing several diseases. The Extra Trees model outperformed the other models achieving an accuracy of 96.92%, a recall of 94.00%, a precision of 99.81%, and an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve of 96% using only 16 of the 28 features.

### [193] [EvoOptiGraph: Weakness-Driven Coevolution via Graph-Based Structural Generation for Optimization Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26578)
*Qingcan Kang,Mingyang Liu,Xiaojin Fu,Shixiong Kai,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EvoOptiGraph 是一种数据与模型协同进化的框架，通过将混合整数线性规划（MILP）表示为属性二分图，并使用保持有效性的进化算子生成结构多样化的实例。该框架通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）机制，利用模型弱点信号生成新实例，形成闭环训练循环，显著提升大语言模型在优化建模任务中的准确率、可执行性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在自动化从自然语言生成优化模型时面临两大挑战：训练语料缺乏结构多样性，且数据生成管道与模型学习过程脱节。为解决这些问题，需要一种能够动态生成多样化训练数据并根据模型缺陷持续优化的方法。

Method: EvoOptiGraph 将每个 MILP 表示为一个带属性的二分图，应用保持有效性的进化操作生成结构多样的实例；通过确定性编译将图转换为求解器代码和自然语言描述，并进行回译验证；采用两阶段训练：先进行监督微调（SFT），再通过基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），以图衍生的弱点信号指导新实例生成，实现数据与模型的协同进化。

Result: 在六个公开数据集上的实验表明，EvoOptiGraph 显著优于更大的通用模型、代理方法和专用基线，在准确性、可执行性和泛化能力方面均表现更优，证明了目标导向的数据-模型协同进化策略在优化建模任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: EvoOptiGraph 通过构建数据与模型的闭环协同进化机制，有效提升了大语言模型在优化建模任务中的性能，展示了结构化数据生成与模型反馈相结合的强大潜力。

Abstract: Automating optimization modeling from natural language with large language models (LLMs) faces two key challenges. First, training corpora lack structural diversity. Second, data generation pipelines remain static and decoupled from model learning. To address these challenges, we propose EvoOptiGraph, a novel framework where data and model co-evolve, driven by model weaknesses. EvoOptiGraph represents each mixed-integer linear program (MILP) as an attributed bipartite graph and applies validity-preserving evolutionary operators to generate structurally diverse instances. The evolved graphs are converted into solver code and natural language via deterministic compilation and verified back-translation. Training proceeds in two stages: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on an initial dataset, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where graph-derived weakness signals guide the generation of new instances targeting the model's failures. This forms a closed loop that continuously updates the training distribution. Empirical results on six public datasets show that EvoOptiGraph significantly outperforms larger generalist models, agentic methods, and specialized baselines in accuracy, executability, and generalization. These results demonstrate that targeted data-model coevolution is an effective strategy for improving LLMs on optimization modeling tasks.

Abstract: With the gradual introduction of AI into telescope scheduling, AI-based decision-making has shown advantages in handling complex multi-constraint problems. However, its outputs often suffer from inconsistent data references, reasoning errors, and non-executable decisions, limiting applicability in high-reliability observational tasks. In this work, we propose a multi-level validation and traceable reasoning framework that performs systematic reliability verification of AI-generated decisions prior to execution, and enables explicit representation of the reasoning process to support traceable decision-making. The framework integrates data reference validation, logical consistency checks, and observational and instrumental constraint verification to filter and correct invalid decisions. It also introduces atomic reasoning units and their dependency relationships, representing scheduling decisions as a sequence of interconnected reasoning steps that support error localization and post hoc analysis. Experiments show that the framework improves executability and reliability of AI scheduling and reduces loss of transient opportunities. In particular, feedback correction and structured validation of reasoning steps enhance the ability to repair and block erroneous decisions, especially in complex scenarios. Compared with pure AI methods, the framework-enhanced approach maintains flexibility while substantially improving reliability and executability. These results demonstrate a feasible and verifiable pathway for applying AI to high-reliability astronomical observation scheduling.

### [198] [SKILL-DISCO: Distilling and Compiling Agent Traces into Reusable Procedural Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26669)
*Zhongxin Guo,Danrui Qi,Hanwen Gu,Peng Cheng,Yongqiang Xiong*

Method: 提出SkillDisCo框架，通过知识蒸馏从成功轨迹中提取可重用的参数化有限状态机（PFSM）子图，并将其编译为可调用、可执行、可验证的程序化技能。该方法基于成功轨迹作为未知转移图中的路径，将技能建模为控制流子图。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebArena基准测试中，SkillDisCo显著提升了任务成功率，并减少了代理执行的回合数，且在不同模型规模下均表现良好，证明了以可复用执行结构表示共享经验的有效性。

Abstract: Agents often repeatedly solve similar task instances from scratch, leading to unnecessary reasoning cost and long execution traces. Prior work has explored workflow reuse and executable skill induction, but it remains unclear which task scenarios admit procedural skills and how the shared procedural structure should be represented across successful traces. We study this problem in FSM-defined scenarios, where successful traces can be viewed as paths in an unknown transition graph, and formulate procedural skills as reusable parameterized control-flow subgraphs. Based on this view, we introduce SkillDisCo, a distillation-and-compilation framework that distills reusable PFSM subgraphs from successful traces and compiles them into callable, executable, and verifiable procedural skills. ### [199] [NebulaExp-8B: An Empirical Post-Training Pipeline via Full-Scale Ablation Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26671)
*Qiaobo Hao,Yangqian Wu,Shunyi Wang,Zhongjian Zhang,Ziqun Li,Yayin He,Muqing Li,Chen Zhong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NebulaExp提出一个完全透明、可复现的后训练流水线，基于Qwen3-8B-base构建通用指令模型与复杂推理专用模型双分支。通过384万条多源SFT样本和20万条可验证RL候选样本，设计端到端数据处理流程，包括响应蒸馏、多维度交叉验证过滤、细粒度难度分级、任务分类与多样性采样。在指令分支上，三阶段SFT将平均得分从55.01提升至60.99，GRPO强化学习进一步提升至61.85；在推理分支上，中等难度GRPO使推理得分从73.88提升至75.17。为缓解强化学习对验证器的依赖，提出单教师与多教师OPD（MOPD），仅用4K样本即在IFEval上超越基线3.26分，整体提升4.43；MOPD融合四个领域专家教师，仅用10K样本实现比基线高4.18的平均性能提升。本研究提供8B级大模型完整可复现的后训练方案，并系统分析了指令遵循、数学推理、代码生成与通用知识间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练方法缺乏透明的数据构建、过滤规则与训练配方，阻碍社区复现与轻量模型优化。本文旨在解决这一问题，提供一个完全透明、可复现且支持消融分析的后训练框架。

Method: 构建基于Qwen3-8B-base的双分支模型体系，包含通用指令模型与复杂推理专用模型。采用384万条多源SFT样本与20万条可验证RL候选样本，设计端到端数据处理流程，涵盖响应蒸馏、多维度交叉验证过滤、细粒度难度分级、任务分类及多样性采样。指令分支采用三阶段优化的监督微调（SFT）与GRPO强化学习；推理分支采用中等难度GRPO。针对强化学习依赖验证器的问题，引入单教师与多教师的OPD（MOPD）策略，利用少量高质量样本实现高性能。

Result: 指令分支：三阶段SFT使平均得分从55.01提升至60.99，GRPO进一步提升至61.85；推理分支：中等难度GRPO使推理得分从73.88提升至75.17。单教师OPD仅用4K样本，在IFEval上超越基线3.26分，整体平均提升4.43；多教师MOPD仅用10K样本，平均性能提升4.18。所有结果均具备高度可复现性。

Conclusion: NebulaExp提供了面向8B规模大语言模型的完整、透明、可复现的后训练方案，有效提升了模型在指令遵循、数学推理、代码生成与通用知识等方面的能力，并揭示了不同能力之间的权衡关系，为后续模型优化与社区协作奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Post-training alignment determines the reasoning and human preference following capabilities of large language models, yet most existing works withhold detailed data construction, filtering rules and training recipes, which hinders community reproducibility and lightweight model optimization. This work presents NebulaExp, a fully transparent, ablation-driven post-training pipeline built on Qwen3-8B-base, covering two orthogonal model branches: general instruct model and complex reasoning-specialized model. We curate a raw corpus of 3.84M multi-source SFT samples and a 200K verifiable RL candidate pool, and design an end-to-end data processing stack including response distillation, multi-dimensional cross-verification filtering, fine-grained difficulty grading, task classification and diversity-aware sampling. For the Instruct branch, our three-stage optimized supervised fine-tuning approach NebulaExp-Ins-SFT improves the average benchmark score from the 55.01 baseline of Qwen3-8B-nothink to 60.99. GRPO reinforcement learning then further elevates the average score to 61.85. For the Reasoning branch, medium-difficulty GRPO RL improves average reasoning score from 73.88 to 75.17. To address RL's dependency on task verifiers, we systematically investigate single-teacher and multi-teacher OPD (MOPD): utilizing merely 4K instruction-following samples and outperforms RL baseline by 3.26 points on IFEval with +4.43 average overall gain; MOPD fuses four domain-specialist teachers with merely 10K samples, lifting average performance by 4.18 over the base model. This report provides a fully reproducible empirical post-training recipe for 8B-scale LLMs, and comprehensively dissects the capability trade-offs among instruction adherence, mathematical reasoning, code generation and general knowledge.

### [200] [Do Safety Guardrails Need to Reason? LeanGuard: A Fast and Light Approach for Robust Moderation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26686)
*Dongbin Na*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了安全护栏是否真的需要链式思维（CoT）推理。通过对比轻量级双向编码器（LeanGuard）与基于大型解码器的推理护栏，发现去除推理过程后，性能不降反升：LeanGuard仅需单次前向传播，395M参数模型在公开基准上达到82.90±0.26的平均F1，且推理计算量减少约100倍，同时在噪声鲁棒性和召回率方面表现更优。研究质疑当前评估基准是否足以体现推理优势，并指出CoT对内容审核的必要性尚未被证实。代码与模型已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全护栏依赖链式思维（CoT）进行决策，但该设计导致模型计算开销大、响应慢，不适合在设备端（如具身机器人）部署。本文质疑：安全护栏是否必须进行逐步推理？

Method: 在相同数据集上训练一个轻量级双向编码器（仅使用标签信息）和一个带推理能力的护栏，保持其余部分不变，仅移除推理模块，进行受控对比实验。

Result: LeanGuard在多项基准上达到与大型推理护栏相当甚至更优的性能，平均F1为82.90±0.26，推理计算量减少约100倍，且在高严格度下仍保持更高召回率，对标签噪声更具鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 链式思维并非提升内容审核准确性的必要条件；当前护栏评估基准可能不足以凸显推理优势；轻量级非推理模型（如LeanGuard）在效率与鲁棒性上更具优势，提示应重新审视CoT在安全护栏中的必要性。

Abstract: In order to screen a prompt or a response, the recent guardrail methods generate a chain-of-thought (CoT) before they issue a verdict. This design follows a common belief that step-by-step reasoning improves a decision. However, CoT also makes the guard heavy and slow, because the model must generate many tokens before it decides. This may not match how guardrails are actually deployed. A guardrail sometimes should not be heavy and slow, and it often runs on-device, for example on an embodied robot. In this paper, we pose a question whether a safety guardrail really needs to reason. To answer this question, we train a lightweight bidirectional encoder and a reasoning guard on the same corpus, and we then remove only the reasoning while we keep everything else fixed. With this controlled same-base comparison, we show that the chain does not improve moderation accuracy. We name the resulting guard LeanGuard. A 395M label-only encoder reaches an average F1 of 82.90 $\pm$ 0.26 over public benchmarks. It matches a reasoning guard that is built on a much larger decoder, while it uses only a single forward pass over an input of at most 512 tokens. This is about a ~100x reduction in inference compute. We further show that this label-only encoder stays robust under training-label noise and retains far more recall at a strict false-positive rate than the reasoning guard, so a heavier reasoning guard is not the more robust choice either. Our finding suggests that the current guardrail benchmarks may not be hard enough to reward reasoning, and that the necessity of CoT for moderation is still not proven. We release all source codes and models including LeanGuard at https://github.com/ndb796/LeanGuard.

</details>


### [201] [Kalman Prototypical Networks for Few-shot Fault Detection in Combined Cycle Gas Turbines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26710)
*Mohammed Ayalew Belay,Lucas Ferreira Bernardino,Adil Rasheed,Rubén M. Montañés,Pierluigi Salvo Rossi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为卡尔曼原型网络（KPN）的度量学习框架，用于解决联合循环燃气轮机（CCGT）故障诊断中因标签数据稀缺导致的难题。通过将类别原型建模为动态系统中的潜在随机状态，减少样本间变异，提升嵌入表示的鲁棒性。基于高保真Modelica仿真生成的模拟数据集，涵盖正常运行与渐进式泄漏故障，在瞬态条件下验证了KPN在少量标注样本下的优越性能，显著优于匹配网络、关系网络和MAML等传统少样本学习方法，具有更高的准确率与稳定性，并加速训练收敛与泛化能力，适用于真实世界中标签数据有限的CCGT故障检测场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联合循环燃气轮机（CCGT）虽高效且环保，但其复杂的热流体与机械交互使得故障检测困难，尤其在缺乏足够标注故障数据的情况下，传统方法难以有效应对。因此需要一种能在少量样本下快速学习并稳定识别故障的智能诊断方法。

Method: 提出卡尔曼原型网络（KPN），将类别原型视为动态系统中的潜在随机状态，利用卡尔曼滤波机制建模原型演化过程，降低少样本任务中的类间方差，增强嵌入空间的稳定性与可区分性。结合高保真模型仿真生成的故障数据，采用少样本学习范式进行训练与评估。

Result: KPN在多种支持集与查询集配置下均表现出更高的诊断准确率与稳定性，相比匹配网络、关系网络和MAML等基准方法，具有更快的训练收敛速度和更强的泛化能力，尤其在渐进式泄漏故障检测任务中表现突出。

Conclusion: 所提出的卡尔曼原型网络（KPN）是一种适用于联合循环燃气轮机少样本故障诊断的有效框架，通过动态建模类别原型提升了嵌入表示的鲁棒性，显著改善了模型在标签数据稀缺条件下的性能，具备良好的工程应用前景。

Abstract: Combined-cycle gas turbines (CCGTs) play a key role in modern power generation, offering both high efficiency and reduced environmental impact. However, their complex thermo-fluid and mechanical interactions complicate fault detection, particularly when labeled fault data are scarce. In this paper, we introduce the Kalman Prototypical Network (KPN), a metric-based few-shot learning (FSL) framework specifically tailored for CCGT fault diagnosis. We model the evolution of class prototypes as latent stochastic states in a dynamic system to reduce episodic variance and improve robustness in embedding representation. Synthetic data sets generated with a high-fidelity Modelica-based dynamic simulation of an offshore CCGT system were used, simulating both normal operation and progressive leak faults under transient conditions. Application of the proposed framework on simulated leak fault detection tasks demonstrate that KPN outperforms conventional FSL methods such as Matching Networks, Relation Networks, and MAML in both accuracy and stability under varying support and query configurations. The proposed framework significantly improves training convergence and generalization by stabilizing class representations, making it well-suited for real-world CCGT fault detection where labeled data is limited.

LithoDreamer captures feature changes between adjacent states to model stage-specific physics-informed latent spaces, in which it controls process intervention exploration and drives subsequent state transitions. ### [204] [Socratic agents for autonomous scientific discovery in high-dimensional physical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26722)

Here we introduce AHOIS, a multi-agent AI scientist that embeds Socratic midwifery into closed-loop experimentation. A physics-critic agent interrogates hypotheses through causal questioning, constraint checking, counterexample generation and falsification-criteria formulation. Without prior encoding schemes, classifiers or speckle models, the system autonomously proposed and validated a random-interference encoding hypothesis, discovered task-adaptive sparse-measurement strategies, diagnosed distinct failure modes (encoding instability, fluorescence contamination and detector noise) and translated a published imaging protocol into an executable workflow on a non-original configuration. Here, we propose formalizing research as meta-optimization, where the optimization objective itself is also being optimized. This limitation primarily arises from the lack of domain-specific optimization guidance, hindering effective exploration of the optimization space. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将加速推理重构为在常微分方程空间中的稳定宏观轨迹外推；利用全局漂移（GD）对齐外推过程以消除特征不一致；引入无导数的重心拉格朗日外推器避免高阶导数噪声；设计有界相位映射约束外推域，抑制震荡误差增长。

Abstract: The adoption of powerful diffusion models is hindered by their significant inference latency. Recent ``cache-then-forecast'' schemes alleviate this issue by accelerating DiTs using derivative-based polynomials, but they suffer from severe quality degradation at high acceleration ratios. Our analysis reveals its root cause: the discrete extrapolation performed on representations that are misaligned with the continuous diffusion trajectory and are numerically unstable. Thus, accelerated DiTs suffer from accumulated spatial errors, noisy derivative amplification, and high-order instability. We therefore reformulate accelerated inference as stable macro-trajectory extrapolation in ordinary differential equation (ODE) space. Instead of predicting intermediate features, we align forecasting with the model's Global Drift (GD), i.e., the end-to-end state evolution, thereby eliminating feature inconsistency and memory overhead. However, even this smooth macro-trajectory remains vulnerable to the derivative fallacy: its higher-order temporal derivatives are intrinsically noisy. Thus, we introduce a derivative-free barycentric Lagrange extrapolator to effectively bypass derivative instability and approximation error. We further propose a bounded Phase Mapping that regularizes the extrapolation domain, suppressing oscillatory error growth. These elements collectively constitute ResilPhase, a noise-resilient acceleration framework. Experiments on FLUX.1-dev and HunyuanVideo demonstrate state-of-the-art fidelity under aggressive acceleration ratios.

### [208] [Memory Depth, Not Memory Access: Selective Parametric Consolidation for Long-Running Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26806)
*Haoliang Han*

TL;DR: 本文研究长周期语言代理中的记忆深度问题，提出通过目标条件化参数存储实现持久行为。引入循环漂移协议作为压力测试，评估EVAF机制在目标保持与卸载后恢复上的表现，结果显示其在仅每200事件进行2-3次参数写入的情况下，有效提升了长期行为一致性。该机制可分解为选择与执行两个可控维度，且其性能受模型依赖性影响。公开的Memora事件流暴露了陈旧记忆失效的未解决问题，表明参数化巩固与检索访问具有互补性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出循环漂移协议作为控制性压力测试，评估模型在工作上下文卸载后的目标保持能力；设计并验证EVAF机制——一种基于意外性和情绪价值的LoRA参数固化方法，通过选择性参数写入实现记忆深度。实验涵盖GPT-2、TinyLlama和Mistral-7B，并通过多种对照实验分离选择与执行因素。

Result: 在浅层事实回忆任务中，检索系统表现优异（准确率0.956–0.973）；而EVAF在目标持久性与卸载后恢复任务上表现更优（0.812–0.904），仅需少量参数写入（2–3次/200事件）。控制实验表明选择与执行可独立调控，且写入强度具有模型依赖性；在Mistral-7B上发现选择与执行间的非对称耦合关系。

Conclusion: 参数化选择性巩固提供了超越传统检索的记忆深度，与检索机制互补。当前仍存在陈旧记忆失效等边界问题，需进一步研究以完善长期记忆管理机制。

Abstract: Long-running language agents need more than memory access. Retrieval systems can fetch past facts at query time, but they do not decide which experiences should continue to shape behavior after the working context is unloaded. We study this separate problem as memory depth: durable goal-conditioned tendencies written into a small parametric store. We introduce the loop-drift protocol, a controlled stress test in which the retrieval index remains intact while working context is unloaded and goal-conditioned behavior must persist under long-loop interference. We evaluate EVAF, a surprise- and valence-gated LoRA consolidation mechanism. Across GPT-2 and TinyLlama, retrieval is strongest on shallow factual recall (short-fact accuracy 0.956--0.973), while EVAF is strongest on goal persistence and post-unload recovery (0.812--0.904) with only 2--3 parametric writes per 200 events. Mechanism controls show that selective consolidation factorizes into two controllable dimensions: selection and actuation. Matched random gates isolate selection beyond sparse writing; fixed-inner controls across GPT-2, TinyLlama, and Mistral-7B show that inner-loop write strength is model-dependent; and a Mistral-7B matched-gate inversion reveals asymmetric selection-actuation coupling under miscalibrated actuation. Public Memora event streams serve as an external diagnostic, exposing stale-memory invalidation as an unresolved boundary. Within this probe, selective parametric consolidation supplies memory depth distinct from and complementary to retrieval access.

*Francois Crespin,Fabian M. Suchanek,Nils Holzenberger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种新方法，让大语言模型在生成文本时能自动从知识库中获取事实知识，实现无需重训练即可更新事实、可追溯知识来源以增强透明性，并使小型模型达到与大型模型相当的事实准确性。核心思想是训练模型生成特殊标记以触发知识库查询。实验表明该方法提升了短文本和长文本生成中的事实准确性，并通过修改知识库而非更新参数实现事实修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在生成内容时依赖于训练时的固定知识，无法动态更新事实，且难以追溯信息来源，同时小模型难以达到大模型的事实准确性。为解决这些问题，需要一种机制让模型能实时访问外部知识库并动态获取最新事实。

Method: 训练模型在生成过程中产生特殊标记（如[KB_QUERY]），这些标记会触发对知识库的查询，从而将最新的事实信息融入生成内容中。通过这种方式，模型无需重新训练即可根据知识库的变化调整输出。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法显著提高了生成内容的事实准确性，无论是在短文本还是长文本生成任务中；同时实现了事实的可追溯性和可编辑性，仅需修改知识库即可完成事实更新，而无需重新训练模型。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于知识库查询的生成机制有效解决了大语言模型的事实更新难、可解释性差和小模型性能不足的问题，为构建更准确、透明和高效的生成系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We propose a new method that allows an LLM to automatically pull in factual knowledge from a knowledge base during token generation. This means that (1)~factual knowledge in the LLM output can be updated without retraining the LLM, (2)~facts in the LLM output can be traced to the knowledge base for transparency and explainability, and (3)~smaller models can achieve the same factual accuracy as larger models. Our core idea is to train the model to produce special tokens that trigger a query to the knowledge base. Our experiments show that our method improves factual grounding in both short and long-form generation, and allows factual revisions to take effect through KB edits rather than parameter updates.

</details>


### [210] [Computational Analysis of Heart Rate Variability in Healthy Adults](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26816)
*María J. Lado,Arturo J. Méndez,Leandro Rodriguez-Liñares,Baltasar García Pérez-Schofield,Pedro Cuesta-Morales,Brais Iglesias-Otero,Xose A. Vila*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过对40名健康成年人（20名男性，20名女性，年龄30-50岁）的心率变异性（HRV）指标进行分析，评估了时域、频域和非线性指标在正常性、稳定性、相关性、可重复性和一致性方面的表现。结果表明，时域和非线性指标（尤其是全局和低频LF）呈正态分布，存在性别差异；大多数指标稳定，但高频HF相关指标除外；HF相关指标间存在高度相关性，提示研究中仅需保留一个即可；与Fantasia数据库对比显示，多数指标误差低于10%，但女性的SD2和SDNN误差超过15%；时域和非线性指标跨研究变异性低，而频域指标变异性高，限制了跨研究比较。推荐使用ApEn、IRRR（全局变异性）、HRVi和SD2（LF）、MADRR或rMSSD（HF）作为最能准确反映HRV特征的指标，以提升其临床与科研应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对健康人群心率变异性（HRV）参数的研究仍不充分，且缺乏统一标准，限制了其在疾病诊断中的临床应用。因此，亟需系统评估HRV指标的统计特性与可靠性，以建立更可靠的参考基准，增强其临床实用性。

Method: 采用计算信号处理与数据分析方法，对40名健康成人的HRV数据进行时域、频域和非线性指标分析，围绕五个核心问题（正常性、稳定性、相关性、可重复性、一致性）展开系统评估，并与公开数据库（Fantasia）进行对比验证。

Result: 时域和非线性指标（如全局、LF）符合正态分布，存在性别差异；多数指标具有稳定性，但HF相关指标例外；HF相关指标间高度相关，具冗余性；与Fantasia数据库相比，多数指标误差小于10%，但女性的SD2和SDNN误差超过15%；时域和非线性指标跨研究一致性高，频域指标变异大，不利于跨研究比较。

Conclusion: 推荐使用ApEn、IRRR（全局变异性）、HRVi和SD2（LF）、MADRR或rMSSD（HF）作为代表HRV核心成分的最优指标，有助于提高心率变异性分析在临床与科研中的准确性与可比性。

Abstract: Heart Rate Variability (HRV) analysis is a key indicator of cardiac physiological state and aids in disease diagnosis. However, research on HRV parameters in healthy individuals remains limited, and no gold standard exists. This study evaluates HRV indices in 40 healthy adults (20 men, 20 women, aged 30-50) to improve HRV's clinical utility. Using computational methods for signal processing and data analysis, time, frequency, and nonlinear indices were analyzed to address five questions: (1) normality, (2) stability, (3) correlation, (4) reproducibility, and (5) consistency. Key findings: (1) Time-domain and nonlinear indices, particularly global and LF (low frequency), follow normal distributions, with gender differences noted. (2) Most indices are stable except HF (high frequency)-related ones. (3) High correlations in HF-related indices suggest redundancy, indicating only one is necessary in studies. (4) Comparisons with the Fantasia database revealed less than 10% error for most indices, except SD2 and SDNN in women (greater than 15%). (5) Time-domain and nonlinear indices show low inter-study variability, while frequency-domain indices exhibit high variability, limiting cross-study comparisons. The selected indices-ApEn and IRRR (global variability), HRVi and SD2 (LF), and MADRR or rMSSD (HF)-are best suited for accurately representing HRV components and enhancing its clinical and research relevance.

### [211] [The Capability Frontier: Benchmarks Miss 82% of Model Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26836)
*Bradley Fowler,Ryan Smith,Daniel Thi Graviet,William Myers,Joshua Greaves,Narmeen Fatimah Oozeer,Antía García,Philip Quirke,Amirali Abdullah,Fazl Barez,Shriyash Kaustubh Upadhyay*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出'能力前沿'（Capability Frontier）以更准确地评估大语言模型在异构数据分布下的真实能力。传统基准测试因仅报告单一模型单次运行的准确率，系统性低估了实际表现。该研究通过整合多模型与多轮生成并最优选择（即通过理想路由），构建帕累托前沿，纠正了单模型评估的低估和单次采样带来的高估偏差。实验覆盖21个LLM在16个基准上的表现，结果显示：修正单模型评估使错误率降低54%；进一步修正单次运行问题，错误率再降82%，且达到SOTA性能仅需85%的成本。模拟表明，查询主题熵越高，理想路由与最佳单模型间的性能差距越显著。结论是集体模型能力被严重低估，对跨领域、异构数据场景的评估与部署具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法仅基于单模型单次运行的准确率，无法反映真实世界中多模型协作和多次生成选择的优势，导致对大语言模型实际能力的系统性低估，尤其在数据分布异构的场景下。因此需要一种更全面的评估框架来揭示模型集体潜力。

Method: 提出'能力前沿'概念，通过构建帕累托前沿，综合考虑多个模型在不同成本下的表现，并采用最优选择策略（即理想路由）来选取最佳模型和生成结果。该方法同时纠正了单模型评估的低估和单次采样带来的过估计偏差。实验在21个大模型上覆盖16个任务，包括编程、推理、医学、事实性、指令遵循及代理任务等。结合概率模拟验证主题熵对性能差距的影响。

Result: 修正单模型评估后，错误率下降54%；进一步修正单次运行后，错误率再下降82%；达到当前最佳性能时，成本可减少85%。模拟显示，随着查询主题熵增加，理想路由相对于最佳单模型的性能优势呈近似单调上升趋势。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的集体能力远超单模型评估所揭示的表现，尤其在数据异构、多领域场景中。现有评估方式严重低估了其真实潜力，亟需采用如能力前沿等更全面的评估范式，以指导实际部署与系统设计。

Abstract: Existing benchmarks typically report accuracy for a single model on a single run. This systematically understates real-world LLM capabilities, particularly under heterogeneous data distributions: (i) different models get different questions correct according to their specializations, and (ii) given a budget, multiple generations can be sampled and selectively retained. To quantify this gap, we introduce the Capability Frontier: a Pareto frontier over a set of models that characterizes the best achievable performance at each cost level under optimal selection across models and generations (i.e., via an oracle). Our construction corrects for two opposing biases: underestimation from single-model evaluation and overestimation from taking maxima over noisy samples. We study 21 LLMs across 16 widely used benchmarks spanning coding, reasoning, medicine, factuality, instruction following, and agentic tasks, comparing Capability Frontier performance at matched cost to each benchmark's top-performing model. Correcting for single-model evaluation yields a 54% error rate reduction; additionally correcting for single runs yields an 82% improvement, with SOTA accuracy matched at 85% cost reduction. Complementing these empirical results, we use controlled probabilistic simulations to show that higher query topic entropy produces a near-monotonic increase in the performance gap between oracle routing and the best single model. Our findings suggest collective LLM capabilities are substantially underestimated, with implications for evaluation and deployment in data-heterogeneous, multi-domain settings.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏通用机制来确定适用的算法配置、组合成有效的解决方案流水线，并评估其性能，尤其是在组织边界、责任划分或数据有限的情况下，需要分解式方法。

Method: 构建一个包含算法模块库、语义数据与算法卡片、问题分类体系、流水线合成器和评估器的框架，通过上下文匹配自动识别并组合适用算法，生成并评估所有有效优化流水线。

Result: 在7个基准实例集上应用该框架，覆盖4类问题，生成了1,063,044种有效优化流水线，验证了框架的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: CASOP框架为仓库运营提供了自动化设计、合成与选择高性能算法流水线的能力，具有广泛的应用前景，相关软件已开源。

Abstract: Order fulfillment in manual picker-to-goods warehouses involves interconnected decisions such as item assignment, order batching, and picker routing. While integrated models capture interactions between these decisions, practical warehouse systems often require decomposed approaches due to organizational boundaries, differing responsibilities, or limited data availability. Existing studies primarily evaluate algorithms for isolated subproblems or fixed subproblem combinations for specific warehouse settings, but lack a general mechanism to determine applicable algorithm configurations, compose them into valid solution pipelines, and assess their performance.
  With Context-Aware Synthesis of Optimization Pipelines (CASOP), we propose a framework for constructing and evaluating context-specific optimization pipelines and apply these to order fulfillment. The framework comprises: (1) a modular repository of algorithms for common order fulfillment problems; (2) semantic data and algorithm cards to describe warehouse context and algorithm requirements; (3) a taxonomy that structures order fulfillment problems into relevant subproblems; (4) a pipeline synthesizer that identifies applicable algorithms for a given warehouse context and composes all valid optimization pipelines; and (5) a pipeline evaluator that assesses all resulting pipelines. We demonstrate the framework on 7 benchmark instance sets covering four problem classes, resulting in 1,063,044 valid pipelines. The framework supports researchers and practitioners in designing, automatically synthesizing, and selecting valid, high-performing algorithmic pipelines for warehouse operations. The software is open-source and available at https://github.com/kit-dsm/ware_ops_pipes and https://github.com/kit-dsm/ware_ops_algos.
  Keywords: Warehouse optimization, Algorithm selection, Pipeline synthesis, Order fulfillment

### [213] [LCAi: Life Cycle Assessment with big data fusion and retrieval-augmented generation-assisted interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26857)
*Georgios Tsironis,Juan D. Medrano-Garcia,Gonzalo Guillen-Gosalbez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于多视角检索增强生成（RAG）的LCA解释框架，通过整合学术、产业、公众舆论和欧盟资助数据，将环境热点的量化改进机会转化为在技术、社会与政策不确定性下的可操作战略路径。该框架包含三步：场景锚定、特定视角微查询与受限检索、以及仅基于存储输出的中立合成。以意大利苹果生产厂氢燃料替代柴油为例，使用GPT-5 nano模型验证，有效降低幻觉风险并保持跨领域多样性，支持更具纪律性的结果转化与面向实施的决策，为大规模技术部署的LCA研究提供新范式。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种视角融合的检索增强生成（RAG）架构，涵盖学术、产业、公众话语及欧盟资助数据；采用三步流程：（1）设定系统边界与脱碳目标的场景锚定；（2）生成针对不同视角的微查询并进行受限检索；（3）仅基于已存储输出进行中立合成，避免二次检索，提升可信度。

Result: 在意大利苹果生产厂氢燃料替代柴油的案例中，该框架成功将环境影响结果转化为多维度战略路径建议，显著降低大语言模型的幻觉风险，同时保留跨领域多样性。结果具备可解释性与实施导向，验证了其在复杂不确定性情境下支持决策的能力。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了从量化影响到战略路径的结构化转化，推动了AI在LCA解释中的可信应用，为未来大规模技术部署相关的生命周期评估研究开辟了新方向，强调了证据驱动与多视角融合的重要性。

Abstract: The interpretation phase of life cycle assessment often lacks structured mechanisms for translating quantified improvement opportunities addressing environmental hotspots into actionable strategic pathways under technological, social, and policy uncertainty. To overcome this limitation, this study introduces a perspective-conditioned retrieval-augmented generation framework for LCA interpretation, where a multi-perspective retrieval and controlled synthesis is incorporated in the artificial intelligence (AI)-assisted LCA. To operationalise large language models in LCA interpretation, a perspective fusion RAG architecture was developed, covering academic, industry, public discourse, and European union (EU) funding datasets. Our approach comprises three steps: (1) a scenario anchor defining system boundaries and decarbonization targets, (2) a set of perspective-specific micro-queries with constrained retrieval, and (3) a neutral synthesis step integrating only ledger-stored outputs without further retrieval. The framework is demonstrated through a hydrogen-enabled diesel reduction use case in an Italian apple production facility using GPT-5 nano as the reasoning model. Overall, the structured retrieval and constrained synthesis are designed to mitigate the risk of hallucination while preserving cross-domain diversity. The approach presented can support more disciplined translation of impact results into strategic pathways and opens up new avenues for the use of advanced AI tools in LCA studies, particularly those focused on technologies that could be deployed at scale. This proof-of-concept demonstrates how AI-assisted, evidence-grounded interpretation can support implementation-oriented decision-making beyond conventional LCA studies.

### [214] [AgentX: Towards Agent-Driven Self-Iteration of Industrial Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26859)
*Changxin Lao,Fei Pan,Guozhuang Ma,Han Li,Huihuang Lin,Jijun Shi,Kangzhi Zhao,Kun Gai,Mo Zhou,Qinqin Zhou,Quan Chen,Ruochen Yang,Shifu Bie,Shuang Yang,Shuo Yang,Wenhao Li,Wentao Xie,Xiao Lv,Xuming Wang,Yijun Wang,Yiming Chen,Yusheng Huang,Zhongyuan Wang,Zibo Zhao,Zijie Zhuang,Baoning Xia,Chao Liu,Chaoyi Ma,Chubo He,Dawei Cong,Feng Jiang,Gang Wang,Guilin Xia,Hanwen Xu,Jiahong Xie,Jiahui Qiao,Jian Liang,Jiangfan Yue,Jing Wang,Jinghan Yang,Jinghui Jia,Kan Qin,Lei Wang,Ming Li,Peilin Song,Pengbo Xu,Qiang Luo,Ruiming Tang,Shiyang Liu,Shuxian Jin,Tao Wang,Tao Zhang,Xiang Gao,Xianghan Li,Yingsong Luo,Yiwen Ning,Yongcheng Liu,Yuan Guo,Zhaojie Liu,Zhenkai Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentX 是一个部署在生产环境中的多智能体系统，通过自动化推荐算法的迭代流程，实现从想法生成到上线评估的闭环。它由四个紧密协作的阶段组成：头脑风暴、开发、评估和自我进化，能够自主生成、实施、评估并从实验中学习，从而突破传统人工依赖的瓶颈，使推荐系统创新实现指数级增长而非线性扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推荐算法的迭代仍高度依赖工程师手动完成从假设提出到A/B测试上线的全过程，导致创新速度受限于人力规模，无法实现基于数据与计算的复利式增长。为解决这一结构性执行瓶颈，需要构建一个能自动且持续优化的系统。

Method: AgentX 采用四阶段闭环架构：(1) Brainstorm Agent 基于历史实验、系统架构、数据分析和外部研究生成可执行的推荐优化提案；(2) Developing Agent 将提案转化为生产就绪代码，并通过多维度验证确保可靠性；(3) Evaluation Agent 安全地进行在线灰度发布，结合护栏机制判断A/B实验结果，将成功与失败均转化为结构化知识；(4) Harness Evolution（SGPO）层从执行轨迹中提炼语义梯度更新，持续优化各智能体自身能力，实现系统的自我进化。

Result: AgentX 实现了推荐算法迭代的自动化与自进化，显著提升实验密度与创新效率，其运行速度远超人工流程，且能持续积累经验以增强自身决策与生成能力，为推荐系统研发提供可持续的工业化引擎。

Conclusion: AgentX 成功将推荐算法迭代从依赖人力的线性模式转变为基于证据、计算与知识积累的自进化范式，标志着推荐系统研发进入工业级智能化新阶段。

Abstract: Recommendation algorithm iteration is moving from an artisanal, engineer-bound process toward an industrialized research loop, but this transition remains blocked by a structural execution bottleneck: the idea-to-launch cycle still depends on human engineers to generate hypotheses, modify production code, launch A/B experiments, and attribute online results. Innovation therefore scales linearly with headcount rather than compounding with evidence, compute, and accumulated experimental knowledge. We present AgentX, a production-deployed multi-agent system that fundamentally restructures this production function. AgentX operates as a self-evolving development engine: it autonomously generates, implements, evaluates, and learns from recommendation experiments at a scale and pace that no manual workflow can sustain.
  The system orchestrates four tightly coupled stages in a closed loop. A Brainstorm Agent synthesizes evidence from historical experiments, system architecture, data analysis, and external research into ranked, executable proposals. A Developing Agent translates each proposal into production-ready code through repository-grounded generation and multi-dimensional reliability verification. An Evaluation Agent conducts safe online rollout with guardrail-vetoed A/B judgment, converting both successes and failures into structured knowledge assets. A Harness Evolution layer (SGPO) then distills execution trajectories into semantic-gradient updates that continuously sharpen the agents themselves -- making the system not merely automated, but self-improving.

### [215] [TAVR-VLM: Risk-Conditioned Causal Grounding for Hallucination-Resistant Report Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26874)
*Zhixiang Lu,Xiwei Liu,Sifan Song,Changkai Ji,Anh Nguyen,Jionglong Su,Imran Razzak,Jinfeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TAVR-VLM 是一种针对经导管主动脉瓣置换术（TAVR）规划的新型框架，通过引入风险条件因果接地注意力（R-CGA），构建了从风险到解剖区域再到文本词的内部结构化接地路径。该方法将多模态输入压缩为因果风险瓶颈，生成全局风险掩码，并在自回归生成过程中通过支持投影的因果一致性目标约束生成内容的解剖学合理性，显著降低诊断幻觉率至8.1%，在M³TAVR数据集上实现0.896的AUROC和0.936的CIDEr得分，达到当前最优性能，提升手术AI的可解释性与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型在高风险医疗场景如TAVR规划中易产生缺乏解剖学依据的诊断幻觉，阻碍其临床应用，亟需一种能确保生成内容与医学影像严格对齐的可靠机制。

Method: 提出R-CGA机制，建立‘风险→区域→词’的内部因果接地路径；通过风险瓶颈压缩多模态输入，生成全局风险掩码；在生成阶段引入支持投影的因果一致性损失，约束文本生成局限于风险定义的支持区域，实现细粒度解剖学对齐。

Result: 在包含1,482名患者的M³TAVR数据集上，TAVR-VLM达到0.896的AUROC、0.936的CIDEr分数，幻觉率降至8.1%，显著优于现有方法，提升了生成结果的准确性与可解释性。

Conclusion: TAVR-VLM通过内置因果接地机制有效抑制了多模态大模型在高风险医疗任务中的诊断幻觉，实现了更安全、可解释的自动决策支持，为手术AI的发展提供了新范式。

Abstract: Transcatheter Aortic Valve Replacement (TAVR) planning requires meticulous multimodal reasoning. However, adapting Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to this high-stakes domain is severely impeded by diagnostic hallucinations, where generated text lacks anatomical grounding. To address this, TAVR-VLM is introduced: a novel framework featuring Risk-Conditioned Causal Grounding Attention (R-CGA) that instantiates a model-internal ``Risk $\rightarrow$ Region $\rightarrow$ Word'' structural grounding pathway. R-CGA compresses multimodal inputs into a causal risk bottleneck, purifying dense visual features into a global risk mask. During autoregressive generation, a support-projected causal consistency objective constrains token-level grounding within the risk-defined support mask. Evaluated on $\text{M}^3\text{TAVR}$, a comprehensive 1,482-patient cohort, TAVR-VLM establishes a new state-of-the-art. It achieves an AUROC of 0.896, boosts CIDEr to 0.936, and drastically reduces the hallucination rate to 8.1\%, thereby improving interpretability for evidence-based surgical AI.

### [217] [Generative Retrieval via Diffusion Transformer with Metric-Ordered Sequence Training and Hybrid-Policy Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26899)
*Chenghao Liu,Yu Zhang,Zhongtao Jiang,Kun Xu,Zhenwei An,Renzhi Wang,Zhao Wang,Jiachen Zhang,Yuxiao Zhang,Kun Xu,Songfang Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为MO-DiT+HPPO的分阶段框架，用于解决模式保持的属性检索问题。在嵌入式检索中，传统方法倾向于返回与查询最相似的项目，但在实际应用中，往往需要在保持种子集细粒度模式的同时，找到满足特定属性且仍符合该模式的新项目。为此，作者引入连续生成式检索，通过模型读取项目嵌入序列并生成查询嵌入以进行最近邻搜索。该框架包括原始序列预训练、多领域度量有序延续预训练、尾部中心微调和HPPO（参考锚定偏好优化）。其中，度量有序训练将稀疏的在线检索标签转化为按预测属性密度从低到高排序的模式轨迹，使模型学会跨领域的度量改进方向；而HPPO则通过混合候选池的在线交集度量标签，结合参考锚点优化，使生成查询分布更贴近真实目标。此外，帕累托对过滤器仅保留不降低同模式纯度的优胜对，从而在不牺牲模式一致性的前提下提升属性指标。实验在四个属性域上进行，采用项目和模式留出协议，在八个域分割中的七个中取得显著提升，一个为微弱平局。消融实验验证了度量预测器的有效性、顺序训练的作用、与CPT/SFT的对比以及候选策略的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生产环境中，嵌入式检索通常只关注与查询最相似的项目，但实际需求往往更为复杂：给定一个表达细粒度模式的种子集合，需要找到既满足特定目标属性又保持原有模式的新项目。传统的平均种子方法虽然能保留模式，但会停留在低属性区域；而全局属性检索则容易偏离原模式。因此，亟需一种能够同时兼顾模式保持与属性满足的新型检索机制。

Method: 提出MO-DiT+HPPO框架，包含四阶段流程：1）原始序列预训练；2）多领域度量有序延续预训练，将稀疏在线标签转化为按属性密度排序的模式轨迹；3）尾部中心微调；4）基于参考锚定的偏好优化（HPPO），利用混合候选池的在线交集度量进行标签化，并优化生成查询分布。同时引入帕累托对过滤器，确保提升属性指标的同时不降低模式纯度。

Result: 在四个属性域上的项和模式留出测试中，度量有序DiT相比预训练生成检索器显著提升了交集指标；随后HPPO进一步优化，7个域分割中实现显著增益，1个为微弱平局。各类消融实验表明，度量预测器有效性、顺序训练作用、与CPT/SFT的对比优势以及候选策略影响均贡献于性能提升。

Conclusion: MO-DiT+HPPO成功实现了在保持模式一致性的前提下高效检索具有目标属性的项目，证明了连续生成式检索与度量有序训练及参考锚定优化相结合的有效性，为复杂场景下的精准推荐与检索提供了新范式。

Abstract: Embedding-based retrieval ranks items by their similarity to a query in a shared vector space and usually aims to return the highest-scoring items. In many production settings this is not what is wanted: given a seed set that expresses a fine-grained pattern, one needs more items that both satisfy a target attribute and stay within that pattern. We formalize this as pattern-preserving attribute retrieval. The two goals pull against each other: averaging the seeds preserves the pattern but stays in a low-attribute region, while global attribute retrieval drifts to unrelated patterns. We approach the task with continuous generative retrieval, where a model reads a sequence of item embeddings and generates query embeddings for nearest-neighbor search. We propose MO-DiT+HPPO, a staged framework with raw-sequence pretraining, multi-domain metric-ordered continuation pretraining, tail-centroid fine-tuning, and HPPO. Metric-ordered training turns sparse online retrieval labels into in-pattern trajectories ordered from low to high predicted attribute density, teaching one model the metric-improvement direction across domains. HPPO aligns the generated query distribution with the true online objective by labeling a hybrid candidate pool with the online intersection metric and applying reference-anchored preference optimization. A Pareto pair filter keeps only winner pairs that do not lower same-pattern purity, raising the attribute metric without sacrificing the pattern. Across four attribute domains under item- and pattern-holdout protocols, metric-ordered DiT improves the intersection metric over a pretrained generative retriever, and HPPO improves it further, with significant gains on seven of eight domain-split cells and a marginal tie on the hardest split. Metric-predictor validation, order ablations, CPT/SFT comparisons, and a candidate-policy ablation show where the gains come from.

</details>


### [218] [Learning to Recover Task Experts from a Multi-Task Merged Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26902)
*Jinwook Jung,Taegyu Kim,Kumju Jo,Sungyong Baik*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReTeX提出一种无需路由器的动态任务专家恢复框架，通过预测参数偏移来消除多任务模型合并中的参数干扰，利用SVD子空间签名在推理时识别任务并恢复超过95%的专家性能，同时实现对未见任务的自适应知识插值，显著提升泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有静态合并方法存在参数干扰问题，而动态合并通常依赖高成本的冗余专家存储与加载；本文从任务专家视角出发，将参数干扰视为可建模的参数扰动，旨在高效恢复专家性能并提升对未见任务的泛化能力。

Method: 将参数干扰建模为仿射变换，并近似为加性偏移；提出ReTeX框架，通过预测偏移量恢复专家性能；引入基于SVD子空间签名的无路由器任务识别机制，在推理阶段根据输入投影残差最小选择最匹配任务。

Result: 在视觉和自然语言处理领域，ReTeX能够恢复超过95%的独立专家性能，显著提升对未见任务的泛化能力，并在分布外任务上实现专家知识的自适应插值。

Conclusion: ReTeX实现了高效、无路由器的任务专家恢复，不仅有效缓解了参数干扰问题，还具备处理未见任务的自适应能力，为多任务模型合并提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-task model merging aims to consolidate several task-specific experts into a unified model, yet static merging consistently suffers from parameter interference. While dynamic merging models aim to bridge this gap, many works rely on the costly storage and loading of redundant expert components at inference. In this work, from the perspective of task expert, we view parameter interference as parameter perturbation introduced to each expert during merging process. We show that such parameter perturbations can be modeled as affine transformation, which can be approximated as additive offsets. Motivated by these, we propose Recover Task eXpert (ReTeX), a framework that predicts those offsets, in order to undo parameter interference and recover task-expert performance from a single merged checkpoint. To recover the appropriate expert when task identity is unknown, we introduce a router-free task identifier based on SVD subspace signatures computed offline before inference. At inference, the identifier selects the task whose subspace yields the smallest projection residual for a given input. As a result, ReTeX recovers over 95% of individual-expert performance in both vision and NLP domains, while significantly improving generalization to unseen tasks. Crucially, we also show that the parameter offset prediction leads to emergent adaptive interpolation of expert knowledge for out-of-distribution (OOD) tasks. ReTeX adaptively interpolates seen expert knowledge to handle unseen tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/BAIKLAB/ReTeX

### [219] [Diagnosing Task Insensitivity in Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26918)
*Jingyu Liu,Xiaopeng Wu,Kehan Chen,Chuan Yu,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大语言模型在长时序任务中的泛化能力问题，发现其对分布外（OOD）任务的适应性差，主要原因是任务不敏感性：模型在面对相似但不同的任务时，会机械地沿用训练中习得的模式，即使指令被语义破坏也无法正确调整。实验表明，当任务描述被替换为另一个相似任务时，模型仍会输出相同动作，且训练过程中注意力逐渐从任务标记转移到局部观察，显示出对捷径的优化偏好。为此，作者提出任务扰动负对数似然（Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization）正则化方法，通过轻量级对比学习增强动作对任务指令的依赖性。大量实验验证该方法显著提升了任务敏感性和分布外泛化能力，同时保持了对任务标记更稳定的注意力机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在执行长时序任务时表现出较强的推理能力，但在面对与训练数据不同但结构相似的任务时，其泛化能力较差。这种失败的根本原因在于模型对任务指令的敏感度不足，容易依赖训练中形成的捷径行为，而非真正理解任务要求。因此，亟需提升模型对任务指令的敏感性以增强其在未知任务场景下的适应能力。

Method: 提出任务扰动负对数似然优化（Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization），一种轻量级对比正则化方法。该方法通过在训练中引入任务描述的扰动版本，强制模型区分原任务与扰动任务，从而增强动作对任务指令的依赖性。同时，通过对比学习机制抑制模型对局部观察的过度关注，防止注意力漂移至非任务相关部分。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了模型在分布外任务上的表现，增强了对任务指令的敏感性，有效缓解了任务不敏感导致的错误行为。同时，模型在训练过程中对任务标记的注意力更加稳定，未出现明显的注意力漂移现象，整体性能优于基线模型。

Conclusion: 任务不敏感是限制大语言模型在复杂、多样化任务中泛化能力的关键因素。通过引入任务扰动的对比正则化策略，可以有效引导模型关注任务指令本身，减少对训练捷径的依赖，从而提升其在真实世界多变环境中的鲁棒性和适应性。

Abstract: Large language models can serve as capable long-horizon agents, but their out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization remains weak. We identify a key source of this failure as task insensitivity: when faced with similar but distinct tasks, models might apply patterns learned during training and fail to solve the task at hand. We show that models often continue with actions aligned with the original task even when the instruction is semantically corrupted and cannot be directly answered. We further find that, when we replace the task description in a trained prompt with another similar but distinct task, the model may still output the same action. This behavior is accompanied by a consistent training-time attention drift away from task tokens and toward local observations, suggesting an optimization bias toward shortcuts. To mitigate this problem, we propose Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization, a lightweight contrastive regularizer that explicitly encourages action dependence on the task instruction. Extensive evaluations show that our intervention improves task sensitivity and OOD generalization while preserving more stable attention to task tokens.

### [220] [Where Do CoT Training Gains Land in LLM based Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26935)
*Jingyu Liu,Zhiwen Wang,Yuxin Jing,Huanyu Zhou,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了链式思维（CoT）推理在语言模型代理中的实际作用，发现CoT训练主要提升了模型基于提示直接预测动作的能力，而非通过推理改变行为。实验表明，随着模型迭代，仅依赖提示的动作质量显著提升，且CoT相对于提示的相对优势未增大，说明CoT并未显著增强推理能力。此外，后期模型更倾向于依赖提示而非根据CoT调整动作。通过有选择地屏蔽部分训练样本的动作监督，研究进一步提升了模型在跨域任务上的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究链式思维（CoT）训练的真实效果：是提升模型通过生成推理来改变行为的能力，还是仅仅提高模型从提示中直接预测动作的能力。

Method: 比较不同模型检查点下仅使用提示的“提示动作”与使用CoT的“CoT动作”的表现；分析模型在交互环境中对两种方式的相对优势变化；观察模型在不同阶段对CoT推理的依赖程度；采用选择性掩码动作标记监督的干预策略以提升泛化能力。

Result: 1. 随着模型迭代，仅依赖提示的动作质量显著提升；2. CoT动作相对于提示动作的相对优势保持稳定，表明CoT训练并未扩大其优势；3. 后期模型更少根据CoT修改动作，表现出更强的提示依赖；4. 选择性屏蔽动作监督可有效提升模型在未见领域的泛化性能。

Conclusion: CoT训练的核心作用并非增强推理驱动的行为修正，而是提升模型从提示中直接预测动作的能力。通过有选择地弱化动作监督，可促进模型学习更鲁棒、泛化能力更强的决策机制。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is widely used in language-model agents, but prior work has shown that verbalized CoT is not always faithful and may instead reflect post-hoc reasoning, which means the model already knows the answer before reasoning. We therefore ask what CoT training is actually improving: is the model getting better at changing its action through generated reasoning, or is it getting better at predicting the action directly from the prompt? We study this question by comparing \emph{prompt actions} (predicting action without CoT) with CoT actions (predicting action with CoT). Across checkpoints, prompt-action quality improves substantially. While interacting with the environment, the relative advantage of CoT actions over prompt actions remains similar, showing that CoT training does not widen the advantage of CoT reasoning, and it helps to improve the quality of prompt actions. We further find that later checkpoints are less likely to revise the action in response to CoT, suggesting greater reliance on the prompt. Motivated by these patterns, we selectively mask action-token supervision on a fraction of training examples. This intervention improves out-of-domain generalization.

</details>


### [221] [Look-Before-Move: Narrative-Grounded World Visual Attention in Dynamic 3D Story Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26964)
*Jiaming Bian,Bingliang Li,Yuehao Wu,Pichao Wang,Zhi Wang,Hailan Ma,Huadong Mo,Zhenhong Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究在动态3D场景中，摄像头如何基于叙事意图主动规划视觉观察，提出“Look-Before-Move”框架，通过语义观察契约、蒙特卡洛视角搜索与语义轨迹锚定，实现叙事一致、几何可行且连贯的相机运动。构建了基于StoryBlender的动态3D故事世界基准，涵盖50个故事、457个场景和1585个镜头，实验表明该方法在主体感知、意图一致性与轨迹质量上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉感知多为被动解读观测数据，而在动态3D环境中，摄像头需主动决策观察内容与时机。本文旨在解决摄像头在动态3D故事世界中的主动视觉注意力问题，使相机能根据叙事意图合理选择观察点并生成连贯运动。

Method: 提出Look-Before-Move框架：1）构建语义观察契约，将导演意图转化为可执行的视觉约束；2）采用蒙特卡洛视角搜索，寻找符合叙事与几何约束的可行视角；3）通过语义轨迹锚定，将选定视角连接成连续、无碰撞、时间连贯的相机运动路径。

Result: 在自建的动态3D故事世界基准上，所提方法在主体感知清晰度、叙事意图一致性以及相机轨迹质量方面显著优于现有基线方法，验证了先组织视觉注意力再生成运动的有效性。

Conclusion: 主动视觉规划在动态3D环境中至关重要，通过分离观察决策与运动执行，可实现更自然、更符合叙事意图的相机控制。本研究为具身智能系统在复杂环境中的视觉注意力机制提供了新范式。

Abstract: As embodied AI and world models increasingly operate in dynamic 3D environments, visual perception must move beyond passively interpreting given observations toward actively deciding what to observe. We study this problem through camera planning in dynamic 3D story worlds, where the camera must not only generate smooth motion, but also decide what visual evidence should be acquired before it moves. We formulate this capability as Narrative-Grounded World Visual Attention, where the camera acts as an embodied observer that determines what to observe, how to compose the observation, and how to shift attention over time under narrative intent and physical 3D constraints. To realize this capability, we propose Look-Before-Move, a camera planning framework that separates observation specification from motion execution. It first builds a Semantic Observation Contract to convert directorial intent into executable visual constraints, then performs Monte Carlo Viewpoint Search to find narrative-compliant and geometrically feasible viewpoints, and finally applies Semantic Trajectory Grounding to connect selected viewpoints into continuous, collision-aware, and temporally coherent camera motion. We further construct a dynamic 3D Story World Benchmark based on StoryBlender, covering 50 stories, 457 scenes, and 1585 shots with animated characters, semantic scene configurations, and executable 3D environments. Experiments show that our framework improves subject perception, intent consistency, and trajectory quality over representative baselines, demonstrating the importance of organizing visual attention before generating camera motion.

</details>

Abstract: Does intelligence require the ability to reason about phenomena beyond direct experience? It is natural to suspect that some complex thought cannot be captured through language alone. However, of particular concern to this work, is whether visualising counterfactual events can complement language as a mechanism for complex thought. We ask whether LLMs can be trained to utilise such visualisation mechanisms, in a way that benefits their reasoning abilities. Motivated by this question, we propose Einstein World Models. EWMs are a blueprint for LLM-based reasoning systems that place visual-temporal rollouts inside the reasoning trace, allowing them to reason in ways that text alone may not support well. In an EWM, the LLM calls a world-module (not to be confused with a world model), to produce short rollouts of scenes under consideration. The returned rollout is treated not as the answer, but as an inspectable hypothesis that can support later reasoning. Einstein World Models extend the capability of LLMs for tool calling (such as web search or code execution), into the domain of visual thought experiments.

### [223] [Adaptive Utility driven Resource Orchestration for Resilient AI (AURORA-AI)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27005)
*Rahul Umesh Mhapsekar,Ilias Cherkaoui,Lizy Abraham,Indrakshi Dey*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AURORA-AI is a framework for adaptive resource orchestration in AI systems, designed to maintain high performance and fairness under dynamic conditions. It uses feedback control, stability monitoring, and utility optimization to adjust computational resources across heterogeneous models in real time.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Static resource allocation fails under non-stationary conditions, leading to degraded performance and compromised fairness and explainability. There is a need for adaptive, resilient AI systems that can maintain utility despite disruptions like concept drift and demographic bias.

Method: AURORA-AI integrates Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman control, Lyapunov-based stability monitoring, and a fairness-aware composite utility function into a closed-loop policy. It dynamically redistributes computational budget to maximize global utility across multiple dimensions including accuracy, fairness, cost, latency, robustness, and interpretability.

Result: In simulations with demographic bias shocks, concept drift, and black-swan events, AURORA-AI recovered from disruptions significantly faster than baselines (88 vs. 22 vs. 0 time steps). It improved alpha-quantile and super-quantile by 29% and 25%, reduced demographic parity gaps, and increased stable operating steps.

Conclusion: Fairness-aware adaptive orchestration grounded in stability theory is both practical and theoretically sound, enabling resilient, human-centric AI deployment under real-world volatility.

Abstract: Modern AI systems are increasingly deployed under non-stationary computational, demographic, and operational conditions in which static resource allocation strategies degrade both predictive performance and human-centric properties such as fairness and explainability. This paper presents AURORA-AI, an Adaptive Utility-driven Resource Orchestration framework for Resilient AI that unifies Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman feedback control, Lyapunov-based stability monitoring, and a fairness-aware composite utility into a single closed-loop policy.The framework continuously redistributes computational budget across a population of heterogeneous AI models so that the global utility, defined jointly over predictive performance, demographic parity, cost, latency, robustness, and interpretability, remains maximised under disruption. The framework is evaluated in a stress-rich discrete-time simulation that concurrently injects demographic bias shocks, gradual concept drift, and abrupt black-swan disruptions, and is compared against five established controllers including Static, Round Robin, Greedy, LinUCB, and a deep reinforcement-learning agent based on Proximal Policy Optimisation. AURORA-AI achieves immediate recovery from the black-swan event compared to eighty-eight time steps for the Static baseline and twenty-two for Proximal Policy Optimisation, lifts the alpha-quantile and the super-quantile by twenty-nine and twenty-five percent respectively, simultaneously reduces the mean and maximum demographic parity gap, and increases the fraction of Lyapunov-stable operating steps. These results indicate that fairness-aware adaptive orchestration grounded in stability theory is a practical and theoretically motivated path toward resilient human-centric AI deployment.
