### [224] [Semantic Early-Stopping for Iterative LLM Agent Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27009)
*Sahil Shrivastava*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究多智能体大语言模型循环中的语义早停机制，提出基于连续草稿嵌入变化和质量提升的停止策略，实现更高效、更智能的终止。通过理论证明确定性收敛，设计低开销的评估协议，并在HotpotQA任务上验证其有效性：无裁判的语义停止器在保持质量的前提下减少38%的运算令牌；而带质量门控的版本因评估成本过高反而不划算。最优轮次选择可显著提升信息得分，揭示了‘何时停止’应转向‘哪一轮最优’这一开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖固定迭代次数（max_iterations）作为终止条件，无法感知答案是否仍在改进，导致对简单问题浪费资源，对复杂问题提前截断。需要一种能根据内容语义变化与质量提升动态判断停止时机的机制。

Method: 提出语义早停策略：当连续草稿嵌入的余弦距离在耐心窗口内不再显著变化且答案质量未进一步提升时停止。构建统一轨迹重放与缓存机制，实现不同停止策略间的公平高效比较；区分操作令牌与评估令牌，降低测量开销。

Result: 在HotpotQA测试集上，无裁判的语义停止器将操作令牌减少38%，质量几乎不变（Delta-IS = -0.004, p = 0.81）；而质量门控版本因每轮需大量评判，成本过高，表现不佳。理想最优轮次选择相比所有实际策略提升显著（+0.115，p ~ 4e-11）。

Conclusion: 语义早停提供了比固定迭代更智能的终止方式，但关键挑战已从‘何时停止’转变为‘哪一轮最好’。未来工作需聚焦于如何高效识别最优回答轮次。

Abstract: Multi-agent large language model (LLM) loops, for example a Writer that drafts and a Critic that revises, are almost always terminated by a fixed iteration cap (max_iterations). This is a syntactic kill-switch: it is blind to whether the answer is still improving, so it over-spends tokens on easy inputs and truncates hard ones. We study semantic early-stopping: the loop halts when consecutive draft embeddings stop changing in meaning (cosine distance with a patience window) and the answer's measured quality stops improving. Our work makes three contributions. First, an honest theoretical footing: we prove deterministic termination and well-definedness and machine-check these claims, while treating the convergence of the distance sequence as an empirically tested conjecture rather than a (previously over-claimed) Banach contraction. Second, a judge-efficient evaluation protocol: we generate each question's full trajectory once, replay every stopping policy over the identical drafts, and cache every LLM-judge call, yielding a strictly paired efficiency-versus-quality comparison at low cost; we further separate operational tokens (charged to a policy) from evaluation tokens (a measurement instrument). Third, an empirical study on multi-hop retrieval-augmented question answering (HotpotQA). On the 60-question test split, a judge-free semantic stopper reduces operational tokens by 38% relative to max_iterations at parity quality (Delta-IS = -0.004, p = 0.81), whereas the full quality-gated variant is counter-productive because its per-round judging dominates cost. An oracle that selects the best round attains +0.115 Information Score over every practical policy (p ~ 4e-11), reframing the problem from "when to stop" (easy) to "which round is best" (open).

</details>


### [225] [How to evaluate clustering with ground truth?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27061)
*Pasi Fränti*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了常用的外部有效性指标，重点分析基于集合匹配的度量方法。推荐使用质心指数（CI），因其直观且结果可解释；若需更精细的点级度量，可选择成对集合指数（PSI）以避免聚类大小偏差，或使用聚类准确率（ACC）等集合匹配方法确保所有点同等重要。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在真实标签的情况下，需要有效的外部指标来评估聚类结果，但现有指标存在直观性、可解释性或偏差问题，因此需要系统梳理并推荐合适的度量方法。

Method: 综述法，聚焦于基于集合匹配的外部有效性指标，比较各类指标的特性与适用场景。

Result: 质心指数（CI）适合直观的聚类级别评估；成对集合指数（PSI）提供无偏的归一化点级评分；聚类准确率（ACC）等集合匹配方法适用于所有点同等重要的情形。

Conclusion: 根据评估需求选择合适指标：追求直观性和可解释性选CI；需要点级精细度且避免大小偏差选PSI；强调每个点平等影响时选ACC或其他集合匹配方法。

Abstract: External indexes can be used for cluster evaluation when ground truth is available. We review the most common external validity indexes focusing on set-matching-based measures. We recommend centroid index (CI), because it is an intuitive cluster-level measure with an explainable result. If we need a more fine-tuned, point-level measure, there are more choices. Pair-set index (PSI) provides a normalized score which is not biased by cluster sizes. If all points should matter equally, then clustering accuracy (ACC) or any other set-matching measure is suitable.

*Shicheng Ye,Chao Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: JERP提出一种联合学习经验规则与策略的方法，通过交互轨迹同时更新长期经验规则池和模型策略，在决策时结合规则与历史信息，提升复杂交互任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将交互经验分为外部规则提示或参数更新，前者易与策略脱节，后者在稀疏奖励场景中对局部错误修正有限。

Method: JERP利用同一交互轨迹同时优化策略和修订规则池，决策时检索相关规则并条件化代理，训练后对比当前与成功轨迹以更新规则和策略。

Result: 在AlfWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，JERP在复杂交互任务中持续提升了决策性能。

Abstract: For LLM agents in multi-step interactive environments, a key challenge is to make effective use of accumulated interaction experience. Existing work has typically separated two uses of such experience: keeping it outside the model as natural-language rules for later prompting, or using trajectories and feedback to update the model parameters. The former is easy to interpret but can fall out of sync with the evolving policy; the latter improves the policy more broadly but provides only limited correction for local mistakes in sparse-reward settings. We present Joint Learning of Experiential Rules and Policies for LLM Agents (JERP), which updates a long-term experiential-rule pool and the policy from the same interaction trajectories. At decision time, JERP retrieves task-relevant rules and conditions the agent on them together with the interaction history. After each episode, it uses the collected trajectories both to optimize the policy and to revise the rule pool by comparing current rollouts with reference successful trajectories. This coupling keeps the rule pool aligned with the evolving policy while allowing stable and effective behaviors to be gradually absorbed into the model itself. Experiments on AlfWorld and WebShop show that JERP yields consistent gains in decision performance for complex interactive tasks.

### [227] [OpenRCA 2.0: From Outcome Labels to Causal Process Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27154)
*Aoyang Fang,Yifan Yang,Jin'ao Shang,Qisheng Lu,Junjielung Xu,Rui Wang,Songhan Zhang,Yuzhong Zhang,Boxi Yu,Pinjia He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PAVE步骤化标注协议，通过已知故障注入干预重构因果传播路径，构建首个跨系统、具有步骤级因果注释的RCA基准OpenRCA 2.0（500个实例）。实验表明，11个前沿LLM在精确恢复根因集合上平均仅达20.7%，但能识别至少一个正确根因服务的比例为76.0%，而将其与症状间验证的因果路径关联的仅为61.5%。这揭示了‘无根基诊断’这一关键失败模式，强调仅有结果评估会掩盖该问题，步骤级因果真值对可信LLM-RCA代理至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RCA数据集仅标注根因，未标注因果传播路径，导致任务简化为模式匹配，无法真实检验LLM的多步推理与工具使用能力。需要更严格的评估机制来揭示LLM在真实因果推理中的缺陷。

Method: 提出PAVE（Propagation-Aware Verification and Explanation）协议，利用故障注入实验中已知的干预手段，反向重建从根因到症状的因果传播路径；采用前向验证机制（从因推果），确保每一步因果链路可验证，从而生成精细的步骤级因果标注。

Result: 基于PAVE构建的OpenRCA 2.0基准包含500个实例，11个前沿LLM在准确恢复全部根因上平均仅20.7%成功；即使放宽标准，仍只有61.5%的模型能将正确根因服务与验证过的因果路径关联，暴露出‘无根基诊断’问题。

Conclusion: 当前仅依赖结果评估的RCA研究忽略了关键的因果路径验证环节。步骤级因果真值是实现可信LLM-RCA评估的必要条件，未来需发展具备因果解释与路径验证能力的模型。

Abstract: Root cause analysis (RCA) poses a holistic test of LLM agentic capabilities, such as long-context understanding, multi-step reasoning, and tool use. However, existing datasets suffer from a fundamental gap: they label only the root cause, not the propagation path connecting it to the observed symptom, which largely simplifies the task to naive pattern matching. To support rigorous evaluation, we introduce PAVE, a step-wise labeling protocol that leverages known interventions from fault injection to reconstruct causal propagation paths. The mechanism is forward verification: reasoning from cause to effect rather than inferring backward from symptoms. Applying PAVE yields OpenRCA 2.0 (500 instances), the first cross-system RCA benchmark with step-wise causal annotations for LLM agents. Across 11 frontier LLMs, recovering the exact root-cause set succeeds in only 20.7% of cases on average. To locate where this difficulty lies, we relax the criterion and find what we call the ungrounded diagnosis: agents identify at least one correct root-cause service in 76.0% of cases, but ground that service in a verified causal propagation path to the observed symptom in only 61.5%. Outcome-only evaluation hides this failure mode; step-wise causal ground truth is the missing piece for trustworthy LLM-based RCA agents.

### [228] [TOPS: First-Principles Visual Token Pruning via Constructing Token Optimal Preservation Sets for Efficient MLLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27161)
*Tinghao Wang,Yichen Guo,Rui Huang,Zheng Lu,Qizhe Zhang,Chenxi Li,Yuan Zhang,Jiajun Cao,Zhirong Shen,Yaosong Du,Guangyan Gan,Wenya Wang,Lin William Cong,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为TOPS的训练无关、模型无关的视觉标记剪枝模块，基于信息论从第一性原理出发，将视觉标记剪枝建模为构建最优保留集（Token Optimal Preservation Sets）。通过任务相关性、信息覆盖度和语义多样性三大原则，实现高效且有意义的标记选择。在7个MMLM骨干网络和14个基准测试中，TOPS表现出色，例如在LLaVA-NeXT上剪除77.8%的视觉标记，同时保持甚至略微提升性能，表明剪枝可缓解幻觉并启发轻量化模型设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉标记剪枝方法存在不足：基于注意力的标准常保留冗余标记，基于多样性的标准忽略用户指令，且缺乏对剪枝本质目标的严谨建模。因此需要从基础原理出发，建立更有效的剪枝框架。

Method: 提出从信息论角度分析视觉标记剪枝问题，定义任务相关性、信息覆盖度和语义多样性三大核心原则，并据此设计无需训练、适用于多种多模态大模型的剪枝模块TOPS。

Result: 在7种多模态大模型和14个基准测试中，TOPS显著优于现有方法；在LLaVA-NeXT 7B和13B模型上分别实现77.8%的标记剪除，性能保持100.0%和100.6%，说明剪枝不仅能提升效率，还可能减少幻觉。

Conclusion: TOPS通过系统性地遵循信息论指导的三大原则，实现了高效、准确的视觉标记剪枝，不仅提升了计算效率，还展现出潜在改善模型鲁棒性和生成质量的能力，为未来轻量化多模态模型设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved strong multimodal reasoning capabilities, but their efficiency is limited by the large number of visual tokens, which introduces substantial computational overhead. Visual token pruning offers a natural solution, yet existing methods are imperfect: attention-based criteria tend to retain redundant tokens, while diversity-based criteria are often agnostic to user instructions. Even methods that combine multiple criteria still lack a principled formulation of the intrinsic objective of token pruning. In this paper, we revisit visual token pruning from a first-principles perspective and formulate it as constructing Token Optimal Preservation Sets. Through a top-down information-theoretic analysis, we identify three fundamental principles for effective token selection: Task Relevance, Information Coverage, and Semantic Diversity. Based on these principles, we propose TOPS, a training-free and model-agnostic pruning module that can be applied to various MLLMs. Extensive experiments on 7 MLLM backbones and 14 benchmarks demonstrate that TOPS outperforms prior methods under diverse pruning settings. Notably, on LLaVA-NeXT, TOPS removes 77.8% of visual tokens while preserving 100.0% and 100.6% performance on its 7B and 13B models, respectively, suggesting that pruning redundant visual tokens can sometimes mitigate hallucination and inspire future lightweight MLLM design.

### [229] [A Process Harness for Uplifting Legacy Workflows to Agentic BPM: Design and Realization in CUGA FLO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27188)
*Fabiana Fournier,Lior Limonad*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Process Harness的新机制，将传统工作流升级为智能业务流程管理（Agentic BPM），无需替换原有工作流引擎。该机制在确定性工作流引擎外层引入一个受策略约束的智能代理层，通过在指定控制点介入，实现推理、自适应和监督功能，同时保持引擎对流程结构的控制权。为此，作者提出了任务-决策-流程（TDF）模型，明确其数据模式和执行语义，将LLM推理分解为三种受策略约束的代理：任务代理（TaskAgent）负责知识密集型任务执行，决策代理（DecisionAgent）负责案例级网关路由，流程代理（FlowAgent）则通过受控钩子机制实现运行时流程自适应。所有代理均在来自过程框架（FRAME）的统一策略下运行，确保一致性与合规性。研究进一步实现了CUGA FLO系统以验证TDF模型，并在贷款审批流程中展示了三类代理及钩子驱动的监管覆盖能力。该方法成功融合了强制性要求（通过确定性执行保障结构合规）与规范性要求（通过策略约束的智能自治在关键节点灵活响应）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统工作流系统难以应对复杂、动态的业务场景，尤其在需要智能推理、自适应和监管干预的环节存在局限。现有方案要么完全替换原有工作流引擎，导致迁移成本高；要么缺乏对智能行为的策略管控，造成合规风险。因此，亟需一种既能保留原有工作流结构与确定性优势，又能引入智能代理能力的轻量级集成机制，以实现从传统流程向智能流程的平稳演进。

Method: 提出并形式化了任务-决策-流程（TDF）模型，定义其数据结构与执行语义；设计三层智能代理架构：TaskAgent（任务执行）、DecisionAgent（决策路由）、FlowAgent（流程自适应）；引入政策框架（FRAME）统一管理所有LLM调用的策略；构建基于钩子机制的运行时干预接口；实现CUGA FLO系统原型并在贷款审批流程中进行验证。

Result: CUGA FLO成功在不改变原有工作流引擎的前提下，实现了对贷款审批流程中任务执行、路径选择与流程调整的智能支持；三类代理协同工作，支持监管规则通过钩子机制动态注入；实验表明该机制能有效兼顾流程结构的确定性与运行时的灵活性，满足合规性与智能化双重需求。

Conclusion: Process Harness通过TDF模型与CUGA FLO系统的实现，证明了在不替换传统工作流引擎的前提下，可高效集成智能代理能力，实现对业务流程的智能化增强。该方法在保证结构性合规的同时，赋予流程在关键节点上的自主推理与动态调整能力，为传统企业系统向智能业务流程管理的演进提供了一条可行且稳健的技术路径。

Abstract: We introduce the process harness, a new mechanism for uplifting legacy workflows into Agentic Business Process Management (Agentic BPM) without replacing the underlying workflow engine. A process harness places a policy-governed agentic layer around a deterministic workflow engine, intercepting designated control points to contribute reasoning, adaptation, and oversight while the engine retains structural authority over the process. To define the process harness rigorously, we develop the Task-Decision-Flow (TDF) model, specifying both its data schema and its execution semantics. TDF decomposes LLM reasoning across three policy-governed agent types: a TaskAgent for knowledge-intensive task execution, a DecisionAgent for per-case gateway routing, and a FlowAgent that governs runtime flow adaptation through a principled hook mechanism. Each agent reasons within an explicit policy drawn from the process FRAME, the aggregate policy set governing all LLM calls in the system. We then present CUGA FLO as the design and implementation realization of the TDF model, and demonstrate it on a loan approval workflow that exercises all three agent types and hook-driven regulatory override. The process harness uniquely reconciles imperative requirements, realized through deterministic workflow execution that enforces structural compliance, with normative requirements, realized through policy-framed agentic autonomy invoked at designated control points wherever the process demands it.

</details>


### [230] [Vulnerability of Natural Language Classifiers to Evolutionary Generated Adversarial Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27215)
*Manjinder Singh,Alexander E. I. Brownlee,Mohamed Elawady*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GAversary is a hybrid Genetic Algorithm for generating adversarial attacks on NLP models without requiring internal model access, using GloVe embeddings to maintain semantic similarity. It achieves significant accuracy drops in target models (e.g., from 76.8% to 5.8%), though it perturbs more words and runs slightly slower.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing adversarial attacks in NLP often require access to model internals or produce low semantic quality. There's a need for effective black-box attacks that preserve meaning while maximizing model disruption.

Method: GAversary uses a Genetic Algorithm with GloVe embeddings as the mutation operator to generate semantically similar adversarial text replacements, guided only by model logits.

Result: GAversary significantly reduces model accuracy compared to BAE and A2T (e.g., down to 5.8% vs. 27.6%), but perturbs nearly twice as many words, has slightly lower semantic similarity, and takes ~5% longer to run.

Conclusion: GAversary provides an effective black-box adversarial attack method for NLP models with strong performance, albeit with minor trade-offs in perturbation size, semantic fidelity, and runtime.

Abstract: Deep learning models have achieved impressive performance across various fields but remain vulnerable to adversarial inputs, particularly in NLP, where such attacks can have significant real-world consequences. Adversarial attacks often involve small, semantically similar token replacements to fool NLP models, and recent methods have become more precise by targeting specific vulnerable words, often by exploiting some level of access to the model's internal structure. This paper proposes GAversary, a hybrid Genetic Algorithm (GA) to generate adversarial attacks on natural language models. The GA is able to treat the target model as a black box, requiring only the logit value output by the model to guide the search. GAversary differs from GAs previously proposed for this problem by using GloVe embeddings to propose word replacements (the mutation operator) to improve the semantic similarity of the adversarial examples. GAversary is applied to several benchmark data sets and well-known target models. GAversary is able to substantially reduce the target model's accuracy on test data compared to the BAE and A2T attacks compared against (in the best case, reducing a 76.8% accuracy to 5.8%, compared to BAE's 27.6%). The trade-off is that GAversary perturbs just under twice as many words as the other two methods, with a slightly lower semantic similarity to the original text and around a 5% increase in run-time.

### [231] [Ask, Don't Judge: Binary Questions for Interpretable LLM Evaluation and Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27226)
*Sangwoo Cho,Kushal Chawla,Pengshan Cai,Zefang Liu,Chenyang Zhu,Shi-Xiong Zhang,Sambit Sahu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BINEVAL 是一种任务无关、无需训练的可解释评估框架，通过将评估标准分解为原子二元问题，利用大语言模型独立回答并聚合结果，生成透明、多维度的评分。该方法在多个基准测试中表现优于或匹配现有基线（如 UniEval 和 G-Eval），尤其在事实一致性任务（如 QAGS）上表现突出，且更贴近人类评分分布，避免了传统 LLM 评估中的评分天花板问题，同时支持迭代提示优化，具备良好的诊断与改进价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型输出评估面临三大挑战：人工评估成本高、词法指标与人类判断相关性差、现有基于 LLM 的评估器产生难以调试的黑箱分数。亟需一种兼具准确性、可解释性和可操作性的评估方法。

Method: 提出 BINEVAL 框架，通过元提示生成细粒度的二元评估问题，由 LLM 对每个生成输出独立回答，得到问题级反馈，并聚合形成可解释的多维评分。

Result: 在 SummEval、Topical-Chat、QAGS 等数据集上，BINEVAL 在与人类判断的相关性、评分分布匹配度、对劣质输出的区分能力方面均优于或等同于现有方法，尤其在事实一致性任务中表现显著；同时其提供的问题级反馈可用于提示优化，在自更新和跨模型更新设置下均有效提升性能。

Conclusion: BINEVAL 提供了一种无需训练、任务通用、高度可解释的评估方案，兼具优异的实证表现与实际诊断与优化价值，是当前 LLM 评估的重要进展。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM outputs remains a major bottleneck in NLP: human evaluation is expensive and slow, lexical metrics correlate poorly with human judgments on open-ended generation, and holistic LLM judges often produce opaque scores that are hard to debug. We propose BINEVAL, a framework that decomposes evaluation criteria into atomic binary questions and aggregates the resulting verdicts into interpretable, multi-dimensional scores. Given a task prompt, a meta-prompt generates fine-grained evaluation questions, and an LLM answers them independently for each output, yielding transparent question-level feedback together with calibrated overall scores. This decomposition makes evaluation easier to inspect, easier to diagnose, and directly usable for prompt improvement. Across SummEval, Topical-Chat, and QAGS, BINEVAL matches or outperforms strong baselines including UniEval and G-Eval, with especially strong results on factual consistency benchmarks such as QAGS. Beyond competitive correlation with human judgments, BINEVAL better matches human score distributions and avoids the ceiling effects common in prior LLM judges, leading to better discrimination between borderline and clearly flawed outputs. We further show that the same question-level feedback supports iterative prompt optimization, improving evaluator prompts on summarization and generation prompts on IFBench under both self-update and cross-model update settings. Overall, BINEVAL provides a task-agnostic, training-free, and interpretable evaluation framework that combines strong empirical performance with practical diagnostic and optimization value.

### [232] [EO-WM: A Physically Informed World Model for Probabilistic Earth Observation Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27277)
*Junwei Luo,Shuai Yuan,Zhenya Yang,Yansheng Li,Zhe Liu,Hengshuang Zhao*

TL;DR: 本文提出EO-WM，一种用于多光谱地球观测（EO）预测的视频扩散变压器，通过物理启发的条件框架建模气象强迫，区分气候基线与异常，并累积异常强迫以捕捉持续的热浪和干旱压力。为评估天气响应行为，引入两个诊断基准：极端夏季基准和季节配对基准。实验表明，EO-WM在预测植被退化幅度误差上相对降低5.63%，方向命中率相对提升7.80%，同时保持像素级指标竞争力。代码与数据将开源。

Conclusion: EO-WM是一种能够有效建模气象驱动下的地球表面动态变化的视频扩散模型，具备更强的物理可解释性和天气响应能力，其提出的诊断基准有助于推动地球观测预测向更真实、可靠的方向发展。

Abstract: Earth Observation (EO) forecasting aims to predict future Earth surface dynamics from satellite observations under changing meteorological conditions. In this paper, we view this task as a partially observed, weather-driven world modeling problem, in which weather acts as a conditioning signal, while forecasting remains uncertain due to sparse observations and unobserved land-surface states. However, existing methods do not fully capture this setting: deterministic models collapse uncertainty into a single future prediction, while diffusion-based methods typically treat weather variables as undifferentiated conditioning signals, and existing benchmarks focus mainly on reconstruction accuracy rather than whether forecasts respond correctly to changed weather forcing.We introduce EO-WM, a video diffusion transformer for multispectral EO forecasting. EO-WM incorporates a physically informed conditioning framework that represents meteorological forcing through a climatological baseline, weather anomalies, and cumulative physical stress signals. Specifically, it separates baseline and anomaly through distinct conditioning pathways, and accumulates anomalous forcing over time to capture sustained heat and drought stress. To evaluate weather-response behavior beyond standard metrics, we introduce two diagnostic benchmarks: an Extreme Summer Benchmark for severity-aware prediction of vegetation degradation under extreme weather, and a Seasonal Matched-Pair Benchmark for testing response fidelity under changed weather forcing. Experiments show that EO-WM reduces the error in predicted Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) decline amplitude by a relative 5.63% and improves directional hit rate by a relative 7.80%, while remaining competitive on standard pixel-level metrics. The benchmarks and model will be made open-source at https://github.com/Luo-Z13/EO-WM.

### [233] [Simulation-based inference for rapid Bayesian parameter estimation in epidemiological models: a comparison with MCMC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27286)
*Alina Bazarova,Johann Fredrik Jadebeck,Henrik Zunker,Carolina J. Klett-Tammen,Torben Heinsohn,Wolfgang Wiechert,Katharina Noeh,Stefan Kesselheim*

TL;DR: 本文研究了使用神经后验估计的模拟基础推断（SBI）作为机制性流行病学模型贝叶斯校准的一种可扩展替代方法，以应对高维非线性系统和频繁近实时分析带来的计算挑战。在德国2020年新冠重症监护病房（ICU）占用数据上，比较了SBI与马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）在多个疫情阶段的表现，包括31天推断窗口和更具挑战性的201天重建问题。结果表明，SBI在31天窗口中与MCMC具有高度一致的后验分布，并准确再现了观察到的ICU轨迹；在201天设置下，尽管不确定性增加，但SBI仍保持了主要后验结构。此外，SBI结合CPU和GPU资源，显著降低了计算时间：31天问题仅需60-70秒（单个GPU），而MCMC需约1000秒；201天问题中，SBI平均仅需157秒，而MCMC超过19,000秒。因此，SBI为机制性流行病模型的贝叶斯校准提供了一种快速、高效的框架，支持重复近实时推断和快速疫情分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用模拟基础推断（SBI）结合神经后验估计，对SECIR机制性流行病模型进行贝叶斯校准，利用德国2020年新冠ICU占用数据，在31天和201天两种推断窗口下与MCMC进行对比。通过Wasserstein距离、Kullback-Leibler散度和后验预测检查评估后验一致性，并比较计算效率。

Result: 在31天窗口中，SBI与MCMC后验分布高度一致，且能准确复现观测的ICU轨迹；在201天长周期重建中，尽管不确定性上升，SBI仍保留主要后验结构。计算效率方面，SBI在单个GPU上仅需60-70秒完成31天任务，而MCMC需约1000秒；201天任务中SBI平均157秒，远低于MCMC的超19,000秒。

Conclusion: SBI是一种快速、高效且可靠的贝叶斯校准方法，适用于机制性流行病模型的反复近实时分析，显著提升计算效率，支持快速疫情响应与决策制定。

Abstract: Mechanistic epidemiological models are widely used to support infectious disease forecasting and public-health decision making. Bayesian calibration of such models is commonly performed using Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), which can become computationally expensive for high-dimensional nonlinear systems and repeated near-real-time analyses. Here, we investigate simulation-based inference (SBI) using neural posterior estimation as a scalable alternative for Bayesian calibration of a mechanistic SECIR epidemiological model using COVID-19 intensive care unit (ICU) occupancy data from Germany during 2020. We compared SBI and MCMC across multiple epidemic phases using both 31-day inference windows and a substantially more challenging 201-day reconstruction problem involving multiple transmission change points. Posterior agreement was evaluated quantitatively using Wasserstein distances and Kullback-Leibler divergences together with posterior predictive checks. Across the 31-day windows, SBI recovered posterior distributions in strong agreement with MCMC while accurately reproducing observed ICU trajectories. In the 201-day setting, SBI preserved the dominant posterior structure despite increased uncertainty. SBI, by combining CPU and GPU resources, substantially reduced computational runtime compared with MCMC, which was restricted to running on CPUs. Whereas MCMC required approximately 1000 seconds for the 31-day inference problems, SBI achieved comparable posterior and predictive performance in approximately 60-70 seconds on a single GPU. For the 201-day inference problem, SBI required an average of 157 seconds, while the MCMC runs took over 19,000 seconds. Our results demonstrate that SBI provides a rapid and computationally efficient framework for Bayesian calibration of mechanistic epidemiological models, supporting repeated near-real-time inference and rapid outbreak analysis.

### [234] [Prompt Injection in Automated Résumé Screening with Large Language Models: Single and Multi-Injection Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27287)
*Preet Baxi,Jiannan Xu,Jane Yi Jiang,Stefanus Jasin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLM）在简历筛选中面临的提示注入攻击问题，即候选人通过微妙的自我推销文本影响LLM评分。实验表明，在简历质量相近且少数人进行操纵时，提示注入能显著提升排名；但随着更多人使用该策略，其效果迅速下降，普遍滥用时几乎失效。当候选人质量差异较大时，提示注入平均效果较差，但仍可能使低质量者超越高质量者，引发公平性担忧。总体而言，LLM筛选系统在操纵罕见且候选人间差异较小时最易被攻破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过受控实验评估提示注入对LLM简历评分的影响，分析不同候选人群体质量分布、注入比例等变量下的排名变化，结合定量数据与案例分析验证其有效性与局限性。

Result: 提示注入在简历质量同质化且注入人数较少时有效提升排名；但随着注入人数增多，效果迅速衰减，普遍滥用时失效；在质量异质场景下，虽整体效果减弱，但存在低质量候选人逆袭的不公平现象。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的简历筛选系统在操纵行为稀少且候选人能力差异小的情况下最为脆弱。为保障公平性，应警惕提示注入风险，并考虑引入对抗性检测或多样性评估机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to screen and rank job applicants, creating incentives for candidates to strategically manipulate algorithmic hiring systems. We study prompt injection in automated résumé screening, defined as subtle self-promotional text that introduces no new qualifications but is designed to influence LLM evaluations. Using controlled experiments, we show that prompt injection reliably improves applicant rankings when résumé quality is homogeneous and few candidates inject. However, its effectiveness rapidly diminishes as more candidates inject, collapsing when manipulation becomes widespread. When candidate quality is heterogeneous, prompt injection is less effective on average, but can occasionally allow lower-quality candidates to outrank higher-quality ones, raising fairness concerns. Overall, LLM-based screening is most vulnerable when manipulation is rare and candidate quality differences are small. Code and resources are publicly available at: https://github.com/preetb1199/Prompt_Injection_ACL26

### [235] [When Does Combining Language Models Help? A Co-Failure Ceiling on Routing, Voting, and Mixture-of-Agents Across 67 Frontier Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27288)
*Josef Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 多模型大语言模型系统（如路由、投票、级联、融合、混合代理）虽能提升准确率，但其增益受限于一个极少被报告的量——所有模型同时出错的比率（beta）。无论采用何种策略，准确率上限为1减去beta。传统的误差相关性指标rho无法捕捉beta，因为不同错误分布可能具有相同的边际和成对相关性但不同的全错率。通过Clopper-Pearson方法对beta的置信区间估计，可给出路由器、投票或级联系统在训练前的最大潜在增益。在67个来自21家提供商的模型中，单因子模型低估了全错尾部：开放数学题中观察到beta=0.052，而67模型高斯耦合模型预测为0.023，低估约2.5倍（90%置信区间1.7–3.4，k=17）。代码执行评分任务中beta=0.079。将GPQA-Diamond题目从选择题改为自由回答形式后，全错率上升至0.127，表明错误集中于答案格式而非主题。在相同质量下，低rho异质集成优于高rho Self-MoA；但在可验证任务中，仅当存在强查询级路由信号时，模型组合才优于最优单模型。真正增益源于模型在不同问题上失败，而非增加模型数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究关注通过多模型系统提升大语言模型性能，但忽视了一个关键限制因素——所有模型同时出错的概率（beta），该因素决定了系统性能提升的理论上限。传统评估指标如平均成对误差相关性rho无法有效识别这一风险，导致对模型集成潜力的误判。

Method: 使用统计建模与实证分析相结合的方法，包括基于高斯耦合的多模型联合错误分布建模（tetrachoric-calibrated single-factor model）、Clopper-Pearson置信区间估计、跨数据集（数学、代码、问答）的多模型实验对比，以及对不同答案格式（选择题 vs 自由回答）的影响测试。

Result: 在67个模型的实证数据中，所有模型同时出错的比率（beta）显著高于单模型模型预测值，尤其在开放性任务中表现突出。自由回答形式显著提高全错率（beta达0.127），说明错误模式受输出格式影响。在可验证任务中，多数情况下单一最佳模型仍优于集成系统，除非具备强查询级路由信号。低ρ异质集成优于高ρ Self-MoA。

Conclusion: 多模型系统的性能增益受制于所有模型共同出错的概率β，该值不可由传统相关性指标ρ准确反映。实际β远高于模型间简单相关性所暗示水平，且受任务形式影响。因此，模型集成的有效性取决于模型在不同问题上的互补性，而非单纯堆叠模型数量。未来优化应聚焦于识别并利用差异化的失败模式，而非盲目扩大模型规模。

Abstract: Multi-model LLM systems such as routing, voting, cascades, fusion, and mixture-of-agents are used to beat single-model accuracy. We show that their gain is capped by a quantity the field rarely reports. For any policy whose output is one member model answer, accuracy cannot exceed one minus beta, where beta is the rate at which every model is wrong on the same query. In contrast, the usual diagnostic, average pairwise error correlation rho, cannot identify beta: error laws with identical marginals and pairwise correlations can have different all-wrong rates. A Clopper-Pearson bound on beta gives a finite-sample certificate on the largest gain any router, vote, or cascade could deliver before training a router.
  Across 67 models from 21 providers, a tetrachoric-calibrated single-factor model still underprices the all-wrong tail: on open-ended mathematics, observed beta is 0.052 versus 0.023 under the full 67-model Gaussian copula, about 2.5 times underpricing, with 90 percent CI 1.7 to 3.4 and k equals 17. The effect recurs on execution-graded code, where beta is 0.079. Re-asking the same GPQA-Diamond questions in free-response rather than multiple-choice form reopens the tail, with beta 0.127 and a five-judge panel with kappa 0.73 to 0.92, locating co-failure in answer format rather than subject. At matched quality, low-rho heterogeneous ensembles beat high-rho Self-MoA, but on checkable tasks in our pool, combining models rarely beats the single best model without a strong query-level routing signal. Gains come from models failing on different questions, not from adding more models.

</details>


### [236] [Language-Based Digital Twins for Elderly Cognitive Assistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27334)
*Mohammad Mehdi Hosseini,Mohammad H. Mahoor,Hiroko H. Dodge*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于语言的数字孪生框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）结合风格特征和上下文元数据，模拟老年人的对话行为。通过多头条件变分自编码器（cVAE）评估其保真度与认知一致性，实验在I-CONECT数据集上表明该框架能有效保留个体特征，并在重建质量和认知评分预测方面表现优异，优于基线GPT生成结果，展示了其在个性化、连续性认知健康监测中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期检测轻度认知障碍（MCI）具有挑战性，而语言和对话模式是非侵入性生物标志物。现有方法难以实现个性化、连续性的认知健康监测，因此需要一种可扩展且非侵入性的新范式。

Method: 提出基于大语言模型的语言数字孪生框架，融合风格特征与上下文元数据以模拟个体对话行为；采用多头条件变分自编码器（cVAE）联合评估重建质量与认知状态预测能力。

Result: 在I-CONECT数据集上的实验表明，该数字孪生模型能有效保持个体特异性特征，重建误差和MoCA评分预测误差与真实数据相当，且显著优于基线GPT生成结果。

Conclusion: 语言基数字孪生为个性化、连续性认知健康监测提供了一种可扩展且非侵入性的新方法，具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: Digital twins have emerged as a promising paradigm for personalized healthcare, enabling modeling of individual behavior and health trajectories. In cognitive health, early detection of Mild Cognitive Impairment (MCI) remains challenging, where language and conversational patterns serve as non-invasive biomarkers. In this work, we propose a language-based digital twin framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to mimic the conversational behavior of elderly individuals by incorporating stylometric cues and contextual metadata. To evaluate fidelity and cognitive consistency, we introduce a multi-head conditional variational autoencoder (cVAE) that jointly measures reconstruction quality and predicts cognitive scores. Experiments on the I-CONECT dataset show that the digital twin preserves identity-specific characteristics and achieves reconstruction and MoCA prediction errors comparable to real data, while outperforming baseline GPT-generated responses. These results highlight the potential of language-based digital twins as a scalable and non-invasive approach for personalized and continuous cognitive health monitoring.

### [237] [Physics-guided Convolutional Neural Network for Domain Growth Prediction in Systems with Conserved Kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26128)
*Vijay Yadav,Madhu Priya,Manish Dev Shrimali,Prabhat K. Jaiswal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于注意力机制的物理引导卷积神经网络作为代理模型，用于学习受Cahn-Hilliard方程支配的二元混合物相分离的微结构演化。该模型在长时间滚动预测中保持稳定与准确，能精确捕捉域尺寸增长并符合Lifshitz-Slyozov域生长定律，且守恒混合物组成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解非线性偏微分方程计算成本高，亟需高效替代方法；现有深度学习代理模型在长期演化和物理一致性方面存在不足，因此需要一种兼具精度与物理约束能力的新框架。

Method: 设计了一种结合注意力机制与物理先验知识的卷积神经网络，利用物理方程（Cahn-Hilliard）指导网络训练，确保模型输出满足质量守恒与动力学规律。

Result: 模型在临界与非临界混合物条件下均实现长期稳定的演化预测，准确反映域尺寸增长行为，与理论预期一致，且保持成分守恒。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架有效建模具有守恒动力学的复杂系统，具备良好的泛化能力，可推广至其他多尺度动态系统建模任务。

Abstract: The spatiotemporal evolution of many physical, chemical, and biological systems is described by nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs). Recently, deep neural network-based surrogate models have gained increasing interest as efficient alternatives to computationally expensive traditional numerical solvers. In this work, we propose an attention-based, physics-guided convolutional neural network as a surrogate model to learn the microstructural evolution of such systems. We train the model to accurately predict the full time-evolution of phase separation in binary mixtures governed by the Cahn-Hilliard equation. We show that predictions from our trained surrogate model remain stable and accurate over long-time rollouts for both critical and off-critical mixtures and preserve the mixture composition throughout evolution. We also show that our model accurately captures the growth of domain size and is consistent with the Lifshitz-Slyozov domain-growth law. The prediction results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework for modeling systems with conserved kinetics and can be extended to other complex dynamical systems.

### [238] [\chisao{}: A GPU-Native Parallel Optimizer for Multimodal Black-Box Functions via Convergence-Anticonvergence Oscillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26164)
*Ira Wolfson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种新型GPU原生种群优化器Chisao，通过并行批量处理和收敛-反收敛振荡机制，在多模态函数优化中实现100%模式恢复，显著优于传统串行方法，在高维（d=64）下速度提升达39倍，且对噪声鲁棒，支持无梯度计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化方法如盆地跳跃、CMA-ES等为串行执行，难以利用现代GPU的并行能力；在高维多模态函数上表现差，且无法可靠发现所有模式。

Method: Chisao采用并行批量采样，结合收敛-反收敛振荡策略：真实峰值处的样本被冻结保留，其余通过动量驱动的反收敛与随机平滑梯度持续探索；通过'驱猴'和'金鸡'两种策略自适应重初始化以维持多样性。

Result: 在Simon Fraser大学优化基准套件全部42个函数上（维度d=2至64），Chisao实现100%模式恢复，而传统CPU方法在d≥8时失效；在Michalewicz (d=64)上速度提升34倍，在旋转超椭球函数上达39倍；即使存在高达σ=1.0的似然噪声，仍保持100%可靠性。

Conclusion: Chisao是一种高效、鲁棒、可扩展的无梯度多模态优化算法，充分利用GPU并行性，适用于复杂科学计算与贝叶斯推断场景，已开源发布于PyPI。

Abstract: Finding all modes of a multimodal black-box function is a fundamental challenge in optimization, Bayesian inference, and scientific computing. Existing approaches -- basin-hopping, CMA-ES, multistart gradient descent -- operate sequentially and cannot exploit the massive parallelism of modern GPU hardware. We introduce \chisao{} (\textbf{C}onvergence-\textbf{H}alt-\textbf{I}nvert-\textbf{S}tick-\textbf{A}nd-\textbf{O}scillate), a GPU-native population optimizer that runs an entire sample batch simultaneously and exploits a deliberate convergence-anticonvergence oscillation cycle to escape local traps while freezing confirmed modes. The structural move is asymmetric: samples that reach true peaks are frozen (``stuck'') and preserved, while the rest keep exploring via momentum-based anti-convergence and stochastically smoothed gradients. Adaptive reseeding via two complementary strategies (Repulse Monkey and Golden Rooster) maintains population diversity throughout. On all 42 functions of the Simon Fraser University optimization benchmark suite across dimensions $d \in \{2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64\}$, \chisao{} achieves \textbf{100\%} mode recovery where all CPU baselines collapse at $d \geq 8$ on the hardest multimodal functions, at up to \textbf{$34\times$} speedup over basin-hopping on functions where all methods succeed (Michalewicz $d=64$) and up to \textbf{$39\times$} on unimodal functions (Rotated Hyper-Ellipsoid $d=64$, pure GPU dividend). All benchmarks evaluate the objective by value alone -- gradients come from finite differences -- so the reported speedups are a derivative-free worst case. Under substantial likelihood noise ($σ_{\mathrm{noise}}$ up to 1.0), mode detection remains 100\% reliable. The algorithm is available as a standalone open-source Python package on PyPI.

</details>


### [239] [Implementation of reinforcement learning in chemical reaction networks: application to phototaxis as curiosity-driven exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26168)
*Ruyi Tang,Grégoire Sergeant-Perthuis,David Colliaux*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从最小认知视角重新审视单细胞藻类的趋光性，将其视为由信息驱动的感官运动过程。通过将部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）与生化反应动力学结合，构建了一个基于贝叶斯更新的内部状态模型，平衡趋光与探索行为，并用化学反应网络微分方程（CRN-ODE）实现。模型引入生物物理光感受机制和信息增益的多项式上界，利用逆强化学习（IRL）分析30条实验记录的衣藻轨迹，推断出与观测行为一致的行为目标。结果表明，该模型能有效再现趋光分布，性能接近标准随机模拟算法（SSA）基准。运行-翻滚交替被解释为一种信息获取策略：翻滚重新定向细胞以采样新感官配置，解决感知模糊性，揭示了细胞内生化网络如何支持适应性信息搜索行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统趋光性模型忽略生物体主动采样环境以减少感知模糊性的能力。本文旨在从最小认知角度，揭示细胞如何通过内在生化网络实现信息驱动的导航行为。

Method: 结合POMDP与生化反应动力学，采用记忆无损的贝叶斯更新建立内部状态模型；使用CRN-ODE实现动态演化；引入生物物理光感受机制与信息增益的多项式上界；通过逆强化学习（IRL）从实验轨迹中推断行为目标。

Result: 模型成功再现实验中的趋光分布，与标准SSA基线性能相当；运行-翻滚交替被解释为信息获取策略，证明了细胞内生化网络支持适应性信息搜索行为。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种融合信息论与生化动力学的细胞导航框架，揭示了运行-翻滚行为本质上是信息采集机制，为理解单细胞生物的认知基础提供了新视角。

Abstract: Living systems navigate environments using noisy and incomplete sensory signals. In unicellular algae, phototaxis is often modeled as a mechanistic run--tumble process driven by stimulus--response rules. However, such descriptions overlook how organisms actively sample their environment to reduce sensory ambiguity. From a minimal cognition perspective, we reframe this navigation as a subjective, information-driven sensorimotor process. To this end, we propose a framework linking a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) with biochemical reaction dynamics. Environmental variables are hidden, while the cell updates a minimal internal state from each observation through a memoryless Bayesian step. These internal dynamics balance orienting toward light with exploratory reorientation and can be implemented through Chemical-Reaction-Network Ordinary Differential Equations (CRN--ODEs). Our model includes a biophysical observation process for photoreception and a chemically computable polynomial bound on information gain. Using Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) on 30 experimentally recorded Chlamydomonas trajectories, we infer the behavioral objective consistent with observed phototactic motion and benchmark the resulting dynamics with standard Stochastic Simulation Algorithm (SSA) baselines. Our model reproduces the empirical alignment-to-light distribution, comparable to objective SSA baselines on this dataset. Within this framework, run--tumble alternation emerges as an information-acquisition strategy: tumbling reorients the cell to sample new sensory configurations and resolve sensor ambiguity, demonstrating how intracellular biochemical networks can support adaptive information-seeking behavior in cellular navigation.

</details>


### [240] [Neural Architecture Search for Generative Adversarial Networks: A Comprehensive Review and Critical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26169)
*Abrar Alotaibi,Moataz Ahmed*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对现有NAS-GAN方法进行系统性文献综述，按搜索策略（如进化算法、基于梯度的方法）、评估指标（如IS、FID及其他新兴指标）和性能表现进行分类与对比分析。

Conclusion: 当前NAS-GAN研究已取得显著进展，但仍面临评估标准不统一、跨数据集泛化能力不足等挑战。未来应发展更智能的搜索策略、构建标准化评估框架，并探索多模态与动态环境下的架构搜索方法。

Abstract: Neural Architecture Search (NAS) has emerged as a pivotal technique in optimizing the design of Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs), automating the search for effective architectures while addressing the challenges inherent in manual design. This paper provides a comprehensive review of NAS methods applied to GANs, categorizing and comparing various approaches based on criteria such as search strategies, evaluation metrics, and performance outcomes. The review highlights the benefits of NAS in improving GAN performance, stability, and efficiency, while also identifying limitations and areas for future research. Key findings include the superiority of evolutionary algorithms and gradient-based methods in certain contexts, the importance of robust evaluation metrics beyond traditional scores like Inception Score (IS) and Fréchet Inception Distance (FID), and the need for diverse datasets in assessing GAN performance. By presenting a structured comparison of existing NAS-GAN techniques, this paper aims to guide researchers in developing more effective NAS methods and advancing the field of GANs.

### [241] [KG-TRACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Mechanistic Grounding in Antimicrobial Resistance Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26179)
*Naman Garg,Sarika Jain,Sourav Yadav,Bharat K. Bhargava,Ghanapriya Singh,Abhishek Srivastava,Parimal Kar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KG-TRACE 是一种新型神经符号框架，将WHO突变知识图谱（KG）作为结构化生物学约束，融合基因组特征与基于RotatE的KG嵌入，通过学习的信念信任门动态权衡神经证据与符号生物学知识。在CRyPTIC结核分枝杆菌队列上，其对异烟肼的预测AUROC达0.9760，虽准确率竞争性强，但核心价值在于生物学可解释性。引入生物基础比率（BGR）量化神经归因与已有生物学的一致性，实现92.5%的符号覆盖，并通过‘不确定’标记识别多重耐药共现伪影，为临床提供可验证的审计路径，增强信任。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于全基因组测序（WGS）的抗生素耐药性（AMR）预测模型虽然精度高，但缺乏将神经网络归因结果与已知生物学通路进行关联的机制，导致临床可信度不足。需要一种能结合神经网络强大表征能力与符号系统明确生物学逻辑的框架，以提升模型可解释性与临床可用性。

Method: 提出KG-TRACE框架，利用WHO突变知识图谱（KG）作为结构化先验知识，通过RotatE算法生成知识图谱嵌入，并设计一个学习的信念信任门（epistemic trust gate），动态融合神经网络提取的基因组特征与符号生物学知识，实现神经与符号信息的协同推理。同时引入生物基础比率（BGR）作为评估指标，衡量神经归因与生物学通路的一致性。

Result: 在CRyPTIC结核分枝杆菌数据集上，KG-TRACE对异烟肼耐药性的预测达到AUROC 0.9760，性能具有竞争力；更重要的是，其92.5%的符号覆盖率表明神经归因高度符合已知生物学机制；同时，通过‘不确定’标签有效识别出多重耐药共现的人工假象，具备临床审计潜力。

Conclusion: KG-TRACE通过神经符号融合实现了对神经模型输出的生物学可解释性增强，不仅提升了模型透明度，还为临床决策提供了可验证的审计路径，推动了从‘黑箱预测’向‘可信赖医学辅助’的转变。

Abstract: While WGS-based AMR prediction has reached high accuracy, existing models lack a mechanism to ground neural attributions in established biological pathways. We present KG-TRACE, a novel neuro-symbolic framework that integrates the WHO mutation knowledge graph (KG) as a structured biological constraint on a neural genomic model. Unlike existing methods that learn statistical patterns in isolation, KG-TRACE fuses genomic features and RotatE-based KG embeddings through a learned epistemic trust gate, dynamically weighting neural evidence against symbolic biological knowledge.
  Evaluated on the CRyPTIC M. tuberculosis cohort, KG-TRACE achieves an AUROC of 0.9760 for isoniazid, achieving competitive accuracy while its primary value lies in symbolic grounding, not predictive uplift. More importantly, we introduce the Biological Grounding Ratio (BGR), a dataset-level metric that quantifies alignment between neural attributions and established biology. Our framework achieves a 92.5% symbolic coverage of isoniazid-resistant predictions and effectively identifies MDR co-occurrence artifacts by issuing laboratory follow-up flags for 'UNCERTAIN' cases. We demonstrate that neuro-symbolic grounding provides a verifiable audit trail for clinicians, bridging the gap between predictive accuracy and clinical trust.

</details>


### [242] [Necessary but Not Sufficient: Temperature Control and Reproducibility in LLM-as-Judge Safety Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26185)
*Hiroki Tamba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大模型作为评分器（LLM-as-judge）在安全评估中的可靠性，发现即使设置采样温度为0，评分结果仍可能不一致。实验基于日本AI安全研究所的开源评估框架aisev，发现默认温度为1.0导致相同输入在多次运行中出现高达50%的通过/失败波动；即使强制贪婪解码（top_k=1），仍有少数边界案例无法完全复现。此外，新版本模型如Claude Opus 4.7/4.8已弃用温度参数，使传统缓解方法失效。作者指出当前评估框架缺乏对评分器分歧的度量，易将噪声误认为安全特性，并发布可复现的测试数据集，建议将评分器一致性作为核心健康指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估框架普遍假设将大模型评分器的采样温度设为0即可获得确定性输出，但这一假设在实际安全评估中可能不成立，尤其当决策涉及部署准入时，结果不可靠会带来严重风险。因此有必要检验该假设的合理性并揭示潜在缺陷。

Method: 在开源安全评估框架aisev上进行实证测试，对比不同温度设置（包括默认值、0和top_k=1）下的评分结果，在两个大模型提供商、三种模型层级和五种采样配置下共执行690次API调用，分析通过/失败结果的重复性与分歧情况。

Result: 1. 默认温度为1.0时，相同输入在20次运行中单个样本的通过/失败分歧率可达约50%；2. 即使固定温度=0且使用贪婪解码，仍有1-2个边界案例在多次调用中结果不一致；3. 新版模型（如Claude Opus 4.7/4.8）已移除温度参数，使原有缓解手段失效。

Conclusion: 当前评估框架若仅报告单次运行结果而忽略评分器分歧，容易将随机噪声误判为系统性安全属性。应将评分器一致性视为关键健康指标，推荐在评估中引入方差和分歧度量以提升可信度。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge ("grader") components are now standard in evaluation harnesses, including safety evaluations where a pass/fail verdict may gate downstream deployment decisions. A widespread assumption is that setting the grader's sampling temperature to 0 makes grading deterministic. We test this assumption against a real safety-evaluation codebase (Japan AISI's open-source aisev) and show it fails on two levels. First, the harness invokes its grader without setting temperature or seed; the underlying provider silently applies its default of 1.0, so items near the decision boundary flip pass/fail across identical runs (per-item disagreement up to ~50% over 20 runs). Second, pinning temperature=0 reduces but does not eliminate flips: across 690 API calls spanning two providers, three model tiers, and five sampling configurations, 1-2 of 7 borderline items remain non-reproducible even under forced greedy decoding (top_k=1). Claude Opus 4.7/4.8 has since deprecated temperature entirely, rendering the primary mitigation inapplicable to newer model generations. These findings expose a structural gap: evaluation harnesses that report single-run verdicts without variance or grader-disagreement metrics can present noise as a safety property. We release a reproduction harness (690 calls, 7 conditions) and recommend that harnesses treat grader disagreement as a first-class health metric alongside the scores themselves.

</details>


### [243] [Clue-Guided Money Laundering Group Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26189)
*Boyang Wang,Jianing Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Clue2Group框架，通过线索引导的渐进式方法实现反洗钱调查中隐蔽犯罪集团的发现，结合局部上下文构建、多语义时空图神经网络与风险-结构-先验模式融合，显著提升实际调查流程中的可操作性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图异常检测方法仅提供节点级风险警报，全局群组发现方法被动搜索全网可疑群体，无法匹配分析师从具体线索出发逐步扩展调查的实际反洗钱工作流程。

Method: 提出Clue-Guided Group Discovery (CGGD)框架，通过构建紧凑的局部调查上下文，利用多语义局部-时间图神经网络估计线索条件下的局部风险场，并融合风险、结构和先验模式证据以恢复连贯的洗钱集团。

Result: 在两个大规模反洗钱基准数据集上的实验表明，Clue2Group能够有效支持以线索为中心的分析，显著提升对真实调查流程的适配性，为图分析研究与实际反洗钱工作之间架起桥梁。

Conclusion: Clue2Group为反洗钱调查提供了切实可行的线索驱动型分析框架，推动了图学习技术在实际金融犯罪侦查中的落地应用。

Abstract: Money Laundering Group Discovery (MLGD) aims to identify hidden criminal groups and recover their complete structures in large-scale financial networks. Existing graph anomaly detection methods mainly produce node-level risk alerts, while global group discovery methods passively search for suspicious groups over the whole network. Both are mismatched with real Anti-money-laundering (AML) investigations, where analysts usually start from a concrete clue and gradually expand the investigation to recover the responsible group. To address this gap, we propose Clue-Guided Group Discovery (CGGD), where a laundering group is progressively recovered from an initial clue set through analyst interaction. We further propose Clue2Group, a framework that first constructs a compact local investigation context to reduce noise and preserve chain-like and cycle-like laundering structures. It then estimates a clue-conditioned local risk field with a multi-semantic local-temporal GNN, and finally integrates risk, structural, and prior-pattern evidence to recover a coherent laundering group. Experiments on two large-scale AML benchmarks show that Clue2Group provides a practical clue-driven analysis framework for AML investigations, offering a feasible step toward bridging the gap between graph-based AML research and real investigation workflows.

### [244] [Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26192)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: FHPLF模型采用三方面创新：(a) 用二值梯度矩阵替代实值梯度，降低计算、存储与通信成本并增强隐私性；(b) 利用投影汉明距离建模相似性，提升二进制位的表达能力；(c) 提出安全二值梯度重装与隐私增强上传策略，减少用户交互泄露风险。

Result: 在四个真实数据集上的实验表明，FHPLF在准确性、效率和隐私保护之间取得良好平衡，优于当前主流的哈希学习与联邦学习方法。

Abstract: Hash Learning (HL) is an efficient representation learning approach that maps real-valued data into compact binary representations. Traditional HL methods typically require users to upload personal data to a central server, which is incompatible with increasingly stringent data security regulations. Federated Learning (FL) provides a decentralized paradigm for learning globally optimal models without centralizing private data. However, most FL methods rely on transmitting large-scale real-valued gradient information, leading to high communication overhead and potential privacy risks. Integrating HL into FL is a promising solution. Nevertheless, existing HL methods suffer from limited representational capacity of binary codes, which may degrade model accuracy. To address this challenge, we propose a Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor (FHPLF) model. FHPLF introduces three key innovations: (a) replacing real-valued gradient matrices with binary gradient-like matrices, significantly reducing computation, storage, and communication costs while enhancing privacy protection; (b) leveraging Projected Hamming Distance for similarity modeling, which captures the importance of individual binary bits to improve representation capability; and (c) proposing a Secure Binary Gradient Reassembly and Privacy-Enhanced Upload (SBG-PEU) strategy to further reduce the risk of user interaction leakage during transmission. Extensive experiments on four real-world datasets demonstrate that FHPLF consistently outperforms state-of-the-art HL and FL methods, achieving a favorable trade-off among accuracy, efficiency, and privacy preservation.

Early mitigation strategies, however, rested on fragile simplifications that limited their effectiveness in complex socio-technical environments. ### [248] [Fast LeWorldModel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26217)
*Yuntian Gao,Xiangyu Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Fast-LeWM 提出一种快速的潜在世界模型，通过将动作前缀作为基本预测单元，取代 LeWM 中重复的一步滚动预测。该方法在规划时可并行编码动作序列前缀并直接预测未来潜在状态，避免了逐步推理带来的累积误差和高计算成本。实验表明，Fast-LeWM 在多个任务上显著提升成功率并大幅降低规划时间，同时保持更低的开放环潜在损失，且随滚动时长增长，误差增长明显减缓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LeWM 在视觉规划中依赖自回归式的一步潜转移模型进行动作序列评估，导致计算开销大且随规划时长远距离产生累积误差。因此需要一种更高效、更准确的规划机制来提升性能并减少误差积累。

Method: Fast-LeWM 采用动作前缀预测机制，将候选动作序列的前缀进行编码，并并行预测执行不同前缀后到达的未来潜在状态。通过以前缀为单位进行监督，模型学习状态在不同动作组合下的连续演化规律，而非仅关注单步转移。规划时，利用编码后的最后一个前缀标记即可评估对应未来状态，无需显式模拟中间状态。

Result: Fast-LeWM 在多个任务中实现更高的平均成功率，显著降低规划时间，同时开放环潜在损失更低，且其随滚动时长增加的损失增长速度明显变慢，表明模型具备更强的长期预测能力。

Conclusion: Fast-LeWM 通过引入前缀级预测机制，有效解决了传统自回归滚动中的计算效率与误差累积问题，在保证高精度的同时大幅提升规划速度，是重建无关视觉世界模型在视觉规划任务中的重要改进。

Abstract: Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs), including recent LeWorldModel (LeWM), have become a promising foundation for reconstruction-free visual world models. For visual planning, however, LeWM evaluates candidate action sequences by repeatedly applying a local one-step latent transition model. This autoregressive rollout makes planning computationally expensive and exposes the predicted trajectory to accumulated latent errors as the horizon grows. We propose Fast LeWorldModel (Fast-LeWM), a fast latent world model that replaces repeated local rollout with action-prefix prediction. Given the current latent and a candidate action sequence, Fast-LeWM encodes its prefixes and predicts the future latents reached after executing those prefixes in parallel. By making action prefixes the basic prediction unit, Fast-LeWM directly models action effects accumulated to different extents over multiple horizons. This prefix-level supervision forces the model to learn how states continuously evolve under different action prefixes, rather than only fitting one-step state transitions. During planning, the predictor can use the last prefix token from the encoded action sequence to evaluate the corresponding future latent without explicitly rolling through each intermediate imagined state. Across multiple tasks, Fast-LeWM improves average success over LeWM while substantially reducing planning time, achieving lower open-loop latent loss whose growth becomes significantly slower as the rollout horizon increases.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DUI方法依赖于不切实际的假设，如需要训练昂贵的影子模型以及访问已知训练样本和确认未参与训练的分布内验证集，这使得它们难以应用于现代大模型和真实的数据所有权争议。

Method: 生成合成非成员样本，提取多样化的成员信号，将数据使用推断问题转化为混合比例估计问题，避免了对影子模型和真实验证数据的需求。

Abstract: How much of my data was used to train a machine learning model? Dataset Usage Inference (DUI) aims to answer this by estimating what fraction of a dataset contributed to a model's training. However, existing DUI methods rely on assumptions that rarely hold in practice: they require training expensive shadow models to imitate the target model, and they assume access to both known training samples and an in-distribution held-out set confirmed to be absent from training. These conditions make current approaches impractical for modern large models and real data ownership disputes. We introduce a practical DUI framework that removes these constraints. Our method requires neither shadow models nor real held-out data. Instead, it generates synthetic non-member samples, extracts diverse membership signals, and casts DUI as a mixture proportion estimation problem to estimate what share of the candidate dataset was used during training. Experiments on large image generative models show that our method reliably quantifies dataset usage, providing a practical tool for data owners to determine how much of their data was used to train a model.

Abstract: Symmetries are important for many deep learning tasks, ranging from applications in the sciences to medical imaging. However, there is an ongoing debate about whether to impose symmetry constraints on the neural network architecture (yielding equivariant neural networks) or learn them from augmented training data. Although equivariant networks are well-studied theoretically, much less is known about data augmentation, since analyzing augmentation requires control over the training dynamics. Inspired by recent results that show that augmented infinite deep ensembles are exactly equivariant, we study data augmentation for Bayesian neural networks (BNNs) trained with variational inference. We focus on variational distributions in the exponential family and derive conditions under which exact equivariance is reached. We furthermore obtain bounds on the equivariance error and introduce three novel symmetrization techniques which boost the effect of data augmentation in this setting. We conduct extensive numerical experiments which show that one of our symmetrization methods (orbit expansion) outperforms the baseline in both equivariance and overall performance. Our code is available at github.com/dmw1998/augment-BNNs

Conclusion: HRM适配器通过结合状态空间模型与平衡截断初始化，实现了高效的长序列建模，在参数效率和性能上均优于传统低秩适配方法，为长上下文任务提供了一种强有力的架构替代方案。

Abstract: While parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) typically targets attention projectors, its efficacy for tasks requiring sequential state accumulation remains under-explored. We examine if PEFT for such tasks can benefit from state space model (SSMs) adapters, and if MLP blocks are better injection sites. We introduce Hankel Reduced order Model (HRM) adapter, an SSM-based residual module initialized via Balanced Truncation of empirical Hankel Grammians. By leveraging the time-invariance of the system matrix $\bar{A}$, HRM enables an exact FFT-based parallel scan, achieving computational parity with LoRA across all context lengths. In iso-parametric evaluations on Mistral-7B (8.4M trainable parameters), HRM outperforms LoRA variants on LongBench tasks, including QuALITY (+34.8\% relative accuracy) and QMSum (+71.6\% relative ROUGE-1). HRM further demonstrates consistent superiority across 18 configurations of synthetic state-tracking (DFA, Parity) and character-level language modeling (enwik8). Gate analysis reveals that HRM adapters effectively learn to modulate recurrence, providing a robust architectural alternative to low-rank adaptation for long-context sequence modeling.

### [252] [The Red Queen Gödel Machine: Co-Evolving Agents and Their Evaluators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26294)
*Alex Iacob,Andrej Jovanović,William F. Shen,Daniel Burkhardt,Meghdad Kurmanji,Nurbek Tastan,Lorenzo Sani,Niccolò Alberto Elia Venanzi,Ambroise Odonnat,Zeyu Cao,Bill Marino,Xinchi Qiu,Nicholas D. Lane*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Red Queen Godel Machine (RQGM)，一种用于非平稳效用下的递归自我改进的进化框架，通过受控的效用演化实现评估与改进的动态循环。在可验证编码任务中，RQGM通过引入代理作为评审者的代码审查信号，在更少的token消耗下提升测试通过率；在科学论文写作、奥林匹克级证明与评分任务中，协同进化的写作者和评分者表现显著优于基线，且能有效对抗AI生成内容的过度接受问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自改进代理依赖静态评估标准，忽略了环境随自身演化而变化的现实，无法适应动态目标。本文旨在将进化中的适应性原则引入自改进过程，使评估本身成为改进的一部分，以应对不断变化的效用环境。

Method: 提出红皇后哥德尔机（RQGM），将搜索划分为固定评估标准的周期，在周期边界更新效用函数，确保每周期内自我改进的可靠性，并支持演化评价者、对抗性目标和动态效用。

Result: 在编码任务中，RQGM提升测试通过率，使用1.35x-1.72x更少的token；在论文写作与评审中，协同进化写作者的接受率提高1.78x-1.86x，评分者真实准确率提升9%；在对抗性场景中，能有效纠正基线评审器对AI生成内容的过度接受问题。

Conclusion: RQGM成功实现了在非平稳效用下的递归自我改进，通过动态评估机制突破了传统静态基准的局限，为复杂、动态任务中的智能体演化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Self-improving agents are state-of-the-art (SOTA) on agentic coding benchmarks and have recently been extended to general domains. However, their search methods generally assume a stationary evaluation criterion: a fixed verifier, benchmark, or labeled dataset that remains valid as the agent improves. This ignores a central feature of evolution: species adapt as their environments change with them. We aim to bring the same principle to recursive self-improvement, making evaluation part of the improvement loop and opening search to evolving evaluators, adversarial objectives, and dynamic utilities that may surpass static benchmarks. We introduce the Red Queen Godel Machine (RQGM), an evolutionary framework for recursive self-improvement under non-stationary utilities. The RQGM makes this possible through controlled utility evolution: search is organized into epochs with a fixed within-epoch evaluation criterion, while the utility can be updated at epoch boundaries, so self-improvement guarantees hold per epoch as the objective evolves across them. We begin by showing that even on verifiable coding tasks, the RQGM improves test pass rate over the prior SOTA by adding a complementary agent-as-a-judge code-review signal. This signal is cheaper and the RQGM uses 1.35x-1.72x fewer tokens. We then turn to scientific paper writing and reviewing, and Olympiad-level proof writing and grading, where the RQGM improves performance over prior self-improving agents: co-evolved writers reach 1.78x-1.86x higher acceptance rates under a diverse agent-as-a-judge panel, while co-evolved graders reach 9% higher ground-truth accuracy. In paper reviewing, the strongest baseline reviewer over-accepts AI-generated papers at up to 1.91x the human rate. The RQGM corrects this by introducing an adversarial objective that discovers reviewers equally stringent on AI and human work.

### [253] [High-Probability PL-SGD with Markovian Noise: Optimal Mixing and Tail Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26316)
*Dhruv Sarkar,Aprameyo Chakrabartty,Vaneet Aggarwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在马尔可夫梯度采样下，满足Polyak-Łojasiewicz（PL）条件的平滑目标函数的第一阶优化方法。针对轻尾情形，通过滞后阻塞法改进了普通随机梯度下降（SGD）的高概率界，首次实现了与期望界一致的$\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$量级，并证明该线性依赖于混合时间的界是紧的。对于重尾情形，在$ p \in (1,2] $的有限$p$阶矩条件下，提出一种全样本截断块方法，利用所有马尔可夫转移并抑制马尔可夫偏差，在总转移数$T$下达到$\widetilde{O}(σ_p^2(t_{mix}/T)^{2(p-1)/p})$的高概率误差，并给出匹配下界。整体上，本工作精确刻画了轻尾情形下混合时间的最优多项式依赖，以及重尾情形下的最优重尾指数和有效样本量依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轻尾情形下基于马尔可夫梯度的SGD方法存在高概率界与期望界之间的差距（$\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}^2/k)$ vs $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$），且缺乏对重尾情形的稳健分析。本文旨在填补这一理论空白，建立紧致的高概率收敛边界，尤其在混合时间与样本效率方面实现最优性。

Method: 针对轻尾情况，采用滞后阻塞技术构造统一高概率界；针对重尾情况，设计全样本截断块算法以充分利用马尔可夫链信息并抑制偏差。结合非平稳分析与低秩扰动技巧，分别推导上界与下界。

Result: 在轻尾情形下，建立了$\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/(k+K_0))$的统一高概率界，并证明其关于混合时间的线性依赖不可改进；在重尾情形下，提出了$\widetilde{O}(σ_p^2(t_{mix}/T)^{2(p-1)/p})$的高概率误差界，并给出匹配下界，揭示最优重尾指数与有效样本依赖。

Conclusion: 本文系统解决了马尔可夫梯度下PL优化的高概率收敛问题，首次实现了轻尾情形下混合时间依赖的紧界，并在重尾情况下确定了最优的重尾指数与有效样本依赖结构，为带噪声或非独立数据的优化提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We study first-order methods for smooth objectives satisfying the Polyak-Łojasiewicz (PL) condition when gradient samples are generated by an exogenous Markov chain. In the light-tailed setting, prior uniform-in-time high-probability bounds for ordinary Stochastic Gradient Descent (SGD) under a standard growth envelope scale as $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}^2/k)$, leaving a gap with the $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/k)$ expectation bounds. We close this gap using a lag-blocking argument to establish a uniform high-probability guarantee with a leading stochastic term of $\widetilde{O}(t_{mix}/(k+K_0))$ under geometric mixing. We prove this linear dependence on the mixing time is optimal via a matching $Ω(σ^2 t_{mix}/k)$ lower bound on a quadratic objective driven by a persistent two-state chain.
  We then extend this framework to heavy-tailed Markovian gradients satisfying a stationary finite-$p$-moment condition, $p \in (1,2]$. We design an all-samples clipped block method that uses every Markov transition while mitigating Markovian bias. Under a transition budget $T$, this algorithm achieves a high-probability stochastic error of $\widetilde{O}(σ_p^2(t_{mix}/T)^{2(p-1)/p})$. We establish a matching lower bound by reducing PL optimization to heavy-tailed mean estimation for a sticky Markov chain. Ultimately, this work tightly characterizes the optimal polynomial dependence on mixing time for light-tailed PL-SGD, and the optimal heavy-tail exponent and effective-sample-size dependence in the robust regime.

*Boyun Zhang,Chao Wang,Kai Wu*

Abstract: In actor-critic reinforcement learning, network architectures are typically manually designed. Automating this design is challenging because each candidate must be trained before evaluation, and the design space is open-ended. To address these challenges, we introduce EVOM, an agentic meta-evolution framework for discovering high-performance actor-critic architectures. We frame architecture search as a bi-level optimization: an inner loop trains weights via the low-fidelity proximal policy optimization (PPO), while an outer loop drives meta-evolution by iteratively refining architecture programs. Crucially, this outer loop is powered by an LLM-based design agent that operates purely as an architecture designer, completely decoupled from policy execution and environment control. Abstract: Reinforcement learning in large or sparse-reward environments suffers from slow temporal-difference reward propagation, as value information spreads only locally across the state space. We propose Mesh-RL, a spatial domain-decomposition framework inspired by the finite element method and domain decomposition theory, which partitions the environment into overlapping subgrids and enforces boundary-consistent temporal-difference updates. Such an approach enables localized learning while ensuring globally coherent value propagation. Unlike hierarchical or model-based approaches, Mesh-RL accelerates long-range credit assignment without modifying the reward function, Bellman operator, or introducing explicit planning mechanisms. We evaluate Mesh-RL on hazard-dense grid-world environments with varying geometries and mesh resolutions. Across Q-learning, SARSA, and Dyna-Q, Mesh-RL consistently improves convergence speed, cumulative reward, and learning stability. Higher mesh resolutions sustain exploration, prevent premature convergence, and substantially accelerate value propagation to distant states. While Dyna-Q already benefits from internal planning, it still achieves additional gains under structured decomposition. Overall, Mesh-RL introduces a principled spatial domain-decomposition mechanism for accelerating temporal-difference learning. Our framework bridges finite element method-inspired boundary-consistency techniques from scientific computing with reinforcement learning to improve sample efficiency in sparse-reward environments. We will release source code of the study.

### [256] [EMA-FS: Accelerating GBDT Training via Gain-Informed Feature Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26337)
*Yan Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出EMA-FS算法，通过指数移动平均（EMA）跟踪每特征分裂增益，仅对前K个高收益特征构建直方图，显著提升LightGBM训练速度。在中高维密集数据上实现最高2.61倍加速，并在保留率70%时提升AUC 0.11点。引入S-EMA-FS统一确定性与随机采样，兼容性好，代码简洁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如随机特征子采样不考虑特征预测能力，导致低效；需一种基于特征重要性的智能筛选机制以减少直方图构建开销，同时保持模型性能。

Method: EMA-FS通过维护各特征历史分裂增益的指数移动平均，动态筛选出高收益特征进行直方图构建，避免对低贡献特征重复计算；S-EMA-FS进一步引入浓度参数beta，实现从确定性选择到随机采样的连续过渡。

Result: 在500维合成数据上提速2.61倍，在IEEE-CIS欺诈数据集上达1.45倍加速；70%保留率下提升AUC 0.11点并提速1.34倍；稀疏数据无提速，因已优化空值处理。

Conclusion: EMA-FS及其变体S-EMA-FS可高效减少直方图构建时间，提升训练效率，且不影响模型性能，具有良好的兼容性和实用性。

Abstract: Gradient Boosted Decision Trees (GBDT), exemplified by LightGBM, spend a dominant fraction of training time -- typically 65-70% -- constructing per-feature histograms. Existing approaches such as random feature subsampling (feature_fraction) discard features without regard for their predictive utility. We propose EMA-based Feature Screening (EMA-FS), an algorithm-level optimization that maintains an exponential moving average (EMA) of per-feature split gains across boosting iterations and, after a short warmup, restricts histogram construction to the top-K features ranked by historical gain. Unlike random subsampling, EMA-FS is informed: it retains high-gain features while screening out low-gain ones. Operating at the per-tree level, it preserves full compatibility with LightGBM's histogram subtraction trick, requiring no changes to core routines.
  We evaluate EMA-FS on datasets spanning financial fraud detection, advertising click-through prediction, industrial quality control, and synthetic benchmarks, with feature dimensionalities from 29 to 968. On dense, moderate-to-high-dimensional data it achieves significant speedups: 2.61x on a 500-feature synthetic benchmark and 1.45x on the 432-feature IEEE-CIS Fraud dataset at 30% retention. At 70% retention it improves AUC by 0.11 points while delivering a 1.34x speedup. On extremely sparse data (Bosch, >90% missing) it yields no speedup, as LightGBM's sparse bin optimization already bypasses empty values.
  We further introduce Stochastic EMA-FS (S-EMA-FS), which replaces deterministic top-K selection with gain-weighted random sampling controlled by a concentration parameter beta, unifying deterministic EMA-FS (beta -> infinity) and random subsampling (beta = 0) in one framework. Both are implemented in ~120 lines of C++ across all six LightGBM tree learners and are fully backward-compatible.

### [257] [Does Aurora Encode Atmospheric Structure? Latent Regime Analysis and Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26361)
*Emma Kasteleyn,Ana Lucic*

LRP reveals the model focuses on 3D vertical structures consistent with the Great Storm of 1987. Perturbation tests show masking relevant regions degrades forecasts 3.31 times more than random masking, indicating Aurora captures meteorological coherence and vertical structure without explicit training.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Spatially pooled PCA to analyze latent space organization; layer-wise relevance propagation (LRP) to identify important input features; perturbation tests comparing degradation from masking relevant vs. random regions.

Result: The latent space is primarily structured by seasonal cycles, not extreme storms. LRP shows attention to 3D vertical storm structures (e.g., Great Storm of 1987). Masking relevant regions causes 3.31× greater forecast degradation than random masking.

Conclusion: Aurora learns physically meaningful meteorological coherence and vertical structure in atmospheric dynamics without explicit instruction, suggesting emergent physical understanding in ML models.

Abstract: ML foundation models are able to emulate atmospheric dynamics accurately and efficiently but operate as opaque ``black boxes''. We investigate the internal representations of the Aurora model using spatially pooled PCA and layer-wise relevance propagation (LRP). We find evidence that Aurora's latent space is primarily organized by seasonal cycles, whereas extreme storm events do not form a linearly separable cluster. LRP indicates that the model attends to features consistent with the 3D vertical structure of the Great Storm of 1987. Perturbation tests show masking relevant regions degrades forecasts $3.31\times$ more than random masking. These findings suggest that Aurora learns meteorological coherence and vertical structure without explicit instruction.

### [258] [SOLAR: AI-Powered Speed-of-Light Performance Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26383)
*Qijing Huang,Sana Damani,Zhifan Ye,Athinagoras Skiadopoulos,Siva Kumar Sastry Hari,Jason Clemons,Sahil Modi,Jingquan Wang,Aditya Kane,Edward C Lin,Humphrey Shi,Christos Kozyrakis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SOLAR 是一个自动推导并验证深度学习模型在目标硬件上理论最小执行时间（SOL）边界的新框架，支持 PyTorch 和 JAX 代码，通过 LLM 前端、确定性中间表示转换和分析后端实现多精度分析，可提供无错误的 SOL 边界，并用于性能头空间分析、优化机会识别、跨平台比较和硬件规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的 Speed-of-Light (SOL) 分析依赖人工推导，过程繁琐且易出错，难以与快速发展的模型开发同步。需要一种自动化、可验证的方法来高效获取模型在特定硬件上的理论性能上限，以指导软硬件协同优化。

Method: SOLAR 采用两阶段流程：首先使用大语言模型（LLM）前端将 PyTorch/JAX 源代码转换为可执行的仿射循环中间表示（Affine Loop IR），并通过输出对比验证正确性；其次将 IR 提升为 einsum 图，由分析后端计算未融合、融合及缓存感知的 SOL 边界。

Result: SOLAR 实现了对多种算子和语言的全面覆盖，生成的 SOL 边界经验证无违反情况，支持多精度分析，能有效揭示性能瓶颈和优化方向；在 KernelBench、JAX/Flax 模型和机器人工作负载上的实验验证了其在头空间分析、优化发现、跨平台探索和硬件规划等四类应用中的有效性。

Conclusion: SOLAR 成功实现了 SOL 分析的自动化与验证，显著提升了性能边界推导的效率与可靠性，为深度学习系统的软硬件协同优化提供了有力工具。

Abstract: How fast could a deep-learning model run on target hardware, and how far is today's implementation from that limit? These questions are central to software, hardware, and algorithm optimizations. Speed-of-Light (SOL) analysis answers them by computing a workload's theoretical minimum execution time on a given architecture. Yet deriving SOL bounds remains manual, error-prone, and disconnected from rapid model development. To close this gap, we introduce SOLAR, a framework that automatically derives validated SOL bounds from PyTorch and JAX source code. SOLAR leverages both generative and deterministic components in its flow: an LLM frontend translates any source programs into an executable Affine Loop IR, validated by output comparison; a deterministic flow lifts the IR into an einsum graph; and an analytical backend computes unfused, fused, and cache-aware SOL bounds. SOLAR provides comprehensive operator and language coverage, produces validated bounds with zero observed SOL violations, and offers multi-fidelity analysis that tightens bounds and surfaces optimization insights. We evaluate SOLAR across KernelBench, JAX/Flax models, and robotics workloads. These experiments demonstrate four use cases: headroom analysis at multiple fidelity levels, identifying optimization opportunities, cross-platform exploration, and inverse-roofline hardware provisioning.

</details>

Abstract: Pre-trained transformers have demonstrated remarkable generalization abilities, at times extending beyond the scope of their training data. Yet, real-world deployments often face unexpected or adversarial data that diverges from training data distributions. Without explicit mechanisms for handling such shifts, model reliability and safety degrade, urging more disciplined study of out-of-distribution (OOD) settings for transformers. By systematic experiments, we present a mechanistic framework for delineating the precise contours of transformer model robustness. We find that OOD inputs, including subtle typos and jailbreak prompts, drive language models to operate on an increased number of fallacious concepts in their internals. We leverage this device to quantify and understand the degree of distributional shift in prompts, enabling a mechanistically grounded fine-tuning strategy to robustify LLMs. Expanding the very notion of OOD from input data to a model's private computational processes, a new transformer diagnostic at inference time is a critical step toward making AI systems safe for deployment across science, business, and government.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种偏好条件的贝尔曼算子，基于切比雪夫标量化设计，通过证明其上界包络性质和单调收敛性，实现对帕累托前沿的覆盖，并支持从Q值估计中提取满足任意偏好的确定性策略。

Abstract: Real-world decision-making often requires balancing multiple conflicting objectives, a challenge that standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) frequently addresses by aggregating rewards into a single scalar signal. While effective for simple tasks, this approach often fails to capture the full spectrum of optimal trade-offs, known as the Pareto frontier. In this paper, we introduce a novel preference-conditioned Bellman operator, motivated from the Chebyshev scalarization, designed to compute deterministic Pareto-optimal policies for Multi-Objective Markov Decision Processes (MOMDPs). We prove that this operator satisfies an enveloping property, where the estimated value functions upper-bound the true Pareto frontier, and demonstrate that it monotonically converges to a coverage set of this frontier. Furthermore, we also show how to extract deterministic policies from these converged Q-estimates. This ensures the agent can recover a policy for any given preference, capturing the entire Pareto-optimal frontier while guaranteeing each synthesized policy remains approximately Pareto-optimal. Experimental results validate that our algorithm successfully recovers complex trade-offs, providing a solution for deterministic Pareto-optimal policy synthesis.

### [263] [Rethinking Training & Inference for Forecasting: Linking Winner-Take-All back to GMMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26424)
*Qiyuan Wu,Katie Z Luo,Bharath Hariharan,Wei-Lun Chao,Mark Campbell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究自动驾驶中的轨迹预测问题，指出现有模型虽采用条件高斯混合模型（GMM）进行建模，但训练时使用赢家通吃（WTA）损失函数导致模式概率不具信息量。作者提出两种后处理方法：测试时基于后验权重的合并策略和一步期望最大化（EM）更新，以软化硬分配，提升模式概率的合理性与稳定性，从而改善预测性能，无需重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轨迹预测模型在训练中使用WTA损失导致模式概率不具信息量，影响模式剪枝效果；其根源在于建模（GMM）与训练（K-means式硬分配）之间的不一致。

Method: 提出两种后处理方法：1）测试时对相近候选轨迹进行后验加权合并；2）通过一步EM算法将硬标签替换为软责任分配，共享邻近模式间的概率质量。

Result: 所提方法在多个WTA训练架构上均提升了模式后验的信息量和排序准确性，显著改善了位移预测指标，且无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了GMM建模与K-means式训练之间的根本矛盾，提出了轻量级、可直接应用的修正方法，使训练目标更契合推理需求，为轨迹预测提供了更合理的模式表示框架。

Abstract: Trajectory forecasting for autonomous driving has advanced rapidly, yet representative models often produce uninformative posteriors over forecast modes, causing problems for mode pruning. We trace this to a modeling-training mismatch: forecasters are typically modeled as conditional Gaussian mixture models (GMMs) but trained with a winner-take-all (WTA) loss that assigns each sample to its nearest mode. We argue that this K-means-like hard assignment (one-hot), while preventing mode collapse, is the source of uninformative mode probabilities: it over-segments the trajectory space, ignores relatedness among nearby modes, and yields assignment instability under small perturbations. Guided by this lens, we introduce two post-hoc treatments: (1) test-time posterior-weighted merging that aggregates nearby candidate trajectories; and (2) a one-step expectation-maximization (EM) update that replaces hard labels with soft responsibilities, sharing probability mass across neighboring modes. Across several WTA-trained architectures, these lightweight steps produce more informative, faithfully ranked mode posteriors and strengthen final forecasts on popular displacement metrics -- without retraining. Our analysis unifies recent design choices through a GMM-vs-K-means perspective and offers principled, practical corrections that better align training objectives with inference.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: DualEval采用潜变量模型-项目校准方法，将模型能力、项目难度与锐度共同建模于共享潜在空间，利用静态标签与人类验证的奖励模型评分进行联合估计。

Abstract: Current LLM evaluation relies on two complementary but often disconnected signals: static benchmarks with objective correctness labels and arena-style preference data that better reflect open-ended user interactions. We introduce DualEval, a latent model-item calibration framework that represents models and evaluation items in a shared space, jointly estimating model ability together with item difficulty and sharpness. Our evaluation uses 18 frontier LLMs, static benchmark labels, and reward-model scores validated against held-out human preferences for open-ended model responses. Empirically, our framework produces reliable and balanced model rankings, and its learned item-level profiles support downstream applications such as benchmark compression for sample-efficient evaluation and anomaly detection for contamination or outlier analysis. Overall, DualEval unifies static and arena-style evaluation through joint model-item calibration, producing model rankings and item-level diagnostics that support more sample-efficient, interpretable, and auditable evaluation pipelines.

### [265] [Embedding Foundation Model Predictions in Discrete-Choice Models with Structural Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26432)
*Yingshuo Wang,Xian Sun,Yanhang Li,Zhichao Fan,Zexin Zhuang*

TL;DR: 提出一种两阶段适配器，将基础模型的预测概率作为特征输入到多项式对数模型的效用中，通过最大似然估计与符号约束拟合结构系数，并在第二阶段引入小规模神经网络校正。该方法保证了边际替代率的数学可计算性，显著提升准确率并保持经济逻辑一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础模型在选择预测任务中虽有高准确率，但其预测常违背经济逻辑，如价格上升导致需求增加、支付意愿估计不合理或不可用选项获得非零概率。需要一种方法使模型预测既准确又符合经济原理。

Method: 两阶段适配器：第一阶段使用带符号约束的最大似然估计拟合多项式对数模型的结构系数；第二阶段冻结这些系数，训练一个小型神经网络对基础模型输出进行校正。

Result: 在三个数据集和两个基础模型上，平均提升6.4个百分点测试准确率，最高达12.8个百分点；保持100%成本单调性；时间价值估计落在已发表交通经济学范围内；在基础模型上下文缩减至10%时仍保持至少6个百分点的性能增益。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models achieve strong accuracy on choice prediction tasks, but their predictions often violate the economic logic those tasks require: raising a price can increase predicted demand, implied willingness-to-pay estimates are frequently negative or implausible, and unavailable alternatives receive nonzero probability. We propose a two-stage adapter that takes a foundation model's predicted choice probabilities as a precomputed feature and embeds them inside a multinomial logit's utility. In Stage 1, we fit the multinomial logit's structural coefficients by maximum likelihood with sign constraints; in Stage 2, we freeze those coefficients and fit a small neural correction operating on the foundation model's predictions. We prove that this composition exactly preserves the multinomial logit's marginal rate of substitution, so analytically computable value-of-time becomes a mathematical guarantee rather than an empirical accident. Across three datasets and two foundation models, the adapter gains 6.4 percentage points (pp) of test accuracy on average over the multinomial logit and up to 12.8 pp, maintains 100% cost monotonicity, and produces values of time within the published transportation-economics range on the transportation datasets. Performance degrades gracefully under foundation-model context restriction, retaining at least 6 pp of accuracy gain even at 10% of the original foundation-model context.
