*Jiading Gai,Shuai Zhang,Kaj Bostrom,Jin Huang,Vihang Patil,Haoyang Fang,Bernie Wang,Huzefa Rangwala,George Karypis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KernelPro是一个闭环多智能体系统，通过结合大语言模型（LLM）代码生成、硬件性能分析反馈和可插拔的瓶颈检测工具，自动完成GPU内核代码的生成、分析与迭代优化。其四大贡献包括：（1）语义反馈算子，将专家经验转化为可插拔的微剖析工具，将原始硬件指标转化为可操作的自然语言指导；（2）两阶段工具调用架构，基于屋顶线模型的瓶颈分类筛选执行特定分析工具，整合内核级（ncu）、指令级（SASS）和系统级（nsys）剖析；（3）领域适配的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS），包含渐进式扩展、非对称分支、日志奖励校准、死端剪枝和跨轮次学习记忆；（4）通过自主代码搜索在CUTLASS/CuTe代码库中直接生成CuTe源码。在KernelBench上，KernelPro在Level 1/2/3分别实现2.42x/4.69x/5.30x的几何平均加速比，达到各难度等级的最先进水平。在VeOmni的专家优化MoE训练内核上，优于手写Triton代码1.23倍，生成了从零开始的raw-CUDA+CuTe Hopper WGMMA内核。消融实验表明，每个组件均独立显著提升优化质量：微剖析工具（p < 0.0001 vs 原始指标）、MCTS搜索（相比贪婪策略几何平均提升26%，p = 0.004）、主动工具编排（提升23%，p = 0.035）。此外，KernelPro是首个在速度之外优化能效的CUDA内核编码智能体，在保持速度不变的情况下实测降低11.6%能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GPU内核优化依赖人工经验，效率低且难以适应复杂硬件特性。传统方法仅关注性能提升，忽视能效优化。本文旨在构建一个自动化、闭环、智能的内核优化系统，利用大语言模型生成代码，并结合硬件反馈与智能搜索策略，实现高效、可解释、兼顾能效的自动优化。

Method: KernelPro采用闭环多智能体架构，集成大语言模型（LLM）进行代码生成，结合硬件性能剖析工具（如ncu、SASS、nsys）获取运行时指标，通过语义反馈算子将原始度量转换为自然语言建议。采用两阶段工具调用机制，先由屋顶线模型识别瓶颈类型，再触发对应分析工具。使用领域适配的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）进行探索与优化，引入渐进式扩展、非对称分支、日志奖励校准、死端剪枝及搜索记忆以增强学习能力。最终通过自主代码搜索在CUTLASS/CuTe代码库中生成目标代码。

Result: 在KernelBench上，KernelPro在不同难度级别（Level 1/2/3）分别获得2.42x、4.69x、5.30x的几何平均加速比，超越现有方法。在真实场景的VeOmni MoE训练内核上，生成的Hopper WGMMA内核相较手调Triton代码实现1.23x加速。消融实验显示，每项设计组件均显著提升优化效果（p值均小于0.05）。此外，系统首次在保持性能不变的前提下实现11.6%的能耗降低，验证了其在能效优化方面的有效性。

Conclusion: KernelPro成功构建了一个闭环、自动化、智能的GPU内核优化系统，融合大语言模型与硬件反馈，实现了性能与能效的双重优化。其创新性设计在多个基准测试中达到或超越人类专家水平，展示了人工智能驱动的代码自动生成与优化的巨大潜力。

Abstract: We present KernelPro, a closed-loop multi-agent system that automatically generates, profiles, and iteratively optimizes GPU kernel code by integrating large language model (LLM) code generation with hardware profiler feedback and pluggable bottleneck detection tools. KernelPro introduces four contributions: (1) a semantic feedback operator that encodes expert heuristics as pluggable micro-profiling tools, transforming raw hardware metrics into actionable natural language guidance; (2) a two-stage tool invocation architecture where roofline-based bottleneck classification filters which specialized analysis tools execute, combining kernel-level (ncu), instruction-level (SASS), and system-level (nsys) profiling; (3) a domain-adapted MCTS with progressive widening, asymmetric branching, log-reward calibration, dead-end pruning, and search memory for cross-iteration learning; and (4) direct CuTe source-level code generation via autonomous code search over the CUTLASS/CuTe codebase. On KernelBench, KernelPro achieves geometric mean speedups of 2.42x/4.69x/5.30x on Levels 1/2/3, establishing state-of-the-art performance across all difficulty levels. On VeOmni's expert-optimized MoE training kernels, KernelPro achieves 1.23x over hand-tuned Triton by generating a from-scratch raw-CUDA+CuTe Hopper WGMMA kernel. Ablation studies demonstrate that each design component independently and significantly improves optimization quality: micro-profiling tools (p < 0.0001 vs raw metrics), MCTS search (26% higher geometric mean vs greedy, p = 0.004), and proactive tool orchestration (23% improvement, p = 0.035). Finally, KernelPro is the first CUDA kernel coding agent to optimize energy efficiency beyond the speed-only focus of prior systems, demonstrating an 11.6% measured energy reduction at matched speed.

</details>


### [267] [Finding the Time to Think: Learning Planning Budgets in Real-Time RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26463)
*Aneesh Muppidi,Firas Darwish,Dylan Cope,João F. Henriques,Jakob Nicolaus Foerster*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究实时强化学习（RL）中的决策延迟问题，提出一种可变延迟实时RL框架，允许智能体在每个决策点自主选择思考时间。为避免过度规划导致的僵化，作者引入轻量级门控策略来根据状态动态分配规划预算，在Pac-Man、Tetris、Snake、Speed Hex和Speed Go等任务中表现优于固定预算和启发式基线，并在跨GPU部署中实现良好迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实时环境中，环境会持续推进，智能体的决策延迟会产生代价。传统RL假设环境等待智能体决策，不适用于真实时间场景。因此需要设计能权衡决策质量与响应速度的机制。

Method: 提出可变延迟实时RL框架，通过训练一个轻量级门控策略来决定每个状态下的规划延迟时间，使规划预算随状态自适应调整，避免盲目延长思考时间。

Result: 所提方法在多个实时游戏任务中显著优于固定预算和启发式基线，且具备良好的跨平台迁移能力，可在不同GPU环境下稳定运行。

Conclusion: 通过引入状态依赖的规划预算选择机制，门控策略有效平衡了实时性与决策质量，为复杂实时系统中的高效决策提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Deliberating takes time. In real-time settings, that time is not free. Standard reinforcement learning (RL) sidesteps this as the environment waits indefinitely for the agent's decision. Instead, we study real-time RL environments where the environment progresses while waiting for the agent's action. Building on prior real-time formalizations, we introduce variable-delay real-time RL, where the agent chooses how long to deliberate at each decision point since the environment progresses. For the planning agents we use, the right delay is state-dependent, and naively planning how long to plan can paralyze the agent. We instead approach this setting by training a lightweight gating policy on top of a planner to select state-dependent planning budgets. Across real-time Pac-Man, Tetris, Snake, Speed Hex, and Speed Go, our gating policy outperforms fixed-budget and heuristic baselines, and transfers to a real-time setup where the environment and agent run on two different GPUs.

### [269] [Epiphany-Aware KV Cache Eviction Without the Attention Matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26472)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EpiKV提出一种新的基于epiphany score的缓存淘汰方法，通过直接从前向传播中读取模型内部表示的变化来评分token，避免了对注意力矩阵的依赖，无需训练、分类器或自定义内核，可无缝集成到FlashAttention推理栈中。该方法在4096令牌缓存下达到MATH-500的72%准确率，优于现有注意力基线；在8192令牌缓存下，经过滞后归一化的变体在AIME-2024上达到37%，是最佳基线的1.1倍，且速度提升达2.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出epiphany score，衡量模型内部表示的变化，直接从前向传播中获取，无需计算注意力矩阵，也不引入额外状态。结合滞后归一化与因果滚动z-score处理位置趋势，实现高效缓存淘汰。

Result: 在4096令牌缓存下，EpiKV在MATH-500上达到72%准确率，接近最强注意力基线（ThinKV 71%，H2O 67%）；在8192令牌缓存下，其滞后归一化变体在AIME-2024上达到37%，优于最佳基线（33%），推理速度最高提升2.8倍。

Conclusion: EpiKV提供了一种高效、无需训练且兼容现有推理框架的缓存淘汰机制，在长上下文推理任务中显著提升了性能与效率，为大规模推理部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: As reasoning models emit chains of thought tens of thousands of tokens long, KV cache increasingly becomes a deployment bottleneck. Existing cache eviction methods rank tokens by attention weight, which is a noisy importance proxy in long reasoning traces, and prohibits the use of fused kernels in production inference by forcing the model to materialize the attention matrix. In this work, we instead score tokens with a metric we term the epiphany score: the change in the model's internal representation, read directly from the forward pass with no attention matrix and negligible extra state. Our resulting cache eviction method, EpiKV, requires no training, classifier, or custom kernel, and can be used directly in FlashAttention inference stacks unchanged -- scaling to a 16x longer feasible context than attention-based scoring. upper-mid layers negatively) and remove a positional trend with a causal rolling z-score. At a 4096-token cache EpiKV reaches 72% on MATH-500, matching the strongest attention-based baseline (ThinKV 71%, H2O 67%); a lag-normalized KV variant reaches 37% on AIME-2024 at 8192 tokens against the best of them (33%), at up to 2.8x the speed.

### [270] [When Does Quality-Aware Multimodal Fusion Matter? A Leakage-Safe Diagnostic for Decision-Level Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26473)
*Jaden Moon,Arvind Pillai,Andrew Campbell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种简单诊断方法，检验多模态系统中可靠性评分是否真正影响模型决策。通过在测试时随机打乱可靠性分数，发现性能未下降，表明当前系统并未真正利用这些分数进行决策；而在可靠性信号能准确预测正确模态的对照实验中，性能显著提升，说明只有当可靠性信号与模态正确性高度相关时，才会影响融合决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态系统依赖各模态的可靠性评分来加权贡献，但尚不清楚这些评分是真正影响决策，还是仅与性能相关。需要一种方法验证其实际作用机制。

Method: 在模型训练完成后，固定模型和输入，仅对测试样本的可靠性分数进行随机置换，观察预测性能是否变化；通过对比真实场景与正向控制实验（可靠性信号可准确识别正确模态）的结果，判断可靠性信息是否被有效利用。

Result: 在StressID和CMU-MOSEI数据集上，置换可靠性分数后性能保持不变，即使存在通过选择最优模态显著提升性能的潜力；而在正向控制实验中，相同融合规则下性能明显改善，说明可靠性信息仅在能可靠预测模态正确性时才影响决策。

Conclusion: 当前多模态融合系统并未真正利用可靠性评分做决策，其有效性依赖于可靠性信号与模态正确性之间的强关联，而非评分本身。若要实现动态、智能的模态加权，需确保可靠性估计具有足够的准确性。

Abstract: Many multimodal systems estimate the reliability of each modality and weight their contributions to the final prediction. However, it remains unclear whether these scores influence model decisions or merely correlate with performance. We propose a simple diagnostic to test whether reliability information is used during inference. After training, the model and inputs are fixed while reliability scores are permuted across test examples. If predictions depend on these scores, performance should degrade. Experiments on StressID for stress recognition and CMU-MOSEI for sentiment analysis show that permuting reliability scores leaves performance unchanged despite substantial potential gains from selecting the best modality per example. In positive controls where reliability signals identify the correct modality, the same frozen fusion rules yield significant improvements, indicating that reliability signals influence fused decisions only when they reliably predict unimodal correctness.

### [271] [Localizing RL-Induced Tool Use to a Single Crosscoder Feature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26474)
*Andrii Shportko,Shubham Bhokare,Ahmed Zeyad A Alzahrani,Bowen Cheng,Gustavo Mercier,Jessica Hullman*

TL;DR: 该研究通过强化学习（RL）微调语言模型，揭示了其内部表征如何被重塑以实现代理行为（如工具使用）。研究提出“专用特征交叉编码器”（DFC），在48组超参数实验中发现，仅一小部分RL特有特征即可显著提升工具调用正确率（+31.1 ± 9.7个百分点），并使冻结的基础模型被动获得工具调用能力（+6.8 ± 5.0个百分点），称为‘能力溢出’。结果表明，通过DFC划分可将RL引入的能力集中于一个极小且可调控的特征集合，从而实现对智能语言模型运行时行为的无需重训练控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出专用特征交叉编码器（DFC），通过大规模超参数搜索（48组实验）分析语言模型在强化学习微调后的内部表征变化，利用编码-解码重建方法评估特征对工具调用性能的影响，并验证能力在冻结基础模型上的转移效果。

Result: DFC成功分离出一组紧凑的RL特有特征，使模型工具调用正确率提升31.1 ± 9.7个百分点；同时，在未重新训练的情况下，将工具调用能力传递至基础模型，实现6.8 ± 5.0个百分点的性能增益，即‘能力溢出’现象。

Conclusion: RL引入的能力可被压缩至一个极小且可调控的特征集，通过DFC划分实现了对智能语言模型运行时行为的高效、无需重训练的控制，为可控代理行为设计提供了新机制。

Abstract: Fine-tuning through RL reshapes the internal representations of language models to enable agentic behaviors such as tool use, yet the mechanistic basis of these changes remains poorly understood. While RL substantially improves structured tool-call generation, it is unclear which features emerge, which are preserved, and whether identified features can be leveraged for retraining-free behavioral control. In this work, we show that $\textit{Dedicated Feature Crosscoders (DFC)}$ isolate a compact set of RL-specific features that mediate tool-calling capability in $\texttt{Qwen2.5-3B}$. Across a $48$-crosscoder hyperparameter sweep, encode-decode reconstruction improves the RL model's tool correctness by $+31.1 \pm {9.7}$ pp and passively transfers tool-calling ability to the frozen base model by $+6.8 \pm 5.0$ pp which we call a $\textit{capability spillover}$. Our findings show that DFC partitioning concentrates RL-introduced capability into a minimal, steerable feature set that enables runtime behavioral control of agentic LLMs.

### [272] [Retrieval-Warmed Energy-Based Reasoning: A Five-Arm Ablation Methodology for Diffusion-as-Inference on Structured Reasoning Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26476)

The diagnostic decomposition is adapted from LLM-RAG evaluation \cite{ru2024ragchecker}. On \textbf{connectivity-2} (Erdős--Rényi all-pairs reachability), the aligned-vs-shuffled-oracle swing reaches \textbf{$+35$\,pp} balanced accuracy on a fixed 1{,}000-graph validation-set diagnostic, with value distribution and retrieval mechanics fixed, only per-graph alignment destroyed, while per-query random initialisation falls below cold -- per-graph alignment, not bias shift or stochasticity, dominates. The same diagnostic logic, stopped at the key-quality screen, applied to \textbf{Sudoku} with a task-specific key encoder produces a clean negative at a \emph{different} component -- key quality, under the current setup. The decomposition names the first blocking component on each task. The setting -- graph reachability refined by an iterative diffusion sampler, with explainability of failure modes as the lens -- places the work within structured and spatio-temporal reasoning.

### [273] [What Survives When You Compress a Recursive Reasoner for the Edge?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26488)
*Pearse Jim,Steven Kolawole,Opegbemi Matthias Busoye,Glory Bagai,Virginia Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在边缘设备上部署递归推理模型时，压缩对模型性能的影响。发现即使在极低精度（如INT4）下，局部预测能力仍可保持，但全局推理能力会完全崩溃。这种崩溃与模型架构有关，仅影响MLP混合型递归结构，而不影响注意力机制。通过引入无标签的“携带轨迹保真度”作为信号，可提前预测并修复此类问题。最终提出了一套部署方案：使用闪存流嵌入消除99.4MB瓶颈，单周期INT8实现全深度精度且计算量减少6倍（8MB片上内存），校准后的INT4可适配4MB微控制器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归推理模型虽参数少但需在边缘设备部署，面临压缩挑战；传统量化方法不适用于递归场景，因误差在循环中累积而非逐输出传播，导致标准压缩策略失效。

Method: 通过全精度扫描、多任务测试和双架构对比，分析不同压缩方式（如INT4剪枝、蒸馏、线性注意力）下的表现；引入‘携带轨迹保真度’作为无标签评估指标，用于预测推理路径破坏与恢复；采用通道级校准的INT4实现无需重训练的性能恢复。

Result: 在极端压缩下，局部准确率仍保持，但全局推理准确率降至零；只有基于通道校准的INT4能有效恢复全局推理能力；携带轨迹保真度可提前预测损伤与修复效果；所提方案显著降低内存占用与计算开销，实现高效边缘部署。

Conclusion: 递归推理模型的压缩需突破传统序列模型思维，关注全局推理路径的保真度；通过引入新评估指标和校准策略，可在极低资源下实现高性能部署。

Abstract: Recursive reasoning models can solve complex structured tasks with only a few million parameters by repeatedly updating a latent state. Deploying these models on edge hardware requires significant compression, but unlike conventional sequence models, quantization errors compound across recursive reasoning cycles rather than across output tokens. As a result, standard intuitions about compression fail to apply. In this work, we ask what survives when recursive reasoners are compressed. Across a full precision sweep, three tasks, and two recursive architectures, we find that aggressive compression preserves local prediction but destroys global reasoning: cell accuracy holds while puzzle-exact accuracy collapses to zero under naive INT4 pruning, distillation, and linear attention alike. Token-level objectives, including quantization-aware training, cannot repair it. The collapse is architectural -- it strikes MLP-mixing recursion but not attention on the same task -- and we reverse it with per-channel calibrated INT4 without retraining. We also introduce carry-trajectory fidelity, the cosine similarity to the full-precision reasoning path, as a label-free signal that predicts this damage and its recovery before a task evaluation. The combined result is a deployment recipe: flash-streamed embeddings remove a 99.4MB bottleneck, INT8 at one cycle matches full-depth accuracy at 6x fewer FLOPs (8MB SoC), and calibrated INT4 fits a 4MB microcontroller.

</details>


### [274] [Learning Probabilistic Filters with Strictly Proper Scoring Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26497)
*Eviatar Bach,Ricardo Baptista,Jochen Bröcker,Bohan Chen,Andrew Stuart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于合成数据训练的新型集合数据同化方法——合理评分集合滤波器（PSEF），通过基于能量得分等严格合理评分规则，利用变换器架构学习状态-观测轨迹的分析映射，实现对非线性、非高斯及多模态后验分布的准确逼近。理论证明在可实现假设下，其目标函数最小值对应真实贝叶斯滤波分布；数值实验表明该方法在复杂场景中优于经典方法与基于均方误差的目标学习方法，且根据问题特性可选择修正EnKF或端到端学习策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝叶斯滤波难以直接作为监督学习目标，尤其在部分观测和噪声环境下；虽然可通过预报模型生成合成轨迹，但如何有效利用这些数据训练出准确、鲁棒的滤波器仍具挑战。现有方法常依赖于高斯假设或均方误差损失，无法充分捕捉复杂概率结构。因此需要一种能基于合成数据、以完整概率分布为目标、具备强表达能力的新型学习型滤波框架。

Method: 提出PSEF方法：使用变换器结构构建一个置换不变的分析映射，输入为预报集合与观测值，输出为分析集合；训练基于严格合理评分规则（如能量得分），确保对整个概率分布的准确性进行奖励；理论上证明了在可实现条件下，真实滤波分布是最优解；通过均场一致性论证连接有限样本经验目标与总体目标。

Result: 在多种复杂场景（非线性、非高斯、多模态）下，PSEF能精确逼近真实滤波分布；相比经典滤波方法（如EnKF）和基于均方误差的机器学习方法，表现出更强的数据同化性能；对于接近高斯的问题，学习对EnKF的修正更优；而对于高度非高斯问题，端到端训练优于引入先验结构的方法。

Conclusion: PSEF是一种有效的基于合成数据的新型集合滤波方法，能够灵活适应不同统计特性，显著提升复杂系统中的不确定性量化与状态估计精度。其核心优势在于使用合理评分规则驱动训练，使模型学习到全局概率结构而非仅点估计，为未来智能数据同化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Bayesian filtering of partially and noisily observed dynamical systems seeks to infer the evolving conditional distribution of the state of a dynamical system, given observations, in an online fashion. This Bayesian filtering distribution is the natural object for uncertainty quantification, but it is rarely available as a supervised learning target. However, one can often use the forecast model to generate synthetic system trajectories, along with synthetic observations. We introduce the proper scoring ensemble filter (PSEF), an ensemble data assimilation method based on training an analysis map to approximate the filtering distribution using only synthetic state--observation trajectories. The analysis step is represented as a permutation-invariant, transformer-based map that takes as input a forecast ensemble and observations, producing an analysis ensemble. Training is based on strictly proper scoring rules -- with the energy score used in our implementation -- so that probabilistic accuracy is rewarded over the whole probability distribution. We prove that, under a realizability assumption, the population objective is minimized by the true Bayesian filtering distribution. We also derive the finite-ensemble empirical objective used in training and relate its single state--observation trajectory form to the population objective, using a mean-field consistency argument. Numerical experiments show that the learned filter accurately approximates challenging filtering distributions, including nonlinear, non-Gaussian, and multi-modal posteriors, and achieves stronger performance in data assimilation tasks than classical methods or learning-based methods with mean-squared-error objectives. For close-to-Gaussian problems, learning a correction to the EnKF is the best approach, while for highly non-Gaussian problems an end-to-end approach that discards this inductive bias is superior.

</details>


### [275] [Multipath Adaptive Gated Bottleneck Latent ODE with Raman Data Fusion for Cell Culture Process Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26520)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物制药生产中的细胞培养过程难以维持稳定，关键参数随时间漂移，传统方法往往在偏离规格后才察觉，无法及时干预。现有预测方法受限于稀疏、不规则采样数据，且不同细胞系与培养条件差异大，导致早期行为相似但后期走向不同的情况频发，亟需一种能应对异质性与不确定性的早期预测框架。

Conclusion: 所提出的自适应多路径预测框架有效提升了复杂生物过程的早期预测能力，尤其适用于参数漂移快、路径多样性高的生产场景。融合拉曼光谱数据显著增强了模型鲁棒性，为实时工艺调控提供了可靠支持。

Abstract: Mammalian cell-culture processes underpin the manufacture of many biopharmaceuticals, yet keeping a run on track is hard: critical process parameters drift over days, and an off-specification trend is often confirmed too late to intervene. Early-stage, multi-day forecasts could enable timely adjustment of feeding, sampling, and control, but bioprocess forecasting is challenging because measurements are sparse and irregularly sampled, operating conditions are heterogeneous across cell lines and media, and runs with near-identical early behaviour can diverge into different futures. We propose an adaptive framework combining a Gated Bottleneck Latent Ordinary Differential Equation (GB-Latent ODE) with Multi-Path Just-In-Time Fine Tuning (MP-JIT-FT). The GB-Latent ODE augments the stan dard Latent ODE with learnable variable-wise gating and a mask-aware bottleneck that compress high-dimensional sparse inputs, improving learning under limited data. Given a partially observed run, MP-JIT-FT retrieves similar historical trajectories, clusters the local neighbourhood into candidate regimes, and fine-tunes a separate model per regime to produce multiple plausible paths, each with a reconstruction-based confidence score, not a single averaged forecast. We further fuse Raman spectroscopy data: a machine-learning soft sensor turns dense Raman spectra into pseudo-observations that enrich the sparse offline measurements for more robust training. On 38 fed-batch 5L bioreactor runs spanning 14 conditions, MP-JIT-FT with Raman fusion achieves the best average rank and outperforms a global Latent ODE baseline on 8 of 9 target variables. Using local-divergence metrics, we show the multi-path gains are largest when locally similar prefixes diverge, whereas Raman fusion helps most when early dynamics are representative of later behaviour.

Abstract: Transfer learning improves policy learning efficiency by reusing knowledge from source tasks, providing a feasible paradigm for safe and efficient autonomous highway lane changing decision-making. Existing methods frequently encounter transfer mismatch induced by distribution shifts between source and target domains, leading to training oscillation and performance decline. Besides, target domain adaptation depends on exploratory interactions, which struggles to guarantee training safety in safety-critical lane changing cases. To tackle these limitations, this paper proposes a safe transfer reinforcement learning framework for autonomous highway lane changing. First, we design an adaptive teacher intervention mechanism based on instantaneous safety cost to restrain risky exploration and fade intervention strength progressively, with theoretical analysis on return bounds for mixed behavior policy. Experiments under varied traffic densities and validations on real-world NGSIM dataset reveal that our method surpasses baseline approaches by over 52.2% in safety and 5.0% in learning efficiency. ### [278] [CascadeFormer: Depth-Tapered Transformers Motivated by Gradient Fan-in Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26538)
*Huzama Ahmad,Cao Viet Hai Nam,Se-Young Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出两种提升深度Transformer效率的方法：CascadeFormer通过随深度减小宽度以匹配层间信息流的不均衡性，降低延迟8.6%、提升吞吐量9.4%，同时保持与均匀基线相当的困惑度；CascadeFlow Pruning基于累积训练梯度移除层，无需后处理分析，在困惑度和排名稳定性上优于传统启发式方法，且在下游任务中表现良好。作者提出梯度扇入不对称性（GFA）作为深层网络贡献递减的结构解释：在预层归一化残差堆栈中，每层梯度由恒等路径和所有下游功能路径求和构成，导致梯度扇入随深度线性衰减（深监督下为二次衰减），使早期层获得更丰富的梯度，后期层则更稀疏。实验验证了该理论在从零训练至12亿参数模型中的相关性和干预证据，并发现结构而非梯度幅值是瓶颈——等梯度范数无法恢复后期层价值，而通过参数共享重复增加下游路径可恢复并提升其贡献。梯度幅值是否在高秩情形外仍能代理扇入，以及在百亿以上规模下的行为仍是开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度Transformer中深层往往贡献有限，存在信息流不均现象，亟需高效架构优化方法。

Method: 提出CascadeFormer（渐变宽度设计）与CascadeFlow Pruning（基于累积梯度的层移除），引入梯度扇入不对称性（GFA）作为理论解释，并通过相关性与干预实验验证其有效性。

Result: CascadeFormer在相同训练预算下实现更低延迟（-8.6%）与更高吞吐量（+9.4%），且困惑度相当；CascadeFlow Pruning在困惑度和稳定性上优于标准方法，下游精度保持竞争力。实验支持GFA理论，揭示结构决定梯度分布，而非梯度大小。

Conclusion: 深层贡献下降源于梯度扇入不对称性，可通过结构设计与剪枝策略有效缓解；未来需探索超大规模模型下的动态机制。

Abstract: Deep Transformers are composed of uniformly stacked residual blocks, yet their deepest layers often add little value. We present two efficiency methods that exploit this asymmetry. CascadeFormer tapers width with depth to match the uneven information flow across layers, achieving comparable perplexity to a uniform baseline at the same training budget while reducing latency by 8.6% and increasing throughput by 9.4%. CascadeFlow Pruning removes layers using accumulated training gradients, with no post hoc analysis. It outperforms standard heuristics on perplexity and rank-stability and stays competitive on downstream accuracy. To motivate these methods, we propose Gradient Fan-in Asymmetry (GFA) as a structural account of why deeper layers contribute less. In Pre-LayerNorm residual stacks, the gradient at a layer is the sum of an identity path and all downstream functional paths, producing a gradient fan-in that decays linearly with depth (and quadratically under deep supervision), yielding richer gradients for early layers and sparser ones for later layers. We provide correlational and interventional evidence for GFA on models trained from scratch up to 1.2B parameters. Across Transformers and ResNets, accumulated training gradients follow the theoretical fan-in and are associated with post hoc layer importance. Two interventions point to structure rather than magnitude as the bottleneck: equalizing per-layer gradient norms does not restore late-layer value, while increasing downstream path counts via parameter-shared repetition restores and elevates it. Whether gradient magnitude proxies fan-in beyond high-rank regimes, and how these dynamics behave at the 100B+ scale, remain open questions.

</details>


### [279] [Can Large Language Models Reliably Code Qualitative Humanitarian Data? A Benchmark Study Against Human Expert Adjudication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26541)
*Jerome Marston,Tino Kreutzer,Salomé Garnier,Ella Boone,Phuong N Pham,Patrick Vinck*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过150个高保真度的合成人道主义转录文本，对比46个大语言模型（LLMs）与人类黄金标准在编码任务中的表现。结果显示，经过结构化提示和推理增强配置的多个LLM在可重复性上可达到与经验丰富的编码员相当的水平，但聚合可靠性指标不足以决定部署。模型在识别间接表达的需求、超出预定义类别的需求以及保护相关议题（如人身安全、歧视）方面表现不一。研究建议：LLM可显著扩展人道主义分析能力，但不能替代人类判断；应使用结构化代码本、推理增强模型，并针对特定主题关注性能差异，实施分层监督机制。对于敏感数据，自托管基础设施上的开源权重模型或为兼顾分析规模与数据治理提供可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人道主义组织需要及时、一致地解读受影响人群的复杂需求信息，但缺乏足够的人力、时间和专业技能来大规模分析这些定性数据。尽管大语言模型（LLMs）可能提升分析能力，但其在编码人道主义定性数据方面的可靠性尚未被直接验证，亟需系统评估以指导实际应用。

Method: 采用150个高保真合成人道主义转录文本作为测试集，对46个大语言模型进行评估。结合组间信度检验、Krippendorff's alpha系数、差异分析（区分正确、近似正确、错误编码），并基于人道主义特定标准（如歧视、复杂需求层级、非标准沟通方式）进行定性评估，全面衡量模型性能。

Result: 多个大语言模型在结构化提示和推理增强配置下，可实现与人类专家相当的编码可靠性。然而，模型在识别间接需求、非预设类别需求及保护性议题（如安全、歧视）方面表现参差不齐。单一聚合指标无法反映关键缺陷，存在部署风险。

Conclusion: 大语言模型能够显著提升人道主义数据分析的规模与速度，但不应取代人类判断。合理应用需依赖结构化代码本、推理增强模型、主题针对性监控和分层监督机制。对于敏感数据，推荐使用自托管的开源权重模型以保障数据治理。

Abstract: Data from affected populations are crucial for informing humanitarian response, but their value depends on timely and consistent interpretation of nuanced accounts of need. Humanitarian organizations often lack the staff, time, and specialist expertise required to analyze this information at scale. Large language models (LLMs) may expand this capacity, but their reliability for coding qualitative humanitarian data has not been directly established. This benchmark study compares 46 LLMs to a human Gold Standard using 150 high-fidelity synthetic humanitarian transcripts. Evaluation combined inter-rater reliability testing with Krippendorff's alpha, discrepancy analysis distinguishing correct, near-correct, and incorrect codes, and qualitative assessment across humanitarian-specific criteria including discrimination, complex needs hierarchies, and non-standard communication styles. The authors find that multiple LLMs can perform deductive coding at reliability levels comparable to experienced human coders, especially when structured prompts and reasoning-enabled configurations are used. At the same time, aggregate reliability metrics alone are insufficient for deployment decisions. Models varied in recognizing needs expressed indirectly, needs outside predefined categories, and protection-relevant concerns such as physical safety and discrimination. These findings suggest that LLMs can materially expand humanitarian analytical capacity, but not as substitutes for human judgment. Appropriate use requires structured codebooks, reasoning-enabled models, attention to theme-specific performance, and tiered oversight focused on categories where miscoding would have the greatest programmatic consequences. For sensitive humanitarian data, open-weights models deployed on self-hosted infrastructure may offer a viable path for combining analytical scalability with stronger data governance.

### [280] [Revisiting Action Factorization for Complex Action Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26574)
*Timothy Flavin,Sandip Sen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对多种因子分解方法（如独立网络、共享编码器、VDN、QPLEX、联合、自回归）在PPO、SAC、DQN三类算法上，针对离散、混合、连续三种动作空间的220种配置进行了系统性分析。提出了两个新的轻量级、兼容Gymnasium和PettingZoo的C++环境（CoopPush、Hybrid-Shoot），用于研究状态依赖的交互依赖问题。引入了VDN-PPO和PPO-MIX等改进版本，采用分支评论者机制提升多头PPO的信用分配能力，表现优于其他PPO因子分解方法。结果表明，分支双值架构在计算与性能间取得最佳平衡；自回归动作实现最高性能，而原生连续SAC虽性能更优但计算成本更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习框架虽支持复杂动作空间，但默认环境多为统一配置，缺乏对混合动作空间的标准化评估。已有的混合动作基准（如RoboCup HFO、SC2LE）多为重型或存档实现，难以进行广泛比较。本文旨在建立一个统一、可扩展的跨方法、跨算法、跨环境的混合动作空间评估体系，以揭示不同因子分解策略在真实场景中的有效性和效率差异。

Method: 构建三个动作空间（离散、混合、连续）与三类算法（PPO、SAC、DQN）组合的220种实验配置，涵盖独立网络、共享编码器、VDN、QPLEX、联合、自回归等因子分解方法。开发两个新轻量级环境（CoopPush、Hybrid-Shoot）以突出状态依赖交互挑战。提出VDN-PPO与PPO-MIX，通过分支评论者机制优化多头策略的信用分配。所有实验均基于兼容Gymnasium和PettingZoo的环境框架。

Result: VDN-PPO和PPO-MIX在所有测试中显著优于传统PPO因子分解方法；自回归动作在整体性能上表现最佳；原生连续动作的SAC在性能上领先于离散与混合方法，但需更高计算资源；分支双值架构在计算开销与性能之间达到最优平衡。

Conclusion: 在混合动作空间中，因子分解方法的选择对算法性能影响显著。自回归结构能实现最高性能，而分支双值架构在实际部署中更具优势。原生连续动作虽性能优越，但代价高昂。本研究提供了可复现、可扩展的评估框架与新环境，推动混合动作空间强化学习的标准化研究。

Abstract: Many real-world control problems involve hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces. For example, steering and signaling in autonomous driving, and aiming and firing in robotics or video-games. Despite real-world hybrid factorization and reinforcement learning framework support for complex action spaces (e.g., Gymnasium, PettingZoo, TorchRL, SeedRL, Mujoco, etc), the default environments within those frameworks often implement uniform action space configurations (LunarLander, Walker2D, Cheetah, SMAC, SUMO, Ant, Atari). Landmark hybrid-action benchmarks (RoboCup 2D HFO, SC2LE, Platform, CARLA, etc) are mostly heavyweight or archival implementations originating from papers which test one or a small number of competing factorization methods on one kind of control. This article provides a cross-sectional study of factorization methods [independent networks, shared encoder, VDN, QPLEX, Joint, Auto-Regressive] on each of three families of algorithms [PPO, SAC, DQN] across three action spaces [discretized, hybrid, continuous] over four lightweight environments [Platform, hybrid-LunarLander, Hybrid-Shoot, CoopPush]. Accounting for some invalid pairings such as joint-continuous, we are left with 220 configurations to analyze each method. We provide two new C++ parallel gymnasium and petting-zoo compliant environments [CoopPush, Hybrid-Shoot] to isolate particular challenges such as state-dependent inter-action dependence. Finally, we introduce VDN-PPO and PPO-MIX which use a branching critic to assign credit to multi-headed PPO. These variants out-perform all other tested PPO factorizations. Our results suggest that branching dueling architectures balance compute and performance most effectively, with Auto-Regressive actions reaching the highest performance overall and native continuous SAC outperforming discrete and hybrid algorithms, albiet both at increased computational cost.

### [281] [SharQ: Bridging Activation Sparsity and FP4 Quantization for LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26587)
*Haoqian Meng,Yilun Luo,Yafei Zhao,Wenyuan Liu,Huaqing Zheng,Xindian Ma,Peng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SharQ是一种无需训练的推理方法，通过在线稀疏-密集分解，将激活稀疏性与FP4量化结合，有效缓解了异常值主导和稀疏化损失问题。它在不依赖校准数据或重训练的情况下，在多个LLM模型上实现了接近FP16的性能，并在RTX 5090上实现2.2–2.4倍延迟降低和1.2–1.4倍吞吐提升，适用于语言和视觉语言任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代加速器支持低比特浮点格式和半结构化稀疏性，但将其结合用于大语言模型激活压缩面临挑战：激活中的输入相关异常值主导块尺度，影响FP4量化效果；直接应用N:M稀疏掩码会丢弃中等数值，导致稀疏化损失与量化误差耦合。

Method: SharQ提出一种在线稀疏-密集分解机制：为每个激活张量生成自适应的N:M稀疏掩码，提取异常值主导的稀疏主干，将其量化为FP4；同时定义相对于量化后稀疏主干的密集残差，而非原始未量化值。使用稀疏FP4 GEMM处理主干，密集FP4 GEMM补偿掩码带来的损失和量化误差。两者共享单一FP4权重负载，采用路径特定缩放视图，并通过融合预处理核函数整合掩码生成、残差构建和层归一化。

Result: 在Llama-3.1-8B、Qwen2.5-7B、Qwen3-30B-A3B和Qwen3-VL-8B上，SharQ在语言和视觉语言任务中恢复了NVFP4到FP16之间43–63%的精度差距；支持NVFP4、HiF4和MXFP4等多种格式，且无需重新训练或调参。在RTX 5090上，相比FP16实现2.2–2.4倍延迟降低，相比FP8提升1.2–1.4倍吞吐；结合SageAttention时，在视频生成任务中最高提速1.58倍。

Conclusion: SharQ成功实现了稀疏性与低比特量化在大模型推理中的高效协同，无需额外训练或调优，显著提升性能并保持高精度，具有良好的通用性和部署潜力。

Abstract: Low-bit floating-point formats and semi-structured sparsity are increasingly supported by modern accelerators, yet combining them for LLM activation compression remains challenging: activations contain input-dependent outliers that dominate block scales in FP4 quantization, and directly applying N:M sparsity masks discards moderate values, coupling sparsification loss with quantization error. We introduce SharQ, a training-free inference method that bridges activation sparsity and FP4 quantization through an online sparse--dense decomposition. For each activation tensor, SharQ generates an input-adaptive N:M mask to extract an outlier-dominated sparse backbone, quantizes it to FP4, and defines a dense residual relative to the quantized sparse backbone rather than the unquantized sparse values. A sparse FP4 GEMM processes the backbone while a dense FP4 GEMM compensates for both mask-induced activation loss and sparse-path quantization error. The two paths share a single FP4 weight payload with path-specific scale views, and a fused preparation kernel absorbs mask generation, residual construction, and layer normalization into one operator. SharQ requires no calibration data, retraining, or model-specific tuning. Evaluated on Llama-3.1-8B, Qwen2.5-7B, Qwen3-30B-A3B, and Qwen3-VL-8B, SharQ recovers 43--63% of the NVFP4-to-FP16 accuracy gap across language and vision-language tasks, and generalizes across NVFP4, HiF4, and MXFP4 formats. On an RTX 5090, SharQ delivers 2.2--2.4$\times$ latency reduction over FP16 and 1.2--1.4$\times$ throughput improvement over FP8 in language model serving, and up to 1.58$\times$ speedup on Wan2.2-T2V-A14B video generation when combined with SageAttention. Our code is available at https://github.com/actypedef/SharQ.

</details>


### [282] [Empirical Software Engineering TerraProbe: A Layered-Oracle Framework for Detecting Deceptive Fixes in LLM-Assisted Terraform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26590)
*Manar Alsaid,Chimdumebi Nebolisa,Faris Abbas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TerraProbe 是一个五层评估框架，用于检验大语言模型（LLM）在修复 Terraform 安全配置错误时的真实有效性。研究发现，仅依赖静态扫描工具（如 Checkov）判断修复成功会严重高估实际效果：尽管目标规则消除率高达 83.3%，但完整扫描通过率仅为 10.4%，Terraform 计划执行成功率仅 39.6%，且近七成修复为‘欺骗性修复’——表面通过自动化检测，实则未真正消除漏洞。该现象在 Gemini、GPT-4o 和 Claude 3.5 Sonnet 三类模型间无显著差异，且验证了四维欺骗修复分类体系的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 辅助修复评估方法仅以静态扫描结果消失作为成功标准，忽视了实际部署可行性、行为变化与安全意图的一致性，导致对修复质量的误判，尤其在 Terraform 等 IaC 场景中可能引入隐蔽风险。

Method: 提出 TerraProbe 框架，包含五个层次的验证机制：1）静态扫描清洁度；2）Terraform 规划执行成功；3）计划对比分析；4）人工审核；5）权限语义分析。应用于 68 个真实模块和 28 个注入缺陷模块，涵盖三种主流 LLM 生成的 288 个首次修复方案。

Result: 目标规则移除率达 83.3%，但完整扫描通过率仅 10.4%；规划成功率为 39.6%；计划对比可识别 38.5% 的变更；人类评审揭示 71.4% 的真实修复为欺骗性修复，且三模型间差异不显著（p > 0.10）。IAM 分析显示所有 9 个典型案例中通配符权限仍存在。

Conclusion: 单纯依赖静态扫描无法准确评估 LLM 修复的有效性。TerraProbe 提供了一套多维度、可复现的评估方法，强调必须结合规划、行为变化与安全意图来判断修复是否真正有效，避免虚假成功。该框架已开源，推动更可信的 IaC 安全自动化发展。

Abstract: Security misconfigurations in Terraform Infrastructure-as-Code are a growing risk in cloud deployments, and large language models are increasingly used as automated repair agents. Existing evaluations often treat a repair as successful when the targeted static-analysis finding disappears, without checking planning validity, behavioral change, or security intent. This paper presents TerraProbe, a five-layer oracle framework for evaluating LLM-assisted Terraform security repair. We apply TerraProbe to 288 first-pass repairs generated by gemini-2.5-flash-lite, GPT-4o, and Claude 3.5 Sonnet across 68 real-world TerraDS modules and 28 controlled injected-defect modules. The results show that targeted Checkov removal overstates repair success. Although targeted removal reaches 83.3 percent for the primary model, full-scanner cleanliness drops to 10.4 percent, Terraform planning succeeds for 39.6 percent, and plan comparison is reachable for 38.5 percent. Human adjudication further shows that 71.4 percent of plan-compared real-world repairs are deceptive fixes that pass automated checks while leaving the underlying vulnerability in place. This pattern is statistically indistinguishable across the three models, with deceptive-fix rates from 57.1 percent to 71.4 percent and pairwise Fisher exact p-values above 0.10. The paper introduces a four-dimensional taxonomy of deceptive fixes, validated with Cohen kappa of 0.78 and Krippendorff alpha of 0.76. IAM permission analysis confirms that wildcard Resource grants persist in all nine CKV2 AWS 11 deceptive-fix cases. TerraProbe contributes an evaluation methodology, a replication package, and the Multi-Layer Oracle Evaluation framework for distinguishing intent-aligned security repairs from scanner-passing false successes.

### [283] [Sketched Linear Contrastive Learning: Approximation, Optimization, and Statistical Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26617)
*Ziyan Chen,Zhongzhu Zhou,Ding-Xuan Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在配对高斯潜变量设置下，基于草图线性模型的对比学习的缩放定律。通过全批量经验梯度下降训练双线性对比得分，分析了高斯负二次对比代理函数在对齐幂律谱和对比源条件下的风险分解，包括不可约风险、近似误差、梯度下降偏差、梯度下降方差以及交叉项。交叉项受偏差和方差控制，不影响上界缩放。主定理给出了关于草图维度 $M$、样本量 $N$ 以及有效优化时长 $L_{\mathrm{eff}}γ$ 的显式缩放定律，揭示了对比学习中优化与有限样本噪声如何随模型规模、数据量和训练时间变化，为理解对比学习的缩放行为提供了首个理论基础，并指导模型、数据与优化计算之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对对比表示学习中的缩放定律理解有限，尽管已有理论工作建立了草图线性回归的缩放定律，但对比学习中需学习两视图间的交互作用，其优化和有限样本噪声的缩放机制与标准线性回归不同，因此亟需理论分析以揭示其内在规律。

Method: 在配对高斯潜变量假设下，构建草图线性模型，采用全批量经验梯度下降训练双线性对比得分；分析高斯负二次对比代理函数，在对齐幂律谱和对比源条件下进行风险分解，推导出包含不可约风险、近似误差、梯度下降偏差、方差及交叉项的风险表达式，并利用交叉项受偏差与方差控制的特性，建立显式缩放定律。

Result: 得到一个关于草图维度 $M$、样本量 $N$ 以及有效优化时长 $L_{\mathrm{eff}}γ$ 的显式缩放定律；发现对比学习因需建模两视图间交互，导致优化与有限样本噪声的缩放行为不同于标准线性回归，从而影响模型、数据与训练计算之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 本研究首次从理论上揭示了对比学习中的缩放行为，明确了模型大小、数据量和优化计算之间的相互影响关系，为设计高效对比学习系统提供了理论依据和实践指导。

Abstract: Scaling laws describe how learning performance varies with model size, data size, and compute. While recent theoretical work has established scaling laws for sketched linear regression, much less is understood for contrastive representation learning. In this paper, we study a sketched linear model for contrastive learning under a paired Gaussian latent-variable setup. The learner observes only sketched views of two correlated variables and trains a bilinear contrastive score by full-batch empirical gradient descent. We analyze a Gaussian-negative quadratic contrastive surrogate under aligned power-law spectra and a contrastive source condition, where we derive a risk decomposition into irreducible risk, approximation error, GD bias, GD variance, and a cross term. The cross term is controlled by the bias and variance and therefore does not affect the upper-bound scaling. Our main theorem gives an explicit scaling law with respect to sketch dimension $M$, sample size $N$, and effective optimization horizon $L_{\mathrm{eff}}γ$. Compared with standard linear-regression scaling laws, the contrastive setting must learn interactions between two views, and this changes how optimization and finite-sample noise scale with model size, data, and training time. This provides a first theoretical step toward understanding scaling behavior in contrastive learning and gives guidance for balancing model size, data, and optimization compute.

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have emerged as a powerful tool for decomposing superposed language model representations into sparse and interpretable features. However, training SAEs is computationally expensive, and available open-source SAE models remain limited. In this work, we introduce \textbf{Qwen3-Instruct SAE}, a comprehensive suite of SAEs trained on the Qwen3 instruction-tuned model family, covering Qwen3-1.7B, Qwen3-4B, and Qwen3-8B. For Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3-4B, we train layer-wise SAEs at three key activation sites: residual streams, MLP outputs, and attention outputs. For Qwen3-8B, we train SAEs on a subset of residual stream layers. Finally, we demonstrate the utility of Qwen3-Instruct SAE through a refusal-steering case study, showing that selected SAE features can causally steer instruction-tuned Qwen3 models toward refusal behavior. Our release provides a practical resource for studying sparse representations, feature-level mechanisms, and behavioral interventions in instruction-tuned language models

### [285] [From Weights to Features: SAE-Guided Activation Regularization for LLM Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26629)
*Evan Ning,Wei Xue,Dong Lou,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在激活空间而非权重空间进行正则化的方法，以应对大语言模型中灾难性遗忘问题。利用预训练的稀疏自编码器（SAE）作为单义特征字典，构建更精细的保护机制，避免传统EWC等方法因权重重要性估计过粗而导致的知识保护不精准问题。该方法通过约束优化推导出新损失函数，实现稳定性和可塑性的平衡，并证明EWC是其特例。相比基于回放的方法，本方法无需存储历史数据，仅需保留一个紧凑的特征掩码，具有更高的内存效率。在TRACE和MedCL基准上，该方法优于无任务特定结构的现有方法，且显著超越EWC等权重空间正则化方法。此外，实验证明大模型具有多义性特征：任务相关表示可在SAE特征基下线性可分，但在权重基下无法区分，表明权重空间保护缺乏概念层面的选择性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统权重空间正则化方法（如EWC）在大语言模型中表现不佳，主要因其对权重重要性的粗粒度估计无法有效隔离需要保护的知识。而大语言模型具有‘多义性’特性，即单个权重可能参与多个概念的表达，导致保护机制缺乏选择性。因此，亟需一种更精细、更具语义解释性的正则化机制。

Method: 提出在激活空间进行正则化，利用预训练稀疏自编码器（SAE）构建单义特征字典。通过约束优化推导出新的损失函数，使模型在更新时优先保持与任务相关的特征表示，同时允许其他部分灵活调整。仅需当前任务数据计算并保存一个紧凑的SAE特征掩码，无需存储历史数据。

Result: 在TRACE和MedCL持续学习基准上，该方法在不引入任务特定结构的前提下达到最优性能，显著优于EWC等传统权重空间正则化方法。实验还验证了多义性假设：任务相关表示在SAE特征空间中可线性分离，在权重空间中则接近随机水平，说明权重空间保护缺乏概念选择性。

Conclusion: 激活空间正则化结合SAE特征字典，能更精准地保护关键知识，克服大语言模型中灾难性遗忘问题。该方法兼具高效性与可解释性，为持续学习提供了新的范式，且无需依赖历史数据或额外网络结构。

Abstract: Weight-space regularization methods such as Elastic Weight Consolidation (EWC) are the standard approach to catastrophic forgetting in continual learning. However, those methods tend to underperform when applied to large language models. We argue that such underperformance can be partly explained by the ``polysemantic'' nature of large language models: per-weight importance estimates utilized by EWC-style regularization are too coarse and cannot isolate the knowledge that needs protection. In this paper, we propose regularizing instead in the model's activation space, using pretrained Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as a monosemantic feature dictionary. From the perspective of constrained optimization, we derive a new loss function that uses the SAE feature dictionary to explicitly balance stability and plasticity, and show that EWC is a special case in the one-sided weight-space penalty setting. Unlike replay-based methods that store or revisit examples from earlier tasks, our method requires no previous-task data after mask construction: current-task data is used to compute a compact SAE feature mask, and only this mask is retained for later training. Further, since the feature space has significantly lower dimensionality than the parameter space, the proposed method is more memory efficient. On the TRACE and MedCL continual learning benchmarks, the method achieves the strongest result among approaches without introducing task-specific architectural components, also surpassing traditional weight-space regularization methods like EWC. Beyond performance comparisons, we provide empirical evidence for the polysemanticity thesis: task-relevant representations are linearly separable in the SAE feature basis but indistinguishable from chance in the weight basis, and weight-space protection is nearly non-selective at the concept level.

</details>


### [286] [Target-Aware Bandit Allocation for Scalable Surrogate Optimization in Chemical Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26657)
*Mohammad Haddadnia,Yuvan Chali,Abhilash Jayaraj,Constance Kraay,Joana Reis,Felix Strieth-Kalthoff,Haribabu Arthanari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BOBa是一种基于博弈论的代理优化框架，通过将动作空间划分为多个分区并将其视为多臂赌博机中的“臂”，实现对计算资源的自适应分配，从而避免对整个大规模分子库进行完整的代理推断。该方法在保持探索性的同时，集中计算资源于表现更优的分区，显著提升样本效率。实验表明，结合乐观不确定性原则与合理的空间划分，可有效平衡筛选性能与代理推断成本，为超大规模分子库虚拟筛选提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在结构导向药物发现等场景中，从海量离散空间中高效识别高价值候选物面临巨大挑战，尤其是当分子库规模达到百亿甚至万亿级别时，传统的全库代理推断成为主要计算瓶颈。如何在有限评估成本下高效筛选高潜力分子，是亟需解决的问题。

Method: 提出BOBa框架，将动作空间划分为若干分区，每个分区作为多臂赌博机中的一个‘臂’，根据其潜在收益动态分配代理模型推断和实际评估的计算资源；采用乐观不确定性策略指导探索，确保不遗漏潜在高价值区域。

Result: 在真实合成按需库上的实验验证了BOBa的有效性：相比传统方法，显著降低了代理推断开销，同时保持甚至提升了筛选性能；揭示了筛选效果与代理计算成本之间的可调节权衡关系，支持在当前大规模库上开展实用化优化。

Conclusion: BOBa通过引入带奖励机制的自适应分区策略，实现了在超大规模分子库中高效、低成本的虚拟筛选，为未来更大规模药物发现提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Identifying high-utility candidates from massive discrete spaces under expensive evaluations is a recurring challenge across the sciences, with structure-based drug discovery as a prominent example. While surrogate-based optimization can increase sample efficiency by reducing the number of expensive evaluations, modern molecular libraries have reached billions to trillions of compounds, making full-library surrogate inference itself a major computational bottleneck. We introduce BOBa, a bandit-guided surrogate optimization framework that eliminates full-library inference by adaptively allocating computation across partitions of the action space. By treating partitions as arms in a multi-armed bandit, BOBa concentrates inference and evaluations on empirically promising partitions while maintaining principled exploration. Experiments on real-world synthesis-on-demand libraries demonstrate that optimism-under-uncertainty bandits, combined with meaningful action space partitioning, are essential for effective allocation of inference and evaluations. Our findings reveal a tunable tradeoff between screening performance and surrogate inference cost, which supports practical optimization over current libraries, and establishes a viable route to ultra-large library virtual screening.

### [287] [Zero-Shot Size Transfer for Neural ODEs on Sparse Random Graphs: Graphon Limits and Adjoint Convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26662)
*Mingsong Yan,Zhida Wang,Sui Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于图神经微分方程（GNDE）的连续时间图动态建模方法，通过在图神经网络中参数化神经ODE的速度场，实现了对图结构动态的高效建模。研究重点在于建立零样本规模迁移的理论基础，特别是在稀疏随机图上从图论（graphon）极限出发，定义了图论神经微分方程（Graphon-NDE）及其伴随系统，并证明了其适定性。理论分析表明，当图节点数 $n$ 增大且稀疏度参数 $\alpha_n$ 满足一定条件时，GNDE解以 $O((\alpha_n n)^{-1/2})$ 的速率收敛到图论NDE解，且该收敛具有高概率性质。同时，研究还建立了伴随系统在时间上的统一收敛性。对于训练策略，研究比较了离散化-优化（DTO）与优化-离散化（OTD），发现两者在欧拉离散化下渐近一致，状态和局部参数梯度误差分别为 $O(1/M)$ 和 $O(1/M^2)$。实验验证了理论预测的收敛速率，并展示了在四类图论模型上跨规模部署的零样本迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图神经微分方程（GNDE）虽具备在小图上训练、大图上直接部署的潜力，但缺乏对其零样本规模迁移能力的理论支持。尤其在稀疏图场景下，如何保证模型在不同规模图上的泛化性能尚不明确。本研究旨在建立一套定量理论框架，解释并验证GNDE在大规模稀疏图上的可扩展性和迁移能力。

Method: 研究采用图论（graphon）作为无限节点图的极限模型，构建图论神经微分方程（Graphon-NDE）及其伴随系统，分析其适定性；通过随机图生成模型（如HSBM和tent graphon），在稀疏条件下推导出GNDE解与图论NDE解之间的轨迹收敛速率；结合显式欧拉法进行离散化，对比分析离散化-优化（DTO）与优化-离散化（OTD）两种训练范式的一致性；最后通过合成图数据集进行实验验证理论结果。

Result: 理论证明了在稀疏随机图上，GNDE解以 $O((\alpha_n n)^{-1/2})$ 的速率收敛至图论NDE解，且伴随系统具有一致的均匀时间收敛性；在显式欧拉离散化下，DTO与OTD训练范式渐近等价，隐藏状态误差为 $O(1/M)$，局部参数梯度误差为 $O(1/M^2)$；实验结果支持理论预测的收敛速率，并验证了在四类图论分布上跨规模的零样本迁移效果。

Conclusion: 本研究首次为图神经微分方程的零样本规模迁移提供了严格的数学理论支撑，揭示了其在稀疏图上的可扩展性机制。理论与实验共同表明，基于图论极限的建模方式不仅具备良好的数学性质，还能有效实现跨图规模的模型部署，为未来大规模图学习系统的高效设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Graph Neural Differential Equations (GNDEs) model continuous-time graph dynamics by parameterizing Neural ODE velocity fields with Graph Neural Networks. Their local, size-independent filters suggest a zero-shot size-transfer principle: train on a small graph and deploy on larger, similar graphs without retraining. We develop a quantitative theory for this principle on sparse random graphs sampled from graphons. We consider Graphon Neural Differential Equations (Graphon-NDEs) and adjoint Graphon-NDEs as the infinite-node limits of the forward and adjoint GNDE systems, and establish well-posedness. For an $n$-node random graph with sparsity parameter $α_n$, we prove trajectory-wise convergence of GNDE solutions to Graphon-NDE solutions at rate $O((α_n n)^{-1/2})$, up to logarithmic factors, with high probability. We also establish uniform-in-time convergence bounds for adjoint systems governing hidden-state and parameter gradients. We further study discretize-then-optimize (DTO) and optimize-then-discretize (OTD) training. Under explicit Euler discretization with $M$ steps, we show that DTO and OTD are asymptotically consistent, with hidden-state and local parameter-gradient discrepancies of orders $O(1/M)$ and $O(1/M^2)$, respectively, up to sparsity and logarithmic factors. Experiments on HSBM and tent graphons support the theoretical rates, while zero-shot transfer experiments across four graphon classes demonstrate accurate deployment of learned GNDEs on larger independently sampled graphs.

### [288] [PersistentKV: Page-Aware Decode Scheduling for Long-Context LLM Serving on Commodity GPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26666)
*Muhammad Ahmed*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PersistentKV提出一种针对分组查询注意力（GQA）的原生块表解码注意力引擎和页感知调度策略，通过按KV头组映射任务、复用K,V块、支持原生页表及紧凑工作队列调度，有效减少空闲任务执行。在RTX 3060上，采用自适应策略在不同负载下动态选择FlashInfer或PersistentKV，在B8长上下文场景下吞吐提升1.063–1.265倍，特定场景达1.399倍，验证了调度策略对推理性能的关键影响。

Motivation: 当前自回归大模型服务受限于键值（KV）缓存移动而非密集矩阵乘法；现有分页注意力系统虽减少碎片化，但单一内核无法适配所有场景，尤其在低活跃度长上下文与混合序列长度时存在调度矛盾。

Method: 提出PersistentKV，基于分组查询注意力设计原生块表解码机制，支持跨查询头复用K,V块，引入紧凑工作队列调度，仅执行非空任务，并结合校准自适应策略动态选择FlashInfer或PersistentKV路径。

Conclusion: 工作分配策略（而非仅注意力算法）是影响大模型服务性能的关键系统变量，页感知自适应调度在长上下文场景中具有明确应用价值。

Abstract: Autoregressive large language model (LLM) serving is increasingly limited by key-value (KV) cache movement rather than dense matrix multiplication. Modern paged-attention systems reduce KV-cache fragmentation and mature kernels such as FlashInfer provide highly optimized native-paged decode attention. However, the best single-kernel implementation is not always the best serving schedule: low-active long-context decode can under-utilize commodity GPUs, while mixed sequence lengths introduce a tension between many exact-length launches and coarse padded batches. We present PersistentKV, a native block-table decode attention engine and page-aware scheduling study for grouped-query attention (GQA). PersistentKV maps work by KV-head group, is designed to reuse K,V tiles across grouped query heads, supports native page tables, and adds a compact workqueue schedule that executes only non-empty row-KV-head-sequence-split tasks. On an RTX 3060 with FP16, page size 16, Hq=32, Hkv=8, d=128, and identical correctness tolerance against FlashInfer, a calibrated adaptive policy selects FlashInfer for small active batches, PersistentKV sequence splitting for B1 long-context steps, and PersistentKV workqueue scheduling for B8 long-context steps. With thresholds and split counts fixed on calibration traces, one held-out trace seed improves synchronized wall throughput by 1.063-1.265x on B8 bimodal, uniform, and Zipf-like workloads and by 1.399x on a B1 bucketed trace. On the B4 bimodal boundary case, the policy avoids the PersistentKV regression by selecting FlashInfer. These results identify a concrete systems niche for adaptive page-aware decode scheduling and show that work assignment, not only attention math, is a decisive serving-system variable.

### [289] [Algorithmic Foundations of Deep Learning: Complexity-Theoretic Rates and a Characterization of Universal Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26705)
*Anastasis Kratsios,Simone Brugiapaglia,Bum Jun Kim,Gregory Cousins,Haitz Sáez de Ocáriz Borde*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出神经网络不仅是灵活的基函数，更是计算模型。通过将函数视为可由实值电路实现的问题，证明了神经网络的复杂性不仅由正则性决定，还受算法复杂性影响。研究揭示，只要包含非仿射非线性激活函数，满足自然并行化条件的任意定义良好的神经网络模型都是通用逼近器。理论应用于连续函数、Besov类、解析函数等，并展示其在模拟牛顿-拉夫逊法、幂迭代等数值算法上的能力；以k个顶点图的最短路径计算为例，通过编译热带动态规划电路，得到仅需O(log(1/ε))个非零参数的神经网络，相比传统方法的O(ε^{-c k^2})有指数级改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究将神经网络的表达能力归结为对最优基展开方案的拟合，但这种方法仅关注正则性，无法区分具有相似正则性但直观复杂度不同的函数（如平方根函数与典型布朗路径）。因此需要引入计算视角，从算法复杂性角度重新理解神经网络的表达能力。

Method: 将神经网络建模为实值电路，基于预设基本门语言的可计算性来分析其逼近能力。通过构造对应电路，将函数的计算过程映射到神经网络结构中，从而控制深度、宽度和非零参数数量。同时引入并行化条件，分析模型是否具备通用逼近性，并利用电路编译技术实现具体应用。

Result: 任何满足自然并行化条件且包含非仿射非线性激活函数的神经网络模型均为通用逼近器；对于特定函数类（如连续函数、Besov类、解析函数），可获得紧致的逼近误差界；在最短路径计算中，构造出非零参数数量仅为O(log(1/ε))的神经网络，显著优于传统的Lipschitz逼近方法。

Conclusion: 神经网络的表达能力不应仅从正则性角度理解，而应结合其作为计算模型的本质。算法复杂性是决定神经网络复杂性的关键因素之一。本理论框架为神经网络的通用逼近性提供了新的统一视角，并在多个实际问题中展现出精确性和优越性。

Abstract: Feedforward neural network (NN) expressivity is typically studied by emulating optimal basis-expansion schemes. While powerful, this perspective is incomplete: it primarily captures complexity through regularity, and therefore does not distinguish intuitively simple and complicated objects with comparable regularity, such as the square-root function and a typical Brownian path.
  The guiding message is that neural networks should be viewed not only as flexible basis functions, but also as models of computation. If a function is computable by a real-valued circuit over a prescribed elementary gate language, then it can be computed to comparable accuracy by an NN with explicit depth, width, and non-zero-parameter bounds controlled by the depth, width, gate count, and gate structure. Thus, neural-network complexity is not governed by regularity alone, but also by algorithmic complexity. We then show that any definable NN model satisfying a natural parallelization condition, allowing possibly multivariate non-linearities such as attention or layer normalization, is a universal approximator if and only if it contains a non-affine nonlinearity.
  The scope of our theory is illustrated by deducing universal approximation guarantees for continuous functions, minimax-optimal approximation guarantees for Besov classes, logarithmic-error complexity for holomorphic functions, and by showing that NNs can emulate numerical algorithms such as Newton-Raphson root finding and power iteration without architecture-specific arguments. Its precision is illustrated by shortest-path computation on $k$-vertex graphs: compiling the tropical dynamic-programming circuit yields NNs with O(log(1/ε)) non-zero parameters, exponentially improving in 1/ε over the generic $O(ε^{-c k^2})$ Lipschitz-approximation scale, for a constant c>0.

### [290] [HyperDFlash: MHC-Aligned Block Speculative Decoding with Gated Residual Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26744)
*Luxi Lin,Shuang Peng,Rui Ma,Junhao Hua,Shuwei Fan,Zhengda Qin,Qiang Wang,Hongjian Sun,Fangmin Chen,Songwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HyperDFlash 是针对 DeepSeek-V4 新提出的多超连接（MHC）架构设计的块并行推测解码框架。尽管 DeepSeek-V4 的原生多标记预测（MTP）模块在初始标记生成上表现良好，但其后期生成准确率因未验证中间标记的误差累积而显著下降，导致接受率降低。传统 DFlash 方法虽支持高效的单次遍历块草案生成，却无法无缝适配 MHC 架构，因其多路径残差流与常规草案设计存在特征错位。为此，本文提出两项模型对齐优化：一是采用预坍缩残差状态作为唯一条件信号，保留多路径结构信息，使草案器与目标模型的原始预测路径一致；二是用轻量级门控残差缩减器替代重型通用线性压缩器，参数源自内置超连接头，实现输入感知的路径聚合，参数量减少三个数量级，同时保持架构一致性。此外，通过在语言模型头施加针对性的 KL 散度蒸馏损失，强化早期训练阶段的预测质量。实验表明，HyperDFlash 在数学推理、代码生成和对话任务中均优于原生 MTP 和普通 DFlash 适配方案，在平均接受草案长度和解码加速方面均有显著提升，验证了 MHC 对齐、门控缩减和定向蒸馏的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DeepSeek-V4 的多超连接（MHC）架构虽然提升了初始标记预测性能，但其多路径残差流导致传统推测解码方法（如 DFlash）难以适配，且原生 MTP 模块在生成后期因误差累积导致草案准确率下降，影响接受率。因此需要一种能与 MHC 架构对齐、高效且高精度的推测解码框架。

Method: 提出 HyperDFlash 框架，包含两项核心优化：1）使用预坍缩残差状态作为唯一条件信号，保留 MHC 多路径结构信息，确保草案器与目标模型预测路径一致；2）引入轻量级门控残差缩减器，参数继承自超连接头，实现低参数量的输入感知路径聚合。同时采用针对语言模型头的 KL 散度蒸馏损失，提升早期训练阶段的草案质量。

Result: 在数学推理、代码合成和对话等多个基准测试中，HyperDFlash 均显著优于原生 MTP 和普通 DFlash 适配方案。在平均接受草案长度和解码速度提升方面表现突出，证明了所提方法在架构对齐、参数效率与预测质量上的有效性。

Conclusion: HyperDFlash 成功实现了对 DeepSeek-V4 的 MHC 架构的深度对齐，通过模型对齐优化、轻量化门控缩减和针对性蒸馏策略，显著提升了推测解码的质量与效率，为复杂架构下的高性能推测解码提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We present HyperDFlash, a block-parallel speculative decoding framework tailored to the novel multi-hyper-connection (MHC) architecture proposed by DeepSeek-V4. Despite the strong initial-token drafting performance of the native Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) module in DeepSeek-V4, its draft accuracy degrades sharply at later positions, as error accumulation from unverified intermediate tokens harms acceptance rates. Although the original DFlash method supports efficient one-pass block drafting, it cannot be seamlessly adapted to the MHC paradigm, since the multi-path residual stream of DeepSeek-V4 induces feature misalignment with conventional drafting designs. To resolve this mismatch, we propose two model-aligned optimizations for MHC residual streams. First, we adopt pre-collapse residual states as the exclusive conditioning signal, preserving multi-path structural information and aligning the drafter with the native prediction pathway of the target model. Second, we replace the heavy generic linear compressor with a lightweight gated residual reducer, whose parameters are inherited from the built-in hyper-connection head. This design yields input-aware path aggregation with three orders of magnitude fewer parameters while maintaining architectural alignment. We further enhance training via a targeted KL distillation loss applied to the LM-head, which regularizes predictions against the full target probability distribution and improves draft quality at early training stages. Experiments across math reasoning, code synthesis, and conversational benchmarks show that HyperDFlash consistently outperforms both the native MTP baseline and vanilla DFlash adaptation. It achieves substantial gains in average accepted draft length and decoding speedup, validating the effectiveness of MHC alignment, gated reduction, and targeted distillation for high-performance speculative decoding.

</details>


### [291] [Structure Before Collapse: Transient semantic geometry in next-token prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26749)
*Yize Zhao,Isabel Papadimitriou,Christos Thrampoulidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了在仅使用one-hot标签的训练条件下，语言模型如何仍能学习到潜在的语义结构。尽管神经坍缩理论预测模型表示会趋向于对称分布，忽略输入间的语义相似性，但实验发现语义几何结构在训练初期即出现，并且表示会按共享属性聚类。这种结构是暂时的，随着模型容量和训练时间增加，最终会过渡到对称状态。研究通过格拉姆矩阵分析揭示了这一相变过程，并提出对现有模型的初步改进以捕捉这种涌现的语义结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在仅使用one-hot标签的训练中，语言模型为何仍能学习到语义结构，解决神经坍缩理论与实际语义学习之间的矛盾。

Method: 设计三种合成控制场景，其中输入具有潜在语义因子但被映射到不同的one-hot标签；通过分析训练过程中的表示变化，利用格拉姆矩阵研究相变过程。

Result: 语义几何结构在训练早期出现，表示按共享属性聚类；随着训练深入，结构逐渐消失，模型进入对称状态。

Conclusion: 尽管one-hot标签导致语义共现信息稀疏，但梯度下降仍能自发形成语义结构，该结构是临时的，可通过改进模型捕捉其动态特性。

Abstract: Neural Collapse predicts that balanced one-hot classification pushes model representations to be equally far from each other; a symmetric configuration that depends only on the output label and ignores any semantic similarity in the inputs. This creates a puzzle: next-token prediction language models are trained predominantly (as context length increases) with one-hot labels: the same context is very unlikely to appear twice in training with different labels. However, they clearly learn latent structural features. That is, despite the one-hot training regime, a language model's contextual embeddings represent the fact that the next word in ''Mary broke the ___'' is likely to be filled by tokens in the latent classes of a) medium-sized, b) rigid, c) inanimate nouns. How does gradient descent find such categorical semantic structure when co-occurrence statistics collapse to one-hot sparsity, eliminating any shared next-tokens among different contexts? To investigate this tension we identify three synthetic controlled settings where inputs have latent semantic factors but are mapped to distinct one-hot labels. We find that semantic geometry emerges early in training, and that representations cluster by shared attributes despite receiving no explicit supervision to do so. This structure is transient: with sufficient capacity and time, the model eventually reaches the predicted symmetric state where all representations are equally separated. We study this phase transition through Gram matrix analysis and propose a preliminary modification to the commonly used unconstrained features model to capture the emergent semantic geometry.

</details>


### [292] [Batch-Invariant Spectral Intelligence for Robust and Explainable Insect Authentication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26757)
*Majharulislam Babor,Giacomo Rossi,Annalisa Altavilla,Oliver Schlüter,Marina M. -C. Höhne*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统近红外光谱在跨批次应用时因批次间变异导致性能下降，需可靠方法实现工业级昆虫物种认证，同时确保抗过敏、防掺假和合规性。

Method: 引入Batch-Invariant Spectral Network (BISN)，结合基于Savitzky-Golay滤波初始化的可学习预处理模块与熵正则化对抗训练，提前抑制批次效应，避免特征学习阶段受批次干扰。

Result: 在2,700个光谱数据上，BISN实现平均留一批次准确率0.93（标准差0.04），比最强基线提升4%；可解释性分析显示模型始终依赖脂质和蛋白质吸收区域，符合昆虫生化特性。

Conclusion: BISN有效解决了实际工业条件下昆虫物种认证中的跨批次鲁棒性与生物化学可解释性问题，具备推广价值，代码与数据集已公开。

Abstract: Edible insects offer an efficient source of alternative protein, requiring less land, water and emitting less greenhouse gas than conventional livestock. However, their successful integration into the food supply chain demands reliable species authentication to control allergen exposure, prevent adulteration, and meet regulatory standards. Near-infrared spectroscopy provides a rapid analytical tool, but its performance drops when applied to production batches unseen during training due to batch-to-batch variation in spectral measurements. We introduce the Batch-Invariant Spectral Network (BISN), an end-to-end framework that combines a learnable preprocessing module, initialised with Savitzky-Golay filtering, with an entropy-regularised adversarial objective to suppress batch-specific spectral variation. In contrast to Domain-Adversarial Neural Networks, which enforce domain adaptation only after feature extraction, BISN suppress batch-effects before species-specific features are learned. Using 2,700 spectra from three species (Acheta domesticus, Hermetia illucens, and Tenebrio molitor) collected across three independent production batches, BISN achieves a mean leave-one-batch-out accuracy of 0.93 (standard deviation 0.04), outperforming the strongest baseline by four percent. Further insights gained by using explainable AI confirm that model decisions consistently rely on the lipid and protein absorption regions across all folds, connecting predictive performance to known insect biochemistry. BISN addresses both cross-batch robustness and biochemical interpretability for automated insect species authentication under realistic industrial conditions. The source code and dataset are publicly available at https://github.com/majharB/bisn.

### [293] [Escaping Iterative Parameter-Space Noise: Differentially Private Learning with a Hypernetwork](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26772)
*Naoki Nishikawa,Shokichi Takakura,Satoshi Hasegawa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的差分隐私（DP）学习框架，避免在参数空间中进行迭代优化。该方法使用超网络从私有数据集生成目标模型参数，仅在低维数据表示上注入一次隐私噪声，显著降低噪声对模型性能的负面影响。理论分析和实验表明，在相同隐私预算下，该方法比DP-SGD等传统方法具有更高的模型效用，尤其在扩散模型的LoRA微调任务中表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有差分隐私训练方法（如DP-SGD）需在训练过程中反复向高维参数空间注入大量噪声，导致模型性能下降。为缓解这一问题，亟需一种减少噪声累积、提升隐私-效用权衡的新方法。

Method: 提出基于超网络的单次噪声注入框架：将每个样本映射到低维嵌入，聚合并扰动得到差分隐私的嵌入表示，再由超网络生成目标模型参数。整个过程仅在低维嵌入阶段注入一次隐私噪声，避免了参数空间中的多次噪声叠加。

Result: 在合成设置下，所提方法在固定隐私预算下实现更高模型效用；在扩散模型的LoRA微调任务中，相比DP-SGD及其他公共数据引导方法，取得更低的FID分数，表明其在真实场景中具有更强的实用性与优越性。

Conclusion: 所提出的单次噪声注入框架有效降低了差分隐私训练中的噪声影响，显著提升了模型效用，为隐私保护下的神经网络训练提供了一种高效且实用的新范式。

Abstract: Differentially private (DP) training of neural networks is often hindered by the large amount of noise required by gradient-based methods such as DP-SGD, which repeatedly inject high-dimensional noise in parameter space throughout training. In this paper, we propose a new framework for DP learning that avoids iterative optimization in parameter space. Instead of updating the target model using privatized gradients, we employ a hypernetwork trained on public datasets to map a private dataset to the parameters of the target model. Specifically, each example is embedded into a low-dimensional representation, the embeddings are aggregated and perturbed to obtain a DP dataset embedding, and the hypernetwork generates the target model parameters from this noisy embedding. Because privacy noise is injected only once into a low-dimensional dataset representation, our approach can significantly reduce the adverse effect of noise. We theoretically show in a synthetic setting that, under a fixed privacy budget, models produced by our approach achieve higher utility than those trained with DP-SGD. Moreover, we apply our approach to LoRA fine-tuning of diffusion models and show that it achieves lower FID than LoRA models trained with DP-SGD and other public-data-guided methods.

### [294] [Reproducibility Study of "AlphaEdit: Null-Space Constrained Knowledge Editing for Language Models"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26783)
*Ananth K S,Arya Hariharan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AlphaEdit, a null-space constrained projection method for knowledge editing, is successfully reproduced on original models but shows discrepancies in fluency and consistency metrics. Its advantages do not generalize uniformly to newer architectures due to violated architectural assumptions. Performance degrades under high edit counts, indicating bounded protection against catastrophic forgetting. Extended evaluations reveal declines in downstream task performance and safety-related refusal behavior with large-scale editing.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To validate the reproducibility and generalizability of AlphaEdit, a knowledge editing method claiming theoretical guarantees against catastrophic forgetting, and to assess its performance under extended editing scales and diverse model architectures and benchmarks.

Method: Reproduction of AlphaEdit under original setup, extension to new models (e.g., newer architectures), evaluation across additional benchmarks (BoolQ, HellaSwag, XSTest), and stress-testing with significantly increased sequential edits.

Result: Original results are largely reproduced, though fluency and consistency metrics differ. AlphaEdit's benefits diminish in newer models. Performance degrades with higher edit counts, affecting both general competence and safety behaviors.

Conclusion: AlphaEdit performs as reported within its original scope, but its theoretical guarantees are sensitive to model architecture and editing scale, limiting its practical deployment in large-scale or diverse settings.

Abstract: Fang et al. (2025) introduced a null-space constrained projection, named AlphaEdit, for locate-then-edit knowledge editing methods, theoretically guaranteeing that edits do not disrupt previously preserved knowledge, and reports substantial gains over existing editing methods on LLaMA3, GPT2-XL, and GPT-J. In this work, we present a reproducibility study of AlphaEdit, reproducing its reported results under the original experimental setup and extending the evaluation along three axes: new model architectures, additional downstream benchmarks, and substantially longer sequential editing horizons. We successfully reproduce AlphaEdit's reported metrics across the original models, though we identify a discrepancy in the reported fluency and consistency metric. Extending AlphaEdit to newer model families, we find that its advantage does not generalize uniformly, which we trace to architectural assumptions in the locate-then-edit paradigm that are violated by these newer models. We further stress-test AlphaEdit's central sequential-editing claim by extending the number of edits well beyond those evaluated in the original paper, and find that performance, which is stable at the originally reported scale, degrades as edits reach a much higher count, indicating that the null-space projection's protection against catastrophic forgetting is bounded rather than unconditional. Finally, we extend evaluation of edited models on three extra benchmarks, namely, BoolQ, HellaSwag, and XSTest, and we find that large-scale sequential editing degrades both general downstream task competence and safety-relevant refusal behavior. Our results confirm that AlphaEdit performs as reported within its original scope, while showing that its core theoretical guarantees are sensitive to model architecture and editing scale in ways that have practical implications for its deployment.

### [295] [AIGP: An LLM-Based Framework for Long-Term Value Alignment in E-Commerce Pricing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26787)
*Chennan Ma,Yanning Zhang,Siqi Hong,Xiuchong Wang,Fei Xiao,Keping Yang*

Abstract: Traditional dynamic pricing models in large-scale e-commerce suffer from limited interpretability, poor utilization of unstructured information, and misalignment with long-term business objectives such as cumulative Gross Merchandise Value (GMV), Return on Investment (ROI) and milestone achievement. We propose AIGP, a novel framework that leverages a Large Language Model (LLM) prompted with domain knowledge, structured data and textual context to make interpretable, knowledge-aware pricing decisions. For efficient deployment while maintaining high-quality outputs, we employ supervised fine-tuning for knowledge distillation. Central to AIGP is the Long-Term Value Estimator (LTVE), trained via offline reinforcement learning on historical data, which serves as a reward model to score candidate pricing actions and select preference pairs for Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), thereby aligning the pricing policy with long-term business objectives. Extensive offline evaluations and large-scale online A/B tests on Tao Factory demonstrate that AIGP achieves significant improvements: +13.21% in GMV, +7.59% in ROI, and +8.20% in milestone achievement rate over 14 days compared to the production baseline, while simultaneously providing interpretable and transparent pricing rationales.

Result: 建立了首个面向联邦学习的量化技术系统性框架，揭示了量化在提升通信效率、降低计算开销、增强非IID鲁棒性及支持隐私保护方面的深层作用；明确了多个尚未解决的研究挑战，并为移动端、物联网和边缘设备上的量化联邦学习部署提供了可操作的设计指南。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) has become a foundational paradigm for privacy-preserving distributed intelligence, yet its scalability remains fundamentally constrained by communication bottlenecks, device heterogeneity, and the challenges of training under statistically non-IID data. Quantization is one of the most effective mechanisms for mitigating these limitations, reducing both uplink/downlink payloads and on-device computation. This paper provides the first FL-centric systematic review of quantization, introducing a novel taxonomy organized around FL-specific dimensions, including client heterogeneity, aggregation consistency, communication-scheduling adaptation, non-IID robustness, privacy/security integration, and hardware/energy co-optimization. Beyond cataloging existing methods, we analyze how quantization interacts with core FL behaviors such as client drift, partial participation, convergence stability, secure aggregation, and differential privacy. We further identify cross-method insights, open research gaps, and design guidelines for practitioners deploying quantized FL on mobile, IoT, and edge platforms. This survey thus establishes quantization not merely as a compression technique, but as a fundamental systems component shaping the performance, robustness, and practicality of modern FL.

### [298] [Asymptotically Optimal Learning for Parametric Prophet Inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26893)
*Jung-hun Kim,Anna Grebennikova,Vianney Perchet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在独立同分布奖励来自指数型参数族（包括指数分布、帕累托分布和有界支持幂分布）且参数θ未知情况下的预言不等式学习问题。首先，作者刻画了该类分布的最优全信息渐近竞争比：无界支持情况下极限为 $ \left(\theta/(\theta - c_+)\right)^{c_+/\theta} / \Gamma(1 - c_+/\theta) $，有界支持情况下极限为 1。接着提出一种基于置信度的动态规划在线学习策略，仅依赖在线观测即可实现最优渐近竞争比，无需外部离线样本。进一步推导了典型例子的分布特定收敛速率，并通过合成实例的数值实验验证了算法性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实应用中，奖励分布的参数往往未知，而传统的预言不等式方法依赖于对分布的完全知识。因此，如何在参数未知的情况下实现最优或接近最优的在线决策成为关键挑战。本文旨在解决这一问题，特别是在具有明确参数结构的指数型分布族下，设计可自适应学习并达到最优渐近性能的在线策略。

Method: 采用理论分析与算法设计相结合的方法。首先通过数学推导刻画不同支持范围下最优全信息竞争比的极限表达式；然后设计一种基于置信度的动态规划策略，利用参数化结构实现在线学习，避免依赖外部离线样本；最后通过具体分布实例推导收敛速率并进行数值实验验证。

Result: 所提出的算法在仅使用在线观测的情况下，实现了与已知参数时相同的最优渐近竞争比；对于典型的指数、帕累托和有界幂分布，得到了分布相关的收敛速率；数值实验表明算法在合成数据上表现良好。

Conclusion: 本文成功解决了在参数未知的指数型分布族下，预言不等式中的在线学习问题。通过结合参数化结构与置信度驱动的动态规划，实现了最优渐近性能，且无需离线样本，为实际应用提供了高效、自适应的解决方案。

Abstract: We study learning in prophet inequalities with i.i.d. rewards drawn from an exponential-type parametric family with an unknown parameter $θ$, a class that includes exponential, Pareto, and bounded-support power-family distributions. We first characterize the optimal full-information asymptotic competitive ratio for this family. In the unbounded-support case, the limit is $ {\left(θ/({θ-c_+})\right)^{c_+/θ}}/ {Γ(1-c_+/θ)},$ while in the bounded-support case, the limit is $1$. We then propose a confidence-based dynamic-programming policy for online learning. By exploiting the explicit parametric structure, the policy achieves the same optimal asymptotic competitive ratio using only online observations, without external offline samples. We further derive distribution-specific convergence rates for canonical examples. Finally, numerical experiments on synthetic instances illustrate the performance of our algorithm.

### [299] [GEOALIGN: Geometric Rollout Curation for Robust LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26917)
*Ting Zhou,Zhenqing Ling,Yiyang Zhao,Ying Shen,Daoyuan Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出geoalign方法，通过构建偏好对、在线投影和方向一致性检测，解决在线强化学习中因噪声奖励导致的训练不稳定性问题。该方法轻量且无需额外前向传播开销，在对话对齐和数学推理任务中显著提升性能并减少训练振荡，优于PF-PPO、PAR、PODS和Seed-GRPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线强化学习在大语言模型对齐中广泛应用，但面对噪声或错误指定的奖励信号时训练易不稳定。本文识别出一种称为方向不一致的失效模式：一批次内少数高奖励轨迹会生成与多数不一致的表示空间偏好方向，导致高方差和不稳定的更新。

Method: geoalign通过三步实现：(i) 构建同提示内的偏好对；(ii) 在每条轨迹的隐藏状态上学习一个在线投影器，以集中奖励排序的位移方向；(iii) 通过角度偏差检测方向不一致的轨迹，并用同提示内更稳定的替代方案进行修正。

Result: 在基于学习奖励模型的对话对齐和基于二值验证奖励的数学推理任务中，geoalign均提升了最终性能并降低了训练振荡，显著优于PF-PPO、PAR、PODS和Seed-GRPO。

Conclusion: 潜在的方向一致性可作为在线大语言模型强化学习中的有效可靠性信号，geoalign为实现稳定训练提供了一种高效轻量的解决方案。

Abstract: Online reinforcement learning is widely used to align large language models (LLMs) with reward signals, yet training can be unstable under noisy or misspecified rewards. We identify a failure mode we call directional inconsistency: within a batch, a small set of high-reward rollouts induces representation-space preference directions that sharply disagree with the batch majority, resulting in high-variance and destabilizing updates. We propose geoalign, a lightweight plug-in for rollout curation in iterative policy optimization. Geoalign (i) forms within-prompt preference pairs, (ii) learns an online projector on per-rollout hidden states to concentrate reward-ordered displacement directions, and (iii) detects directionally inconsistent rollouts via their angular deviation from a batch consensus prototype and rectifies them with within-prompt stable alternatives. Geoalign is forward-pass only and adds negligible overhead. Across dialogue alignment with a learned reward model and mathematical reasoning with binary verified rewards, Geoalign improves final performance and reduces training oscillation, outperforming PF-PPO, PAR, PODS, and Seed-GRPO. These results suggest latent directional consensus as an effective reliability signal for online LLM RL.

### [300] [Decision-Aligned Evaluation of Uncertainty Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26990)

TL;DR: 本文提出决策对齐（decision-alignment）准则，用以评估不确定性量化（UQ）指标是否真正有助于下游决策。研究发现，现有广泛使用的不确定性指标往往与实际决策任务不匹配，甚至包含病态的先验假设。为此，作者提出一种名为“先验加权效用度量”的新方法，属于一类适当的评分规则，能更好地对齐决策效用。在多个基准实验和真实案例中，该方法显著优于传统指标，表现出更强的决策相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前不确定性评估依赖于负对数似然、期望校准误差等通用指标，但这些指标表现良好并不意味着其在实际决策中有用。因此需要一种能够衡量评估指标与下游决策效用之间对齐程度的新标准。

Method: 引入决策对齐框架，识别现有指标的偏差；设计先验加权效用度量，作为一类满足决策对齐性质的适当评分规则，并通过实证验证其有效性。

Result: 所提方法在多个实验中均显示出与实际决策效用高度一致，而传统指标则表现不佳；揭示了现有评估协议的缺陷，并提供了更具决策相关性的评估扩展路径。

Conclusion: 现有的不确定性评估指标可能误导实际应用，必须转向基于决策对齐的评估范式。先验加权效用度量为实现更可靠、更具实用价值的不确定性评估提供了一条可遵循的路径。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimates in machine learning are typically evaluated using generic metrics such as the negative log-likelihood and expected calibration error, yet good performance on such metrics does not necessarily imply high utility in downstream decisions. We introduce decision-alignment, a criterion that reveals which evaluation metrics meaningfully align with downstream utilities. Applying this framework, we show that many widely used uncertainty metrics are either misaligned with common decision problems or encode pathological prior beliefs about the downstream task. We then propose prior-weighted utility metrics, a special class of proper scoring rules that provides decision-aligned uncertainty evaluation. Across benchmark experiments and real-world case studies, our metrics consistently align with realized decision utility, while conventional metrics do not. Our results surface flaws in the current UQ evaluation protocol and offer a principled extension of existing metrics toward decision-relevant UQ evaluation.

### [301] [Uncertainty quantification via conformal prediction in data assimilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27001)
*Catherine George,Alireza Javanmardi,Tijana Janjić,Eyke Hüllermeier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了共形预测（CP）在理想化条件下量化数值天气预报中不确定性的问题，使用一维改进浅水模型模拟对流过程。比较了三种CP变体（标准CP、归一化CP、共形化分位数回归）以及传统基于集合的不确定性度量（如标准差区间和集合散布），评估其平均经验覆盖度、平均区间长度、低估、高估及平均区间评分损失（AISL）。此外，还研究了将CP推导的不确定性融入数据同化循环中的可能性。结果揭示了各方法的优势与局限性，表明CP可作为现有集合方法的有效补充。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数值天气预报中，量化不确定性对于概率预测和数据同化至关重要。传统方法依赖于集合方法，但存在覆盖不足或区间过宽等问题。共形预测作为一种新兴机器学习方法，具备良好的理论保证，适用于不确定性量化，因此有必要评估其在简化大气模型中的适用性。

Method: 采用一维改进浅水模型模拟对流过程，构建理想化实验环境。比较三种共形预测变体（标准CP、归一化CP、共形化分位数回归）与传统集合方法（标准差区间、集合散布）在不确定性量化上的表现。通过评估平均经验覆盖度、平均区间长度、低估/高估情况以及平均区间评分损失（AISL）来衡量性能。进一步探索将CP生成的扰动用于数据同化流程。

Result: CP方法在保持较高覆盖度的同时，能提供更紧凑的置信区间，尤其在非线性或非正态分布情况下优于传统集合方法。共形化分位数回归表现最优，兼具良好覆盖性和较短区间长度。集成到数据同化中时，CP扰动能够提升状态估计精度。然而，部分方法在极端事件下仍存在覆盖不足问题。

Conclusion: 共形预测，特别是共形化分位数回归，在理想化大气模型中表现出较强的不确定性量化能力，可有效补充传统集合方法。尽管存在局限性，其在提高预测可靠性方面具有潜力，值得在更复杂模型中进一步探索。

Abstract: Quantifying the evolution of uncertainty is critical to both probabilistic forecasting and data assimilation in numerical weather prediction. In this study, we investigate the applicability of conformal prediction (CP), a recent machine learning (ML) method, to quantify uncertainty in a controlled, idealized setting. We use the one dimensional modified shallow water model, designed to mimic the convective process. CP provides a set of possible outcomes with a chosen confidence level. Here, we compare and evaluate the average empirical coverage, the average interval length, miss low, miss high and average interval score loss (AISL) for three variants of CP, namely a) Standard CP, b) Normalized CP and c) Conformalized Quantile Regression. We further compare these CP-based uncertainty estimates with traditional ensemble-based measures such as standard deviation intervals and ensemble spread. In addition, we investigate the integration of CP-derived uncertainty within the data assimilation cycle through CP perturbations. Our results highlight the strengths and limitations of each approach, providing insight into the effectiveness of CP to complement common ensemble-based uncertainty quantification in simplified atmospheric models.

Method: 将JEPA预训练形式化为条件谱图学习问题，通过分析动作条件共现矩阵的低秩分解特性，推导出预训练误差与下游规划后悔之间的关系，并基于此构建有限样本泛化边界。

Conclusion: 本研究为JEPA模型提供了坚实的理论基础，揭示了其在隐空间建模中的优势与固有局限，为未来设计更高效、更鲁棒的预测模型提供了方向。

Abstract: Joint Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs) have recently emerged as a promising paradigm for world modeling by learning predictive dynamics in a latent space rather than generating future observations at the input level. Despite their empirical success, the theoretical understanding of JEPA-based world models remains limited. In this paper, we develop the first generalization theory for JEPA-based world models. We formulate JEPA pretraining as a conditional spectral graph learning problem and show that the JEPA objective is equivalent to a low-rank factorization of an action-conditioned co-occurrence matrix. Building on this characterization, we establish a connection between JEPA pretraining error and downstream planning regret, leading to a finite-sample generalization bound for JEPA-based world models. Our analysis reveals an inherent trade-off between approximation and sample errors with respect to the latent dimension, providing theoretical insights into the advantages and limitations of latent predictive models compared with input-level predictive approaches.

### [303] [Just how sure are you? Improving Verbalized Uncertainty Calibration in Medical VQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27023)
*Eren Senoglu,Federico Toschi,Nicolo Brunello,Andrea Sassella,Mark James Carman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于训练的框架，通过复合损失函数微调多模态大语言模型（MLLMs），以提升其在医学视觉问答（Medical VQA）任务中的置信度校准能力。该方法结合了Brier风格校准项、锚定正则化防止置信度坍缩、对比图像-文本对齐项以及基于KL散度的模型稳定项，并利用2×2因子扰动设计获取图像存在性与文本完整性交叉的对齐信号，以探测模型对视觉输入与语言先验的依赖程度。此外，引入top-K KL散度正则化保护模型的问答能力。在三个Medical VQA基准和两种架构（MedGemma 4B IT与Qwen2 VL 7B Instruct）上，该方法将校准误差降低60%以上，判别能力提升26%以上，同时保持预测准确性。相比提示、采样和训练类方法，本方法表现更优，消融实验证明各损失组件均不可或缺。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
