Method: 提出一种基于训练的框架，采用复合损失函数进行微调：包含Brier风格校准项、锚定正则化防止置信度极端化、对比图像-文本对齐项（基于2×2因子扰动设计）、以及基于KL散度的模型稳定项；并通过top-K KL散度正则化保护模型的推理能力。

Result: 在三个Medical VQA基准上，校准误差降低60%以上，判别能力提升26%以上，同时保持预测准确性；优于提示、采样和训练类方法；消融实验表明各损失组件均必要。

Conclusion: 所提出的多模态校准框架能有效提升医学VQA中多模态大语言模型的置信度校准性能，且具备良好的可迁移性和实用性，代码已开源，具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) applied to Medical Visual Question Answering (VQA) tend to produce overconfident outputs regardless of actual correctness, and existing verbalized confidence calibration methods, developed primarily for text only LLMs, do not account for the multimodal nature of medical image understanding.
  This work proposes a training based framework that finetunes MLLMs to improve their calibration using a composite loss function combining a Brier style calibration term, an anchor regularizer that prevents confidence collapse toward extreme values, a contrastive image text alignment term, and a KL based model stabilization term. The alignment signal is derived from a $2 \times 2$ factorial perturbation design that crosses image presence with text integrity, probing the reliance of the model on visual modality input versus language priors. Finally, a top K KL divergence regularizer is used to protect the answering ability of the model during finetuning.
  Across three Medical VQA benchmarks and two architectures (MedGemma 4B IT and Qwen2 VL 7B Instruct), our method reduces calibration error by 60% or more, and improves discrimination by 26% or more, while preserving predictive accuracy. On average across benchmarks, the technique outperforms prompting based, sampling based, and training based approaches, and ablation experiments confirm that each component of the loss function is indeed necessary for improving the calibration. All code for the experiments is publicly available.

### [304] [Symplectic Neural Networks for learning Generalized Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27029)
*Harsh Choudhary,Vyacheslav Kungurtsev,Chandan Gupta,Melvin Leok,Georgios Korpas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于隐式辛积分器的哈密顿神经网络（HNN）训练方法，通过利用伴随系统辛离散化获得与反向传播一致的敏感性，实现高效参数更新。结合预测-校正型求解器与固定点迭代，有效降低隐式时间步长带来的计算开销，显著提升训练效率和内存性能。实验表明，该方法在非可分、混沌系统的系统辨识与能量守恒方面表现优异，并通过后处理的逆误差分析得到更精确的修正哈密顿量，无需依赖更高精度的流映射离散化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从噪声观测中准确识别哈密顿系统的哈密顿量具有挑战性，而传统方法在保证长期行为忠实性（如能量守恒）时面临计算成本高、反向传播困难的问题。需要一种既能保持几何结构又具备高效训练能力的方法。

Method: 采用隐式辛积分器构建HNN模型，利用伴随系统辛离散化等价于反向传播敏感性的特性，避免直接对隐式求解器进行反向传播；结合预测-校正型ODE求解器与固定点迭代，降低计算复杂度；引入后处理的逆误差分析以改进学习到的哈密顿量精度。

Result: 实验验证了该方法在非可分、混沌系统上的优越系统辨识能力与能量保持性能；同时实现了更低的计算开销与内存占用；通过逆误差分析得到的修正哈密顿量更接近真实哈密顿量，且无需增加离散化精度。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于隐式辛积分器的HNN训练方法在保持物理一致性的同时，显著提升了训练效率与模型精度，为复杂动力系统建模提供了高效可行的新路径。

Abstract: Hamiltonian Neural Networks (HNNs) integrate physical priors into neural models by learning a system's Hamiltonian, improving generalization and sample efficiency. Identifying the system Hamiltonian from noisy observations of state variables is a challenging task. For simulations to faithfully reflect the long-term behavior of Hamiltonian systems, especially energy conservation, it is essential to use symplectic integrators, which preserve the system's geometric structure. This fidelity comes at a cost: implicit symplectic integrators are more computationally intensive and make backpropagation through the ODE solver non-trivial. However, by leveraging the fact that symplectic discretizations of the adjoint system yield the same sensitivities associated by backpropagation, we obtain an efficient method of training the Neural Network parameters. In our work, we explore this alternate method of HNN training under noisy observation of trajectories with our HNN model based on an implicit symplectic integrator. Computationally, a predictor-corrector based ODE solver and fixed point iteration help to mitigate the computational cost of the implicit timestepping, resulting in more efficient generation of gradient updates. We showcase the numerical advantage, in experiments, in system identification and energy preservation on a range of non-separable, chaotic systems and the efficient computation and memory complexity of our method. We also observe that the post-processing of the learned Hamiltonian using backward error analysis yields a modified Hamiltonian that is a more accurate approximation of the true Hamiltonian without the need to use more accurate discretizations of the flow map.

### [305] [State Representation Matters in Deep Reinforcement Learning: Application to Energy Trading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27032)
*Jesper Klicks,Sander Vržina,Vincent François-Lavet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在水电站储能套利环境中，状态表示对强化学习代理能源交易决策的影响。通过固定其他因素，仅改变市场特征（绝对价格/日历特征、相对特征、预测特征及其组合），发现单一特征表现不佳，而结合绝对、相对与预测特征的组合显著提升性能：在测试集上达到55.6%收益，跨区域中位数达47.5%，远超单一特征或基准策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能源交易不仅依赖当前市场价格，还需考虑未来市场预期和运行约束，因此状态表示是强化学习中关键设计问题。现有研究较少系统评估不同市场特征对储能交易策略的影响，尤其在跨市场迁移能力方面存在空白。

Method: 使用固定结构的Double DQN代理，在HydroDam环境上训练不同状态表示策略。对比绝对价格/日历特征、相对特征（与近期历史比较）、预测特征及它们的组合。所有实验保持环境、动作空间、奖励函数、网络结构和训练协议一致，仅改变输入状态特征。

Result: 绝对特征单独使用时在测试集上仅达28.8%，跨区域中位数为5.7%；相对或预测特征单独使用也低于滚动价格得分基准。而绝对+相对特征组合提升至49.9%（测试集）和39.8%（跨区域中位数），加入预测特征后进一步提升至55.6%和47.5%，显著优于单一特征。

Conclusion: 状态表示不是简单的预处理步骤，而是储能交易强化学习策略设计的核心。实现稳健跨市场迁移需融合价格尺度、近期相对价格上下文以及短期预测信息，单一特征家族无法满足复杂交易需求。

Abstract: Energy trading decisions depend not only on current market prices, but also on expected future market conditions, and operational constraints. This makes the state representation given to a reinforcement learning agent an important design choice. We study this in HydroDam, a pumped-storage arbitrage environment, using a fixed Double DQN agent. The environment, action space, reward function, network, and training protocol are kept fixed; only the market features are changed. We compare absolute price/calendar features, relative features that compare current prices with recent market history, forecast features, and all combinations of these three feature families. Policies are trained and selected using 2007--2011 Belgian day-ahead prices and evaluated on two test settings: a later same-market test set from 2012--2025 and 39 other ENTSO-E market zones. Absolute features only reaches 28.8% on the test set and a median 5.7% across zones. Relative-only and forecast-only states also stay below a rolling price-score heuristic in the cross-zone median. Combining feature families is much stronger: absolute + relative reaches 49.9% on the test set and a 39.8% cross-zone median, while absolute + relative + forecast reaches 55.6% and 47.5%. These results suggest that state representation is not a minor preprocessing choice in storage-trading RL, but a central part of the policy design: robust transfer requires combining price scale, recent relative price context, and short-horizon forecast information, rather than relying on any single feature family.

</details>


### [306] [Finding Stationary Points by Comparisons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27082)
*Helin Wang,Chenyi Zhang,Xiwen Tao,Yexin Zhang,Tongyang Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在仅通过比较预言机访问目标函数值时，如何找到非凸函数的驻点。对于具有李普希茨梯度和海森矩阵的二阶可微函数，提出了一种算法，使用$\widetilde O(n^2/ε^{1.5})$次查询即可达到$ε$-驻点；同时设计了估计归一化海森矩阵精度为$δ$的子程序，需$\widetilde O(n^2\log(1/δ))$次查询。进一步在量子比较预言机模型下，提出了首个量子算法，以$\widetilde O(n/ε^{1.5})$次查询实现$ε$-驻点寻找。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无法直接获取函数梯度或值的情况下，仅通过比较两个点的函数值来寻找非凸函数的驻点是一个重要但挑战性的问题。传统优化方法依赖于梯度信息，而本研究探索在仅有比较信息时的高效求解策略，尤其在高维和低精度要求场景下具有实际意义。

Method: 提出一种基于比较预言机的优化算法，结合对海森矩阵的归一化估计子程序，利用梯度与海森矩阵的光滑性条件，通过迭代逼近实现驻点搜索；在量子模型中，利用量子叠加态进行并行查询，显著降低查询复杂度。

Result: 在经典模型下，算法复杂度为$\widetilde O(n^2/ε^{1.5})$次查询；在量子模型下，首次实现$\widetilde O(n/ε^{1.5})$次查询的量子加速。

Conclusion: 该研究为无梯度、仅靠比较信息的非凸优化提供了高效算法框架，揭示了量子计算在该类问题中的潜力，拓展了优化理论在受限信息环境下的应用边界。

Abstract: We study the problem of finding stationary points of non-convex functions when access to the objective is provided only through a comparison oracle that, given two points, outputs which has the larger function value. For a twice differentiable $f\colon\mathbb R^n\to\mathbb R$ with Lipschitz gradient and Hessian, we develop an algorithm that visits an $ε$-stationary point using $\widetilde O(n^2/ε^{1.5})$ queries. Our approach uses a subroutine that estimates the normalized Hessian to accuracy $δ$ using $\widetilde O(n^2\log(1/δ))$ queries. We further study this problem with a quantum comparison oracle model where queries can be made in superpositions, and develop the first quantum algorithm that finds an $ε$-stationary point, which takes $\widetilde O(n/ε^{1.5})$ queries.

</details>


### [307] [Data-Free Reservoir Features for Efficient Long-Horizon Cold-Start Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27095)
*Augustinas Jučas,Yangchen Pan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CIRCLE提出一种无需图像数据训练的特征提取器，结合固定二维随机共振特征与流式线性判别分析头，在冷启动类增量学习中实现无回放、无骨干网络更新的高效学习。通过多实例特征集成与预测平均，平衡偏差-方差，显著优于现有基线方法，尤其在长任务序列下表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有冷启动类增量学习方法面临两难：持续训练骨干网络虽能缓解语义漂移但计算成本高；冻结骨干网络则导致初始类别偏差且性能受限。因此需要一种无需训练骨干、低开销且具备强泛化能力的新范式。

Method: 采用固定双向二维随机共振（BiRC2D）特征提取器，结合流式线性判别分析（SLDA）分类头，通过多随机实例生成特征集成，并对独立SLDA头的softmax输出进行平均，实现可调的偏差-方差权衡。整个模型仅需样本级训练，无需回放、任务边界信息或反向传播。

Result: 在CIFAR-100、TinyImageNet、ImageNet-Subset和ImageNet-1k上，CIRCLE在10-20个任务时表现竞争力，在50、100和500任务时显著超越强基线方法，且训练速度远超依赖骨干网络重训练的方法。消融实验证明BiRC2D特征、SLDA头及特征/预测集成均对性能有贡献。

Conclusion: CIRCLE证明了完全不训练骨干网络的可行性，在冷启动类增量学习中实现了高效、稳定且可扩展的性能，为资源受限场景下的持续学习提供了新思路。

Abstract: Cold-start exemplar-free class-incremental learning requires learning a growing set of classes without replay, external pretraining, or a large initial task. Existing cold-start methods typically either train the backbone throughout the stream and compensate for semantic drift, or freeze a backbone after the first task, producing features biased toward the initial classes. These choices also create a computational tension: drift-compensation methods require repeated backbone training and increasingly expensive updates as the task horizon grows, while frozen-backbone methods are cheap but weak under cold start. We study a third option: a feature extractor that is never fit to image data at all. We propose CIRCLE, a class-incremental classifier built from fixed bidirectional two-dimensional reservoir features, adapted from BiRC2D for image classification, and streaming linear discriminant analysis heads. CIRCLE groups multiple random reservoir instantiations into feature ensembles and averages the softmax outputs of independent SLDA heads, yielding a tunable bias-variance tradeoff between richer random features and prediction-level ensembling. Because the feature extractor is fixed and the head admits streaming closed-form updates, CIRCLE performs sample-wise training without replay, task-boundary information, or backbone backpropagation. On CIFAR-100, TinyImageNet, ImageNet-Subset, and ImageNet-1k, CIRCLE is competitive at 10-20 task splits and substantially outperforms strong CS-EFCIL baselines at 50, 100, and 500 task splits, while training much faster than trained-backbone drift-compensation methods. Ablations show that the BiRC2D-style extractor, SLDA head, and balanced feature/prediction ensembling each contribute to the final performance.

</details>

Abstract: Transformer-based models have recently attracted increasing attention for Raman spectral classification. A bacterial Raman dataset comprising 5,417 single-cell spectra from six bacterial species and nine independent measurement replicates was used. The transformer consistently achieved the highest classification performance across independent test replicates and significantly outperformed all conventional approaches. Analysis of the learned latent feature space revealed improved class separation compared with PCA- and ICA-based representations. Furthermore, the transformer maintained superior performance when applied directly to raw Raman spectra without preprocessing, demonstrating robust behavior across measurement replicates. These findings highlight the potential of transformer-based models for robust Raman spectral classification and emphasize the importance of replicate-aware validation for realistic model evaluation.

Abstract: Uplift modeling, crucial for estimating individual treatment effects (ITE), faces dual challenges: flexibly leveraging inter-group similarity to enhance discriminative power and debiasing under unobserved confounding scenarios. In this paper, we propose the Cross-Head Attention Uplift Network (CHAUN) and Robust Adversarial Inverse Propensity Score (RA-IPS) method to address these limitations. CHAUN employs shared feature embeddings and cross-head attention mechanisms to dynamically integrate treatment-specific and control-specific representations, enhancing inter-group correlation modeling. Theoretically, we prove that access to the true propensity scores ensures ITE identifiability even with unobserved confounders. The results validate the effectiveness of our proposed methods in real-world causal inference tasks.

### [311] [Kolmogorov Arnold networks (KAN) for aerodynamic prediction: a comparison with MLPs and GNNs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27126)
*Miguel Jaraiz,Fermin Gutierrez,Pablo Yeste,Miguel Sánchez-Domínguez,Eusebio Valero,Gonzalo Rubio,Lucas Lacasa*

TL;DR: KANs show good performance in fluid dynamics surrogate modeling for predicting airfoil pressure distributions, with strong interpolation across Mach numbers and angles of attack, but are marginally inferior to well-trained MLPs and outperformed by GNNs with longer training. Despite lower model complexity and faster training, KANs suffer from training instabilities and require careful hyperparameter tuning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: The study compares KANs, MLPs, and GNNs on the task of predicting pressure coefficients over subsonic and transonic airfoils, assessing performance across varying Mach numbers and angles of attack, including training speed, model complexity, and stability.

KANs have lower complexity and faster training but exhibit training instabilities and high sensitivity to hyperparameters.

Conclusion: While KANs offer advantages in model simplicity and training speed, their performance is not consistently superior to MLPs or GNNs in this domain, and their practical use is limited by training instability and sensitivity to hyperparameter settings.

Abstract: Kolmogorov Arnold networks (KAN) have recently been introduced as a (deep) neural network architecture whose trainable parameters adapt the activation functions, instead of the coefficients of the affine transformations at the core of traditional architectures such as deep multilayer perceptrons (MLPs). This architecture builds on the Kolmogorov-Arnold theorem, which endows it with universal approximation properties. While the advent of KANs has been received with excitement, there is a current debate about the possible KAN supremacy over deep multilayer perceptrons (MLPs) for classic fields such as symbolic regression, generic-purpose machine learning, natural language processing or computer vision. Here we assess the performance of KANs --and its nuanced comparison against MLPs and graph neural networks (GNNs)-- in the realm of fluid dynamics surrogate modelling. To that aim, we consider the task of predicting the surface pressure distribution over subsonic and transonic airfoils, a canonical task in aerodynamics. Our results show that KAN models show good performance in predicting the whole pressure coefficients and is able to interpolate across Mach numbers and angles of attack, however its performance is comparable --marginally inferior-- to a suitably trained MLP, where best performance is achieved by a GNN at the expense or requiring lengthier training. While the optimal KAN model have typically much lower complexity than MLP and GNN --hence resulting in faster training--, we find that KANs suffer from training instabilities, and their performance is highly dependent on a proper hyperparameter optimisation.

### [312] [fTNN: a tensor neural network for fractional PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27140)
*Qingkui Ma,Hehu Xie,Xiaobo Yin*

TL;DR: 提出了一种确定性的张量神经网络子空间方法（fTNN），用于求解带有分数阶拉普拉斯算子的边界域问题，包括分数阶泊松方程和时变分数阶对流-扩散方程。通过几何自适应积分分解策略，将分数阶拉普拉斯算子分解为近场、内部远场和外部远场三部分，并采用高斯-雅可比、高斯及确定性角向积分相结合的方式实现全确定性积分框架。针对低正则性解和损失函数，构建了包含边界奇异性特征的试函数，并提出两种自动选择主导指数和评估损失的方法。对于时变问题，设计了时空可分离的神经网络与交替优化策略，显著提升训练效率。数值实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试中具有高精度，尤其在强边界奇异性与长时模拟下优于现有fPINN和蒙特卡洛方法。

Method: 采用几何自适应积分分裂策略，将分数阶拉普拉斯算子分解为近场、内部远场和外部远场；使用高斯-雅可比积分处理奇异径向积分，高斯积分处理常规径向积分，确定性角向积分处理角向变量；构建含边界奇异性信息的试函数；提出自动选取主导指数与损失函数评估策略；设计时空可分离的神经网络结构与交替优化算法以提高训练效率。

Result: 所提方法在多种典型分数阶问题上实现了高精度求解，特别是在强边界奇异性与长时间演化场景中，相比现有fPINN和蒙特卡洛方法有显著性能提升，验证了其有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: fTNN是一种高效、高精度的确定性张量神经网络方法，能够有效处理分数阶算子带来的奇异性与低正则性问题，适用于复杂分数阶偏微分方程的求解，具备良好的泛化能力与计算效率。

Abstract: We develop the fTNN, a deterministic tensor neural network subspace method for problems involving the fractional Laplacian on bounded domains, taking the fractional Poisson equation and time-dependent fractional advection-diffusion equation as typical representatives. The work employs a geometry-adapted integration split featuring a spatially dependent near-field radius, which decomposes the fractional Laplacian into three contributions: a singular near field, a regular interior far field, and an analytical exterior far field. Then the singular radial integrals are treated by Gauss-Jacobi quadrature, the regular radial integrals by Gauss quadrature, and the angular variables by deterministic angular quadrature, yielding a fully deterministic integration framework of the fractional Laplacian operator. To accurately resolve low-regularity solutions and the associated loss functional, we construct boundary-singularity-aware trial functions enriched with explicit boundary features, and propose two strategies for automatically selecting the leading exponent and evaluating the loss function from the singularity structure induced by the fractional operator, or jointly by the fractional operator and the source term. For time-dependent fractional PDEs, we design a spatiotemporally separable neural network that factorizes the time-space residual into a sum of low-dimensional temporal and spatial integrals, and we integrate this representation with an alternating neural network subspace optimization strategy for efficient training. Numerical experiments show that the proposed framework attains high accuracy on the tested benchmarks and improves substantially over existing fPINN and Monte Carlo baselines, particularly for problems with strong boundary singularities and long-time simulations.

</details>


### [313] [Stochastic Gradient Optimization with Model-Assisted Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27171)
*Jonne Pohjankukka,Jukka Heikkonen*

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of variance in stochastic gradient estimation for machine learning optimization. Deep learning relies on mini-batch methods such as stochastic gradient descent, which approximate full gradients but introduce noise, creating trade-offs between convergence stability, speed, and generalization. Existing methods, including variance reduction techniques (e.g., SVRG and SAG) and adaptive optimizers, aim to mitigate gradient noise but may introduce additional computational overhead. We propose a model-assisted sampling framework that interprets mini-batch gradients through survey sampling theory, treating the dataset as a fixed finite population and gradients as sample-based estimates. Our aim is to bridge machine learning optimization and survey sampling theory by combining their perspectives on sample-based estimation and variance reduction. By incorporating auxiliary gradient-prediction models, we construct more efficient gradient estimators, with uniform sampling arising as a special case when no auxiliary information is used. Our approach integrates easily with existing optimizers, improving efficiency without altering their dynamics. Empirical results on synthetic and six benchmark datasets show performance gains in 71-86% of the experiments, particularly for medium-sized input spaces in our benchmarks. Notably, with momentum-based optimizers such as AdamW, the proposed estimator achieves clearly better generalization in roughly half the training epochs compared to baseline estimator.

Abstract: Medical device recalls are a critical regulatory mechanism for protecting patient safety. Existing studies mostly address recall occurrence prediction or root-cause analysis separately, while joint modeling of recall severity and root-cause categories has received limited attention. We develop an automated recall triage framework using 54,165 FDA medical device recall records from openFDA, covering the period from 2002 to October 2025. We first evaluate classical machine learning and boosting-based models for recall severity and root-cause category prediction. We then develop RecallRisk-BERT, a multi-task model that combines PubMedBERT-based textual representations of recall narratives with embedding-based representations of structured categorical features, including product code, regulation number, and medical specialty. Performance was evaluated using accuracy, macro-averaged precision, recall, F1-score, and ROC-AUC. Model-derived risk rankings were strongly consistent with observed root-cause severity patterns (rho = 0.983, p = 1.936e-6). These findings indicate that text--tabular learning can support scalable post-report recall triage, regulatory decision support, and model-based root-cause risk analysis.

### [315] [Automating Potential-based Reward Shaping with Vision Language Model Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27180)
*Henrik Müller,Daniel Kudenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出VLM-PBRS框架，利用视觉语言模型（VLM）的偏好反馈自动学习潜在函数，以实现基于势能的奖励塑形（PBRS），从而在无需人工设计奖励函数的情况下提升强化学习中的稀疏奖励问题。通过使用轻量级VLM生成偏好标签，降低了计算成本，尽管准确性较低，但仍能有效加速学习过程。实验在Meta-World和Franka Kitchen环境中验证了该方法在样本效率和抗奖励欺骗方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入VLM-PBRS框架，通过轻量级视觉语言模型对图像对进行偏好判断，收集偏好数据并训练一个潜在函数模型。该方法基于势能奖励塑形（PBRS），保证原始最优策略不变，并避免专家设计奖励项。同时采用小规模高效VLM以降低计算开销。

Result: 在Meta-World和Franka Kitchen环境中，VLM-PBRS显著提升了样本效率，增强了对奖励黑客的鲁棒性，且即使使用低精度偏好标签仍能有效加速学习。实验证明了偏好准确率与学习效率之间的正相关关系。

Conclusion: 本工作首次将基于VLM偏好的学习应用于构建PBRS的潜在函数，提出了一种低成本、可扩展的自动化解决方案，并通过充分实验验证其在提高学习效率和安全性方面的有效性。

Abstract: Sparse rewards are inherently challenging for reinforcement learning agents as they lack intermediate feedback to guide exploration and to correctly attribute the sparse success rewards to relevant parts of the trajectory. Naive reward shaping can induce reward hacking, yielding policies that exploit auxiliary signals instead of solving the intended task. Potential-based reward shaping (PBRS) guarantees preservation of the optimal policy set, but requires the definition of a heuristic potential function over the state space. In this work, we introduce the VLM-guided PBRS framework VLM-PBRS that learns the potential function directly from vision language model (VLM) feedback. We query a lightweight VLM to obtain preferences over image pairs and train a model of the potential function using these preferences. As this approach is based on potential-based reward shaping, it preserves the original optimal policies, and removes the need for expert-designed reward shaping terms. Because large VLMs are prohibitively expensive to invoke repeatedly during policy learning, we employ smaller, more computationally efficient VLMs. Although the resulting preference labels are less accurate, empirical evidence shows that the preference labels can still be used to accelerate learning. We validate our method empirically in the Meta-World and Franka Kitchen environments and highlight the connection between VLM preference label accuracy and sample efficiency improvements. Our contributions are threefold: (1) the first application of VLM preference-based learning to synthesize a potential function for PBRS, (2) a principled, low-cost solution that leverages small VLMs, and (3) extensive empirical demonstration of improved sample efficiency and robustness to reward hacking.

### [316] [Explaining Temporal Graph Neural Networks via Feature-induced Information Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27201)
*Ping Xiong,Thomas Schnake,Klaus-Robert Müller,Shinichi Nakajima*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的归因方法，用于解释事件驱动的时序图神经网络（ETGNNs）中的信息流。该方法基于归一化相关性度量（NRM）框架，全面分析从事件嵌入到事件诱导变量的整个信息流动路径，解决了现有方法仅关注部分信息流的局限性。通过模块化分解过程，该方法能够系统地构建复杂架构下的相关性结构，并支持高阶事件交互分析。在合成数据集和真实世界政治事件网络数据集上的实验表明，该方法在定性和定量评估中均优于现有方法，且生成的解释更具人类可读性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的解释方法仅关注从事件相关嵌入到输出的信息流，忽略了事件诱导变量在节点间交互中的关键作用，这些变量对于捕捉长程时间依赖性至关重要。因此，需要一种能全面分析所有事件相关变量信息流的新方法，以提升ETGNNs的可解释性。

Method: 提出基于归一化相关性度量（NRM）框架的新型归因方法，结合模块化分解技术，系统构建复杂ETGNN架构下的信息流相关性结构，实现对事件嵌入及事件诱导变量信息流的显式量化，并支持跨层可比性和高阶事件交互分析。

Result: 在两个合成数据集（流行病追踪与社会动态）和一个真实世界政治事件网络数据集上进行的实验表明，所提方法在定性和定量评价中均显著优于现有解释方法，生成的解释更符合人类认知，具备更强的可解释性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的归因方法有效克服了传统解释方法忽略事件诱导变量信息流的问题，通过全面分析事件相关变量的信息流动，显著提升了ETGNNs的可解释性，为复杂时序图神经网络的可信应用提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Event-based Temporal Graph Neural Networks (ETGNNs) have demonstrated strong performance across a wide range of applications, including social network analysis, epidemic tracing, recommender systems, and political event forecasting. However, their increasing complexity poses significant challenges for explainability. Existing explanation methods focus only on a subset of the information flow within ETGNNs, typically tracing contributions from the event-related embeddings to the output. Consequently, they overlook the important pathways through event-induced variables, which mediate interactions between nodes and thereby play a central role in capturing long-range temporal dependencies. To overcome this limitation, we propose a novel attribution method that analyzes the \emph{entire} information flow through all event-associated variables. Our method is built upon the recent Normalized Relevance Measure (NRM) framework, which enables explicit quantification of information flow originating from event embeddings as well as information flow passing through event-induced variables. It also ensures comparability of latent variables across layers, and supports higher-order analysis of interactions between events. To handle the architectural complexity of ETGNNs, we extend the NRM framework with a modular decomposition procedure that facilitates the systematic construction of relevance structure for complex neural architectures. We evaluate our approach on two synthetic datasets for epidemic tracing and social dynamics, as well as a real-world dataset of political event networks. Our qualitative and quantitative experiments show that our method consistently outperforms existing explanation approaches while producing more human-interpretable explanations.

### [317] [Graph Neural Networks Applications Across Domains: All Insights You Need](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27202)
*Abderaouf Bahi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该综述将图神经网络领域组织在一个统一的设计空间中，从共同的原理推导出谱域和空间域的公式，并将模型表达能力与Weisfeiler-Leman同构检验层次联系起来，明确指出当前架构能够和不能区分的内容。基于这一方法论基础，分析了十二个应用领域，包括推荐系统、社交网络、知识图谱、药物发现、医疗健康、计算机视觉、交通与城市计算、能源系统、无线通信、网络安全、工业预测、材料科学和气候建模。针对每个领域，阐述了图构建策略及其代价，识别主导架构及其原因，并区分真实性能提升与弱基线或有利数据划分带来的虚假增益。跨领域的比较揭示了若干共性模式：异质性与规模挑战普遍削弱某些模型的表现，时序图仍比静态图更难处理，而排行榜领先的架构往往未被实际部署。文章将过平滑、过挤压、鲁棒性、分布偏移、公平性和可解释性视为决定技术采纳的关键约束，而非可选项。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构建统一的设计空间，从第一性原理出发推导谱域与空间域的图神经网络形式，结合Weisfeiler-Leman同构检验理论分析模型的表达能力；并以跨领域实证分析方式，考察不同应用场景中的图构建策略、主流架构及性能提升的真实性。

Result: 揭示了图神经网络在不同场景下的有效性边界：异质性与大规模数据削弱多数现有模型性能；时序图建模仍具挑战；公开榜单领先模型未必适合实际部署；过平滑、过挤压、鲁棒性、公平性等非性能指标成为技术落地的关键制约因素。

Abstract: Graph neural networks have moved from a niche representation-learning technique to the default model class wherever data carry relational structure. The interesting question is no longer whether message passing helps on a given dataset, but where graph structure earns its computational cost and where it does not. This survey organises the field around a single design space, derives the spectral and spatial formulations from shared first principles, and connects expressive power to the Weisfeiler-Leman hierarchy with explicit statements of what current architectures can and cannot separate. Against that methodological backbone we examine twelve application domains, among them recommendation and social networks, knowledge graphs and language-model integration, drug discovery and molecular property learning, healthcare and neuroscience, computer vision, traffic and urban computing, power and renewable-energy systems, wireless and sixth-generation networks, fraud and cybersecurity, industrial prognostics, materials science, and climate modelling. For each domain we specify the graph-construction choices and their costs, identify which architecture families dominate and why, and separate reported gains from artefacts of weak baselines or favourable splits. A cross-domain comparison exposes recurring patterns: heterophily and scale undercut the same models almost everywhere, temporal graphs remain harder than their static counterparts, and the architectures that top public leaderboards are seldom the ones that reach deployment. We treat over-smoothing, over-squashing, robustness, distribution shift, fairness, and explainability not as a closing checklist but as the constraints that decide adoption.

### [318] [The Geometry of Updates: Fisher Alignment at Vocabulary Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27242)
*John Sweeney*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需训练的源选择方法，针对具有共享词汇表的语言模型家族（如SMILES、蛋白质和基因组序列），在共享输出头设置下，通过头Fisher对齐的余弦值来捕捉激活、误差及耦合因素，实现高效、轻量级的任务签名（16KB）和流式状态（192KB/任务），适用于大规模词汇场景。该方法克服了传统表示相似性度量在无标签条件假设下的信息不足问题，并在激活相似性无效时仍保持有效性，可用于任务相似性诊断与模型分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在科学字符串领域（如化学、生物序列）中，候选语料库共享同一分词器但目标预测不同，导致传统表示相似性度量失效，而经典更新几何度量计算成本过高，亟需一种高效、可扩展的源选择机制。

Method: 提出FisherSketch方法，利用头Fisher对齐作为联合激活-误差空间中核均值嵌入之间的余弦值，直接在单次流式遍历中估计，避免显式构建费舍尔矩阵，实现低存储开销的任务签名与动态状态。

Result: FisherSketch可在仅16KB任务签名和192KB流式状态条件下，实现K=128,256的头Fisher对齐；实验表明其在激活相似性无法区分任务时仍具判别力，且支持跨层验证与模型诊断，优于传统表示相似性指标。

Conclusion: FisherSketch为大规模语言模型家族中的训练自由源选择提供了高效、可扩展的解决方案，揭示了任务间相似性的深层结构，不仅提升源选择性能，还为理解模型更新机制提供新工具。

Abstract: Training-free source selection for LLM families with shared vocabularies arises in scientific string domains such as SMILES, protein, and genomic sequences, where candidate corpora share a tokenizer but differ in prediction targets. This creates an activation-dark regime: representation-similarity metrics can be uninformative without assumptions about label-conditioned error geometry, while classical update-geometry metrics are computationally prohibitive at vocabulary scale. We show that, in a shared-output head setting, representation metrics (e.g., CKA) are non-identifiable for transfer; models can share identical representations yet have orthogonal head updates. The key identity is that head Fisher alignment is exactly a cosine between kernel mean embeddings in the joint activation-error space, exposing activation, error, and coupling factors rather than requiring a materialized Fisher matrix. FisherSketch estimates this cosine directly in a single streaming pass, making K=128,256 head Fisher alignment practical with a 16 KB task signature (m=4096) and a 192 KB per-task streaming state, small enough to store next to a model hash, but encoding transfer-relevant update structure. Beyond source selection, the same signatures and marginals provide a diagnostic instrument for studying whether LLM task similarity is driven by activations, errors, or their coupling; shared-parameter and internal-layer validations, together with Llama-3.1-8B verbalizer-shift experiments, show that FisherSketch remains informative when activation similarity cannot distinguish tasks.

</details>


### [319] [Effective Covariance Dynamics in Solvable High-Dimensional GANs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27246)
*Andrew Bond,Zafer Doğan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个可解的高维生成对抗网络（GAN）训练模型，其中线性生成器从具有结构化潜在协方差的数据中学习低维子空间。扩展了先前仅适用于无条件信号和对角潜在协方差的可解GAN分析，引入了类别相关、相关且非零均值的潜在结构。对于二次能量判别器，所有异质性通过概率加权的有效二阶矩进入动态过程。证明了在高维极限下，随机微观训练过程收敛到由该有效协方差决定的确定性常微分方程。在匹配协方差特例中，稳定性分析给出了由学习率和噪声水平决定的模式可解区间：学习开始于主要有效特征值超过下界，而完全恢复要求所有相关有效模式保持在区间内。揭示了一种信号增强机制：低秩相关可将弱方向提升至可学习阈值之上，但过强的相关性会破坏恢复稳定性。数值模拟验证了常微分方程、相变边界和增强机制。在MNIST、FashionMNIST和CIFAR-10上的实验进一步表明，知情的生成器协方差能改善与数据驱动参考子空间的对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解GAN分析通常假设无条件信号且潜在协方差为对角阵，难以刻画真实数据中常见的类别相关、非零均值及潜在变量间的相关结构。本文旨在拓展可解框架以包含更复杂的潜在结构，从而理解其对训练动态和学习能力的影响。

Method: 构建一个高维线性生成器与二次能量判别器构成的可解GAN模型，考虑类条件、相关且非零均值的潜在结构；利用大维度极限下的平均场理论，推导出训练过程的确定性常微分方程；通过有效协方差分析系统动态，并在匹配协方差情形下进行稳定性分析，获得可学习区间。

Result: 发现所有潜在结构异质性可通过概率加权的有效二阶矩统一表征；训练过程在高维极限下收敛至确定性常微分方程；提出信号增强机制：低秩相关可提升弱学习方向至可学习阈值以上，但过强相关会引发不稳定；数值实验验证了模型预测的相变边界和增强效应；实际图像数据实验显示，合理设计生成器协方差可显著提高与数据子空间的对齐度。

Conclusion: 本文通过建立一个可解的高维GAN模型，揭示了潜在结构（尤其是相关性和非零均值）如何通过有效协方差影响训练动态和学习能力。核心发现是低秩相关可“增强”弱信号以实现学习，但过度相关则导致崩溃。这一机制为改进生成器初始化或正则化策略提供了理论依据，推动了对复杂潜在结构下GAN行为的理解。

Abstract: We study a solvable high-dimensional model of generative adversarial network (GAN) training in which a linear generator learns a low-dimensional subspace from data with structured latent covariance. Prior solvable GAN analyses assume unconditional signals with diagonal latent covariance; we extend the multi-feature discriminator setting to class-dependent, correlated, and non-zero-mean latent structure. For the quadratic energy discriminator, all such heterogeneity enters the dynamics through a probability-weighted effective second moment. We prove that the stochastic microscopic training process converges, in the high-dimensional limit, to deterministic ordinary differential equations governed by this effective covariance. In the matched-covariance specialization, the stability analysis yields a mode-wise solvable interval determined by the learning rates and noise level: learning begins when the leading effective eigenvalue crosses the lower threshold, while full recovery requires all relevant effective modes to remain within the interval. This reveals a signal-boosting mechanism: low-rank correlations can lift weak directions above the learnability threshold, whereas overly strong correlations destabilize recovery. Numerical simulations validate the ODE, phase boundary, and boosting mechanism. Experiments on MNIST, FashionMNIST, and CIFAR-10 further show that informed generator covariance improves alignment with the data-driven reference subspace.

### [320] [RSPC: A Benchmark for Modeling Stress and Psychiatric Conditions in Digitally Mediated Relationships using Psychiatrist Annotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27247)
*Parmitha Vangapandu,Sai Ganesh Mokkapati,Sathwik Narkedimilli,MSVPJ Sathvik,Timothy Liu,Simon See,Johannes C. Eichstaedt*

We introduce the Relational Stress and Psychiatry Corpus (RSPC) containing 1,799 Reddit posts annotated by psychiatrists for diagnostic categories, including the most prevalent mood disorders (anxiety and depression), relational stressor triggers, and indications of relationship phase. We benchmark seven fine-tuned transformer models and five large language models across multi-label disorder classification, relational trigger detection, and temporal phase prediction tasks. We find clear task-dependent differences between model families, with Claude-3-Haiku achieving the best disorder classification performance (Macro-F1 = 0.538) and GPT-4o obtaining the strongest relational trigger detection performance (Macro-F1 = 0.519), suggesting distinct model capabilities. Overall, RSPC establishes a benchmark for NLP tasks that consider relational context and supports a shift from individual-centric to context-aware mental health modeling that captures the social and temporal dynamics of distress.

### [322] [How Good Can Linear Models Be for Time-Series Forecasting?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27282)
*Lang Huang,Jinglue Xu,Luke Darlow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了时间序列预测中通过扩大模型规模来提升精度的主流观点，提出通过优化预处理（如上下文长度、局部归一化、正则化和数据增强）即可在较低成本下实现显著性能提升。以岭回归为测试模型，研究发现最优历史窗口长度具有强序列特异性且非单调，基于学习的局部归一化优于全局归一化，且同一数据集内不同序列的最佳超参数差异大，表明跨序列共享应灵活调整。优化后的预处理策略在多数场景超越已有线性模型，并在八个基准中的六个上超过Transformer、MLP和CNN等复杂模型。此外，这些超参数本身可作为数据结构的诊断工具，揭示出大模型隐式吸收但难以解释的模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时间序列预测研究倾向于通过扩大模型规模（如通用基础模型）来提升精度，但本文质疑这一假设，认为预处理优化可能在更低代价下实现更优效果。

Method: 使用岭回归作为测试模型，因其具有闭式解和可解释权重；系统搜索八项标准基准上的上下文长度、局部归一化、正则化与数据增强等超参数，分析其对预测性能的影响。

Result: 发现三个关键模式：(1) 最优历史窗口长度强依赖于序列，且不随预测时长单调变化，幂律指数从+0.46到-0.19不等；(2) 基于学习的尾部片段局部归一化优于整体归一化；(3) 同一数据集内不同序列的最优超参数差异大，表明共享策略应灵活。优化后的方法在多数任务上超越线性模型，在六项基准上超过Transformer、MLP和CNN。超参数本身可揭示数据内在结构。

Conclusion: 预处理优化是提升时间序列预测性能的重要途径，其效果甚至可媲美大规模模型，且能提供对数据本质的可解释洞察，未来应重视而非忽视预处理设计。

Abstract: Time-series forecasting research has been moving steadily toward larger architectures, from specialized transformers to general-purpose foundation models, on the assumption that capacity is what unlocks accuracy. We take the opposite position: most of the gap can be closed at far lower cost by tuning preprocessing rather than scaling models. We use Ridge regression as the testbed, since it has a closed-form solution and interpretable weights, which let the optimal hyperparameters be read off the search directly. We search over context length, local normalization, regularization, and augmentation on eight standard benchmarks and find three patterns. (1) Optimal lookback is strongly series-specific and often non-monotonic in forecast horizon, with fitted power-law exponents ranging from $+0.46$ on ETTm2 to $-0.19$ on Exchange and Traffic, challenging the convention that longer horizons need longer history. (2) Normalizing over a learned trailing fraction of the context, rather than its entirety, is almost universally preferred. (3) Series within the same dataset often disagree on hyperparameters; the optimal degree of cross-series sharing varies from fully shared to fully per-series. The resulting models beat prior linear forecasters on most dataset-horizon entries and exceed Transformer, MLP, and CNN baselines on six of eight benchmarks. The optimized hyperparameters also serve as a diagnostic on the data itself, revealing structures that larger models absorb silently into their learned parameters.

### [323] [Recovering Governing Equations from Solution Data: Identifiability Bounds for Linear and Nonlinear ODEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27285)
*Yang Pan,Helmut Bölcskei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究从观测解数据中学习微分方程的理论基础，提出使用解集上的Hausdorff距离作为比较微分方程的自然度量，以刻画在所有初值条件下的最坏情况差异。通过该度量，作者建立了各类微分方程（从线性到Lipschitz连续向量场的非线性系统）的可识别性边界，并推导了相关ODE类别的度量熵估计，进而分析了样本复杂度，量化了可靠恢复控制方程所需的解观测数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学机器学习中从解数据学习控制方程的研究缺乏理论支持，尤其是对真实常微分方程能否唯一且稳定地从多个解观测中识别的条件尚不明确，且无定量的样本复杂度分析。

Method: 引入解集上的Hausdorff距离作为衡量微分方程差异的自然度量，利用该度量分析不同结构方程类的可识别性，结合度量熵理论推导样本复杂度边界。

Result: 建立了线性及非线性（Lipschitz/Hölder连续）常微分方程类的可识别性条件，给出了度量熵估计和样本复杂度的定量结果，揭示了恢复真实方程所需观测数据的下限。

Conclusion: 本工作为从解数据学习微分方程提供了首个系统性的理论框架，明确了可识别性条件与样本需求，推动了科学机器学习中的可解释性和可靠性发展。

Abstract: Learning governing equations from observed solution data is a fundamental challenge in scientific machine learning \cite{bruntonDiscoveringGoverningEquations2016,kovachkiNeuralOperatorLearning2023,longPDENetLearningPDEs2018,rudyDatadrivenDiscoveryPartial2017,raonicConvolutionalNeuralOperators2023}, yet the theoretical conditions under which a ground-truth ODE can be uniquely and stably identified from multiple solution observations remain largely undeveloped, and no quantitative analysis of the sample complexity of such learning tasks exists in the literature. To address this gap, we introduce the Hausdorff distance on solution sets as the natural metric for comparing differential equations, since it captures the worst-case separation between two equations over all admissible initial conditions and thus encodes the minimax structure of the identification problem. We establish identifiability bounds for governing ODEs across a wide class of structure equations--ranging from linear ODEs to nonlinear classes with Lipschitz (Hölder)-continuous vector fields--characterizing precisely when two distinct equations can be distinguished from solution data. Using this metric, we derive metric entropy estimates for the relevant ODE classes and analyze sample complexity bounds, quantifying how many solution observations are needed to reliably recover the governing equation.

### [324] [Designing Reward Signals for Portable Query Generation: A Case Study in Industrial Semantic Job Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27291)
*Ping Liu,Qianqi Shen,Jianqiang Shen,Wenqiong Liu,Rajat Arora,Yunxiang Ren,Chunnan Yao,Dan Xu,Baofen Zheng,Wanjun Jiang,Andrii Soviak,Kevin Kao,Jingwei Wu,Wenjing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于强化学习从AI反馈（RLAIF）的端到端框架，用于生成可移植的求职查询，以抽象求职者特定标识并保留通用资质。研究发现，在无评判器优化器中，性能主要由稳健的奖励设计决定，而非优化算法的选择。尽管RLOO和REINFORCE++能天然抵抗奖励欺骗，但GRPO因组相对优势归一化对虚假奖励信号敏感，易被利用。引入基于规则的确定性奖励下限可有效缓解此问题，使跨家族评估裁判下的质量提升0.147。此外，训练时奖励模型使性能增益放大2.4倍，表明训练成功关键在于奖励设计规范，而非优化器选择。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种端到端的RLAIF框架，通过结构化奖励工程与规则驱动的奖励下限设计，对抗奖励欺骗行为；采用多种基准优化方法（如RLOO、REINFORCE++、GRPO）进行对比实验，分析不同优化机制在奖励污染环境下的表现差异。

Result: 实验表明，无评判器优化器的性能高度依赖于奖励设计；引入规则基奖励下限后，查询质量显著提升0.147；训练阶段的奖励模型使性能增益放大2.4倍，说明奖励塑造比优化器选择更为关键。

Conclusion: 在面对高度对抗性的奖励表面时，成功的求职查询生成依赖于严谨的奖励工程与规则约束，而非优化算法本身。强化学习的成功应建立在对奖励信号的系统性控制之上。

Abstract: Job-search platforms rely on low-bandwidth query interfaces that often fail to capture the high-dimensional complexity of candidate profiles. We present an end-to-end RLAIF (Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback) framework to generate \emph{portable} job search queries, terms that abstract away seeker-specific identifiers while preserving generalizable qualifications. This task introduces a highly adversarial reward surface where policy optimization frequently exploits flaws in LLM-as-judge rubrics, resulting in degenerate verbatim-copying behaviors.
  We conducted comprehensive empirical experiments to isolate the impact of optimization mechanics against structured reward engineering. Our results demonstrate that for critic-free optimizers, performance is overwhelmingly dictated by robust reward shaping, rendering the specific choice of algorithm largely immaterial. While critic-free per-rollout baseline methods (RLOO and REINFORCE++) natively resist reward-hacking, the group-relative advantage normalization in GRPO appears uniquely sensitive to spurious reward signals, making it disproportionately susceptible to exploitation. We show that introducing a deterministic, rule-based reward floor to correct for rewards assigned to verbatim copying mitigates this failure mode, resulting in a substantial $+0.147$ quality improvement on a cross-family evaluation judge. Ultimately, we show that the training-time reward model inflates performance gains by $2.4\times$, confirming that the training success is fundamentally dependent on enforcing reward-shaping disciplines rather than selecting alternative optimizers.

Motivation: 实际部署深度学习模型在基于导波的结构健康监测（GWSHM）中面临标签实验数据稀缺和高保真仿真数据生成成本高的挑战，亟需一种高效且低依赖标注数据的解决方案。

Method: 构建融合轻量级物理模拟、卷积自编码器（CAE）深度特征学习、前馈神经网络及少量实验测量的多保真度迁移学习框架；利用一维时域谱元模型生成大规模合成数据进行预训练，并通过迁移学习将模型适应到真实实验域，仅需少量标注数据完成微调。

Result: 模型在损伤定位上的R²超过0.93，在损伤尺寸估计上R²达到0.99；在未见过的损伤场景中仍保持高预测精度，展现出强泛化能力；整体方案具有高精度、低计算开销和良好的工程适用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的多保真度迁移学习框架为实际应用中的导波结构健康监测提供了准确、高效且可行的技术路径，有效缓解了数据稀缺与计算成本问题，具备显著的工程推广价值。

Abstract: Guided wave-based structural health monitoring (GWSHM) with onboard transducers offers significant potential for the early diagnosis of damage in engineering structures. However, the practical deployment of deep learning models is often hindered by the limited availability of labelled experimental data and the high computational cost of generating large-scale high-fidelity simulation datasets. This study presents a multifidelity transfer learning framework that integrates lightweight physics-based simulations, convolutional autoencoder (CAE)-based deep feature learning, a feed-forward neural network, and limited experimental measurements for accurate damage localisation and sizing in plate-like structures instrumented with piezoelectric transducers. A computationally efficient one-dimensional time-domain spectral element model is employed to generate a large synthetic dataset for pretraining, while transfer learning adapts the model to experimental domains using only a small amount of labelled data. The CAE-based transfer learning framework significantly outperforms its CNN-based counterpart in damage localisation accuracy. The model achieves excellent predictive performance with $R^2$ scores exceeding 0.93 for damage localisation and 0.99 for damage sizing. Its generalisation capability is demonstrated on previously unseen data, showing high prediction accuracy for damage scenarios not represented during pretraining or fine-tuning. The results establish the proposed framework as an accurate, computationally efficient, and practically viable solution for real-world GWSHM applications.

### [326] [Blackwell Approachability and Gradient Equilibrium are Equivalent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27315)
*Brian W. Lee,Nika Haghtalab,Michael I. Jordan,Ryan J. Tibshirani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了梯度均衡（GEQ）与Blackwell可接近性在算法层面的等价性，表明GEQ可被转化为黑盒查询问题，并且能以无渐近损失的方式求解。该结果结合已知的可接近性、后悔最小化和校准之间的等价关系，进一步证明GEQ与这些在线学习框架等价。研究还提供了高效的归约方法，可用于将乐观性、强自适应性等精细保证从后悔最小化转移到GEQ。此外，文章还给出了GEQ成立的充要条件，并建立了不同设定下（如无约束与有约束决策集）的GEQ概念之间的归约关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管梯度均衡（GEQ）与已知的在线学习框架（如后悔最小化）具有相似之处，但先前研究表明GEQ误差与后悔之间不可比较，导致对GEQ在在线学习整体框架中的定位缺乏清晰理解。因此，本文旨在明确揭示GEQ与其他核心在线学习范式之间的关系。

Method: 通过建立梯度均衡（GEQ）与Blackwell可接近性之间的算法等价性，提出双向归约方法：一方面，将任何Blackwell可接近性问题转化为对黑盒GEQ oracle的查询；另一方面，也能用GEQ解决可接近性问题，且不引入渐近误差。同时，利用已知的可接近性与后悔最小化、校准之间的等价关系，推导出GEQ与这些框架的等价性。此外，分析了不同决策集设置下的GEQ形式，并给出其成立的必要与充分条件。

Result: 1. GEQ 与 Blackwell 可接近性在算法上等价，且归约保持误差率不变。2. 借助已有等价关系，证明 GEQ 与后悔最小化、校准等框架等价。3. 提出了高效归约机制，支持将后悔最小化中的精细性质（如乐观性、强自适应性）迁移至 GEQ。4. 确定了 GEQ 成立的充要条件，并建立了不同形式的 GEQ 之间的归约关系。

Conclusion: 本研究系统地揭示了梯度均衡（GEQ）在在线学习框架中的核心地位，证明其与黑格威尔可接近性、后悔最小化及校准等经典框架在算法层面等价。这一统一视角不仅深化了对GEQ的理解，也为跨框架的理论迁移和算法设计提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Gradient equilibrium (GEQ) is a recently introduced online optimization framework that generalizes first-order stationarity from offline optimization and abstracts problems like online conformal prediction. While GEQ has curious similarities with known online learning frameworks, namely regret minimization, prior work has shown that GEQ error and regret are incomparable objectives, leaving open a precise understanding of how GEQ fits into the broader online learning landscape. In this work, we show that GEQ is equivalent to Blackwell approachability in the algorithmic sense. That is, a Blackwell approachability problem can always be solved using queries to a black-box GEQ oracle, with no asymptotic loss in the oracle's error rate, and vice versa. Taken together with known equivalences between approachability, regret minimization, and calibration, these results imply that GEQ is equivalent to these frameworks, as well. Our reductions are efficient and can be used to transfer refined guarantees, such as optimism and strong adaptivity, from regret minimization to GEQ. Along the way, we also identify necessary and sufficient conditions for GEQ, and establish reductions between different notions of GEQ with unconstrained and constrained decision sets.

### [327] [Beyond the Hard Budget: Sparsity Regularizers for More Interpretable Top-k Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27321)
*Nathanaël Jacquier,Maria Vakalopoulou,Mahdi S. Hosseini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出两种与Top-$k$稀疏自编码器（SAE）架构兼容的稀疏正则化方法，分别基于未选中单元的$\ell_1$惩罚和尺度不变的$\ell_1/\ell_2$比率惩罚，均作用于批量活跃单元。实验表明，这两种正则化在不损害重建质量的前提下，显著提升特征的单义性，并增强对推理时$k$值选择的鲁棒性，尤其$\ell_1/\ell_2$惩罚能更集中信息，改善小预算线性探测性能。核心发现是：硬性架构稀疏与软性正则化具有互补性而非互斥性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Top-$k$ SAE虽避免了早期SAE中$\ell_1$惩罚的缺陷，但存在固定预算$k$、对训练$k$过拟合等问题。现有方法未将其与显式稀疏正则化结合，限制了其表现潜力。因此亟需一种既能保持架构稀疏性优势，又能通过软性正则化进一步优化表示质量的方法。

Method: 提出两种新正则化项：(1) 对未被选中的单位施加$\ell_1$惩罚；(2) 采用尺度不变的$\ell_1/\ell_2$比率惩罚，聚焦于将激活集中在更少有效单元上。二者均仅作用于在批次内至少一次被Top-$k$选中的活跃单元，以保留结构稀疏性并增强泛化能力。

Result: 在两个数据集、三种视觉基础模型及多种$k$值设置下，两种正则化均一致提升单义性，且不影响重建质量；其中$\ell_1/\ell_2$惩罚进一步压缩信息分布，提高对推理阶段$k$选择的鲁棒性，并显著改善小预算线性探测性能。

Conclusion: 硬性架构稀疏（如Top-$k$）与软性稀疏正则化并非互斥，而是可协同工作的互补机制。合理结合两者，能够更有效地构建高质量、高解释性的模型表示。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have become a leading tool for interpreting the representations of vision foundation models, decomposing their polysemantic activations into a larger set of sparse, more monosemantic features. The Top-$k$ SAE, a now-standard variant, enforces sparsity architecturally through its activation function, retaining only the $k$ most active latents per input. Because it was designed precisely to avoid the $\ell_1$ penalty used by earlier SAEs and its known drawbacks, it has not been combined with an explicit sparsity regularizer, despite retaining limitations of its own, such as a budget $k$ that is fixed regardless of input complexity and a tendency to overfit to the training value of $k$. We introduce two sparsity regularizers compatible with the Top-$k$ architecture, both acting on the activations before the Top-$k$ selection: an $\ell_1$ penalty on the unselected (off-support) units, and a scale-invariant $\ell_1/\ell_2$-ratio penalty that concentrates the code onto fewer effective units. Both penalties are applied only to the batch-active units, those selected by the Top-$k$ operator at least once within the batch. Across two datasets, three vision foundation models, and a range of $k$, both regularizers consistently improve monosemanticity at no cost to reconstruction quality. The $\ell_1/\ell_2$ penalty further concentrates information into fewer latents, making reconstruction more robust to the inference-time choice of $k$ and improving small-budget linear probing. Our central finding is that hard architectural sparsity and soft sparsity regularization are complementary rather than mutually exclusive.

</details>


### [328] [Hallucination in World Models is Predictable and Preventable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27326)
*Nicklas Hansen,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对生成式世界模型中幻觉问题的系统性解决方案，通过构建大规模数据集MMBench2和设计覆盖感知采样与幻觉预测机制，实现对低覆盖率区域的精准检测与数据高效优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式世界模型虽能生成流畅视觉序列，但常在状态-动作空间的低覆盖率区域出现幻觉，导致模拟偏离真实动态，亟需有效检测与缓解方法。

Method: 引入MMBench2数据集（427小时、210个任务），训练350M参数世界模型；识别出三种幻觉模式（感知型、动作边缘型、场景偏离型），并设计对应信号进行预测；提出覆盖感知采样策略用于训练时补全数据覆盖，同时利用幻觉预测作为好奇心奖励驱动在线数据收集，实现仅用50条真实轨迹即可适配新环境的高效微调。

Result: 实验表明，幻觉主要集中在低覆盖率区域；所提信号可准确预测失败位置；覆盖感知采样与基于幻觉预测的在线学习显著提升模型在未见环境中的泛化能力，验证了幻觉本质为数据覆盖不足的问题。

Conclusion: 幻觉在世界模型中本质上是数据覆盖不足所致，且用于检测幻觉的信号也可直接用于引导数据采集与模型优化，实现高效、鲁棒的模型适应。

Abstract: Modern generative world models render increasingly realistic action-controllable futures, yet they frequently hallucinate: rollouts remain visually fluent while drifting from the ground-truth dynamics. We hypothesize that hallucination concentrates in low-coverage regions of the state-action space, where lightweight data-centric signals can both detect it and guide mitigation. To test this, we introduce MMBench2, a 427-hour, 210-task dataset for visual world modeling with ground-truth actions, rewards, and live simulators, and train a 350M-parameter world model on it. We identify three distinct hallucination modes: perceptual, action-marginalized, and scene-diverging -- each anchored to a different stage of the pipeline, and develop three signals that accurately predict where the model will fail. To close coverage gaps at training time, we develop a coverage-aware sampling technique; to close them online, our hallucination predictors serve as curiosity rewards for targeted data collection, yielding a data-efficient finetuning recipe that adapts the pretrained world model to entirely unseen environments with as few as 50 real environment trajectories. Overall, our findings reveal that hallucination in world models is inherently a data coverage issue, and that the same signals used to detect it can also be used for mitigation.
  An interactive web version of our paper is available at https://www.nicklashansen.com/mmbench2

### [329] [Error-Conditioned Neural Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27354)
*Haina Jiang,Liam Wang,Peng-Chen Chen,Min Seop Kwak,Seungryong Kim,Brian Bell,Jeong Joon Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为误差条件神经求解器（ENS）的新方法，通过将PDE残差场作为输入直接指导网络迭代修正预测，克服了传统神经代理模型在约束违反和分布外泛化上的局限。相比依赖残差优化的混合方法，ENS避免了高昂计算成本且在多种偏微分方程（PDE）任务中显著提升预测精度，尤其在病态系统中表现更优，具备良好的零样本参数迁移与跨方程泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经代理模型在处理偏微分方程（PDE）求解时，通常将其视为纯统计问题，训练后难以纠正自身约束违反或外推至训练分布之外；虽然近期混合方法尝试通过最小化PDE残差来增强物理一致性，但继承了经典优化器的计算开销与不稳定性。此外，研究发现残差最小化在病态系统中并非重建准确性的可靠代理，导致这些方法即使残差低也未必预测准确。因此亟需一种更鲁棒、高效且能自适应纠错的新型求解框架。

Method: 提出误差条件神经求解器（ENS），其核心思想是不再将PDE残差作为优化目标，而是将其作为每一步迭代中的直接输入特征，使网络能够感知自身预测的空间误差结构，并学习一个可迭代更新的修正策略。该方法通过端到端训练获得具有自校正能力的神经求解器，无需依赖外部优化器进行梯度下降或高斯-牛顿步。

Result: 在四个不同类型的PDE家族上测试，ENS在绝大多数场景下实现了最高的预测精度，特别是在湍流科莫戈罗夫流动中性能提升达10倍；同时，其计算开销远低于传统混合方法。更重要的是，ENS在分布外泛化方面表现出色，包括零样本参数变化和跨方程迁移，在病态系统中优势尤为明显。

Conclusion: ENS通过引入残差场作为输入而非优化目标，构建了一种更稳定、高效且具备强泛化能力的神经求解机制。该方法有效解决了传统神经代理模型在物理一致性与外推能力方面的关键缺陷，为复杂系统建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Neural surrogate models offer fast approximate mappings from PDE parameters to solutions, but they typically treat solving as a purely statistical task: once trained, they struggle to correct their own constraint violations and extrapolate beyond the training distribution. Recent hybrid methods promote physical correctness by targeting the PDE residual via gradient descent or Gauss--Newton steps, but inherit the compute cost and instability of the underlying classical optimizers. We show, theoretically and empirically, that numerically minimizing the PDE residual can be an unreliable proxy for reconstruction accuracy in ill-conditioned systems, explaining why these methods often do not make accurate predictions despite achieving low residuals. We propose error-conditioned Neural Solvers (ENS), built on a different principle: rather than an optimization target, the PDE residual field is passed as a direct input to the network at each iteration, enabling it to read the spatial structure of its own errors and learn an update policy to iteratively correct its predictions. Across four PDE families, ENS attains the highest prediction accuracy in the large majority of settings, with gains reaching $10\times$ on turbulent Kolmogorov flow, while avoiding the expensive compute cost of hybrid methods. ENS's learned correction policy generalizes under distribution shift, including zero-shot parameter changes and cross-equation transfer, where its relative advantage is largest in the ill-conditioned regimes where residual minimization is least reliable. Project website: https://neuralsolver.github.io/.

</details>


### [330] [Autoregressive Boltzmann Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27361)
*Danyal Rehman,Charlie B. Tan,Yoshua Bengio,Avishek Joey Bose,Alexander Tong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的自回归玻尔兹曼生成器（ArBG），克服了传统基于流的玻尔兹曼生成器在表达能力与计算效率上的局限。ArBG采用自回归框架，摆脱了流模型的拓扑约束，支持推理时的序列干预，并具备更好的可扩展性，尤其适用于大分子系统如10残基的Chignolin肽。实验表明，ArBG在多个基准测试中显著优于现有方法，特别是在大系统上表现突出。研究还推出了一个1.32亿参数的可迁移模型Robin，其在8残基系统的零样本能量误差上相比之前最优方法降低了60%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统玻尔兹曼生成器依赖于归一化流（NFs），受限于严格可逆性导致表达能力不足，或连续时间模型带来高昂的似然计算成本。因此亟需一种更高效、更具表达力且可扩展的生成框架来实现分子系统在热力学平衡下的快速采样。

Method: 提出自回归玻尔兹曼生成器（ArBG），采用自回归建模结构，摆脱了流模型对可逆性的要求，通过序列化生成方式实现灵活的推理干预，并利用类大语言模型的架构提升可扩展性。结合重要性采样校正以保持精确似然性。

Result: ArBG在所有测试基准上均优于基于流的模型，尤其在10残基的Chignolin等大型肽系统中表现显著提升。所提出的Robin模型在8残基系统上将零样本能量误差（E-W₂）降低超过60%，达到新状态水平。

Conclusion: ArBG提供了一种高效、可扩展且表达能力强的替代方案，突破了传统流式玻尔兹曼生成器的瓶颈，为复杂分子系统的快速平衡采样提供了新范式。

Abstract: Efficient sampling of molecular systems at thermodynamic equilibrium is a hallmark challenge in statistical physics. This challenge has driven the development of Boltzmann Generators (BGs), which allow rapid generation of uncorrelated equilibrium samples by combining a generative model with exact likelihoods and an importance sampling correction. However, modern BGs predominantly rely on normalizing flows (NFs), which either suffer from limited expressivity due to strict invertibility constraints (discrete time) or computationally expensive likelihoods (continuous time). In this paper, we propose Autoregressive Boltzmann Generators (ArBG) -- a novel autoregressive modelling framework -- that overcomes these limitations by departing from the flow-based BG paradigm. ArBG circumvents the topological constraints of flows and enables sequential inference-time interventions, while offering enhanced scalability by leveraging architectures effective in Large Language Models. We empirically demonstrate that ArBG leads to significant improvements over flow-based models across all benchmarks, but particularly in larger peptide systems such as the 10-residue Chignolin. Furthermore, we introduce Robin, a 132 million parameter transferable model trained with the ArBG framework which improves over the previous state-of-the-art, reducing the zero-shot energy error, E-W$_2$, on 8-residue systems by over 60$\%$. The code can be found at the following link: https://github.com/danyalrehman/autobg.

### [331] [Reinforcement Learning without Ground-Truth Solutions can Improve LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27369)
*Yingyu Lin,Qiyue Gao,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Xunpeng Huang,Kun Zhou,Tongtong Liang,Zhewei Yao,Yi-An Ma,Yuxiong He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RiVER 是一种无需真实答案即可训练大语言模型的强化学习框架，通过基于执行反馈的连续奖励进行优化。它解决了规模主导和频率主导两大挑战，采用实例级比较与奖励校准机制，显著提升模型在多个编程任务上的表现，尤其在无真值解的任务中仍能有效提升通用编码能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法依赖真实答案作为奖励信号，限制了其在缺乏真值解的任务中的应用。本文旨在开发一种不依赖真值解、可利用分数优化任务进行训练的新框架。

Method: 提出 RiVER 框架，结合群体相对强化学习与校准奖励机制，利用实例间比较和对高排名解的强调来缓解奖励偏差问题，并使用确定性执行反馈作为连续监督信号。

Result: 在 12 个 AtCoder 任务上训练后，RiVER 在 ALE-Bench 上使 Qwen3-8B 和 GLM-Z1-9B-0414 的评分排名分别提升 8.9% 和 9.4%；同时在 LiveCodeBench 和 USACO 等精确解基准上也取得平均 2.4% 和 3.5% 的绝对提升，优于仅使用原始执行分数的基线方法。

Conclusion: 基于分数优化的任务配合适当的奖励校准，可在无真值解的情况下有效训练出具备通用编程能力的大语言模型，为大规模代码生成提供了新路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for training LLMs typically rely on ground-truth answers to assign rewards, limiting their applicability to tasks where the ground-truth solution is unknown. We introduce a \textbf{R}anking-\textbf{i}nduced \textbf{VER}ifiable framework (RiVER) that trains LLMs on score-based optimization tasks without ground-truth solutions, using deterministic execution feedback as continuous-valued supervision. When applying group-relative RL to such continuous rewards, we identify two key challenges: \emph{scale dominance}, where uncalibrated score magnitudes across test instances distort policy updates, and \emph{frequency dominance}, where repeatedly sampled suboptimal solutions can outweigh rare but stronger candidates. RiVER addresses these challenges with calibrated reward shaping that uses instance-wise comparisons and emphasizes top-ranked solvers while retaining bounded feedback for other valid solutions. We train on 12 AtCoder Heuristic Contest tasks and evaluate on Algorithm Engineering Benchmark (ALE-Bench), LiveCodeBench, and USACO. RiVER advances Qwen3-8B and GLM-Z1-9B-0414 by 8.9\% and 9.4\% in ALE rating rank. More importantly, despite training exclusively on score-based tasks without any ground-truth solutions, RiVER also improves the backbones across exact-solution benchmarks such as LiveCodeBench and USACO by an absolute average improvement of 2.4\% and 3.5\%. By contrast, baselines trained with raw execution scores improve ALE rating but fail to transfer to exact-solution benchmarks. These results suggest that score-based optimization tasks, combined with proper reward calibration, can serve as effective training environments for general coding ability without ground-truth solutions.

</details>
